### [1] [Deposition and Growth of the AlCoCuFeNi High-Entropy Alloy Thin Film: Molecular Dynamics Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19582)
*Oleksandr I. Kushnerov,Valerij F. Bashev,Sergey I. Ryabtsev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文利用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）建模，系统研究了高熵AlCoCuFeNi合金薄膜在硅（100）衬底上的生长过程。模拟采用嵌入原子模型（embedded atom model）和Lennard-Jones势能等描述原子间相互作用，发现薄膜生长初期形成小团簇，约5 ns后开始结晶，最终形成面心立方、体心立方、密排六方和非晶相等多种相结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金（high-entropy alloy）薄膜的微观生长机制尚不明确，尤其是多主元原子在衬底上的沉积、成核和结晶过程缺乏原子尺度的理解。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）建模，利用嵌入原子模型（embedded atom model）描述Al、Co、Cu、Ni、Fe原子间的相互作用，用Lennard-Jones势能描述合金原子与Si衬底的相互作用，用Stillinger-Weber势能描述硅原子间的相互作用，总模拟时长为50 ns。

Result: 沉积初期形成小团簇；约5 ns后开始结晶，此时特征团簇尺寸约为2 nm。50 ns模拟结束时，薄膜中包含面心立方（face-centered cubic, FCC）、体心立方（body-centered cubic, BCC）、密排六方（hexagonal close-packed, HCP）和非晶相（amorphous phase）。径向分布函数（radial distribution function）分析确定了最近邻距离并估算了各相的晶格参数。

Conclusion: 高熵AlCoCuFeNi合金薄膜在硅衬底上的生长经历团簇形成、结晶和多相共存等阶段，分子动力学方法能够有效揭示其微观结构演化规律。

Abstract: The growth of a thin film of a high-entropy AlCoCuFeNi alloy on a silicon (100) substrate was studied using molecular dynamics modeling. The simulation was carried out using the embedded atom model to describe the interactions among Al, Co, Cu, Ni, and Fe atoms. The interaction between Al, Co, Cu, Fe, Ni atoms and the Si substrate was modeled using the Lennard-Jones potential, while the interaction between silicon atoms was described using the Stillinger-Weber potential. The total simulation time was 50 ns. It was found that small clusters were formed at the first stage of deposition and that crystallization started after approximately 5 ns of simulation, when the characteristic cluster size was about 2 nm. At the end of the simulation, after 50 ns of modeling, the simulated film contained face-centered cubic, body-centered cubic, hexagonal close-packed, and amorphous phases. Analysis of the radial distribution function made it possible to determine nearest-neighbor distances and estimate the lattice parameters of these phases.

</details>


### [2] [Charge-state control of carbon-related optical absorption in AlN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19615)
*Helen C. Robinson,Daniil Danilin,Md Shafiqul Islam Mollik,Darshana Wickramaratne,John L. Lyons,Vladimir Fedorov,Sergey Mirov,M. E. Zvanut*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过光诱导电子顺磁共振（photo-EPR）与光学吸收光谱实验，结合第一性原理计算，证实了AlN中2–4 eV亚带隙光学吸收的微观起源为氮位取代碳的中性电荷态（C$_N$）到价带的跃迁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AlN在2 eV至4 eV范围内普遍存在亚带隙光学吸收（sub-bandgap optical absorption），但其微观起源长期存在争议，亟需通过实验与理论相结合的手段加以澄清。

Method: 在相同样品上同时开展光诱导电子顺磁共振（photo-induced electron paramagnetic resonance, photo-EPR）和光学吸收光谱实验，以关联吸收带与缺陷电荷态；采用混合泛函（hybrid functional）计算光学吸收谱，模拟C$_N$到价带的跃迁过程。

Result: 实验表明该吸收带与氮位取代碳的中性电荷态（C$_N$）相关；混合泛函计算显示C$_N$到价带的跃迁发生在约3.3 eV处，与实测2–4 eV范围内的吸收峰吻合良好。

Conclusion: AlN中2–4 eV亚带隙吸收的微观起源可归因于C$_N$中性电荷态的光激发跃迁；该结论依赖于photo-EPR调控碳缺陷电荷态的能力，以及考虑价带色散和光学矩阵元能量依赖性的第一性原理吸收线形计算。

Abstract: Sub-bandgap optical absorption in AlN between 2 eV and 4 eV is widely observed, but its microscopic origin remains contested. Using photo-induced electron paramagnetic resonance (photo-EPR) and optical absorption spectroscopy on the same samples, we demonstrate a correlation between this absorption band and the neutral charge state of substitutional carbon on the nitrogen site (C$_N$). Hybrid functional calculations of the optical absorption spectra show that a transition involving C$_N$ and the valence band occurs near 3.3 eV, which agrees well with a peak identified within the measured optical absorption between 2 eV and 4 eV. This conclusion requires the combined ability to manipulate the charge state of carbon using photo-EPR and to use first-principles calculations of the absorption line shape that account for the dispersion of the valence band and the energy dependence of the optical matrix elements.

</details>


### [3] [Coordination-Sensitive Nanoscale Analysis of Defect-Driven Phase Transformation in Si-Doped (AlXGa1-X)2O3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19653)
*Shaon Das,Jith Sarker,Christopher Chae,Lingyu Meng,Joel B. Varley,Hongping Zhao,Jinwoo Hwang,Baishakhi Mazumder*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种配位敏感型原子探针层析（coordination-sensitive atom probe tomography）框架，通过定量解析局域阳离子配位数的降低，将缺陷驱动的相不稳定性与纳米尺度的结构转变直接关联起来，并在Si掺杂β-(Al_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3异质结构中验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超宽禁带氧化物（ultrawide bandgap oxides）中缺陷驱动的相不稳定性（defect-driven phase instability）严重影响结构可靠性，但缺乏将局域化学信息与结构转变直接联系的纳米尺度定量指标。

Method: 开发了配位敏感型原子探针层析（coordination-sensitive atom probe tomography）框架，结合二维组分映射、最近邻分析（nearest-neighbor analysis）和径向分布分析（radial distribution analysis），并通过关联扫描透射电子显微镜（correlative scanning transmission electron microscopy）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行验证。

Result: 在Al含量升高（6-17%）且重Si掺杂（10^17-10^20 cm^-3）条件下，γ相夹杂物仅在两者共同存在时出现；二维组分映射显示显著的横向Al/Ga不均匀性；最近邻和径向分布分析定量解析出第一壳层Ga配位数的显著降低；DFT表明Al掺入降低单斜晶格稳定性，与施主诱导空位形成共同促进空位介导的阳离子重排和配位塌缩。

Conclusion: 配位损失（coordination loss）可作为缺陷驱动相不稳定性的可测量纳米尺度特征，该框架为掺杂和合金化超宽禁带半导体中缺陷驱动相不稳定性的探测提供了一种通用方法。

Abstract: Defect-driven phase instability critically influences the structural reliability of ultrawide bandgap oxides, yet direct nanoscale metrics linking local chemistry to structural transformation remain limited. Here, we introduce a coordination-sensitive atom probe tomography framework that quantitatively resolves reductions in local cation coordination and links them directly to defect-driven phase transformation. Using Si-doped beta-(AlxGa1-x)2O3 heterostructures with controlled Al composition (6-17%) and doping levels (10^17-10^20 cm^-3), we show that gamma-phase inclusions emerge exclusively under the combined conditions of elevated Al content and heavy Si doping. Two-dimensional compositional mapping reveals pronounced lateral Al/Ga inhomogeneity in these regions, while nearest-neighbor and radial distribution analyses quantitatively resolve a significant reduction in first-shell Ga coordination, consistent with local cation deficiency. Correlative scanning transmission electron microscopy confirms that these coordination-depleted regions coincide spatially with gamma-phase inclusions. Density functional theory further supports this mechanism, demonstrating that Al incorporation reduces monoclinic lattice stability and, in conjunction with donor-induced vacancy formation, facilitates vacancy-mediated cation rearrangement and coordination collapse. Together, these results establish coordination loss as a measurable nanoscale signature directly linked to defect-driven phase instability. This framework provides a generalizable approach for probing defect-driven phase instability in doped and alloyed ultrawide bandgap semiconductors.

</details>


### [4] [HEACalculator: An Open-Source Python Tool for Thermodynamic Property Calculation and Solid Solution Prediction in High-Entropy Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19661)
*Doğuhan Sarıtürk,Yunus Eren Kalay,Raymundo Arróyave*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: HEACalculator是一个开源Python软件包，用于计算高熵合金（HEA）的热力学和结构描述符，并评估八种已发表的固溶体形成规则，提供命令行、图形界面和Python API三种访问模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金（high-entropy alloys, HEAs）设计中的一个重复性问题是判断候选成分是否会形成单相固溶体（single-phase solid solution）还是分离为多相或金属间化合物（intermetallic compounds）。该问题处于合金设计流程的早期阶段，决定了哪些成分需要进一步的热力学分析、合成和实验验证。

Method: HEACalculator是一个开源的Python软件包，整合了经过筛选的元素和二元相互作用数据集（elemental and binary-interaction dataset），计算十六种常用物理量，包括混合焓（mixing enthalpy）、构型熵（configurational entropy）、价电子浓度（valence electron concentration）、Hume-Rothery电子-原子比、原子尺寸失配（atomic size mismatch）、电负性失配（electronegativity mismatch）以及Omega、Lambda、Phi等衍生的稳定性参数，并评估八种已发表的预测判据。软件提供三种访问模式：命令行界面（CLI）、桌面图形用户界面（GUI）和Python应用程序编程接口（API）。

Result: 该软件包能够在单一平台上统一计算高熵合金研究中常用的热力学和结构描述符，并评估多种固溶体形成规则，支持交互式使用和程序化批量筛选工作流。

Conclusion: HEACalculator为高熵合金设计提供了一个开源、统一的计算工具，有助于在研究工作流早期阶段加速对候选成分的筛选与评估。

Abstract: High-entropy alloys (HEAs) have attracted sustained interest since their introduction by Cantor et al. and Yeh et al. because multi-principal-element compositions can exhibit unusual combinations of strength, thermal stability, and functional performance. A recurring problem in HEA design is determining whether a candidate composition is likely to form a single-phase solid solution or instead separate into multiple phases or intermetallic compounds. That question sits early in the alloy-design workflow because it shapes which compositions require further thermodynamic analysis, synthesis, and experimental validation. HEACalculator is an open-source Python package for calculating thermodynamic and structural descriptors used in HEA research and for evaluating published solid-solution formation rules in a single place. It computes sixteen commonly used quantities, including mixing enthalpy, configurational entropy, valence electron concentration, Hume-Rothery electron-to-atom ratio, atomic size mismatch, electronegativity mismatch, and derived stability parameters such as Omega, Lambda, and Phi, and it evaluates eight published prediction criteria. The package combines a curated elemental and binary-interaction dataset with three access modes: a command-line interface (CLI), a desktop graphical user interface (GUI), and a Python application programming interface (API) for programmatic use in notebooks and screening workflows.

</details>


### [5] [Enhanced electronic correlations and altermagnetic ground state of two-dimensional CsCr3Sb5 monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19740)
*Z. H. Guan,Z. L. Peng,W. Z. Zhuo,G. Tian,Z. P. Hou,D. Y. Chen,Z. Fan,X. B. Lu,X. S. Gao,M. H. Qin,J. M. Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，研究了二维Cr3Sb5和CsCr3Sb5单层的电子结构，发现平带和范霍夫奇点（vHSs）均靠近费米能级（EF），且拉伸应变可进一步将其调控至EF附近；同时揭示了交替磁（altermagnetic）基态的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 块体CsCr3Sb5中的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities, vHSs）远离费米能级（Fermi level, EF），而将vHS有效调控至EF附近对于探索有趣的电子输运性质至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究可能从块体材料机械剥离得到的二维Cr3Sb5和CsCr3Sb5单层的电子结构。

Result: Cr3Sb5单层中，平带（flat bands）和vHSs同时紧邻EF，表明电子关联增强；拉伸应变（tensile strain）可进一步将两个单层的平带和vHSs移至EF附近；同时，由于两个子晶格之间保留了镜像对称性（mirror symmetry），两个单层均呈现交替磁（altermagnetic）基态。

Conclusion: 该工作推进了对二维CsCr3Sb5单层电子性质的理解与调控，强化了其在探索非常规量子现象（unconventional quantum phenomena）和交替磁性（altermagnetism）方面的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Recently, layered corrected kagome metal CsCr3Sb5 have garnered significant attention attributed to its flat bands near the Fermi level (EF) and altermagnetic ground state [ Yi Liu et al., Nature 632, 1032 (2024)]. However, the van Hove singularities (vHSs) in bulk CsCr3Sb5 are far away from the EF, while an effective modulation of VHS toward the EF is essential for exploring intriguing electron transport properties. In this work, using first-principles calculations, we investigate electronic structures of two-dimensional (2D) Cr3Sb5 and CsCr3Sb5 monolayers which may be mechanically exfoliated from bulk materials. Notably, it is revealed that both flat bands and vHSs simultaneously reside in close proximity to the EF in Cr3Sb5 monolayer, signifying enhanced electronic correlations. Importantly, a tensile strain further shifts the incipient flat bands and vHSs of two monolayers simultaneously to the vicinity of the EF, suggesting strain tunable electronic correlations and concomitant quantum effects. Furthermore, altermagnetic ground state is also revealed due to retained mirror symmetry between two sublattices in these two monolayers. Thus, this work advances understanding and modulations of electronic properties of 2D CsCr3Sb5 monolayers, strengthening their great potential for exploring unconventional quantum phenomena and altermagnetism.

</details>


### [6] [Thickness-Dependent Interlayer Coupling and Semiconductor-to-Semimetal Crossover in Arsenene Multilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19780)
*Jeonghwan Ahn,Seoung-Hun Kang,Jaron T. Krogel*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文结合扩散量子蒙特卡洛（diffusion quantum Monte Carlo, DMC）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT），研究了砷烯多层膜中层间耦合随厚度的演化。DMC表明块体灰砷为致密结构，而少层体系保持较大层间距。堆叠序列（stacking sequence）从A₁A₁向A₁B₁再向块体状A₁B₋₁转变，这种结构交叉与依赖于堆叠的能带隙闭合（band-gap collapse）同时发生，间隙闭合由增强的层间As p_z杂化驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状材料中层间相互作用通常被认为可以从双层外推到块体，但当化学活性面外轨道参与成键时，该假设可能失效。本文旨在检验这一假设在砷烯多层膜中的适用性。

Method: 采用扩散量子蒙特卡洛（DMC）和密度泛函理论（DFT）相结合的方法，系统研究砷烯多层膜中层间耦合的演化规律，并用DMC基准检验多种泛函的准确性。

Result: DMC显示块体灰砷为致密结构，而少层砷烯保持显著更大的层间距。SCAN+rVV10泛函最接近DMC的平衡层间距和堆叠能量。预测了厚度驱动的堆叠序列转变：A₁A₁ → A₁B₁ → 块体状A₁B₋₁，该结构交叉伴随依赖于堆叠的DFT能带隙闭合。

Conclusion: 仅凭层间堆叠方式（registry）不足以决定键合状态；厚度和配位数共同重塑了层间相互作用。层间As p_z杂化的增强是能带隙闭合的关键驱动因素。

Abstract: Interlayer interactions in layered materials are often assumed to transfer from the bilayer to the bulk, but this assumption can fail when chemically active out-of-plane orbitals participate in bonding. We combine diffusion quantum Monte Carlo (DMC) and density functional theory (DFT) to determine how interlayer coupling evolves in arsenene multilayers. DMC shows that bulk gray arsenic is compact, whereas the corresponding few-layer structures remain at substantially larger interlayer separations despite sharing the same nominal A$_{1}$B$_{-1}$ adjacent-layer registry. Registry alone therefore does not determine the bonding regime; thickness and coordination reshape the interlayer interaction. Among the tested functionals, SCAN+rVV10 most closely reproduces DMC equilibrium separations and stacking energetics. Using the DMC-benchmarked SCAN+rVV10 calculations, we predict a thickness-driven stacking sequence from A$_{1}$A$_{1}$ to A$_{1}$B$_{1}$ and finally bulk-like A$_{1}$B$_{-1}$. The structural crossover coincides with a stacking-dependent DFT band-gap collapse driven by enhanced interlayer As p$_{z}$ hybridization.

</details>


### [7] [MinSurf: resolving the atomic-scale stability landscape of mineral surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19798)
*Fengzijun Pan,Zhoulin Liu,Pingyang Zhang,Jiaqiu Xu,Zepeng Fan,Dawei Wang,Jianzhong Pei*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了MinSurf高通量框架，通过表面枚举、DFT标记、机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials）和Wulff构造（Wulff construction）的系统集成，解决了矿物表面选择中原子终止面（atomic termination）的预测问题。该框架在十个代表性矿物上构建了764个表面板数据集MinSurfSet，并训练了MinNEP模型，其预测DFT表面能的平均绝对误差为0.0119 eV/Å²，加速比达1.14×10⁴倍，能够准确再现平衡晶体形貌（equilibrium crystal morphology）和Wulff暴露面（Wulff-exposed facets）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矿物表面在碳矿化、地质能源储存、污染物固定、多相催化和电化学界面工程中控制着界面反应性，但传统原子模拟常依赖常用晶面或面级稳定性判据，同一晶向（crystallographic orientation）下不同原子终止面因实验表征和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算成本高昂而很少被系统解析。

Method: MinSurf框架整合了表面枚举、DFT标记、机器学习原子间势和Wulff构造四个模块，以预测稳定终止面、表面能景观（surface-energy landscape）和平衡晶体形貌。通过十个代表性矿物构建MinSurfSet数据集（含764个表面板及90个取向单胞作为体参考），并在此基础上训练MinNEP模型。

Result: MinNEP模型预测DFT表面能的平均绝对误差（MAE）为0.0119 eV/Å²，相对于DFT实现1.14×10⁴倍的总体加速。模型保留了DFT推导的形貌决定性表面能层级结构，并再现了主要Wulff暴露面；α-石英基准的X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）提供了独立的晶体学一致性验证。

Conclusion: MinSurf通过连接原子终止面、表面能和平衡形貌，为能源、环境和先进无机材料领域的矿物界面高通量模拟提供了可重复且具有物理代表性的表面模型。

Abstract: Mineral surfaces govern interfacial reactivity in carbon mineralization, geo-energy storage, contaminant immobilization, heterogeneous catalysis and electrochemical interface engineering. Yet atomistic simulations often rely on commonly used facets or facet-level stability criteria, while distinct atomic terminations of the same crystallographic orientation are rarely resolved systematically because experimental characterization and density functional theory (DFT) calculations remain costly across large surface spaces. Here we present MinSurf, a high-throughput framework that resolves mineral surface selection as a surface-energy and morphology problem. MinSurf integrates surface enumeration, DFT labelling, machine-learning interatomic potentials and Wulff construction to predict stable terminations, surface-energy landscapes and equilibrium crystal morphologies. Applied to ten representative minerals, MinSurfSet comprises 764 surface slabs, with 90 corresponding oriented unit cells constructed as bulk references for surface-energy evaluation. The resulting MinNEP model predicts DFT surface energies with a mean absolute error of 0.0119 eV per Angstrom squared and achieves an overall acceleration of 1.14 x 10^4 relative to DFT. MinNEP preserves the DFT-derived morphology-determining surface-energy hierarchy and reproduces the dominant Wulff-exposed facets, while X-ray diffraction provides an independent crystallographic consistency check for alpha-quartz benchmark. By linking atomic terminations, surface energies and equilibrium morphologies, MinSurf provides reproducible and physically representative surface models for high-throughput simulations of mineral interfaces across energy, environmental and advanced inorganic materials.

</details>


### [8] [Strain- and Electric-Field-Tunable Valley Polarization in Mo0.75V0.25Te2(Mo3VTe8) for Valleytronic Application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19954)

Abstract: Valley polarization in 2D TMDs is promising for low-power valleytronic and spin-valley information processing, but time-reversal symmetry in pristine nonmagnetic TMDs keeps the K+ and K- valleys degenerate, limiting device applications. In this work, we investigated the structural stability, electronic properties, and tunable valley polarization of V-alloyed MoTe2 monolayer, Mo0.75V0.25Te2, using first-principles density functional theory (DFT) calculations. Substitutional alloying of MoTe2 with V introduced magnetic exchange interaction, which, together with spin-orbit coupling (SOC), lifted the valley degeneracy at the unequal valleys. The alloyed structure was found to be energetically and dynamically stable due to the absence of imaginary phonon modes. In pristine MoTe2, SOC produced spin splittings of 34.0 meV and 218.9 meV in the conduction bands and valence bands, respectively, but no valley polarization was observed. In contrast, Mo0.75V0.25Te2 exhibited spontaneous valley polarization of 37.3 meV in the conduction band and 78.2 meV in the valence band. The valley polarization was further enhanced by external electric fields and biaxial strain. A transverse electric field along the crystal c axis produced the maximum valley splitting of 132.8 meV in the valence band, whereas biaxial tensile strain increased the valence band valley splitting up to 160.8 meV. The maximum conduction band valley splitting reached 54.4 meV under 2% biaxial compressive strain. These results demonstrated that V alloying, combined with electric-field and strain engineering, provides an effective strategy for achieving large and tunable valley polarization in MoTe2. Thus, Mo0.75V0.25Te2 can be considered a promising 2D platform for tunable valleytronic device applications, such as transistors and sensors.

*Bhautik R Dhori,Deepak Upadhyay,Prafulla K Jha*

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）、通用堆垛理论（general stacking theory）和自旋劳厄对称性分析（spin-Laue symmetry analysis），提出并表征了耦合准交变磁态；通过二维Lieb晶格材料Mn2WS4及其Janus衍生物Mn2WS2Se2进行案例验证。

Here, using first-principles calculations, general stacking theory, and spin-Laue symmetry analysis, we propose a coupled quasialtermagnetic state representing a distinct subclass of altermagnetism, in which reversible type-IV NRSS is controlled through interlayer sliding. We establish a direct correspondence between reciprocal-space spin splitting and real-space switching between the two quasi-altermagnetic states. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在LAPW框架中，通过一致地构造径向基函数（radial basis functions）和核心轨道（core orbitals），使其与HF哈密顿量（HF Hamiltonian）相容，从而克服标准方法在非局域交换处理上的限制。

Result: 该方法使分子和固体的总能量精度达到数个μHa；为14种半导体和绝缘体提供了参考数据；标准方法基于（半）局域势构建径向基函数和核心轨道，在相对能量（如分子和固态形成能、Si自间隙缺陷形成能）方面仍保持高精度。

Abstract: This study establishes a route to the Hartree--Fock (HF) limit for molecules and solids within the linearized augmented plane wave (LAPW) framework. We remove current limitations of the standard LAPW approach to nonlocal exchange by constructing radial basis functions and core orbitals consistently with the HF Hamiltonian. The presented method yields total energies of molecules and solids with a precision of a few $μ$Ha, and we use it to provide reference data for 14 semiconductors and insulators. For the systems considered in this study, the standard approach based on (semi)local potentials for constructing radial basis functions and core orbitals remains highly precise for practical relative energies, including molecular and solid-state formation energies and Si self-interstitial defect formation energies. More broadly, the results provide stringent all-electron benchmarks for basis-set and pseudopotential assessment, improve error control in hybrid-functional calculations within LAPW, and open the way to X-ray spectroscopy simulations within LAPW based directly on hybrid-functional core orbitals.

### [13] [Large spin splitting at ferromagnetic surfaces of bulk antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20178)
*William A. Schaarman,Sophie F. Weber*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory）和模型哈密顿量（model Hamiltonian）揭示，在低对称性的反铁磁体（antiferromagnet, AFM）表面，由于对称性允许的净磁化与体态简并解除，可以实现从约10 meV到约1 eV的大幅自旋劈裂（spin splitting），为在反铁磁材料中实现功能性自旋劈裂提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找兼具反铁磁体（AFM）的鲁棒性和超快动力学特性与大自旋劈裂（spin splitting）功能的新材料平台，而大自旋劈裂通常仅局限于铁磁体（ferromagnet）。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）和模型哈密顿量（model Hamiltonian）进行计算分析；以$\mathrm{Cr_2O_3}$和$\mathrm{FeF_2}$为例进行第一性原理计算验证。

Result: 发现两种铁磁表面构型可实现最大自旋劈裂：单未补偿磁子格（sublattice）终止面和双子格表面（体态中磁性与电子补偿，但表面截断后晶体场环境不同）。后者可产生类铁磁自旋劈裂幅度，同时净磁化强度可忽略不计；而由相对论性倾斜（canting）产生的表面磁化则自旋劈裂较小。$\mathrm{Cr_2O_3}$和$\mathrm{FeF_2}$的计算结果显示劈裂范围在约10 meV到约1 eV之间。

Conclusion: 本征表面对称性破缺（intrinsic surface symmetry breaking）是在更广泛的反铁磁材料中实现大、功能性自旋劈裂的有效途径。

Abstract: We use density functional theory and model Hamiltonians to reveal large spin splitting of bands localized at low-symmetry, ferromagnetic surfaces of bulk antiferromagnets (AFMs). There is great interest in finding new material platforms combining the robustness and ultrafast dynamics of AFMs with large, functional spin splitting which is often restricted to ferromagnets. Here, we show that a subset of AFM surfaces which have symmetry-allowed magnetization can host large spin splitting via bulk degeneracy lifting of sublattice-resolved exchange splittings. Using model Hamiltonians, we show that the spin splitting is maximized for two ferromagnetic surface motifs: terminations with single uncompensated magnetic sublattices, and two-sublattice surfaces whose sublattices are magnetically and electronically compensated in the bulk, but acquire distinct crystal field environments via surface truncation. The latter case can yield FM-like spin splitting magnitudes while also having vanishingly small uncompensated magnetization. In contrast, when surface magnetization arises from relativistic canting on symmetry-connected sublattices, the spin splitting is expected to be small. We confirm these predictions with first-principles calculations of $\mathrm{Cr_2O_3}$ and $\mathrm{FeF_2}$, finding splittings from $\sim10\mathrm{meV}$-$\sim1\mathrm{eV}$ depending on the surface in question. Our findings point to intrinsic surface symmetry breaking as a route to large, functional spin splitting in an expanded range of AFM materials.

### [14] [On representation of macroscopic crack in periodic fine-scale discrete mechanical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20253)
*Jan Raisinger,Jan Eliáš*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文评估了三种新型边界条件（Tessellation BC、Percolation-path-aligned BC、带位移突变的球形周期BC）在异质软化材料多尺度建模中的适用性，并将其应用于二维/三维混凝土离散颗粒模型。结果表明：Percolation-path-aligned BC存在严重缺陷；Tessellation BC能稳定产生形态明确的局部化带；带位移突变的球面周期BC有时会错误产生类似标准周期BC的裂纹模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多尺度建模中，细尺度模型的边界条件（boundary conditions, BC）会显著影响应变局部化模式与宏观响应。标准周期边界条件在局部化带倾斜方向与周期方向不匹配时会产生虚假的延性行为和过高的能量耗散，因此需要开发或评估能够适应局部化带演化的新型边界条件。

Method: 本研究在二维方形与圆形模型以及三维立方体模型上，分别施加标准周期BC、Tessellation BC、Percolation-path-aligned BC以及带位移突变的球面周期BC，对混凝土中尺度离散颗粒模型进行单轴拉伸模拟，比较不同加载方向下的应变局部化行为。

Result: Percolation-path-aligned BC会导致多个局部化带且弱约束部分易出现虚假应变局部化；Tessellation BC则始终产生单一明确的局部化带，其长度仅由模型几何决定；带位移突变的球面周期BC在某些情况下会错误地产生与标准周期BC相似的裂纹模式。

Conclusion: 在所评估的新型边界条件中，Tessellation BC表现最优，适用于异质软化材料的多尺度建模；Percolation-path-aligned BC存在显著缺陷不推荐使用；带位移突变的球面周期BC的可靠性仍存在局限，需进一步改进。

Abstract: In multiscale modeling of heterogeneous softening materials, boundary conditions (BC) in the fine-scale model strongly influence the strain localization pattern and the macroscopic response. For rectilinear models (e.g., squares or cubes), standard Periodic BCs produce artificially ductile behavior with excessive energy dissipation when the localization band inclination does not match the periodicity directions. Recently proposed Tessellation and Percolation-path-aligned BCs promise to address this by adapting the periodicity frame to align with the evolving localization bands. Alternatively, spherical/circular models provide an orientation independent response by design. Unfortunately, the standard Periodic BCs do not allow development of proper localization band crossing spherical model's boundaries. A recently proposed modification addresses this by adding a displacement jump to the spherical periodic BCs.
  This study evaluates the applicability of these novel BCs to a mesoscale discrete particle model of concrete. Two-dimensional square and circular models under uniaxial tension with different loading directions are analyzed, with the selected approaches extended to three-dimensional cube models. Results show that Percolation-path-aligned BCs exhibit major shortcomings: they can lead to multiple localization bands due to uneven straining of the two boundary sections and their weakly constrained section can be prone to spurious strain localization. In contrast, Tessellation BCs consistently yield a well-defined localization band, whose length is determined solely by the model geometry, making it straightforward to account for in post-processing. Periodic boundary conditions augmented with a displacement jump applied to a circular model sometimes incorrect produce crack patterns similar to those under the standard Periodic BCs.

</details>


### [15] [Anomalous magneto-optical response at $\mathrm{RuO_2 / WSe_2}$ van der Waals interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20262)
*Muhammad Hassan Shaikh,Abhijith Puthiya Veettil,Collin Maurtua,Dai Q. Ho,Subhash Bhatt,David T. Plouff,Malitha Gulawita,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,John Q. Xiao,Anderson Janotti,Chitraleema Chakraborty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用范德华异质结中单层二硒化钨（WSe₂）与二氧化钌（RuO₂）界面的磁邻近效应（MPE），通过温依赖磁光光谱测量发现异常激子能移和非传统Varshni行为，揭示RuO₂表面存在弱磁性态，从而提供了一种无需额外铁磁层即可直接光学探测表面弱磁性的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RuO₂虽被提出作为交变磁性（altermagnetic）候选材料，但其磁基态仍存在争议，亟需一种直接且灵敏的手段来探测其表面弱磁性态。

Method: 构建(001)取向RuO₂薄膜上覆盖单层WSe₂的范德华异质结，利用磁邻近效应（MPE, magnetic proximity effect）进行探测；采用温依赖磁光光谱学（magneto-optical spectroscopy）测量激子能量位移，并辅以偏振分辨（polarization-resolved）测量分析谷分裂（valley splitting）行为。

Result: 在55 K以下观察到异常激子能移及偏离传统Varshni经验公式的行为，且该异常能移在外加反向磁场场冷（field cooling）时符号反转，表明源于磁性；WSe₂/RuO₂中的谷分裂近乎与磁场无关且存在涨落，与对照样品中传统的线性塞曼分裂（linear Zeeman splitting）形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 上述结果说明WSe₂的谷态主要由RuO₂表面弱磁性态产生的界面交换场（interfacial exchange fields）主导；基于MPE的光学探测方法可直接探测弱表面磁性而无需引入额外铁磁层，为解决具有争议磁态的材料研究提供了新工具。

Abstract: Ruthenium dioxide ($\mathrm{RuO_2}$) has been proposed as an altermagnetic candidate, although its magnetic ground state remains controversial. Here, we probe weak interfacial magnetic states at the surface of (001)-oriented $\mathrm{RuO_2}$ films using the magnetic proximity effect (MPE) in a van der Waals heterostructure consisting of monolayer tungsten diselenide ($\mathrm{WSe_2}$) atop $\mathrm{RuO_2}$. Temperature-dependent magneto-optical spectroscopy reveals an anomalous excitonic energy shift and a deviation from conventional Varshni behavior below 55 K that are absent in an encapsulated $\mathrm{WSe_2}$ control sample. The anomalous shift reverses sign upon field cooling with opposite magnetic field polarity, indicating a magnetic origin. Polarization-resolved measurements further show a nearly field-independent and fluctuating valley splitting in $\mathrm{WSe_2 / RuO_2}$ in strong contrast to the conventional linear Zeeman splitting observed in the control bare $\mathrm{WSe_2}$ sample. These results suggest that the valley states are governed predominantly by interfacial exchange fields associated with weak surface magnetic states in $\mathrm{RuO_2}$, which do not produce a conventional linear Zeeman response within the applied magnetic field range. Importantly, this approach enables direct optical probing of emergent surface magnetism without introducing an additional ferromagnetic layer, positioning MPE-based optical probing as a tool for investigating weak surface magnetism and offering new possibilities for studying magnetic materials with controversial magnetic states.

</details>


### [16] [Exciton Transport in Disordered Perovskite Nanocrystal Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20275)
*Simon Solari,Enrique Arévalo Rodríguez,Antonella Cutrupi,Amalia Coro,Marc Meléndez,Alicia De Andrés,Almudena Torres-Pardo,Beatriz H. Juárez,Ferry Prins*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过解析激子（exciton）在空间、时间和能量维度上的动力学行为，揭示了胶体卤化铅钙钛矿（lead halide perovskite, LHP）纳米晶体（nanocrystals, NCs）薄膜中结构无序（structural disorder）与能量无序（energetic disorder）对激子输运的不同影响，发现能量无序是主导激子传输效率的关键因素，而长烷基链配体虽能提高单分散性却反而会加剧能量无序并降低输运效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体LHP纳米晶体薄膜在光电器件（如LED、激光器、太阳能电池）中具有巨大潜力，但其固有的尺寸和形状多分散性（polydispersity）会引入结构和能量两种形式的无序，目前尚不清楚这两种无序对激子输运的具体影响机制。

Method: 在空间、时间和能量三个维度上解析激子动力学行为，系统考察不同烷基胺配体（alkylamine ligand）链长对纳米晶体单分散性及激子输运性能的影响。

Result: 短烷基链配体导致高多分散性，长烷基链配体则生成更单分散但尺寸更小的颗粒，量子限域效应（quantum confinement）增强，能量无序增大；尽管长链配体固体具有显著更高的单分散性，其激子输运效率反而更低。

Conclusion: 能量无序而非结构无序是主导激子输运效率的关键因素，配体工程（ligand engineering）在设计基于杂化LHP纳米晶体的高性能光电器件中具有关键作用。

Abstract: Solution-processed thin films of colloidal lead halide perovskite (LHP) nanocrystals (NCs) show great potential for the implementation into optoelectronic devices such as light-emitting diodes (LEDs), lasers, and solar cells. However, these hybrid LHP NC solids exhibit non-negligible size and shape polydispersity, which introduces both structural and energetic disorder. Here, we resolve the exciton dynamics in space, time, and energy to elucidate the impact of different forms of disorder (structural and energetic) on exciton transport. We show that the disorder depends sensitively on the length of the alkylamine ligand used in the synthesis. While shorter alkyl chain lengths lead to high polydispersity, longer alkyl chains lead to more monodispersed and smaller particles where quantum confinement becomes more pronounced and, consequently, lead to increased energetic disorder. Strikingly, we find that exciton transport is less efficient in NC solids with long alkyl chain ligands, despite having a significantly more monodisperse ensemble. This demonstrates that energetic disorder, rather than structural disorder, is the dominant factor for predicting exciton transport within these materials. These findings reveal the critical role of ligand engineering in designing high-performance optoelectronic devices based on hybrid LHP NCs, providing new insights into energy transport dynamics in disordered systems and highlighting the versatility of these materials for advanced photonic and optoelectronic applications.

</details>


### [17] [Tunable Flat Bands and magnetism in Triangulene-based Superatomic Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20321)
*Wenya Zhai,Tingfeng Zhang,Fengkun Chen,Xiuqin Lu,Yunlong Xia,Zengfu Ou,Ye Chen,Donghui Guo,Meifang Zhu,Zhengfei Wang,Jingcheng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过自下而上的表面合成方法，利用磷掺杂的三并苯（triangulene）作为构筑单元成功制备了超级原子石墨烯（superatomic graphene）。扫描隧道显微镜/谱学证实了其蜂窝状晶格及狄拉克带（Dirac band）与平带（flat band）电子结构；密度泛函理论（DFT）计算揭示了平带源自磷掺杂三并苯单元的面内pₓ,ᵧ型前线轨道，导致本征半金属行为。氧气功能化还可实现电子结构与磁序的可控调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超级原子石墨烯平台承载了丰富的平带驱动奇异量子特性，但其实验实现仍然极具挑战。因此，本工作旨在通过实验合成方法突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 采用自下而上的表面合成（on-surface synthesis）方法，以磷掺杂的三并苯为构筑单元构建超级原子石墨烯；利用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）和扫描隧道谱（STS）表征晶格与电子结构；结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算揭示平带起源与电子性质；并引入氧气功能化（oxygen functionalization）调控电子结构与磁有序。

Result: 成功制备出具有明确蜂窝状晶格的超级原子石墨烯；实验观测到特征性的狄拉克带和平带电子结构；DFT计算表明平带源于磷掺杂三并苯的面内pₓ,ᵧ型前线轨道，赋予体系本征半金属（half-metallic）行为；氧气功能化可实现电子结构及磁序的确定性调控。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个具有可调平带特性的关联量子材料（correlated quantum materials）通用设计平台。

Abstract: Superatomic graphene platforms host a rich portfolio of flat-band-driven exotic quantum properties, yet their experimental realization remains challenging. Here, we report the bottom-up on-surface synthesis of superatomic graphene using phosphorus-doped triangulene as building blocks. Scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy measurements resolve the well-defined honeycomb lattice of as-fabricated superatomic graphene and demonstrate the characteristic Dirac band and flat band electronic structures. Density functional theory calculations reveal that the flat bands originate from the in-plane p$_x,_y$-like frontier orbitals of the phosphorus-doped triangulene units, leading to intrinsic half-metallic behavior. Furthermore, oxygen functionalization of the molecular precursor enables deterministic modulation of the electronic structure and magnetic ordering. This work establishes a general platform for designing correlated quantum materials with tunable flat band properties.

</details>


### [18] [Effective masses, Burstein-Moss shift, and bandgap renormalization in degenerate Al-doped ZnO from broadband ellipsometry and Hall measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20349)
*S. Mishra,L. A. Enrique,D. Cespedes,E. Perez,E. Serquen,F. Bravo,P. Llontop,F. Ruske,L. Korte,J. A. Guerra*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种通过全局拟合载流子浓度依赖的带隙与等离子体能量来提取简并半导体中电子和空穴有效质量的综合方法，明确包含能带非抛物线效应，并成功应用于溅射Al掺杂ZnO薄膜，验证了Nilsson模型在描述非抛物线性和分离Burstein-Moss位移与带隙重整化方面的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 简并半导体中有效质量的准确提取对于理解能带结构至关重要，但传统的抛物线近似在宽载流子浓度范围内存在偏差，且Burstein-Moss位移与带隙重整化的分离缺乏系统方法。

Method: 采用宽带光谱椭偏仪（spectroscopic ellipsometry）结合霍尔效应（Hall effect）分析，精确测定带隙、等离子体能量和载流子浓度。介电函数建模在基本吸收区使用基于Elliott的模型（包含重叠激子跃迁和Urbach尾巴），自由载流子吸收采用修正的Sernelius公式。对比了Pisarkiewicz（球对称带+阶梯函数近似费米-狄拉克分布）和Nilsson（包含热和杂质效应）两种非抛物线模型。

Result: Nilsson模型能够准确捕获能带非抛物线性（band nonparabolicity），得到的有效质量和非抛物线参数与带隙演化一致。该方法定量分离了Burstein-Moss位移和带隙重整化（bandgap renormalization），在宽浓度范围内重现载流子依赖的带隙移动。忽略价带贡献会引入系统性偏差。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了一种可靠的提取能带结构参数和带隙移动的方法，可推广至其他透明导电氧化物（transparent conducting oxides），并可用于确定Mott临界浓度（Mott critical concentration）和基本吸收边起点。

Abstract: A comprehensive methodology is developed to extract electron and hole effective masses in degenerate semiconductors through a simultaneous global fit of carrier concentration dependence of bandgap and plasma energy, explicitly incorporating band nonparabolicity. Broadband spectroscopic ellipsometry combined with Hall effect analyses enables accurate determination of the bandgap, plasma energy and carrier concentrations. The dielectric function of sputtered Al-doped ZnO thin films are modeled in the fundamental absorption region using an Elliott based model with overlapping excitonic transitions and Urbach tails, while free carrier absorption is described by a modified sernelius formula. Wide carrier concentrations are achieved via controlled deposition and post-annealing, revealing changes in electron effective masses and deviations from parabolic dispersion. Two nonparabolic models are compared, Pisarkiewicz, assuming spherically symmetric band with a step-function approximation of the Fermi-Dirac distribution and Nilsson, incorporating thermal and impurity effects. The latter is shown to capture accurately band nonparabolicity, yielding effective masses and nonparabolicity parameter consistent with bandgap evolution. This approach quantitatively separates Burstein-Moss shift and bandgap renormalization, reproducing carrier dependent bandgap shifts across a wide concentration range. Neglecting valence band contributions introduces systematic bias. Bandgap renormalization is further evaluated using plasmon pole and random phase approximations, underscoring the importance of many-body screening. This framework also enables determination of the Mott critical concentration and the fundamental absorption edge onset. Collectively, these results establish a reliable methodology for extracting band-structure parameters and bandgap shifts, extendable to other transparent conducting oxides.

</details>


### [19] [Breaking symmetry to create a parallel-plate varactor dielectric with unparalleled microwave performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20371)
*Florian Bergmann,Matthew R. Barone,Zishen Tian,Aiden Ross,Gerhard H. Olsen,Meagan C. Papac,Samuel Freed,Bryan T. Bosworth,Nicholas R. Jungwirth,Eric J. Marksz,Tomasz Karpisz,Noah Schnitzer,Lopa Bhatt,David A. Muller,Dylan Sotir,Akash Surampalli,Veronica Goian,Christelle Kadlec,Stanislav Kamba,Asher Hansen,Nathan Rongitsch,Dmitri A. Tenne,Ichiro Takeuchi,Long-Qing Chen,Lane W. Martin,Nathan D. Orloff,Darrell G. Schlom*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过理论指导，将Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）相材料设计为具有破缺面外对称性的薄膜，首次实现了低损耗、面外可调的平行板交容器（varactor），在10 GHz下将面外可调电介质的品质因子（figure of merit）提升了10倍，为新型可调单片微波集成电路（MMIC）奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可调电介质交容器在微波电路中性能优越，但通常存在高介电损耗的问题；而Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）介电薄膜虽具有极低的微波损耗，但其晶体对称性限制了面外（out-of-plane）平行板交容器结构的设计，无法实现小型化和最大化可调介质的电场强度。

Method: 基于理论指导，将广泛研究的可调微波电介质BaxSr1-xTiO3中的原子组装到首个具有破缺面外对称性（broken out-of-plane symmetry）的Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）相中，制备出低损耗、面外可调的介电薄膜。最优成分为(ATiO3)nAO，其中A = Ba0.45Sr0.55，n = 8。

Result: 在10 GHz频率下，该薄膜将面外可调电介质的品质因子（figure of merit）提升了10倍。

Conclusion: 该成果为新一代可调单片微波集成电路（monolithic microwave integrated circuits, MMICs）的开发铺平了道路。

Abstract: Voltage-tunable capacitors (varactors) are key to microwave circuits. Tunable dielectric varactors outperform competing technologies in almost every relevant metric but usually suffer from high dielectric loss. In contrast, Ruddlesden-Popper (RPs) dielectric thin films have remarkably low microwave loss. Unfortunately, their crystallographic symmetry has until recently dictated an in-plane device structure, precluding the favorable out-of-plane parallel-plate varactor design for minimized size and maximized electric field in the tunable dielectric. Guided by theory, we report RPs akin to the widely studied tunable microwave dielectric BaxSr1-xTiO3. Assembling these same atoms into the first RP phase with broken out-of-plane symmetry, we achieve a low-loss, out-of-plane tunable dielectric thin film. The highest performing film, (ATiO3)nAO film with A = Ba0.45Sr0.55 and n = 8, unlocks a tenfold improvement in the figure of merit for out-of-plane tunable dielectrics at 10 GHz, paving the way for a new generation of tunable monolithic microwave integrated circuits.

</details>


### [20] [A Defect-Free Model of Amorphous Silicon with Pristine Electronic Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20500)
*Louise A. M. Rosset,Chinonso Ugwumadu,Stephen R. Elliott,David A. Drabold,Volker L. Deringer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过机器学习驱动的分子动力学（machine-learning-driven molecular-dynamics）模拟构建无缺陷的理想非晶硅模型，并结合混合泛函密度泛函理论（hybrid-level density-functional theory）计算，准确复现了实验观测的电子带隙（electronic bandgap），并与Wooten-Winer-Weaire (WWW)键交换方法及其他理想a-Si模型进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶硅（amorphous silicon, a-Si）被理解为典型的连续随机网络（continuous random network）材料，理想状态下应具有完全的四重配位（fourfold coordination）。准确复现其电子带隙是验证模型真实性的关键，但目前尚需明确缺陷-free的理想模型能否达到这一目标。

Method: 使用机器学习驱动的分子动力学模拟构建无缺陷理想a-Si模型，随后采用混合泛函密度泛函理论计算评估其电子结构。将该模型与Wooten-Winer-Weaire (WWW)键交换方法及其他近期提出的理想a-Si近似模型进行对比。

Result: 该无缺陷理想a-Si模型能够准确复现实验观测的电子带隙，优于或可比于其他现有模型。

Conclusion: 该工作为研究非晶硅中的带尾态（band tails）、光学性质（optical properties）及输运性质（transport）提供了计算平台。

Abstract: Amorphous silicon (a-Si) is understood to be the canonical continuous random network material, ideally defined by fully fourfold coordination. Here, we show that a defect-free ('ideal') model of a-Si from machine-learning-driven molecular-dynamics simulations [L. A. M. Rosset et al., Nat. Commun. 16, 2360 (2025)], subsequently evaluated with hybrid-level density-functional theory computations, can accurately reproduce the experimentally observed electronic bandgap. We compare this model with one resulting from the Wooten-Winer-Weaire (WWW) bond-switching approach and with other recent approximants to ideal a-Si. More broadly, our work provides a platform for studies of band tails, optical properties, and transport in a-Si.

</details>


### [21] [Controllable Quantum Spin Hall Phases in Bi$_2$Te$_3$-Family van der Waals Heterobilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20541)
*Emmanuel V. C. Lopes,Pedro H. Sophia,Felipe Crasto de Lima,Adalberto Fazzio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算和Wannier紧束缚方法，展示了由Bi₂Te₃家族的两个平庸五重层堆叠形成的范德华异质结中量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）相的出现，并证明其边缘态可通过层间应变和外电场进行开关调控，且对层间扭转保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑边缘/表面态的可调谐性与控制对于新型器件应用至关重要，因此需要探索在二维体系中创建和操控拓扑相的新途径。

Method: 结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和基于Wannier函数的紧束缚方法（Wannier-based tight-binding methods），堆叠两个来自Bi₂Te₃家族的平庸五重层（quintuple layers）形成范德华异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）。

Result: 在堆叠的异质结中观察到量子自旋霍尔相（quantum spin Hall phases）的出现；边缘态可通过层间应变（interlayer strain）和外电场（external electric field）进行开关调控；量子自旋霍尔边缘通道（edge channels）对层间扭转（interlayer twist）保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究为在Bi₂Te₃家族体系中创建和操控二维拓扑相提供了新方法，对拓扑场效应晶体管和自旋电子器件等实际应用具有潜在价值。

Abstract: The tunability and control of topological edge/surface states are crucial for the development of new device applications. In this work, by combining first-principles calculations and Wannier-based tight-binding methods, we show the emergence of quantum spin Hall phases in van der Waals heterostructures formed by stacking two trivial quintuple layers from the Bi$_2$Te$_3$ family. We demonstrate the tunability of the edge states under interlayer strain and external electric field effects, suggesting the possibility of switching topological edge states on/off by external control. Additionally, the quantum spin Hall edge channels remain robust against interlayer twist, highlighting their stability against external perturbations. Our results provide a new way to create and manipulate two-dimensional topological phases in systems based on Bi$_2$Te$_3$ family, which can be valuable for practical applications, such as topological field effect transistors and spintronic devices.

</details>

### [22] [Physics-Informed Discovery of Yield Functions in Plasticity via Convex Neural Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19375)
*Hyeonbin Moon,Donghyuk Cho,Jecheon Yu,Jeong Whan Yoon,Seunghwa Ryu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于物理信息的框架（physics-informed framework），用于从全场位移数据和反力数据中识别各向异性屈服函数（anisotropic yield function），无需应力观测、塑性应变测量、直接屈服面数据或预设参数化屈服函数。该框架通过凸神经网络（convex neural network）表示屈服函数，并嵌入可微的弹塑性应力更新（differentiable stress update）和基于物理信息的力平衡损失（physics-informed force equilibrium loss）进行训练，在多个有限元基准研究中验证了其对von Mises、Hill 1948和Yld2000-2d屈服函数的识别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性屈服函数的标定面临多重困难：屈服现象无法在全场力学测量中被直接观测，方向性标定需要大量加载方向，且选择合适的解析形式并不容易。现有方法通常依赖应力观测、塑性应变测量或预设的屈服函数形式，限制了其在实际复杂场景中的适用性。

Method: 该方法将屈服函数作为弹塑性应力积分（elastoplastic stress integration）中力学约束的本构组件（constitutive component）进行识别，而非通过直接的应力空间监督。屈服函数由凸神经网络表示，强制满足凸性（convexity）和一次正齐次性（positive homogeneity of degree one），并施加了拉压对称性（tension-compression symmetry）假设；通过可微分的应力更新和跨多个加载案例的物理信息力平衡损失进行训练。

Result: 使用von Mises、Hill 1948和Yld2000-2d屈服函数的有限元基准研究验证了该框架的性能，评估了屈服轮廓一致性（yield contour agreement）、位移噪声敏感性（displacement-noise sensitivity）、通过塑性活跃应力状态（plastically active stress states）的可识别性、认知不确定性（epistemic uncertainty）以及多项式代理部署（polynomial-surrogate deployment）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一条力学约束的路径，用于从位移和力数据中识别各向异性屈服函数，同时使识别得到的组件保持在弹塑性应力积分的结构框架内。

Abstract: Identifying anisotropic yield functions remains challenging since yielding is not directly observed in full-field mechanical measurements, directional calibration can require many loading directions, and selecting an appropriate analytical form is nontrivial. This study proposes a physics-informed framework for discovering yield functions from full-field displacement data and reaction force data, without stress observations, plastic strain measurements, direct yield surface data, or a prescribed parametric yield function. The framework identifies the yield function as a mechanically constrained constitutive component inside elastoplastic stress integration, rather than through direct stress-space supervision. The yield function is represented by a convex neural network that enforces convexity and positive homogeneity of degree one while imposing the assumed tension-compression symmetry, and this neural yield function is trained with a differentiable stress update and a physics-informed force equilibrium loss across multiple loading cases. The proposed framework is validated using finite element (FE) benchmark studies with von Mises, Hill 1948, and Yld2000-2d yield functions, assessing yield contour agreement, displacement-noise sensitivity, identifiability through plastically active stress states, epistemic uncertainty, and polynomial-surrogate deployment. This study provides a mechanics-constrained pathway for discovering anisotropic yield functions from displacement and force data while keeping the identified component within the structure of elastoplastic stress integration.

</details>


### [23] [A Hybrid GNN-FEM Framework for Phase-Field Fracture Simulation. Physics-Preserving Hybridization for Generalizable Surrogate Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19378)
*Hyeonbin Moon,Yongjin Choi,Seunghwa Ryu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种混合图神经网络-有限元法（GNN-FEM）框架，用于高效且可泛化的相场断裂模拟。该框架在常规交错求解方案中，用图神经网络代理替代相场更新步骤，同时保留基于有限元法的位移求解器以施加力学平衡与边界条件。通过保留增量求解结构，框架保持与历史依赖断裂演化的一致性，并利用无量纲特征设计、网格图表示及物理信息损失函数，实现跨几何、荷载、材料属性和离散化的强泛化能力。数值实验验证了该方法在降低计算成本的同时保持精度，并在多种问题设定下表现出稳健的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学机器学习（SciML）在加速复杂物理系统模拟方面具有潜力，但对非线性、历史依赖问题实现物理一致且可泛化的预测仍是一个核心挑战。相场断裂方法提供稳健的变分框架，但其求解耦合、非线性且历史依赖系统的计算成本过高，限制了实际应用。

Method: 将图神经网络（GNN）代理集成到常规交错求解方案中，仅替代每个荷载增量步中的相场更新步骤，而保留基于有限元法（FEM）的位移求解器以强制执行力学平衡和边界条件。采用无量纲特征设计、基于网格域（mesh-based domains）的图形式以及源于控制相场方程的物理信息损失（physics-informed loss）来增强泛化能力。

Result: 数值实验表明，与常规有限元法相比，该混合框架降低了计算成本，同时保持了准确性。该方法在多种问题设定（不同几何、荷载条件、材料属性和离散化）下展现出稳健的预测性能。

Conclusion: 该选择性代理策略强调识别物理上有意义且增量结构化的学习目标，而非依赖暴力数据生成来学习整个断裂过程。通过保留增量求解结构，框架实现了与历史依赖断裂演化的一致性，为高效且可泛化的计算断裂力学提供了一种有前景的途径。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning (SciML) has emerged as a promising approach for accelerating simulations of complex physical systems, yet achieving physically consistent and generalizable predictions for nonlinear, history-dependent problems remains a central challenge. In this study, we propose a hybrid GNN--FEM framework for efficient and generalizable phase-field fracture modeling. While phase-field approaches provide a robust variational framework for simulating complex crack evolution, their high computational cost limits practical applications because they require solving coupled, nonlinear, and history-dependent systems within an incremental finite element procedure. To address this challenge, a graph neural network surrogate is integrated into the conventional staggered scheme, replacing the phase-field update at each load increment while retaining the FEM-based displacement solver to enforce mechanical equilibrium and boundary conditions. By preserving the incremental solution structure, the framework remains consistent with history-dependent fracture evolution without requiring the surrogate to approximate the full solution trajectory. This selective surrogate strategy emphasizes the identification of a physically meaningful and incrementally structured learning target, rather than relying on brute-force data generation to learn the full fracture process. The proposed framework achieves strong generalization across varying geometries, loading conditions, material properties, and discretizations through dimensionless feature design, a graph-based formulation on mesh-based domains, and a physics-informed loss derived from the governing phase-field equation. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the hybrid approach reduces computational cost while maintaining accuracy compared with conventional FEM, and exhibits robust predictive performance across diverse problem settings.

</details>


### [24] [Critical Percolation as a Synthetic Data Model for Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20347)
*Aryeh Brill,Tom Ingebretsen Carlson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于临界逾渗（critical percolation）簇的层级合成数据集，用于评估神经网络可解释性方法；该数据集具有稀疏性、分形结构、幂律分布和分析可解性，比传统合成数据集更真实地反映自然数据的层级多尺度结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用于评估可解释性方法的合成数据集缺乏自然数据所具有的层级多尺度结构（hierarchical, multi-scale structure），作为现实玩具模型（toy model）的价值有限。本文旨在弥合这一差距。

Method: 设计一族基于高维空间中临界平均场逾渗簇（critical mean-field percolation clusters）的层级函数合成数据集。利用逾渗簇、随机树（random trees）与可加凝聚（additive coalescence）之间的映射关系，提出一种近线性时间算法，可联合采样随机树及其层级隐变量分解（hierarchical latent decomposition），支持任意规模的数据生成。

Result: 通过探针实验（probing experiments）发现，模型的真实隐变量（ground-truth latent variables）可从神经网络激活（neural network activations）中被线性解码（linearly decoded）。

Conclusion: 稀疏性（sparsity）、自相似性（self-similarity）、幂律统计（power-law statistics）和分析可解性（analytical tractability）使临界逾渗成为可解释性研究（interpretability research）的一个原则性测试平台（principled testbed）。

Abstract: Neural networks learn features that reflect the hierarchical, multi-scale structure of natural data. Synthetic datasets used to evaluate interpretability methods typically lack this structure, limiting their value as realistic toy models. To close this gap, we introduce a family of synthetic datasets consisting of hierarchical functions defined on critical mean-field percolation clusters embedded in a high-dimensional data space. The percolation data consists of sparse, low-dimensional fractal clusters with a power-law size distribution. Latent variables modeling a taxonomic hierarchy generate each data point's target value. The data model is analytically tractable with known critical exponents that fix its properties without requiring hyperparameter tuning. We leverage a mapping between percolation clusters, random trees, and additive coalescence to propose an almost linear-time algorithm to jointly sample a random tree and its hierarchical latent decomposition, enabling data generation at arbitrary scale. Using probing experiments, we find that the model's ground-truth latent variables can be linearly decoded from neural network activations. Together, sparsity, self-similarity, power-law statistics, and analytical tractability make critical percolation a principled testbed for interpretability research.

</details>

### [25] [Precision mass measurements of multistrange baryons and their antiparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20144)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于LHC-ALICE实验的质子-质子对撞数据，利用K⁰_S和Λ介子质量校标，对Ω⁻和Ξ⁻重子及其反粒子的质量进行了高精度测量（分数不确定度约60 ppm），将奇异重子谱学（strange-baryon spectroscopy）的精度提升至新基准，并显著降低了格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）计算中的标度不确定度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ω⁻重子对于确立夸克（quark）作为物质基本组分具有关键历史意义，但其质量的世界平均值仍依赖四十多年前的测量，且缺乏系统不确定度的稳健评估。格点QCD计算广泛使用Ω⁻或Ξ⁻质量来设定物理标度（scale setting），因此高精度测量是确保第一性原理研究（如夸克禁闭、手征对称性破缺）可靠性的必要前提。

Method: 利用大型强子对撞机（LHC）的ALICE探测器，在质子-质子对撞中通过衰变产物的不变质量重建（invariant-mass reconstruction）确定Ω⁻和Ξ⁻重子及其反粒子的质量；借助ALICE优异的径迹追踪和粒子鉴别能力，精确重建这些短寿命粒子的位移衰变顶点（displaced decay vertices）；以精确已知的K⁰_S和Λ质量进行校标。

Result: 每个质量测量的分数不确定度约为60 ppm，例如反Ω⁺质量M_{Ω̄⁺} = 1672.558 ± 0.034 (统计) ± 0.102 (系统) MeV/c²。该结果建立了奇异重子谱学（strange-baryon spectroscopy）的新精度基准，并在多奇异强子扇区实现了对CPT不变性（Charge-Parity-Time invariance）的严格检验。

Conclusion: 该测量显著降低了格点QCD计算中的标度不确定度，例如可使得子强子真空极化对缪子反常磁矩贡献的理论预测达到亚千分之一（sub per mille）精度，从而为强相互作用的第一性原理研究和标准模型检验提供了更精确的输入。

Abstract: The $Ω^-$ baryon, composed of three strange quarks (sss), was predicted by the quark model and discovered in 1964, playing a pivotal role in establishing quarks as fundamental constituents of matter. Despite its importance, experimental knowledge of its mass remains limited, with the current world average relying on measurements performed more than four decades ago and lacking robust estimates of systematic uncertainties. This is notable given the central role of the $Ω^-$ mass, and alternatively that of the $Ξ^-$(dss), in lattice QCD calculations, where it is widely used to set the overall physical scale. Precise scale setting is essential for first-principles studies of quark confinement, chiral symmetry breaking, and stringent tests of the Standard Model. Here we report high-precision measurements of the masses of the $Ω^-$ and $Ξ^-$ baryons and their antiparticles, determined from invariant-mass reconstruction of their decay products in proton$-$proton collisions at the LHC. The analysis exploits the excellent tracking and particle-identification capabilities of the ALICE experiment, enabling accurate reconstruction of the displaced decay vertices characteristic of these short-lived particles. Each mass is measured with a fractional uncertainty of about 60 parts per million, for example $M_{\barΩ^+}=1672.558\,\pm\,0.034\,({\rm stat.})\,\pm\,0.102\,({\rm syst.})$ MeV/$c^2$. The precisely known K$^0_{\rm S}$ and $Λ$ masses are used for calibration. These results establish new precision benchmarks in strange-baryon spectroscopy and enable stringent tests of Charge-Parity-Time invariance in the multistrange-hadron sector. Our measurement reduces the scale uncertainty in lattice QCD calculations, enabling for instance sub per mille precision for the hadronic vacuum-polarization contribution to the muon anomalous magnetic moment.

</details>


### [26] [Probing Strange-Quark Hadronization via (Multi-)Strange Hadron Multiplicity Distributions in Small Collision Systems with ALICE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20213)
*Sara Pucillo*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ALICE合作组在LHC上测量了质子-质子（pp）碰撞中奇异粒子（K_S^0, Λ, Ξ, Ω）的事件-by-事件（event-by-event）产额概率分布，首次将奇异粒子产生的研究从平均产额扩展到概率分布层面，为检验产生机制和蒙特卡洛模型提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异粒子增强（strangeness enhancement）被认为是夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）形成的标志之一，但仅基于平均产额的理解尚不充分。为更深入探究奇异粒子产生机制，需要超越平均产额、从事件-by-事件层面来研究奇异粒子数的概率分布。

Method: ALICE合作组在质子-质子（pp）碰撞中，在质心能量√s = 5.02 TeV下，测量了同一种奇异粒子（K_S^0, Λ, Ξ, Ω）每个事件中产生给定数目的概率分布。该方法首次采用基于事件-by-事件粒子计数（event-by-event particle counting）的技术。

Result: 实验提供了奇异粒子产额概率分布，并用于探测奇异与非奇异成分之间严重失衡的事件。结果与常用的蒙特卡洛事件生成器（Monte Carlo event generators）中先进的现象学模型（phenomenological models）进行了比较。

Conclusion: 该测量超越了平均产额，为奇异粒子产生机制提供了新的测试平台，并增强了对奇异粒子产生背后动力学（dynamics）的敏感性。

Abstract: Strangeness enhancement is defined as the increased relative production of strange hadrons in heavy-ion collisions compared to proton--proton (pp) interactions. It was originally proposed as one of the signatures of quark--gluon plasma (QGP) formation. At the LHC, the ALICE experiment observed that strange-hadron-to-pion yield ratios rise with increasing charged-particle multiplicity at midrapidity, independently of collision energy ($\sqrt{s}$) and system size, from pp to p--Pb and up to Pb--Pb collisions. To gain deeper insight into the mechanisms of strangeness production, the ALICE collaboration has measured the probability distribution of producing a given number of strange particles ($K^{0}_{S}$, $Λ$, $Ξ$, and $Ω$) of the same species per event in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s}~=~5.02$ TeV. This measurement extends the study of strangeness production beyond the mean particle yield by employing, for the first time, a technique based on event-by-event particle counting. It provides a new test bench for production mechanisms, probing events with large imbalances between strange and non-strange content. The results are compared with state-of-the-art phenomenological models implemented in commonly used Monte Carlo event generators, offering enhanced sensitivity to the underlying dynamics of strangeness production.

</details>


### [27] [Measurements of charged-particle pseudorapidity and transverse momentum distributions in O+O and Ne+Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}} = 5.36$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20257)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器在LHC采集的O+O和Ne+Ne碰撞数据（质心系能量$\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}}=5.36$ TeV），测量了带电粒子的横动量（transverse momentum）谱、多重数（multiplicity）和平均横动量作为赝快度（pseudorapidity）和碰撞中心度（collision centrality）的函数，并将结果与流体动力学（hydrodynamic）计算进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过测量小系统（O+O和Ne+Ne）中带电粒子的横动量谱、多重数和平均横动量随赝快度和碰撞中心度的变化，研究小系统碰撞中的粒子产生机制，并与流体动力学模型进行比较，以检验该模型在小系统中的适用性。

Method: 利用ATLAS实验在LHC记录的27.7 μb⁻¹（O+O）和53.1 μb⁻¹（Ne+Ne）数据，通过ATLAS前向量能器（forward calorimeters）测量总横能量来表征碰撞中心度；使用内探测器（inner detector）在|η|<2.5和0.27<p_T<5 GeV的准直范围内重建带电粒子运动学；以5%宽度中心度区间（覆盖5-80%）和1%宽度区间（覆盖0-5%）报告结果；拟合p_T依赖关系以估算外推至0<p_T<5 GeV的dn/dη和⟨p_T⟩值；同时基于π介子质量假设计算快度（rapidity）并进行比较。

Result: 给出了O+O和Ne+Ne碰撞中带电粒子的每事件赝快度密度dn/dη和平均横动量⟨p_T⟩随η的变化，以及不变每事件产额（invariant per-event yield）随η和p_T的分布，覆盖了5-80%中心度区间（5%宽度）和0-5%中心度区间（1%宽度）。

Conclusion: 准直范围（fiducial range）内和外推后的结果与流体动力学（hydrodynamic）计算结果进行了比较，评估了使用赝快度代替快度的影响。

Abstract: Measurements of charged-particle transverse momentum spectra, multiplicity, and mean transverse momentum are presented as a function of pseudorapidity and collision centrality in O+O and Ne+Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{_\text{NN}}}= 5.36$ TeV using 27.7 $μ\text{b}^{-1}$ and 53.1 $μ\text{b}^{-1}$ data sets recorded by the ATLAS experiment at the LHC. The collision centrality is characterized by the total transverse energy measured in the ATLAS forward calorimeters. The kinematics of charged particles are reconstructed with the inner detector over the fiducial pseudorapidity and transverse momentum ranges $|η|<2.5$ and $0.27 < p_{\text{T}} < 5$ GeV using data from the ATLAS inner detector. The per-event charged-particle pseudorapidity density $dn/dη$ and mean transverse momentum $\langle p_{\text{T}}\rangle$ are measured over this fiducial range as a function of $η$. The results are reported in 5%-wide centrality intervals covering the 5-80% centrality range, and in 1%-wide intervals covering the 0-5% centrality range. Invariant per-event yields are evaluated as a function of $η$ and $p_{\text{T}}$. Their $p_{\text{T}}$ dependence is fitted to estimate extrapolated $dn/dη$ and $\langle p_{\text{T}}\rangle$ values over $0 < p_{\text{T}} < 5$ GeV. To evaluate the impact of using pseudorapidity instead of rapidity, measurements are also performed as a function of rapidity computed using a pion mass hypothesis. The fiducial and extrapolated results are compared with hydrodynamic calculations.

### [28] [Symplectic duality for the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20277)
*Igor Chaban*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了几何艾森斯坦级数（geometric Eisenstein series）中常值项的拟映射空间（quasimap space）上同调，该上同调具有库仑支集（Coulomb branch）的交换子代数作用，并证明了其与向量丛的局部上同调在参数一般范围内的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在将拟映射空间上同调范畴化（categorify）GL群上仿射抛物子群（mirabolic parabolic subgroup）的几何艾森斯坦级数常数项，并理解该上同调与库仑支集（Coulomb branch）及曲面奇点（surface singularity）之间的深层代数结构联系。

Method: 通过构造对应代数（algebra of correspondences）在拟映射空间上同调上的自然作用，从中提取交换子代数作为库仑支集的正则函数环（ring of regular functions），并利用C上秩一局部系统（rank-one local system）引入étale基本群在库仑支集上的作用，进而研究概形论不动点（scheme-theoretic fixed locus）上的自然向量丛。

Result: 主要结果：在参数的一般范围内，拟映射空间的上同调与该向量丛的局部上同调（local cohomology）之间存在同构。

Conclusion: 该同构揭示了拟映射空间上同调与库仑支集几何之间的一种对偶性，为几何表示论中Eisenstein级数常数项的范畴化提供了新视角，并建立了与A_n型曲面奇点（A_n-surface singularity）的代数几何联系。

Abstract: We study the cohomology of a quasimap space that categorifies the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series for the mirabolic parabolic subgroup of $GL$ over the function field $\mathbb{F}_q(C)$ of a smooth projective curve $C$. This cohomology carries a natural action of an algebra of correspondences whose commutative subalgebra is the ring of regular functions on the Coulomb branch, which here is the $A_{n}$-surface singularity. A choice of rank-one local system on $C$ induces an action of the étale fundamental group on the Coulomb branch; the scheme-theoretic fixed locus carries a natural vector bundle. Our main result identifies the cohomology of the quasimap space with the local cohomology of this vector bundle, for a generic range of parameters.

### [29] [sft-wick: A formalism and package for Feynman-diagram expansion and evaluation in stochastic field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19480)
*Zheng Zhang*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个名为 sft-wick 的开源 Python 包，它能够从随机场论（stochastic field theory）的路径积分（path-integral）表述中枚举拓扑不同的费曼图（Feynman diagrams），计算代数系数并数值积分，从而避免组合爆炸式的 Wick 收缩扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机场动力学（stochastic field dynamics）在路径积分框架下进行微扰论展开时，Wick 配对数量呈阶乘增长，且张量值顶点上的分量指标路由问题使组合复杂度急剧增加，急需一种自动化工具来生成结构化的图表格而非原始收缩列表。

Method: sft-wick 在枚举空间拓扑（spatial topologies）之后再进行分量指标路由，避免了逐个收缩的 Wick 展开。在枚举过程中同时强制执行响应场约束（response-field constraints），包括响应-响应收缩为零、伊藤规则（ito prescription）以及因果响应回路的禁止。

Result: 该工具可为任意作用量和观测量枚举拓扑不同的费曼图，推导代数系数，并利用用户提供的响应函数（response function）和累积量函数（cumulant function）数值计算图积分。与直接朗之万模拟（Langevin simulation）的对比验证显示，预测结果在模拟统计噪声范围内一致。

Conclusion: sft-wick 为多分量、多维度的随机场系统提供了一种系统化、可扩展的费曼图计算框架，有效克服了组合爆炸问题，并通过数值验证证明了其正确性。

Abstract: When stochastic field dynamics are cast into a path-integral formulation, perturbation theory becomes systematic but the resulting expansion quickly grows combinatorially large. The setting targeted here includes multi-component, multi-dimensional fields with matrix propagators, tensor-valued couplings, and non-Gaussian driving noise specified by arbitrary $n$-point cumulants. Wick pairings grow factorially, and component indices must be routed through the tensor-valued vertices. The useful output is not a raw contraction list, but a diagram table: one entry per topology, with multiplicities, coupling sums, signs, and causal constraints resolved. We present sft-wick, an open-source Python package that constructs these diagram tables and computes their integrals numerically. Given an action and an observable, it enumerates topologically distinct Feynman diagrams, derives their algebraic coefficients, and evaluates the resulting diagram integrals from user-supplied response and cumulant functions. The core algorithm enumerates spatial topologies before routing component indices, avoiding contraction-by-contraction Wick expansion. Response-field constraints, including vanishing response-response contractions, the ito prescription, and the absence of causal response loops, are enforced during enumeration. Predictions are validated against direct Langevin simulation, agreeing to within the simulation's statistical noise.

</details>


### [30] [The Heat Kernel Expansion: Curvature for Shock Detection in Higher-Order Financial Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19860)
*Mohammad Elsayed,Sara Najem*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文以挪威九年间月度金融网络为研究对象，将董事视为节点、公司视为面，构建单纯复形（simplicial complex）模型。通过欧拉示性数（Euler characteristic）、挠率（torsion）和高阶聚类系数（higher-order clustering coefficients）三种拓扑测度分析网络演化，提出基于热核级数展开系数的几何曲率（curvature）作为新指标，该曲率能灵敏捕捉法律变动带来的网络冲击，而前两种拓扑测度则无法可靠反映此类影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拓扑测度（如欧拉示性数和挠率）在检测金融网络因外部政策（如法律）引发的结构性冲击方面存在局限，需要一种更灵敏的几何度量来捕捉网络中的突变。

Method: 将挪威九年间月度董事与公司关联数据建模为单纯复形，董事为节点，公司为面；计算三种拓扑测度（欧拉示性数、挠率、高阶聚类系数），并提出一种基于热核（heat kernel）时间幂级数展开系数的几何曲率作为新指标。

Result: 欧拉示性数和挠率无法捕捉法律对董事关联施加的影响；而新提出的曲率能灵敏反映因立法导致的网络变化，其拐点（inflection points）对应外部冲击，极小值（minima）对应冲击到达时间。挠率的分量也出现尖锐转变，高阶聚类系数则呈现平滑变化。

Conclusion: 并非所有拓扑测度都能可靠捕捉网络中的冲击；新提出的基于热核的几何曲率是检测金融网络外部冲击的敏感指标。

Abstract: This work follows the evolution of financial networks in Norway over a period of nine years at a monthly rate. The data consist of board directors and their affiliations to companies, which we model as simplicial complexes. In this framework, directors are represented as nodes and companies as faces of the complex. To characterize the latter, we focus on three topological measures: the Euler characteristic, computed through the Betti numbers, torsion computed through the reduced determinant of the higher-order Laplacians, and higher-order clustering coefficients. The first two fail to capture the effect of imposed law on representation, unlike our notion of curvature which is a geometrical measure computed from the coefficients of the series expansion of the heat kernel in powers of time, which is our major contribution in this work. In particular, the Euler characteristic integrates curvature, and thus local information is lost. Subsequently, not every topological measure can reliably capture shocks in networks. Further, the number of spanning trees may undergo significant changes at the lowest order, yet these changes need not be reflected in the torsion. Conversely, the change in the curvature revealed variation in the board interlock due to legislation, and serves as a sensitive measure for detecting shocks in networks. Inflection points in curvature are associated with external forcing, and minima with shock arrival times. Sharp transitions are also observed in the components of torsion, while smooth changes are observed in higher-order clustering.

</details>

### [31] [Bootstrapping Pion Form Factors at Large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19420)
*Jan Albert,Dilara Kosva,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用 bootstrap 方法研究大 N 极限下 QCD 中的介子形状因子（pion form factor），通过解析性、幺正性（unitarity）与 Regge 有界性等约束，得到了低能形状因子系数的严格界以及基于微扰 QCD 输入的现象学界，从而将强子 bootstrap 与微观 QCD 拉格朗日量联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大 N 极限下系统地建立介子形状因子的 bootstrap 研究，利用局域规范不变的探针（gauge-invariant probes）在强子层次与微观 QCD 拉格朗日量之间构建规范的桥梁。

Method: 考虑大 N QCD 中矢量流两点函数、介子矢量形状因子（pion vector form factor）及介子散射振幅（pion scattering amplitude）组成的混合系统。利用解析性（analyticity）、幺正性（unitarity）与 Brodsky-Farrar 渐近标度行为（asymptotic scaling）得到第一类严格普适的界；引入 Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov 类型的方法，通过在有限标度输入微扰紫外行为，获得第二类现象学界。

Result: 获得了低能形状因子系数的严格界，以及关于介子衰变常数（pion decay constant）、渐近自由（asymptotic freedom）标度下界和介子电荷半径（pion charge radius）的现象学约束。组合这些输入后，允许的手征拉格朗日量（chiral Lagrangian）空间收缩到预期的大 N QCD 所在区域。

Conclusion: 局域规范不变的探针能够作为强子 bootstrap 与微观 QCD 拉格朗日量之间的规范桥梁，而 bootstrap 方法在大 N 极限下可有效约束 QCD 的低能参数。

Abstract: We initiate a bootstrap study of pion form factors in large $N$ QCD. We consider the mixed system of the vector-current two-point function, the pion vector form factor, and the pion scattering amplitude in the chiral limit. At large $N$ these observables are meromorphic, with spectral data constrained by unitarity, crossing symmetry, and Regge boundedness. We obtain bounds of two kinds. The first are rigorous and universal: from analyticity, unitarity and the asymptotic Brodsky-Farrar scaling, we constrain low-energy form-factor coefficients. The second are more phenomenological, of the Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov type: feeding in the perturbative ultraviolet behavior at a finite scale lets us bound the pion decay constant, convert a large $N$ lattice measurement into a lower bound on the scale at which asymptotic freedom sets in, and constrain the pion charge radius. Combining these inputs, the space of allowed chiral Lagrangians shrinks toward the region where large $N$ QCD is expected to sit. Our results illustrate how local gauge-invariant probes provide a canonical bridge between the hadronic bootstrap and the microscopic QCD Lagrangian.

### [32] [Calabi-Yau Orientifold Hypersurfaces and their F-theory Uplifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19423)
*Bjoern Hassfeld,Jakob Moritz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种算法，用于构建卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）三维折痕（orientifold）及其F-理论（F-theory）提升到椭圆纤维化（elliptically-fibered）的卡拉比-丘四维流形，这些流形嵌入在环面簇（toric varieties）中，分别余维数为1和2。所得到的四维流形来自6维自反多面体（reflexive polytopes）的三角剖分，除孤立终端奇点外光滑。对于许多四维流形，对偶流形（mirror manifold）的构成立即实现，从而可计算四维流形周期（periods）及七-膜超势（seven-brane superpotential）。算法基于 $\mathtt{CYTools}$ 实现，并通过 GitHub 仓库公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建卡拉比-丘三维折痕及其 F-理论提升到四维流形是弦论唯象学研究中的重要步骤，但现有方法在系统性和计算效率上存在局限。本文旨在提供一种系统化的算法，以高效构建此类流形并计算相关的七-膜超势。

Method: 基于环面几何（toric geometry）和折痕数据（orientifold data），通过构造6维自反多面体的三角剖分生成椭圆纤维化的卡拉比-丘四维流形。算法利用 $\mathtt{CYTools}$ 工具实现，并集成在公开的 GitHub 仓库中。

Result: 算法成功构建了多个卡拉比-丘三维折痕及其F-理论提升的四维流形。许多四维流形的对偶流形可直接构造，从而能够计算四维流形周期和七-膜超势。给出了多个示例以验证算法能力。

Conclusion: 该算法为弦论中卡拉比-丘流形与F-理论模型的系统构造提供了有效工具，尤其在计算七-膜超势方面具有优势。算法基于 $\mathtt{CYTools}$ 并开源，便于社区复现和扩展。

Abstract: We present an algorithm that constructs Calabi-Yau threefold orientifolds and their $F$-theory uplifts to elliptically-fibered Calabi-Yau fourfolds, embedded in toric varieties at codimension one and two respectively. The resulting Calabi-Yau fourfolds arise from triangulations of $6d$ reflexive polytopes -- which our method constructs from orientifold data -- and are smooth away from isolated terminal singularities. For many of our fourfolds, the construction of the mirror manifold is immediate, enabling the computation of fourfold periods, and thus the seven-brane superpotential. We present multiple examples that demonstrate these capabilities. Our algorithms work with $\mathtt{CYTools}$ and are available through a GitHub repository.

### [33] [Moduli Stabilisation for ADD and the Dark Dimension Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19440)
*Andreas P. Braun,Michele Cicoli,Riccardo Milioli,Roberto Valandro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在IIB型大体积弦紧致化框架中，通过K3纤维化Calabi-Yau三折叠，提出了一种模稳定机制，实现了具有一到两个大额外维度的各向异性弦紧致化，对应于ADD和暗维度（Dark Dimension）两种场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦理论中各向异性紧致化（anisotropic compactification）可以自然产生大额外维度（large extra dimensions），但相关模稳定（moduli stabilisation）机制尚未充分建立。本文旨在提供一个该场景下的具体模稳定方案。

Method: 采用IIB型大体积场景（Large Volume Scenario），将Calabi-Yau三折叠选为K3纤维化（K3 fibration）于一个$\mathbb{P}^1$基底的几何结构。利用弦圈（string loops）和高阶导数效应（higher-derivative effects）等微扰修正，将4D K3纤维的体积稳定在较小值，而2D $\mathbb{P}^1$基底的体积则呈指数级大。复结构模（complex structure moduli）的稳定可动态形变$\mathbb{P}^1$基底，对应于Tyurin退化极限（Tyurin degeneration limit），使内部几何有效发展出一个大的一维循环（1D cycle）。

Result: 实现了两种大额外维度场景的统一描述：各向异性极限对应暗维度场景，对称替代极限对应ADD场景。势能可能出现反德西特真空（dS vacuum）或精粹跑动（quintessence runaway），但均需一定程度的精细调节以匹配观测到的宇宙学常数尺度。还提供了一个显式的Calabi-Yau定向折叠（orientifold）例子，包含一致的膜配置（brane setup）、蝌蚪抵消（tadpole cancellation）和模稳定。分析了模谱及相关的唯象约束，包括超对称破缺（supersymmetry breaking）、宇宙学模过产生（cosmological moduli overproduction）和第五力（fifth force）界限。

Conclusion: 该模稳定机制为弦理论中的各向异性紧致化提供了可行实现路径，并能够统一描述ADD和暗维度两种大额外维度场景。同时，显式的定向折叠构造和唯象约束分析为进一步研究该场景的实验可探测性奠定了基础。

Abstract: We provide a moduli stabilisation mechanism for realising anisotropic string compactifications with one or two large extra dimensions, corresponding to the ADD and Dark Dimension scenarios. This is achieved within the type IIB Large Volume Scenario, where an exponentially large Calabi-Yau volume in string units can naturally generate a parametrically low Kaluza-Klein scale. Anisotropy is realised by considering a Calabi-Yau threefold which is a K3 fibration over a $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. The volume of the 4D K3 fibre is stabilised at relatively small values by perturbative corrections to the effective action, in particular string loops and higher-derivative effects, leaving an exponentially large volume of the 2D $\mathbb{P}^1$ base. We argue that complex structure moduli stabilisation can dynamically deform the $\mathbb{P}^1$ base, corresponding to a Tyurin degeneration limit where the internal geometry effectively develops a single large 1D cycle. Within a unified description, the ADD case is instead recovered as a symmetric alternative limit. The potential can feature either a dS vacuum or a quintessence runaway, although in both cases some degree of tuning is required to match the observed cosmological constant scale. We also present an explicit Calabi-Yau orientifold example with consistent brane setup, tadpole cancellation and moduli stabilisation. We analyse the resulting moduli spectrum and associated phenomenological constraints, including supersymmetry breaking, cosmological moduli overproduction and fifth force bounds.

</details>


### [34] [Membrane instantons and non-perturbative effects in $\mathrm{AdS}_{4}/\mathrm{CFT}_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19467)
*Stefan A. Kurlyand*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Freund-Rubin背景（$\mathrm{AdS}_{4}\times \mathrm{Y}_7$）中的欧几里得M2-膜瞬子（M2-brane instanton）。作者证明了在弱$G_2$流形$\mathrm{Y}_7$上，M2-膜的BPS条件等价于近乎平行$G_2$结构下的结合性条件；在Sasaki-Einstein流形中，BPS M2-膜对应继承Sasakian结构的特殊三维子流形。通过分析涨落，将单圈配分函数（one-loop partition function）表达为等变指标（equivariant indices），并在$S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$及$(p,q)$-模型几何中应用该公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解AdS紧化背景中M2-膜瞬子的BPS条件（BPS condition）及其量子修正，特别是单圈配分函数的计算，以推广已知的$S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$瞬子结果，并探索更一般的BPS循环。

Method: 采用数学物理方法：将M2-膜包裹三维循环的BPS条件分别与弱$G_2$流形上的结合性条件（associativity condition）及Sasaki-Einstein流形中的不变子流形结构相联系；通过二次涨落分析将问题约化为横截椭圆复形（transversely elliptic complexes），并利用等变指标公式（equivariant index formula）计算单圈配分函数。

Result: 得到了BPS M2-膜瞬子在两类七维流形（弱$G_2$与Sasaki-Einstein）中的几何刻画；在$S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$背景下，恢复了已知的$S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$瞬子单圈配分函数结果；并推广到$(p,q)$-模型几何中的$S^3$-商空间瞬子。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了M2-膜瞬子BPS条件与特定$G_2$结构几何之间的严格对应，并提供了一个系统的指标理论框架来计算瞬子单圈配分函数，有助于深入理解M-理论（M-theory）在AdS/CFT对应（AdS/CFT correspondence）中的非微扰效应。

Abstract: We study Euclidean M2-brane instantons in Freund-Rubin backgrounds $\mathrm{AdS}_{4}\times \mathrm{Y}_7$. For a seven-dimensional weak $G_{2}$ manifold $\mathrm{Y}_7$, we show that the BPS condition for an M2-brane wrapping a three-cycle $Σ\subset \mathrm{Y}_7$ is equivalent to the associativity condition with respect to the nearly parallel $G_{2}$-structure. When $\mathrm{Y}_7$ is Sasaki-Einstein, we identify a special class of BPS M2-branes that preserve both real internal Killing spinors and correspond to invariant three-dimensional submanifolds inheriting a Sasakian structure. We analyse the quadratic fluctuations around BPS M2-brane instantons in these backgrounds. For the special class of M2-branes in Sasaki-Einstein manifolds, the fluctuation problem reduces to transversely elliptic complexes, and the one-loop partition function can be expressed in terms of the corresponding equivariant indices. We then apply the index formula for the one-loop partition function to invariant M2-branes in $S^{7}/\mathbb{Z}_{k}$, recovering the known result for the $S^3/\mathbb{Z}_k$ instantons and discussing more general invariant BPS cycles. As a further application, we consider M2-brane instantons with $S^3$-quotient worldvolumes in the $(p,q)$-model geometry.

</details>


### [35] [Generating Function of single-centered Black Hole Index in CHL Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19479)
*Ranveer Kumar Singh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文构建了在一般 $\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL模型中单中心黑洞配分函数（generating function of single-centered black hole index）的方法。通过从一个由亚纯Siegel模形式（meromorphic Siegel modular form）描述的四分之一BPS二子的指标中减去双中心黑洞的配分函数来实现。利用CHL模型中的黑洞束缚态嬗变（black hole bound state metamorphosis）来构造双中心黑洞指标的配分函数，并证明了在 $N=2,3$ 情况下该配分函数的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 $\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL模型中，单中心黑洞的配分函数难以直接获得。此前已知四分之一BPS二子（quarter BPS dyons）的指标由亚纯Siegel模形式描述，其中包含了单中心与双中心黑洞（two-centered black holes）态的混合贡献，因此需要一种系统方法将两者分离。

Method: 首先利用四分之一BPS二子的指标（由亚纯Siegel模形式描述）作为出发点；然后通过黑洞束缚态嬗变（black hole bound state metamorphosis）机制构造双中心黑洞指标的配分函数；最后从总指标中减去双中心部分的贡献，从而得到单中心黑洞指标的配分函数。

Result: 成功构建了一般 $\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL模型中单中心黑洞指标的配分函数；对于 $N=2,3$ 的情况，证明了该配分函数的收敛性（convergence）。

Conclusion: 该工作为CHL模型中单中心黑洞状态计数提供了严格的构造方案，并验证了其在低阶情况下的数学收敛性，为后续研究更高阶情况或推广到其他模型奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present the construction of the generating function of single-centered black hole index in general $\mathbb{Z}_N$ CHL models. This is done by subtracting from the index of quarter BPS dyons, described by a meromorphic Siegel modular form, the generating function for the index of two-centered black holes. We use black hole bound state metamorphosis in CHL models for the construction of the generating function of two-centered black hole index. We prove the convergence of the generating function for the cases $N=2,3$.

</details>


### [36] [Operational Tube-Sector Theory of Quantum State Distinguishability Under Generalized Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19678)
*Song He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在多体系统中建立了量子态可区分性（quantum-state distinguishability）的变分原理（variational principle），该原理适用于包括不可逆情况（noninvertible cases）在内的广义对称性（generalized symmetries），并由融合范畴（fusion categories）描述。标准保真度（fidelity）和对称性分辨（symmetry-resolved）诊断被视为更精细操作结构的粗粒化极限。最优测量结构由边界管代数（boundary tube algebra）的中心唯一确定，其原始幂等元（primitive idempotents）定义了管区概率（tube-sector probabilities），从而细化了基于保真度和对称性分辨的描述。该构造在融合范畴间具有普适性，且不依赖于微观实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量子态可区分性诊断（如保真度和对称性分辨）缺乏对广义对称性（包括不可逆对称性）约束下精细操作结构的理论描述。本文旨在建立一个更完善的变分原理框架，以揭示对称性约束下量子态可区分性的根本结构。

Method: 定义了对称性约束测量资源理论（symmetry-constrained measurement resource theory）中物理上可允许的仪器（instruments）所满足的条件：完全正定性（complete positivity）、纠缠截断局域性（entanglement-cut locality）、边界模协变性（boundary-module covariance）和序列稳定性（sequential stability）。通过边界管代数的中心唯一确定了最优测量结构。

Result: 最优测量结构由边界管代数的中心唯一确定，即 $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{phys}} = Z\!\left(\mathrm{Tube}_{\mathcal{C}}(\mathcal{M}_A)\right)$，其原始幂等元定义了管区概率。相应的管区正算子值测度（tube POVM）是极端的（extremal），并在对称性约束下实现最优的一击假设检验可区分性（one-shot hypothesis-testing distinguishability）。

Conclusion: 该构造在融合范畴间具有普适性，且不依赖于微观实现的具体细节，为广义对称性约束下的量子态可区分性提供了统一的数学框架。

Abstract: A variational principle for quantum-state distinguishability is established in many-body systems with generalized symmetries, including noninvertible cases described by fusion categories. Standard fidelity and symmetry-resolved diagnostics emerge as coarse-grained limits of a more refined operational structure. When symmetry actions terminate at entanglement cuts, distinguishability is governed by boundary tube algebras within a symmetry-constrained measurement resource theory. The physically admissible instruments are characterized by complete positivity, entanglement-cut locality, boundary-module covariance, and sequential stability. The resulting optimal measurement structure is uniquely fixed by the center of the boundary tube algebra, $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{phys}} = Z\!\left(\mathrm{Tube}_{\mathcal{C}}(\mathcal{M}_A)\right)$, whose primitive idempotents define tube-sector probabilities that refine fidelity-based and symmetry-resolved descriptions. ### [43] [Macroscopic Black-Hole Remnants in a Nonlocal Field Theory: Towards Hawking Radiation in SFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20314)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将一个无质量标量场与动力学黑洞背景的相互作用进行修正，引入弦场论中的模糊化算子（smearing operator）$e^{\ell^2\Box}$，其中 $\ell$ 是弦长尺度（string length scale）。通过计算推迟时间（retarded time）$u$ 下出射霍金粒子的时间依赖期望值 $\langle \hat{N}(u) \rangle$ 来刻画辐射演化。

Conclusion: 辐射提前终止的物理机制在于：塌缩的壳（collapsing shell）对跨普朗克模式（trans-Planckian modes）变得有效不可见。这一结果意味着黑洞会留下一个宏观残余物（macroscopic remnant），从而为黑洞信息悖论提供了一种替代性解决方案。

Abstract: We demonstrate that, for a large black hole of radius $a$, Hawking radiation terminates around the scrambling time $u_{\text{scr}} \equiv 2a \log(a/\ell)$ due to the nonlocal, exponential suppression of trans-Planckian interactions inherent in string field theory (SFT). This early shutoff reflects the property that the collapsing shell becomes effectively invisible to trans-Planckian modes, offering an alternative resolution to the black hole information paradox via a macroscopic remnant.

These extended-scale correlations are able to `feel around' the region where a closed trapped surface is about to form, and to react by nucleating fuzzball structure that destroys semiclassical spacetime.
