Motivation: 超越BPS态计数，探究扭转为二（twist-two）形变如何修改BPS上同调（BPS cohomologies）的显式形式，并检验单调态与偶然态扇区之间的动力学关联性。

Method: 在D1D5 CFT中，针对不同中心荷（central charge）计算扇区 (h,j)=(1,0) 的超荷作用，导出初态（primary states）的显式表达式；比较自由极限（free regime）与引力极限（gravity regime）下的受保护三点耦合，并分析态映射与超荷对易性约束。

Result: 发现两种描述之间的一致性要求对单调态与偶然态的识别施加非平凡约束；特别地，联系不同中心荷理论的映射必须且可以与定义上链复形（cochain complex）的超荷对易。找到一个显式例子：两个单调态与一个偶然态之间存在非零耦合，表明两扇区动力学连通。

Conclusion: 单调态与偶然态扇区并非动力学退耦（dynamically decoupled），而是通过三点耦合相互连接；这一结果对D1D5 CFT中偶然性机制的理解和态映射的构造具有重要约束。

Abstract: We reconsider the "fortuity'' mechanism in the D1D5 CFT focusing on the K3 symmetric orbifold. Going beyond the counting of BPS states, we investigate perturbatively how the explicit form of the BPS cohomologies is modified by the twist-two deformations. We calculate the action of the supercharges in the sector $(h,j)=(1,0)$ for different values of the central charge and derive explicit expressions for the primary states. Equipped with this information, we compare some protected three-point couplings in the free and the gravity regime. We show that agreement between the two descriptions imposes non-trivial constraints on the identification of monotone and fortuitous states. In particular, we argue that the map relating theories with different values of the central charge must and can be defined so as to commute with the supercharges that define the cochain complex. We then study the three-point correlators between the fortuitous and monotone states identified in our analysis to assess whether the two sectors are dynamically decoupled. We find an explicit example of a non-vanishing coupling between two monotone and a fortuitous state, providing evidence that the two sectors are dynamically connected.

</details>


### [46] [Shadow Completion in Celestial OPEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20433)
*Reiko Liu,Zijian Liu,Wen-Jie Ma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证了天体OPE（celestial OPE）必须补充影子基算子（shadow-basis operators）。虽然影子变换（shadow transform）不引入新的体（bulk）自由度，但它在边界天体理论（boundary celestial theory）中提供了不同的原初态（primary state）。通过OPE一致性条件，证明普通天体OPE仅在梅林基（Mellin-basis）交换下不自洽，必须同时包含影子基代表。由此得到影子完备的OPE（shadow-completed OPE），其影子OPE系数由普通共线系数（collinear coefficient）通过普适影子因子（universal shadow factor）确定。本文讨论了对应的边界希尔伯特空间（Hilbert-space）解释，将论证推广到胶子（gluon）和引力子（graviton），并通过树级正则天体振幅（regular celestial amplitudes）直接验证了影子交换，包括标量2→n分析和显式五点例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有天体OPE仅在梅林基交换下无法自洽闭合，需要引入影子基算子来完善OPE结构，从而解决边界天体理论中的描述完备性问题。

Method: 通过OPE一致性条件（OPE consistency）推导影子基算子的必要性；计算影子OPE系数与普通共线系数的关系；利用树级正则天体振幅进行直接验证，包括标量2→n分析和五点例子；并推广至胶子和引力子情形。

Result: 影子基算子是天体OPE自洽闭合的必要补充；影子OPE系数由普通共线系数乘以普适影子因子唯一确定；在树级振幅中（包括标量和胶子/引力子情形）直接验证了影子交换的存在。

Conclusion: 天体OPE必须由影子基算子补充才能实现自洽闭合；影子变换不引入新的体自由度，但在边界理论中表现为不同的原初态；影子完备OPE在树级振幅中得到了直接验证。

Abstract: We argue that celestial OPEs must be supplemented by shadow-basis operators. Although the shadow transform does not introduce new bulk degrees of freedom, it provides a distinct primary state in the boundary celestial theory. From OPE consistency, we show that the ordinary celestial OPE does not close on Mellin-basis exchanges alone. Rather, the same exchanged bulk particle must also appear through its shadow-basis representative. This leads to a shadow-completed OPE, with the shadow OPE coefficient fixed by the ordinary collinear coefficient through the universal shadow factor. We discuss the corresponding boundary Hilbert-space interpretation, extend this argument to gluons and gravitons, and verify the shadow exchange directly in tree-level regular celestial amplitudes, including a scalar $2\rightarrow n$ analysis and an explicit five-point example.

### [47] [Cosmological history after higher dimensional inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20486)
*Luis A. Anchordoqui,Ignatios Antoniadis,Jules Cunat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种宇宙学历史模型，将高维暴胀（higher dimensional inflation）与标准宇宙学衔接，通过稳定额外维（extra dimensions）并在暴胀结束后避免体引力子（bulk gravitons）的过度产生，从而解释引力微弱与宇宙尺度巨大之间的层级问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释粒子物理与宇宙学中的两大层级（hierarchies）——实际引力微弱与可观测宇宙的巨大尺度——之间的关系，并确保高维暴胀结束后额外维的稳定机制与引力子不过度产生。

Method: 提出一种宇宙学历史模型，描述暴胀结束后至再加热温度（reheating temperature）期间的宇宙演化过程，前提是假设额外维在暴胀结束时存在某种稳定化机制。

Result: 只有约微米大小的一个或两个额外维才与观测到的近似标量不变的原初密度扰动功率谱（scale invariant power spectrum of primordial density perturbations）一致；该宇宙学历史能保证早期宇宙中体引力子不出现过度产生。

Conclusion: 所提出的宇宙学历史成功连接了高维暴胀时期与标准宇宙学的开端，为解释两大层级提供了一个自洽的暴胀后演化框架。

Abstract: It was proposed that extra dimensions can acquire large size by higher dimensional inflation connecting two large hierarchies in particle physics and cosmology, namely the weakness of the actual gravitational force to the largeness of the observable universe, in terms of one fundamental scale. This proposal is consistent with the observed approximate scale invariant power spectrum of primordial density perturbations only for one or two extra dimensions of around the micron size. Assuming a stabilisation mechanism of the extra dimensions at the end of inflation, here we propose a cosmological history that describes the Universe evolution after the end of inflation up to the reheating temperature, that guarantees the absence of bulk gravitons at earlier times, avoiding their overproduction in the early universe. The proposed cosmological history connects the period of higher dimensional inflation to the beginning of the standard cosmology.

### [48] [Sequential replica exchange with solute tempering for atomistic modeling of supramolecular polymer structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19418)
*Hadi H. Arefi,Takeshi Yamamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种逐步构建的序列性溶质回火（sequential REST）方法，用于高效建模一维自组装超分子聚合物。该方法通过逐个添加单体并对新单体进行增强采样，在降低计算成本的同时，有效提升了副本遍历效率，并成功生成了具有特征氢键模式的聚合物结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全原子分子动力学模拟在预测自组装体系的精细原子结构方面仍面临挑战。现有的全局性溶质回火（REST）方法虽然原则上能预测任何形貌，但存在因有序-无序转变导致的副本遍历效率低下、以及副本数量随体系规模增长等计算缺陷。

Method: 在一维聚合假设下，采用逐步构建方式模拟超分子聚合物：逐个向体系添加新单体，仅对新单体施加REST增强采样，基于能量评分函数寻找其最优结合位点；重复单体添加与增强采样过程，直至获得目标长度的聚合物结构。

Result: 在显式溶剂模型超分子聚合物测试中，该方法以降低的计算成本生成了具有特征氢键（H-bonding）模式的聚合物结构，并显著提升了副本遍历效率。

Conclusion: 序列性REST方法对于超分子聚合物建模具有实用价值，尤其适用于全局REST模拟计算代价过高的场景。

Abstract: Predicting detailed atomistic structures of self-assembling systems remains a challenge for all-atom molecular dynamics simulations. Replica exchange with solute tempering (REST) has been used to study those systems by accelerating all monomers in a global and uniform manner. While such a global approach can in principle predict any morphology of the system, it has computational drawbacks such as inefficient replica traversal due to order-disorder transitions and the growing number of replicas with system size. To address these issues, here we propose an alternative, stepwise construction approach to modeling supramolecular polymers under the assumption of one-dimensional polymerization. Specifically, we generate polymer structures by adding new monomers one by one to the system and applying REST to the new monomers to find their optimal binding positions based on an energy-based scoring function. The monomer addition and enhanced sampling are repeated sequentially until a polymer of desired length is obtained. We test the above procedure using a model supramolecular polymer in explicit solvent, and show that it can generate a polymer structure with characteristic H-bonding patterns at reduced computational costs, while also improving the efficiency of replica traversal significantly. We thus expect that the sequential REST will be useful for modeling supramolecular polymers, particularly for cases where global REST simulations are too demanding computationally.

### [49] [Collective phases in overdamped magnetic self-propelled spherocylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19498)
*Francisca Guzmán-Lastra,Néstor Sepúlveda*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过二维自推进磁椭球柱体（self-propelled spherocylinder）的集体动力学模拟，发现粒子伸长与分布式磁荷（distributed magnetic charge）共同提供了一套最小化且实验可调的调控手段，可控制气体、极性群、链条、涡旋对齐及锁定二聚体等多种集体态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有点偶极（point-dipole）或圆盘模型无法捕捉磁力矩与空间位阻对齐之间的竞争效应；磁活性物质（magnetic active matter）中如何通过粒子几何与磁矩分布实现集体态调控仍不清楚。

Method: 采用哑铃模型（dumbbell model），将磁偶极矩（magnetic dipole moment）建模为两个相反单极子 $\pm Q$，沿粒子指向（director）方向相距 $\ell$；结合自推进椭球柱体几何，独立改变单极子间距与偶极强度，在二维空间中进行集体动力学模拟。

Result: 系统展现出五种集体态：气体相（gas）、极性群相（polar flock）、链条相（chain）、涡旋对齐相（vortex-alignment）和锁定二聚体相（locked-dimer）。粒子伸长与分布式磁荷是调控这些相干态的关键参数。

Conclusion: 粒子伸长与分布式磁荷构成一套最小化且实验可访问的调控旋钮（tuning knobs），可用于控制磁性活性物质中的相干态，为自组织磁性微泳体（self-organized magnetic microswimmer）和活性胶体组装体（active colloidal assembly）的设计提供直接指导。

Abstract: We study the collective dynamics of self-propelled spherocylinders carrying magnetic dipole moments in two dimensions. Magnetic interactions are modeled as two opposite monopoles $\pm Q$ separated by a distance $\ell$ along the particle director, a dumbbell model that remains well-defined at short range and introduces an explicit geometric lever arm for the magnetic torque. This approach, combined with the elongated particle geometry, produces a torque that competes with steric alignment in a manner inaccessible to point-dipole or disk models. By independently varying monopole separation and dipole strength (parameters that map directly onto the geometry and magnetization of cylindrical magnets) we show that the system navigates a rich landscape of collective states: gas, polar flock, chain, vortex-alignment, and locked-dimer phases. Our results establish that particle elongation and distributed magnetic charge together provide a minimal, experimentally accessible set of tuning knobs for controlling coherent states in magnetic active matter, with direct implications for the design of self-organized magnetic microswimmers and active colloidal assemblies.

### [50] [Epithelia Realize Nematopolar Topological Defect Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19844)
*Tianxiang Ma,Niels de Graaf Sousa,Valeriia Grudtsyna,Farzan Vafa,Amin Doostmohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于细胞形状的极性序参量（shape-based polar order parameter），证明了该参量可作为整合上皮单层（epithelial monolayer）中向列取向、主应力和细胞运动信息的统一生物力学度量。实验和建模结果表明，上皮组织组织成一种混合极性-向列相（mixed polar-nematic phase），其形成由主动应力与极性-向列弹性的耦合驱动，为上皮单层作为向列极性物质（nematopolar matter）的行为提供了直接实验证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上皮单层中细胞的集体行为涉及复杂的力学与极性相互作用，但缺乏一个能够整合结构向列取向（nematic directors）、主应力（principal stresses）和细胞运动等多种物理信息的统一度量。

Method: 首先引入基于细胞形状的极性序参量以捕捉细胞结构不对称性；结合明场成像（bright-field imaging）和牵引力显微镜（traction force microscopy）测量形状极性（shape polarity）的力学相关性；通过机械扰动（mechanical perturbations）改变基底刚度（substrate stiffness）和细胞-细胞粘附（cell-cell adhesion），观察缺陷密度和畴壁长度变化；最后构建极性-向列活性物质（polar-nematic active matter）的最小连续模型（minimal continuum model）解释实验现象。

Result: 形状极性可整合向列取向、主应力和细胞运动信息；组织自发形成整数（±1）与半整数（±1/2）缺陷共存的混合极性-向列相；基底刚度和细胞-细胞粘附调控缺陷密度以及连接同号正半整数缺陷的畴壁长度。

Conclusion: 上皮单层表现为向列极性物质，其活跃状态由极性弹性与向列弹性之间耦合共同塑造；混合相的驱动力来自主动应力与极性-向列弹性的相互作用。

Abstract: We introduce a shape-based polar order parameter that captures the structural asymmetry of cells within epithelial monolayers. By combining bright-field imaging and traction force microscopy, we demonstrate that shape polarity serves as a unifying biomechanical metric, integrating the physical information encoded by nematic directors, principal stresses, and cellular motion. Furthermore, we show that the tissue organizes into a mixed polar-nematic phase, characterized by the coexistence of integer ($\pm 1$) and half-integer ($\pm 1/2$) defects. Through mechanical perturbations, we demonstrate that both substrate stiffness and cell-cell adhesion modulate the density of these excitations and the length of domain walls binding like-signed positive half-integer defects. Using a minimal continuum model of polar-nematic active matter, we establish that this mixed phase is fundamentally driven by the interplay of active stresses and polar-nematic elasticity. These findings provide a direct experimental evidence that epithelial monolayers behave as nematopolar matter, in which coupled polar and nematic elastic interactions jointly shape the active state

</details>


### [51] [Shear-Induced Electrophoretic Migration Perpendicular to the Electric Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19916)
*Andrés Rodríguez-Galán,Raúl Fernández-Mateo,Pablo García-Sánchez,Antonio Ramos*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展浓差极化（concentration polarization）理论，揭示了表面电导介电粒子在剪切流和外加电场共同作用下发生横向迁移（lateral migration）的物理机制，推导出迁移速度表达式，并预测了在杜欣数（Dukhin number）为1量级时迁移方向的反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期微通道电泳与压力驱动流结合的实验观察到微粒垂直于外加电场方向发生横向迁移，但流体惯性（fluid inertia）效应在此条件下可忽略，现有理论无法解释该现象的物理机制，因此需要提出新的理论模型。

Method: 在先前浓差极化理论的基础上，考虑一个具有表面电导（surface conductance）的介电粒子（dielectric particle），同时受到外加电场（external electric field）和剪切流（shear flow）的作用，通过对称性分析与理论推导建立横向迁移速度模型。

Result: 剪切流打破了粒子周围离子浓度场在垂直于外加电场方向上的对称性，从而驱动横向迁移；迁移速度由电泳（electrophoretic）和扩散泳（diffusiophoretic）两种贡献组成，其显式表达式依赖于ζ电位（zeta potential）和杜欣数，典型速度量级为μm/s；模型还预测当杜欣数接近1时，迁移方向发生反转。

Conclusion: 该理论成功解释了实验观测到的微粒横向迁移现象，阐明了浓度极化与剪切流耦合的物理机制，为理解复杂微流控系统中的粒子输运提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Recent experiments combining electrophoresis with pressure-driven flows in microchannels have revealed that microparticles undergo lateral migration perpendicular to the applied electric field. Although fluid inertia has been proposed as a possible explanation, inertial effects are negligibly small in these regimes, leaving the underlying physical mechanism an open question. In this study, we address these observations by extending previous theoretical work on concentration polarization,i.e., the external-field-induced modification of the ionic concentration field surrounding a dielectric object. We consider a dielectric particle with surface conductance subjected simultaneously to an external electric field and a shear flow. We show that the shear flow breaks the symmetry of the ionic concentration around the particle in the direction perpendicular to the applied field, thereby driving lateral migration. We demonstrate that the resulting migration velocity comprises two distinct contributions: an electrophoretic and a diffusiophoretic component. Our theory yields an explicit expression for the velocity magnitude as a function of the zeta potential and the Dukhin number, predicting typical speeds on the order of $\mathrmμ$m/s for representative experimental parameters. Notably, the model also predicts a reversal in the migration direction for Dukhin numbers of order unity.

### [52] [Electrostatic effects in nano-reactor-confined charge regulated macroions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20040)
*Manit Klawtanong,Petch Khunpetch,Huaqiong Li,Shigeyuki Komura*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个包含电荷调节（charge regulation）大分子离子（macroions）的纳米反应器（nano-reactor）热力学模型，基于线性化Debye-Hückel近似求解Poisson-Boltzmann方程，分析了非均匀电解质分布、大分子离子电荷特征及对反应器壁压力的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在描述纳米尺度下带电大分子离子与电解质溶液耦合行为时，往往忽略了大分子表面电荷解离（charge dissociation）的动态调控机制，亟需建立一个能够同时包含电荷调节（charge regulation）与Poisson-Boltzmann静电学的理论框架。

Method: 基于电荷调节（charge regulation）形式论，在Poisson-Boltzmann静电学框架下纳入大分子表面分子基团的电荷解离效应；采用线性化的Debye-Hückel型近似求解平衡方程，分析非均匀电解质分布与大分子离子电荷特征。

Result: 大分子离子的表面电荷不对称性/对称性对静电势空间分布有显著影响；有效屏蔽长度（effective screening length）呈现非单调行为，源于外部溶液与大分子有效电荷之间的复杂耦合；纳米反应器边界总压力随反应器半径和本体盐浓度增大而单调减小，且受反应器表面电荷密度及大分子离子数量的强烈影响。

Conclusion: 电荷调节机制与大分子表面电荷不对称性是决定纳米反应器内静电特性和渗透压的关键因素，为调控纳米尺度反应器中的离子输运与力学平衡提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We formulate a thermodynamic model of a nano-reactor containing charge-regulated macroions within an electrolyte-permeable enclosure. The model is then formalized within the Poisson-Boltzmann electrostatics augmented by the consistent inclusion of the charge dissociation of molecular groups residing on the surface of the entrapped macroions via charge regulation formalism. By solving the basic equilibrium equations in the linearized Debye-Hückel type approximation, we analyze the salient features of the inhomogeneous electrolyte distribution and macroion charge. We found that the surface charge asymmetry/symmetry of the macroions strongly affects the spatial profile of electrostatic potential. The effective screening length shows the non-monotonic behavior, arising from the complex interplay between the bathing external solution and macroion effective charges, which govern charge regulation equilibria. The total pressure at the nano-reactor enclosure boundary decreases monotonically as the enclosure radius and the ionic bulk salt concentration increase. Also, the resulting pressure is strongly influenced by the surface charge densities of the nano-reactor and the number of confined macroions.

### [53] [Constraint-Limited Tube Orientation of Entangled Polymers in Oscillatory Shear Deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20049)
*Dario Nichetti,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于分子层面提出缠结聚合物在振荡剪切变形中非线性指数（NLI）的描述，核心假设是管取向张量的剪切分量存在几何上限 S_xy ≤ 1/2，由此导出约束限制的取向闭合，使 NLI 渐进逼近最大值 3，并给出半饱和应变 γ_s 和非线性起始应变 γ_c 的分子表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缠结聚合物在振荡剪切下的非线性指数缺乏分子层面的理论描述，现有模型常依赖人为截断而非物理机制来解释 NLI 的上限行为。

Method: 假设管取向张量的剪切分量存在几何上限 S_xy ≤ 1/2，结合对流约束释放（CCR）、链拉伸和管膨胀效应，构建约束限制的取向闭合（constraint-limited orientation closure），使得 NLI 随应变振幅先近似增长后渐进趋近极限值 NLI_max = 3，而非通过人为截断实现。

Result: 导出半饱和应变 γ_s 的分子表达式，定义为 NLI(γ_s)=3/2，表达式包含缠结数、振荡频率以及剩余取向约束的临界数；进一步推导了线性、稀疏长链支化和规整支化聚合物的非线性起始应变 γ_c 的架构依赖表达式。

Conclusion: 所得框架在傅里叶谐波分析、基于 CCR 的管动力学以及高度形变缠结聚合物液体中取向记忆的逐步丧失之间建立了简洁的桥梁。

Abstract: We develop a molecularly motivated description of the nonlinear index (NLI) in oscillatory shear deformation of entangled polymers. The central assumption is that the shear component of the tube-orientation tensor cannot grow without bound. Convective constraint release (CCR), chain stretch, and tube dilation progressively reduce the number and lifetime of orientational constraints, but the maximum shear alignment of a tube segment is geometrically limited by $S_{xy}\leq 1/2$. This motivates a constraint-limited orientation closure in which the NLI first grows approximately with strain amplitude and then approaches the limiting value $\mathrm{NLI}_{\max}=3$ asymptotically rather than through an artificial cutoff. The same framework yields a molecular expression for the characteristic half-saturation strain $γ_s$, defined by $\mathrm{NLI}(γ_s)=3/2$, in terms of the entanglement number, oscillation frequency, and a critical number of remaining orientational constraints. We further derive architecture-dependent expressions for the nonlinear onset strain $γ_c$ for linear, sparsely long-chain-branched, and more regularly branched polymers. The resulting framework provides a compact bridge between Fourier harmonic analysis, CCR-based tube dynamics, and the progressive loss of orientational memory in highly deformed entangled polymer liquids.

</details>


### [54] [\textit{E.\ coli} bacterium near corrugated surfaces: near-suface swimming, escape, and hydrodynamic trapping}](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20070)
*Pierre Martin,Gonçalo C. Antunes,Holger Stark*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过流体力学模拟，系统分析了非翻滚大肠杆菌在波浪形无滑移曲面附近的游泳行为。结果表明，表面曲率从低到高会依次引发：近表面持久游动（顺时针轨迹）、脊处逃逸（存在临界曲率）、以及沿沟槽方向的振荡游动（逆时针轨迹），从而揭示了表面形貌（surface topography）在细菌表面探索中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细菌常在复杂环境中游动，其中的表面普遍存在且很少是平坦的；表面形貌（surface topography）和曲率（curvature）对细菌运动、表面附着及生物膜（biofilm）形成具有重要影响，因此理解表面几何形状的作用具有重要的生物物理与生态意义。

Method: 研究者对非翻滚大肠杆菌（Escherichia coli）在正弦波状无滑移表面附近的游泳行为进行流体动力学模拟。细菌模型由刚性的球柱形（spherocylindrical）细胞体和基于Kirchhoff杆理论（Kirchhoff rod theory）的柔性鞭毛组成；周围流体则采用多粒子碰撞动力学（multi-particle collision dynamics, MPCD）方法进行模拟。

Result: 在低曲率下，细菌表现出近表面持久游动与顺时针（clockwise）轨迹，与平直无滑移壁面附近的行为一致。随曲率增加，游向脊（ridge）的细菌可从表面脱离，据此估算出临界曲率（critical curvature）。更高曲率下，表面几何诱导沿沟槽（groove）方向的振荡游动，减少逃逸机会并增强细菌捕获；沟槽附近的约束使得游泳方向由顺时针反转为逆时针（counter-clockwise）。

Conclusion: 波浪形表面的三维形貌（three-dimensional surface topography）对细菌表面探索行为具有显著影响，不同曲率尺度可分别促进附着、逃逸或捕获，这为理解微生物在复杂界面环境中的行为提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Bacteria often swim in complex environments where surfaces are ubiquitous and rarely flat. Surface topography and curvature can strongly affect bacterial motility, with important consequences for surface exploration, adhesion, and biofilm formation. Here, we investigate the swimming of a non-tumbling \textit{Escherichia coli} bacterium near an undulating no-slip surface using hydrodynamic simulations of a detailed model bacterium. The latter is described by a rigid spherocylindrical cell body and flexible flagella modeled with the Kirchhoff rod theory, while the surrounding fluid is simulated using the method of multi-particle collision dynamics. At low curvatures of the sinusoidal surface modulations, the bacterium exhibits persistent near-surface swimming and clockwise trajectories, consistent with the known behavior near flat no-slip walls. As the curvature increases, bacteria swimming toward a ridge can escape from the surface, which we use to estimate a critical curvature where surface detachment is more likely. At larger curvatures, we find that the surface geometry promotes oscillatory swimming along the groove direction, which reduces escape opportunities and, therefore, enhances bacterial trapping. Indeed, the confinement around the groove reverses the swimming of the bacterium from clockwise to counter-clockwise, as we demonstrate by two minimal models. Thus our work highlights the importance of the three-dimensional surface topography in bacterial surface exploration.

</details>


### [55] [Independent Control of Transport and Order in a Ratcheted Colloidal Suspension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20190)
*Sudipta Mandal,Dipanjan Chakraborty,Debasish Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模分子动力学模拟，研究了二维排斥性相互作用胶体悬浮液在随机非对称分段线性闪烁棘轮驱动下的定向输运。频率调谐与棘轮不对称性提供了两种独立控制粒子流的方法，分别通过耦合结构重组或保持六角取向序来实现对输运的调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在驱动胶体悬浮液中，如何通过频率调谐和棘轮不对称性这两种手段独立控制粒子流，并理解二者对输运行为及微观结构的不同影响机制。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，对二维排斥性相互作用胶体在随机非对称分段线性闪烁棘轮（stochastic asymmetric piecewise-linear flashing ratchet）驱动下的定向输运进行研究。

Result: 在固定不对称性下，粒子流随棘轮频率呈现共振行为，由相互作用粒子的集体弛豫动力学决定；输运增强伴随缺陷介导的结构变化，呈现密度依赖的六角相（hexatic）和类固态（solid-like）状态，较大电流通常对应较弱的排序。固定频率下，改变棘轮不对称性主要调节定向偏向强度，可显著增强电流，但六角序基本保持不变；在平衡六角熔化（hexatic-melting）区域附近，可在不大幅破坏六重取向序（sixfold orientational order）的条件下产生显著定向电流。

Conclusion: 频率调谐将输运与结构重组相耦合，而不对称性调谐主要控制输运而保持结构基本不变，两者为调控驱动胶体悬浮液中的输运与有序性提供了不同且互补的途径。

Abstract: We study directed transport in a two-dimensional suspension of
  repulsively interacting colloids driven by a stochastic asymmetric
  piecewise-linear flashing ratchet using large-scale molecular
  dynamics simulations. The driving frequency and the ratchet
  asymmetry offer two independent ways of controlling the particle
  current, but they affect the suspension differently. At fixed
  asymmetry, the current shows a resonance with ratcheting frequency
  that is set by the collective relaxation dynamics of the interacting
  particles. The resulting increase in transport is accompanied by
  defect-mediated structural changes, showing density-dependent
  hexatic and solid-like states, with larger currents generally
  associated with weaker ordering. By contrast, at fixed frequency,
  changing the ratchet asymmetry mainly alters the strength of the
  directed bias and can significantly enhance the current while
  leaving the hexatic order largely unchanged. Near the equilibrium
  hexatic-melting regime, this makes it possible to generate
  substantial directed currents without strongly disrupting sixfold
  orientational order. These results show that frequency tuning
  couples transport to structural reorganization, whereas asymmetry
  tuning primarily controls transport leaving the structure largely
  unaltered, providing distinct and complementary routes for
  manipulating transport and order in driven colloidal suspensions.

</details>


### [56] [On the Renormalization Group Flow of Active Flocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20552)
*Kevin T. Grosvenor,Subodh P. Patil*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用统计场论中的MSRDJ作用量形式，研究了马尔萨斯群团（Malthusian flocks）的主动重整化，通过广义伽利略对称性（generalized Galileon symmetry）及其Ward恒等式，在二维各向同性扩散极限下计算了耦合常数的全阶重整化，发现了由Δ/κ=2π处的边缘顶点不稳定性（marginal vertex instability）分隔的高斯相与强相互作用对称性保护无带隙相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主动群团（active flocks）作为非平衡系统的典型代表，其重整化群行为长期以来存在争议，尤其是在Toner-Tu理论框架下，不同文献对长程有序（long range order）的稳定性提出了相互矛盾的论断。本文旨在通过严格的统计场论重整化分析，澄清这些争议并统一理解。

Method: 采用MSRDJ作用量形式（MSRDJ action formulation）描述随机系统的统计场论，在二维空间各向同性扩散极限下工作；利用广义伽利略对称性的非线性实现（non-linear realization）及其对应的Ward恒等式，计算耦合常数的重整化和反常维度（anomalous dimensions）至所有阶。

Result: 发现一条固定点线（line of fixed points）以及在Δ/κ=2π处的一个边缘顶点不稳定性。该不稳定性将系统分为高斯相（Gaussian phase）和强相互作用的对称性保护无带隙相（symmetry-protected gapless phase）。当Δ/κ低于临界值时，无带隙激发（gapless excitations）的存在源于广义伽利略对称性的软定理（soft/Adler zero theorems），暗示长程有序的持续存在。

Conclusion: 本文的结果调和了文献中的多项相互矛盾的论断；该分析可推广至各向异性扩散以及密度涨落重新引入的群团系统，为理解主动物质中超越传统Wilson-Fisher临界性的非平衡临界行为提供了统一框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the statistical field-theoretic renormalization of active flocks via the MSRDJ action formulation for stochastic systems, focusing on the Toner-Tu theory of `Malthusian flocks', or polar-ordered, momentum non-conserving active fluids where relaxation times for density fluctuations are so short that they can be eliminated as a hydrodynamic variable. Working in the limit of isotropic diffusion in two spatial dimensions, we compute the renormalization of the couplings and their anomalous dimensions to all orders, facilitated by a non-linear realization of a generalized \textit{Galileon} symmetry and its associated Ward identities. We find a range of behavior depending on the parameters of the theory. If $κ$ is the diffusion coefficient and $Δ$ is the variance of the noise, we find a line of fixed points and a marginal vertex instability at $Δ/κ= 2π$. This instability separates Gaussian, and strongly interacting, symmetry-protected gapless phases, realizing non-equilibrium critical behavior beyond conventional Wilson--Fisher criticality. The existence of gapless excitations in both phases can be traced to the soft (Adler zero) theorems associated with the generalized Galileon symmetry, and implies the persistence of long range order when $Δ/κ$ is below the critical value. We revisit and contextualize various claims and counter-claims in the literature in light of our findings, and discuss extensions of our analysis to anisotropic diffusion, and towards flocks where density fluctuations are reintroduced.

</details>


### [57] [Activity driven buckling and pattern formation in shells of oriented solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20261)
*Niels de Graaf Sousa,Varun Venkatesh,Amin Doostmohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究活性定向固体壳层（shells of active oriented solid）的屈曲不稳定性与非线性模式。通过线性稳定性分析发现，活性应力驱动了被动脉壳中不存在的新型屈曲失稳，其模态由向列取向（nematic orientation）和活性符号选择，包括轴向、周向和螺旋形变形。周向模式在极小活性下即失稳。非线性模拟进一步揭示了稳态菱形图案以及振荡、传播畴壁和行波等持久动态状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索嵌入可变形弹性表面的定向有序活性粒子所构成的活性定向固体壳层的行为，特别是活性应力如何驱动传统被动脉壳中不存在的屈曲失稳与非线性模式。

Method: 采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）研究圆柱几何活性壳层的失稳模式，并通过完全非线性模拟（full nonlinear simulations）验证线性分析结果并探索非线性动力学行为。

Result: 活性应力驱动了轴向、周向和螺旋形三类屈曲模式，模式由向列取向和活性符号选择；周向模式在任意小活性下即失稳（因无拉伸代价）；非线性模拟发现了稳态菱形图案以及振荡、传播畴壁和行波等持续动态状态。

Conclusion: 建立了活性定向固体壳层材料的基本屈曲模态和涌现模式，对活性生物组织和工程响应材料具有潜在意义。

Abstract: We investigate shells of active oriented solid, materials in which orientationally ordered active particles are embedded in a deformable elastic surface. Focusing on cylindrical geometries, we show that active stresses drive a new class of buckling instabilities and nonlinear patterns absent in passive shells. Linear stability analysis reveals that the unstable buckling mode is selected by the nematic orientation and activity sign, leading to axial, circumferential, and helical deformations. Remarkably, circumferential modes become unstable at arbitrarily small activity due to the absence of stretching costs. The results of the linear stability analysis are corroborated by full nonlinear simulations, which further uncover steady diamond shaped patterns and persistent dynamical states including oscillations, traveling domain walls, and propagating waves. Our results establish fundamental buckling modes and emergent patterns in shells of active oriented solid materials, with potential relevance to active biological tissues and engineered responsive materials.

</details>


### [58] [Multi-particle gates on driven one-dimensional paths: probing deep traps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20294)
*Harsh Jain,Shankar Ghosh,Archishman Raju*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了在具有深势阱的周期性路径上驱动过阻尼胶体颗粒（overdamped colloidal particles）的单文件输运（single-file transport）现象。在小陷阱极限下，当颗粒数超过临界值 n_c 时，颗粒流从零跃迁为有限值，n_c 个颗粒在陷阱后聚集并呈现集体关联运动，而剩余的“额外”颗粒循环运动产生有限流。通过过阻尼布朗动力学模拟和光学涡旋实验实现了这一行为的观察与表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在深势阱周期性路径上驱动过阻尼胶体颗粒的单文件输运行为，特别是小陷阱极限下粒子流从零到非零的临界转变机制，以及集体关联运动的形成条件。

Method: 采用过阻尼布朗动力学模拟（overdamped Brownian dynamics simulations）进行数值研究，并利用光学涡旋（optical vortex）驱动微米级胶体颗粒进行实验实现。

Result: 在小陷阱极限下，当路径上的颗粒数超过临界数 n_c 时，颗粒流从零跃迁为有限值；n_c 个颗粒在陷阱后聚集并表现出集体关联运动（collective correlated motion），而剩余的“额外”颗粒循环运动产生有限电流。实验观察表征了深达数百 k_BT 的势阱。

Conclusion: 单文件输运中颗粒流存在由颗粒数决定的临界转变行为，该现象由深势阱下的集体关联运动与额外颗粒循环共同驱动，且可通过光学涡旋实验在微米尺度胶体系统中实现和观测。

Abstract: We study single-file transport of driven overdamped colloidal particles on a periodic path with deep potential wells. In the small trap limit (i.e., trap size smaller than particle size), the particle current transitions from zero to finite as the number of particles on the path exceeds a critical number $n_c$. Beyond this threshold, $n_c$ particles cluster behind the trap, demonstrating collective correlated motion. The remaining `extra' particles circulate, giving a finite current. We study this phenomenon numerically using overdamped Brownian dynamics simulations, and present an experimental realization of this behaviour for micron-scale colloidal particles driven in an optical vortex. Using our experimental observations, we present results characterizing potential wells as deep as several hundred $k_BT$.

### [59] [Polymer-polymer interdiffusion: effects of entanglements and a polymeric source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20462)
*Avraham Moriel,Howard A. Stone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用双流体形式（two-fluid formalism）研究了存在或不存在聚合物流源（polymeric source）条件下，缠结与非缠结聚合物-聚合物互扩散（polymer-polymer interdiffusion）问题，导出了标度关系（scaling relations）、自相似约化（self-similar reductions）和解析解，并通过数值模拟验证。源项的引入破坏了自相似结构，但扩散前沿的空间特征与无源情形类似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多工业应用和生物场景涉及两种聚合物物种的互扩散；受生物亚细胞源驱动过程（source-driven processes）的启发，研究者希望系统理解在有无聚合物流源条件下，缠结（entangled）与非缠结（unentangled）聚合物的互扩散行为。

Method: 采用双流体形式（two-fluid formalism）建立理论框架，推导标度关系、自相似约化（self-similar reductions）和解析解；通过一维和二维数值模拟对理论结果进行验证。

Result: 源项的引入会破坏自相似结构，改变边界条件和积分域（domain of integration）。然而，无论是否存在源，扩散液滴（diffusing droplet）的前沿特征（front characteristics）均展现出相似的空间结构。

Conclusion: 研究结果有助于深入理解聚合物-聚合物互扩散与非线性输运（nonlinear transport），尤其是在存在源的情形下。

Abstract: Many industrial applications and biological scenarios involve the interdiffusion of two polymeric species. Motivated by biological subcellular source-driven processes, we study polymer-polymer interdiffusion problems in the absence or the presence of a polymeric source, for both unentangled and entangled scenarios. Utilizing a two-fluid formalism, we arrive at scaling relations, self-similar reductions, and analytical solutions, which are confirmed with one- and two-dimensional numerical simulations. The introduction of a source term breaks the self-similar structure, modifying the boundary conditions and the domain of integration. Nevertheless, we show that the front characteristics of the diffusing droplet exhibit similar spatial structures as in the absence of a source. Our results allow deeper understanding of polymer-polymer interdiffusion and nonlinear transport, especially in the presence of a source.

</details>

### [60] [The ESSnuSB Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19391)
*Monojit Ghosh*

TL;DR: 本文介绍了ESSnuSBplus项目（ESSnuSB第一阶段）的物理规划。ESSnuSB是欧洲未来长基线中微子振荡实验，旨在以空前精度在第二振荡极大值处测量$δ_{\rm CP}$。除束流物理外，大型远探测器还可研究太阳、大气和超新星中微子。ESSnuSBplus还将建设低能监控束流和低能nuSTORM设施用于截面测量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: ESSnuSBplus将建设一个长基线中微子振荡实验设施，包含高精度束流、大型远探测器，以及一个低能监控束流（low energy monitored beam）和一个低能nuSTORM设施（low energy nuSTORM facility），用于截面测量。

Conclusion: ESSnuSBplus（ESSnuSB第一阶段）将成为一个多功能的中微子物理平台，同时覆盖振荡参数精确测量、天体物理中微子研究以及截面测量等多方面物理目标。

Abstract: In this proceedings, we will describe the physics program of the ESSnuSBplus, phase-I of the ESSnuSB project. ESSnuSB is a future long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiment in Europe which aims to measure $δ_{\rm CP}$ at the second oscillation maximum with with unprecedented precision. Apart from studying the beam based physics, the large far detector is also capable of studying various other physics cases involving solar, atmopsheric and supernova neutrinos. Under the ESSnuSBplus project, there will be a low energy monitored beam and a low energy nuSTORM facility for the measurement of cross-section.

### [61] [Towards Engineering Scaling Laws with Pretraining Data Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19781)
*Jan-Lucas Uslu,Kevin Greif,Daniel Whiteson,Benjamin Nachman*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文研究了粒子物理领域中大型模型的神经缩放定律（neural scaling laws），发现其性能随算力、模型规模和数据集规模呈幂律（power law）提升。与自然语言或图像领域不同，高能物理拥有廉价的高保真模拟器，可低成本生成合成数据，从而有利于数据驱动而非参数驱动的缩放机制。通过在高能粒子束碰撞产生的强子喷注（hadronic jets）分类任务中引入更多样、更对齐下游任务的预训练数据，能够将缩放行为引导至需要更多数据而非更大模型的方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索粒子物理领域大模型是否也遵循类似语言模型的神经缩放定律，并利用该领域特有的高保真模拟器优势，研究是否能主动调控缩放行为，以降低对模型规模增长的依赖。

Method: 在强子喷注分类任务中，通过构建更多样、与下游任务更对齐的预训练数据集，实证研究模型性能随计算量、参数规模和数据集规模的缩放关系。

Result: 在粒子物理领域，模型性能同样随计算量、模型规模和数据集规模呈幂律缩放。通过工程化预训练数据（增加多样性和下游对齐度），可以将缩放偏好调整为需要更多数据而非更大模型。

Conclusion: 高能物理领域由于低成本合成数据的可得性，可以主动设计数据分布以影响神经缩放行为，实现“数据高效”而非“参数高效”的缩放机制，为领域专用大模型的训练策略提供新方向。

Abstract: Neural scaling laws describe how model performance improves as a power law in compute, model size, and dataset size. While well-established for large language models, these relationships are emerging for large models in particle physics. As with language, empirical studies show that the performance scales as a power law. However, unlike natural language or image domains, fundamental physics has high-fidelity simulators that produce synthetic data cheaply. This favors scaling regimes where additional data is cheaper than additional parameters, and allows the pretraining dataset itself to be engineered to influence the scaling. For the task of classifying hadronic jets produced in collisions of high-energy particle beams, we show that the scaling behavior can be engineered towards requiring more data rather than larger models by inclusion of pretraining data which is more diverse and better aligned with the downstream classification task.

</details>


### [62] [Resonant heterodyne conversion applied to a low-frequency haloscope for dark matter axion searches in the 1-35 MHz range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20422)
*Navarro-Madrid Jose R.,Reina-Valero José,Díaz-Morcillo Alejandro,Gimeno Benito*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文研究利用RADES-BabyIAXO谐振腔中的外差上转换（heterodyne up-conversion）方法来搜索低质量暗物质轴子（axion），通过对轴子电动力学（axion electrodynamics）的推导、有限轴子线宽的显式建模以及BI-RME 3D全波公式的扩展，确定了准TE011-准TM010模对为最优构型。在热噪声受限且充分抑制泵浦泄漏的条件下，该实验在90%置信水平下可将轴子-光子耦合灵敏度提升至10⁻¹⁵ GeV⁻¹，显著优于此前的外差搜索方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低质量暗物质轴子的探测是粒子物理与宇宙学的重要课题。现有外差搜索方案灵敏度有限，且微波腔中轴子引起的微弱信号难以直接提取，需要发展更精确的理论模型和实验方案。

Method: 从轴子电动力学出发推导轴子诱导源项和读出模提取功率，显式计入有限轴子线宽，引入有效品质因子描述泵浦-轴子混合、检测带宽和信号功率。将BI-RME 3D全波公式扩展到包含泵浦泄漏的实际两端口腔体外差检测场景。

Result: 确定准TE011-准TM010模对为RADES-BabyIAXO谐振腔的最佳构型，可覆盖0.9–34.6 MHz轴子频率。解析与全波预测在共振时高度一致，全波模型在非共振时更精确并能刻画泵浦泄漏。推导出最大化扫描率的最优端口耦合。在低温铜和超导铌腔条件下，灵敏度可达10⁻¹⁵ GeV⁻¹（90%置信水平）。

Conclusion: 该外差上转换方案可显著提升低质量轴子探测灵敏度，为未来实际实验提供了理论框架和设计指导。

Abstract: We study resonant heterodyne up-conversion in the RADES-BabyIAXO haloscope as a method to search for low-mass dark matter axions using microwave cavities. Starting from axion electrodynamics, we derive the axion-induced source term and the power extracted through a readout mode, explicitly accounting for the finite axion linewidth. This leads to effective quality factors that determine the pump-axion mixing, detection bandwidth, and detected signal power. We extend the BI-RME 3D full-wave formulation to heterodyne axion detection in a realistic two-port cavity, including pump leakage into the readout channel. Applying the formalism to the largest RADES-BabyIAXO cavity identifies the $\mathrm{quasi\textrm{-}TE}_{011}-\mathrm{quasi\textrm{-}TM}_{010}$ mode pair as a favorable configuration, enabling sensitivity to axion frequencies between 0.9 and 34.6 MHz. Analytical and full-wave predictions show excellent agreement at resonance, while the full-wave model provides a more accurate description off resonance and allows a precise characterization of the pump leakage. We also derive the optimal port couplings that maximize the scanning rate. Sensitivity projections for cryogenic copper and superconducting niobium cavities indicate that, under thermal-noise-limited conditions and assuming sufficient pump-leakage rejection, the experiment could probe axion-photon couplings down to $10^{-15}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ at 90% confidence level, representing a significant improvement over previous heterodyne-based searches.

</details>


### [63] [HEPTv2: End-to-End Efficient Point Transformer for Charged Particle Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20437)
*Siqi Miao,Shitij Govil,Jack P. Rodgers,Mia Liu,Javier Duarte,Shih-Chieh Hsu,Yuan-Tang Chou,Pan Li*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出HEPTv2，一种端到端点变换器（point-transformer）架构，用于高能物理中的带电粒子径迹重建（charged-particle tracking）。该模型通过局部敏感哈希编码器和扇区分化解码器，无需图构建、聚类或滤波等辅助阶段，即可直接从探测器击中点（hits）预测完整径迹。在TrackML数据集上，HEPTv2以98.6%的双多数追踪效率（double-majority tracking efficiency）和0.8%的假阳性率（fake rate）实现了精度与延迟的最优权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）对粒子径迹重建的精度与效率提出了极高要求。现有的图神经网络（graph neural networks）虽表现优异，但图构建与处理的计算开销巨大；而基于变换器的方法依赖辅助阶段，无法实现端到端优化。因此，需要一种既能保持高精度又具备低延迟、可端到端训练的径迹重建方法。

Method: HEPTv2采用端到端点变换器架构，包含一个局部感知点编码器（locality-aware point encoder）和一个径迹解码器（track decoder）。编码器利用探测器坐标空间中的局部敏感哈希（locality-sensitive hashing）保留几何信息并实现高效局部注意力机制。解码器通过扇区化解码（sectorized decoding）直接进行击中点到径迹的预测，并在联合编码器-解码器监督下实现整个流水线的端到端优化。

Result: 在TrackML数据集上，HEPTv2达到98.6%的双多数追踪效率、0.8%的假阳性率；在NVIDIA A100 GPU上每事件推理时间约15毫秒，峰值内存0.4 GB。与最强先前的变换器方法相比，追踪效率提升4.5%，延迟降低7倍；与优化的图基流水线相比，效率提升1.1%–2.2%，延迟降低38–52倍。延迟与内存使用在高达5×10^5个击中点的范围内近似线性扩展。

Conclusion: HEPTv2证明了端到端变换器能够同时满足HL-LHC对精度与实时性的要求，在径迹重建的精度-延迟权衡中建立了新的最先进水平（state of the art）。

Abstract: Charged-particle tracking -- reconstructing trajectories from sparse detector measurements -- is a fundamental high-energy-physics inference problem and a canonical example of learning under extreme combinatorial ambiguity. At the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC), tracking must remain accurate and efficient despite unprecedented collision densities. Graph neural networks perform strongly, but incur substantial costs from graph construction and processing, while transformer-based approaches rely on auxiliary stages that prevent end-to-end optimization. To address this, we present HEPTv2, an end-to-end point-transformer architecture that reconstructs tracks from detector hits in one trainable pipeline. HEPTv2 combines a locality-aware point encoder with a track decoder that predicts complete trajectories without graph-building, clustering, or filtering. The encoder uses locality-sensitive hashing in detector coordinate space to preserve tracking-relevant geometry while enabling efficient local attention. The decoder resolves ambiguities through sectorized decoding and direct hit-to-track prediction under joint encoder-decoder supervision, allowing the full pipeline to be optimized end-to-end. On TrackML, HEPTv2 achieves 98.6% double-majority tracking efficiency at a 0.8% fake rate, while requiring only $\sim$15~ms inference time and 0.4~GB peak memory per event on a NVIDIA A100 GPU. Latency and memory scale approximately linearly for events with up to $5\times10^5$ hits. HEPTv2 establishes a new state of the art in the accuracy-latency trade-off, improving efficiency by 4.5% over the strongest prior transformer and by 1.1--2.2% over optimized graph-based pipelines, while reducing latency by factors of 7 and 38--52, respectively. These results show end-to-end transformers can deliver the accuracy and efficiency required for real-time particle reconstruction at the HL-LHC.

</details>


### [64] [Observation of electroweak production of pairs of Z bosons in proton-proton collisions at 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20558)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CMS实验报告了通过双喷注伴随的Z玻色子对（ZZjj → ℓℓννjj）的电弱（EW）产生过程的首次证据，在13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据中测得截面为0.37 fb，与标准模型预言一致，合并四轻子道后信号显著性达到5.0个标准差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标准模型（Standard Model）中电弱（electroweak, EW）产生过程Z玻色子对与双喷注（ZZjj）的预言，并寻找超出标准模型的新物理信号，特别是通过反常四标量规范耦合（anomalous quartic gauge couplings）进行约束。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在质心能量√s = 13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子（pp）对撞数据，选取同味异号双轻子（ℓℓ）、大缺失横向动量（missing transverse momentum）以及大快度间隔和大不变质量的双喷注（jj）事件，分析ZZjj → ℓℓννjj末态。

Result: 在 fiducial 体积内测得的电弱产生截面为σ_EW = 0.37⁺⁰·¹⁴_₋₀.₁₂（统计）⁺⁰·⁰⁶_₋₀.⁰⁶（系统）fb，与标准模型预言值0.39 ± 0.06 fb相符。信号观测（预期）显著性为3.1（2.8）个标准差。与四带电轻子道ZZ衰变结果合并后，观测（预期）显著性提升至5.0（4.5）个标准差。基于维度-8有效场论算符（dimension-8 effective field theory operators）给出了反常四标量规范耦合的限制。

Conclusion: CMS实验首次获得ZZjj电弱产生过程的证据，测量结果与标准模型预言一致；合并多衰变道后显著性的提升确立了Z玻色子对电弱产生的观测，同时为反常四标量规范耦合提供了新的实验约束。

Abstract: The first evidence of electroweak (EW) production of pairs of Z bosons in association with two jets (jj) in the final state ZZjj $\to$ $\ell\ellνν$jj, where $\ell$ = e, $μ$, is reported by the CMS experiment. The analysis is based on a data sample of proton-proton (pp) collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Events are selected by requiring exactly two leptons of same flavor and opposite charge, large missing transverse momentum, and two jets with a large rapidity separation and large invariant mass. The EW production cross section in a fiducial volume is $σ_{\mathrm{EW}}$(pp $\to$ ZZjj $\to$ $\ell\ellνν$jj) = 0.37$^{+0.14}_{-0.12}$ (stat)$^{+0.06}_{-0.06}$ (syst) fb, in agreement with the standard model prediction of 0.39 $\pm$ 0.06 fb. The observed (expected) significance of the signal is 3.1 (2.8) standard deviations. Limits on anomalous quartic gauge couplings are derived in terms of dimension-8 effective field theory operators. A combination with the previously reported result from the ZZ decay channel with four charged leptons yields an observed (expected) significance of 5.0 (4.5) standard deviations for the EW production of Z boson pairs.

### [65] [Linear Stability Analysis of Two-phase, Two-Component Flow in Porous Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19922)
*Paulo Lee Kung Caetano Chang,Kundan Kumar*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）研究了部分混相流（partially miscible flow）中黏性指进（viscous fingering）的不稳定性，重点考察了相间传质（interphase mass transfer）对位移前沿稳定性的影响，发现传质主要通过降低黏度对比和改变激波属性发挥稳定作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在提高石油采收率、CO2封存和地下水修复等应用中，黏性指进不稳定性会显著降低流体驱替效率。尽管完全非混相和完全混相情形的线性稳定性分析已有大量研究，但介于两者之间的部分混相流——涉及有限的相间传质——尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 针对一个两相两组分系统，纳入重力效应、分流量（fractional flow）、毛管力、机械弥散（mechanical dispersion）和相间传质，构建特征值问题（eigenvalue problem）以刻画扰动增长率（growth rate）和截止波数（cutoff wavenumber）。所得常微分方程组在两相流到纯液流的过渡处具有不连续系数，导致特征函数导数不连续；为此推导了导数处的跳跃条件，并采用匹配初值问题法（matched initial value problem method）求解。

Result: 相间传质主要通过降低黏度对比和改变位移前沿的激波属性发挥稳定作用；该稳定效应在高黏度对比下尤为显著，并能抑制向上驱替中的重力诱导不稳定性。传质对扰动增长率的影响最为明显，对截止波数的影响相对较弱。研究还识别出一个无量纲纵向弥散系数（longitudinal dispersion coefficient）的临界值，在该值处增长率和截止波数均达到最大，表明毛管力与机械弥散之间存在复杂的相互作用。

Conclusion: 相间传质对部分混相驱替中的黏性指进主要起稳定作用，尤其在黏度对比高和重力影响显著的场景下。该发现对优化工程驱替策略具有潜在指导意义。

Abstract: Viscous fingering instabilities during fluid displacement in porous media can compromise the efficiency of applications such as enhanced oil recovery, CO2 sequestration, and groundwater remediation. While extensive research exists on linear stability analysis for fully immiscible and fully miscible displacements, the intermediate case of partially miscible flow with limited mass transfer between phases remains largely unexplored. This study extends linear stability analysis to a two-phase, two-component system that accounts for gravity effects, fractional flow, capillary forces, mechanical dispersion, and interphase mass transfer, focusing on the case where a partially miscible gaseous fluid displaces a liquid. We formulate an eigenvalue problem to characterize instability growth rates and cutoff wavenumbers. The resulting ordinary differential equations have discontinuous coefficients at the transition from two-phase to pure-liquid flow, resulting in discontinuous eigenfunction derivatives. We derive jump conditions for the derivatives at this transition, and solve the eigenvalue problem using the matched initial value problem method. Results demonstrate that mass transfer has a pre-dominantly stabilizing effect by reducing viscosity contrast and altering shock properties at the displacement front. This stabilizing influence is particularly pronounced for high viscosity contrasts and dampens gravity-induced instability in upward displacements. Mass transfer most significantly affects the perturbation growth rate, while its effect on the cutoff wavenumber is less pronounced. We identify a critical value for the dimensionless longitudinal dispersion coefficient where both growth rate and cutoff wavenumber are maximized, suggesting complex interactions between capillary forces and mechanical dispersion.

</details>

### [66] [$K$-Theoretic Obstructions to Linearizing QCA Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19657)
*Mattie Ji,Bowen Yang*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文针对量子元胞自动机（QCA）表示中的线性化问题，发展了一种基于代数K-理论谱的障碍理论，并完全计算了复代数与酉情形下QCA空间在点、直线和平面上的同伦类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 投影表示（projective representation）能否线性化是物理学与表示论中的基本问题。本文旨在研究带有度量空间X所施加的局域性约束的QCA表示中类似的线性化问题。

Method: 在任意域F上，利用作者前期工作中构造的QCA代数K-理论谱（algebraic K-theory spectrum），发展了一套用于QCA表示线性化的障碍理论。该障碍由QCA空间的同伦型（homotopy type）控制，从而提取出线性化的普遍障碍类（universal obstruction classes）。

Result: 在复代数情形与酉情形下，完全计算了点、直线和平面上的QCA空间的同伦型。

Conclusion: 该障碍理论为QCA表示的可线性化性提供了系统的判定框架，其障碍完全由QCA空间的拓扑性质刻画。

Abstract: Projective representations arise naturally in physics and representation theory, and determining whether they can be linearized has been a fundamental problem. In this work, we study the analogous problem for quantum cellular automata (QCA) representations, which incorporate locality constraints imposed by a metric space $X$. Over an arbitrary field $\mathbb{F}$, we develop an obstruction theory for the linearization of QCA representations, using the algebraic $K$-theory spectrum of QCA constructed in previous work of the authors. The resulting obstructions are governed by the homotopy type of the QCA spaces, from which we extract universal obstruction classes to linearization. In the complex algebraic and unitary case, we also fully compute the homotopy types of the QCA spaces over a point, a line, and a plane.

### [67] [Once more: Leaky MHD waves in coronal magnetic flux tubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20019)
*Hans Goedbloed,Rony Keppens*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 通过对比日冕磁通量管中的泄漏磁流体动力学波与电介质中的泄漏电磁波，发现后者可通过截断外部均匀区贡献的正规化方法被归整为准正规模（quasi-normal modes），而磁通量守恒禁止前者进行此类处理。因此，泄漏磁流体动力学波无法系统性地应用于日冕地震学（coronal seismology），即通过比较谱与观测谱来反演场平衡分布的反谱问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨泄漏磁流体动力学（magnetohydrodynamic, MHD）波能否像电介质中的泄漏电磁波那样被归整为准正规模，并评估其系统应用于日冕地震学（coronal seismology）的可行性。

Method: 对日冕磁通量管中的泄漏MHD波与电介质中的泄漏电磁波进行详细比较，重点分析二者在正规化（normalisation）和截断外部均匀区贡献方面的异同。

Result: 电介质中的泄漏电磁波可通过截断外部均匀区贡献的正规化方法被归整为准正规模（quasi-normal modes）；而磁通量守恒（conservation of magnetic flux）禁止对泄漏MHD波进行此类处理。

Conclusion: 泄漏MHD波不能系统性地应用于日冕地震学，即通过比较谱与观测谱来反演场平衡分布的反谱问题（inverse spectral problem）。

Abstract: By a detailed comparison of leaky magnetohydrodynamic waves in coronal magnetic flux tubes with leaky electromagnetic waves in dielectric media it is shown that the latter kind may be called quasi-normal modes, since they can be regularised by a normalisation which systematically cuts off the contribution of the external homogeneous region, whereas such a possibility is forbidden for the former kind by the conservation of magnetic flux. Consequently, leaky magnetohydrodynamic waves cannot be systematically applied to coronal seismology, i.e. to the inverse spectral problem of determining the different equilibrium distributions of the fields by comparing the spectra they produce with the observed ones.

</details>

### [68] [Eppur non si trovano Vol. 3: Phoebe -- a Mirage of a Primordial Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19442)
*Andrzej Udalski,Przemek Mróz*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文对Key等人报告的一颗被命名为"Phoebe"的恒星短暂增亮事件进行了独立再分析，通过纳入2020和2021年的额外观测数据，发现该天体经历了至少三次独立的低振幅增亮事件及长期光度变化，表明其是普通变星而非短时标微引力透镜事件，从而解决了与先前微引力透镜实验结果之间的明显矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Key等人最近预测报告了在大麦哲伦云（Large Magellanic Cloud）中发现一颗名为"Phoebe"的恒星短暂增亮，并解释为由银河系暗物质晕（dark matter halo）中的月球质量原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）产生的短时标微引力透镜（gravitational microlensing）事件。本文旨在对该事件进行独立的重新分析，以检验这一解释的可靠性。

Method: 研究对公开可用的DECam观测数据进行了独立再分析（re-analysis），并纳入了2020和2021年的额外观测数据，对Phoebe的光变曲线进行了多时间段、多增亮事件的综合分析。

Result: 该天体除了平均星等的长期变化外，还经历了至少三次独立的低振幅增亮（low-amplitude brightenings），其中一次被误认为是短时标微引力透镜事件。这些光变特征表明Phoebe是普通变星（ordinary variable star），而非微引力透镜事件。

Conclusion: 这一发现消除了与早期微引力透镜实验结果之间明显的矛盾，那些实验排除了月球质量和行星质量原初黑洞构成暗物质主要部分的假说。

Abstract: Recent preprints by Key et al. reported the discovery of a short-lived brightening of a star (nicknamed "Phoebe") located in the Large Magellanic Cloud that was interpreted as a short-timescale gravitational microlensing event produced by a lunar-mass primordial black hole (PBH) in the Milky Way dark matter halo. Here, we present an independent re-analysis of the publicly available DECam observations of this object, incorporating additional data from 2020 and 2021. The object underwent at least three distinct, low-amplitude brightenings (one of which was misinterpreted as a short-timescale microlensing event) in addition to long-term variations of its mean magnitude. These characteristics indicate that Phoebe is an ordinary variable star rather than a microlensing event. This finding resolves the apparent tension with the results from earlier microlensing experiments that rule out the hypothesis that a substantial fraction of dark matter is composed of lunar- and planetary-mass PBHs.

</details>

### [69] [Exact Solution of the Non-minimally Coupled Klein-Gordon Equation in the Schwarzschild Star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19433)
*Reynan A. Dulinayan,Kevin T. Grosvenor*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次给出了含非最小曲率-标量耦合的大质量Klein-Gordon方程在Schwarzschild恒星（均匀密度理想流体球对称星）中的精确解，该解以一般Heun函数表示，并揭示了隐藏的Fuchsian结构。在低致密极限下恢复了已知的前导和次前导阶结果；在Buchdahl极限下推导了静态模的正则条件，并解析描述了动态模在接近恒星中心压力奇异性时的发散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究缺乏该系统中大质量Klein-Gordon方程的精确解析解，特别是包含非最小曲率-标量耦合（non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling）的情形，从而限制了对其完整动力学行为的理解。

Method: 通过一种几何诱导的代数坐标变换（geometry-induced algebraic coordinate transformation），揭示了问题中隐藏的Fuchs型结构（Fuchsian structure），从而将方程化为可用一般Heun函数（general Heun function）精确求解的形式。

Result: 得到了包含非最小耦合项的Klein-Gordon方程的精确解析解；在低致密极限下恢复了已知的前导（leading-order）和次前导阶（next-to-leading-order）结果；在Buchdahl极限下导出了静态模的正则条件（regularity condition），并解析描述了动态模在靠近恒星中心压力奇异性时振幅和振荡波矢的发散行为。

Conclusion: 该精确解为在Schwarzschild恒星背景下研究标量场的动力学提供了完整的数学框架，尤其是揭示了Buchdahl极限附近场的奇异性行为，对理解极端致密天体的物理具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present for the first time the exact solution of the massive Klein-Gordon equation in the Schwarzschild star (perfect-fluid, uniform-density, spherically-symmetric star), including the non-minimal curvature-scalar coupling. The solution is expressed in terms of the general Heun function. A geometry-induced algebraic coordinate transformation reveals a hidden Fuchsian structure that underlies the exact solvability. Known leading- and next-to-leading-order results are recovered in the low-compactness limit. In the Buchdahl limit, we derive a regularity condition for static modes and describe analytically the divergence in amplitude and oscillation wave vector of dynamic modes as they approach the pressure singularity at the center of the star.

</details>


### [70] [Deriving effective descriptions and signal predictions for dynamical gravitational systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19435)
*Steven B. Giddings,Madhur Mehta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究引力系统（如双星系统）辐射的有效描述，提出基于空腔边界作用量的有效方法，并展示其与可观测量（波形和相位偏移）的联系，旨在系统推断黑洞经典行为修正对引力波信号的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主要动机是建立一种系统性的方法，用以推断黑洞经典行为的修正（例如受量子力学一致性或其他新物理模型启发的修正）对引力波信号的影响；特别地，相位偏移被认为能够灵敏地探测旋近阶段（inspiral phase）中的微小新效应。

Method: 采用自上而下（top-down）推导有效描述的方法，基于空腔（cavity）边界上的作用量（action）来参数化单体周围的动力学，并给出黑洞及其修正模型的空腔描述示例，同时展示空腔有效描述与可观测量（波形和相位偏移）之间的连接。

Result: 给出了黑洞和修正黑洞行为简单模型的空腔描述示例；阐明了空腔有效描述如何与详细波形和累积相位偏移等可观测量相联系；论文主要以标量辐射（scalar radiation）为例说明基本原理和方法，并概述了向引力波（gravitational wave）背景的推广。

Conclusion: 空腔有效描述为系统性地推断黑洞经典行为修正对引力波信号的影响提供了途径；尽管论文主要聚焦于标量辐射示例，但该方法可推广至引力波语境。

Abstract: We investigate top-down derivations of effective descriptions for radiation from gravitational systems such as binaries. With a specified cutoff prescription, one can derive worldline effective field theories, but the cutoff dependence also complicates their description. We investigate a related effective approach, based on parameterizing dynamics in terms of an action on the boundaries of cavities encompassing individual bodies. We give examples of such cavity descriptions for black holes and for simple models for modifications of their behavior. We also show how cavity effective descriptions connect to observable quantities -- detailed wave profiles, and importantly, accumulated phase shift of emitted signals. A primary motivation is to have a systematic approach to inferring effects of modification of classical black hole behavior, such as those motivated by the need for black hole evolution to be consistent with quantum mechanics, or by other models for new BH behavior, on gravitational wave signals; the latter phase shifts have in particular been argued to provide sensitivity to small new effects from the inspiral phase. To illustrate basic principles and methods, this paper largely focuses on examples with scalar radiation, but we outline extension of the analysis to gravitational wave contexts.

</details>


### [71] [Dynamical Tidal Response of Neutron Stars: from Effective Field Theory to Gravitational Waveforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19446)
*Thomas Apostolidis,Valerio De Luca,Leonardo Gualtieri,Takuya Katagiri,Paolo Pani,Luca Santoni*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究首次在完全相对论性框架下推导了中子星频率二阶的动力学潮汐响应（dynamical tidal response），包含普遍的对数跑动项（logarithmic running term），并证明了动力学效应对引力波信号的高低能物理修正（high-precision gravitational-wave modeling）具有不可忽略的影响，尤其对第三代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）的测量至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，中子星的潮汐响应多限于静态近似（static approximation），而实际双星并合过程中动力学效应（dynamical effects）可能显著。该工作旨在系统推导完全相对论性框架下频率二阶的动力学潮汐响应，并评估其对引力波波形和物态方程（equation of state）推断的影响。

Method: 结合世界线有效场论（worldline effective field theory）与相对论性恒星模型微扰论（perturbation theory of relativistic stellar models），在维度正规化（dimensional regularization）框架下通过一致匹配程序（consistent matching procedure）导出动力学潮汐变形，包含对数跑动项与方案依赖的有限项。

Result: 动力学效应不能仅由模式激发（mode excitations）完全描述，额外贡献依赖于恒星致密度（compactness）、物态方程和跑动项。较小致密度下动力学Love数（dynamical Love numbers）显著大于静态Love数；尽管形式上进入引力波相位在8阶后牛顿（8th post-Newtonian order），但在晚期旋近（late inspiral）中贡献不可忽略。Fisher矩阵分析表明，第三代探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）可测量多种质量和物态方程下的动力学Love数；忽略该效应会导致静态Love数及核物态方程推断出现显著偏差。

Conclusion: 动力学潮汐效应对未来高精度引力波建模（high-precision gravitational-wave modeling）至关重要，必须纳入双星动力学和引力波信号的分析中。

Abstract: We investigate the fully relativistic dynamical tidal response of neutron stars up to second order in the frequency. Combining the worldline effective field theory for extended gravitating bodies with perturbation theory of relativistic stellar models, we derive the tidal deformation induced by an external time-dependent field, including a universal logarithmic running term. In the effective theory, we work in dimensional regularization and, through a consistent matching procedure, obtain for the first time the complete leading-order dynamical tidal corrections to both the conservative dynamics and the gravitational-wave signal of compact binaries, including the scheme-dependent finite terms in addition to the running. We show that, in the relativistic regime, dynamical effects cannot be fully captured by mode excitations alone. The magnitude of the additional contribution depends on the stellar compactness, the equation of state, and the running term. Dynamical Love numbers are significantly enhanced with respect to their static counterparts for relatively small compactness. As a result, although they formally enter the gravitational-wave phase at 8th post-Newtonian order, dynamical tidal effects yield a non-negligible contribution during the late inspiral. Using a Fisher-matrix analysis, we show that third-generation detectors such as the Einstein Telescope could measure dynamical Love numbers for a range of neutron-star masses and equations of state. Conversely, neglecting these effects can lead to significant biases in the inference of static Love numbers, and hence on the nuclear equation of state. Our results highlight the importance of dynamical tidal effects for high-precision gravitational-wave modeling with future detectors.

</details>


### [72] [Exact vacuum FLRW solutions in $q$-deformed Brans-Dicke cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19563)
*Salih Kibaroğlu,Mustafa Senay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在空间平坦的FLRW时空下研究了Brans-Dicke引力的q-变形扩展，通过耦合函数修改有效引力强度并导出广义Friedmann方程。在无物质情形下获得了尺度因子和标量场的精确解析解，发现标量扇区的状态方程参数和减速参数均为常数，仅依赖于Brans-Dicke耦合参数ω和变形函数，从而可在参数空间的受限区域模拟辐射、物质或暗能量行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Brans-Dicke引力在q-变形框架下的扩展，从而获得更丰富的宇宙学演化行为，并考察标量场能否在无需引入额外物质的情况下有效模拟不同宇宙成分。

Method: 采用q-变形推广的耦合函数修改Brans-Dicke理论中的有效引力强度，在空间平坦FLRW度规下推导广义Friedmann方程；在无物质情形下求解放缩因子和Brans-Dicke标量场的精确解析解，并将标量贡献重构为有效流体形式。

Result: 获得了无物质情形下尺度因子和Brans-Dicke标量场的精确解析解；标量扇区对应的状态方程参数（equation-of-state parameter）和减速参数（deceleration parameter）均为常数，仅由Brans-Dicke耦合参数ω和变形函数决定；在参数空间的特定受限区域内，标量扇区可呈现类似辐射、物质或暗能量的行为。

Conclusion: 该q-变形扩展的Brans-Dicke引力理论在无物质情形下能够通过标量扇区单一成分模拟辐射、物质或暗能量的宇宙学演化，为统一描述不同宇宙时期提供了理论可能性。

Abstract: We study a $q$-deformed extension of Brans-Dicke gravity in a spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker space-time. The deformation enters through a coupling function that modifies the effective gravitational strength and leads to generalized Friedmann equations. In the matter-free sector, we obtain exact analytic solutions for the scale factor and the Brans-Dicke scalar field, and recast the scalar contribution as an effective fluid. We show that the corresponding equation-of-state parameter and the deceleration parameter are constants and depend only on the Brans-Dicke coupling $ω$ and the deformation function, allowing the scalar sector to mimic radiation-, matter-, or dark-energy-like behavior for a restricted region of parameter space.

</details>


### [73] [Graviton Floor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19757)
*Himeka Matsuo,Asuka Ito,Kazunori Kohri,Teruaki Suyama,Ryutaro Tomomatsu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙光子背景在银河系和耀变体喷流（blazar jets）中的磁场作用下转化为引力子（gravitons）的过程，发现耀变体喷流贡献占主导，且该引力子背景将成为高频引力波探测器搜寻新物理时的“引力子地板”（graviton floor），类似于中微子地板（neutrino floor）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙中普遍存在从射电波到伽马射线的宇宙光子背景（cosmic photon background），作者旨在探究该背景在磁场影响下能否转化为引力子，并评估其对高频引力波探测器的影响。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究了宇宙光子背景在银河系磁场和耀变体喷流磁场中转换为引力子的过程，并比较了两类区域的贡献大小。

Result: 结果表明，产生的引力子背景主要由耀变体喷流贡献，且该背景构成了高频引力波探测器搜寻新物理时的“引力子地板”。

Conclusion: 该引力子背景对高频引力波探测实验构成了不可忽略的噪声下限，其意义类似于中微子地板之于暗物质直接探测实验。

Abstract: It has been observed that the Universe is permeated by the cosmic photon background, ranging from radio waves to gamma rays. We investigate the conversion of the photon background into gravitons in the presence of background magnetic fields in the Milky Way Galaxy and in blazar jets. We find that the resulting graviton background is dominated by the contribution generated in blazar jets. Importantly, this graviton background constitutes a graviton floor for high-frequency gravitational wave detectors searching for new physics, analogous to the neutrino floor.

### [74] [Polarization-Dependent Photon Propagation, Quasinormal Modes, and Gravitational Lensing in Higher-Curvature Effective Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19773)
*Takamasa Kanai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在有效场论框架下研究了高曲率修正对光子传播的影响，推导了偏振依赖的有效度规，并分析了在光子球偏移、似正规模以及强引力透镜可观测量的后果，表明来自广义相对论之外的效应可在准正规模谱和强引力透镜中被探测到，从而为有效场论提供约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究高曲率修正（higher-curvature corrections）在有效场论（effective field theory）框架下对光子传播的影响，并揭示其在强引力场中的观测后果，从而为超越广义相对论（general relativity）的效应提供可检验的预言。

Method: 采用几何光学近似（geometrical optics approximation）推导描述光子传播的有效度规（effective metric），并基于此计算光子球（photon sphere）偏移、eikonal极限下的似正规模（quasinormal modes）以及偏振依赖的引力透镜偏转角（deflection angle）。

Result: 高曲率修正导致光子轨迹出现偏振依赖的修正，并在光球偏移、准正规模谱和强引力透镜观测中产生可区分的信号，这些信号体现了超越广义相对论贡献的具体表现形式。

Conclusion: 本文结果表明，来自超越广义相对论的效应可以通过似正规模谱和强引力透镜观测来探测，并有望对有效场论施加有意义的约束。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of higher-curvature corrections on photon propagation within an effective field theory framework and explore their observational consequences in strong gravitational fields. In particular, we consider polarization-dependent modifications to photon trajectories induced by higher-order curvature terms and analyze their effects in static and spherically symmetric spacetimes, focusing on Schwarzschild and Reissner-Nordström backgrounds.
  Using the geometrical optics approximation, we derive the effective metric governing photon propagation and study the resulting shifts in the photon sphere. Based on this modified propagation, we compute the quasinormal modes in the eikonal limit and examine their dependence on the polarization modes. We further analyze gravitational lensing observables, focusing on the deflection angle, incorporating the polarization-dependent corrections.
  Our results clarify how contributions from beyond-general-relativity effects manifest in both quasinormal mode spectra and strong gravitational lensing observables. These findings further suggest the possibility of placing meaningful constraints on effective field theories.

</details>


### [75] [Photon surfaces extension in general spherical dust collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19809)
*Roberto Giambò,Camilla Lucamarini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将光子表面（photon surface）分析从边缘束缚（marginally bound）情形推广至一般非边缘束缚的球对称尘埃塌缩，证明外部的光子球面 $r=3M$ 向内部塌缩尘埃云的唯一物理解析延拓是一类类光超曲面（null hypersurface），并确立了光子表面到达中心奇点当且仅当奇点裸露的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作（arXiv:2509.01368）仅处理了Lemaître–Tolman–Bondi（LTB）模型中能量函数 $k(x)=0$ 的边缘束缚情形，本文旨在将其推广到 $k(x)\neq 0$ 的一般情形，以更完整地理解球对称尘埃塌缩中的光子表面行为及其与奇点因果结构的关系。

Method: 从之前工作的动力学系统（dynamical-systems）形式出发，推导一般LTB度规下 $k(x)\neq 0$ 时光子表面方程，将其转化为非自治一阶动力学系统；利用文献中已有的隐式解及常微分方程的比较定理（comparison theorems）进行分析。

Result: 外部的光子球面 $r=3M$ 向内部塌缩尘埃云的唯一物理解析延拓是由外向径向类光测地线（outgoing radial null geodesics）生成的类光超曲面；光子表面到达中心奇点当且仅当该奇点是裸露的（naked）。

Conclusion: 将边缘束缚情形下已知的光子表面与奇点因果结构之间的对应关系推广到一般LTB模型，并探讨了裸奇点与覆盖奇点（covered singularity）之间结构二分法（structural dichotomy）在黑洞阴影（black-hole shadows）早期演化中的可能观测特征。

Abstract: We extend the analysis of photon surfaces in spherical dust collapse to the general, non-marginally bound case, i.e.\ allowing the \textit{energy function} $k(x)$ of the Lemaître--Tolman--Bondi (LTB) model to be non-zero. Starting from the dynamical-systems formulation developed in our previous work for the marginally bound case (arXiv:2509.01368), we derive the photon surface equations for the LTB metric with $k(x)\neq 0$, and we recast the geometric condition for a timelike hypersurface to be a photon surface as a non-autonomous first-order dynamical system. Even though the LTB evolution equation does not integrate in closed form when $k(x)\neq 0$, the implicit solutions available in the literature, together with comparison theorems for ordinary differential equations, are sufficient to show that the only physically acceptable extension of the exterior photon sphere $r=3M$ into the collapsing dust cloud is a null hypersurface, generated by outgoing radial null geodesics. Combining this fact with the known results on the causal structure of the general LTB model, we then establish that the photon surface reaches the central singularity if and only if the singularity is naked, thereby extending to the general case the picture already known in the marginally bound regime. The structural dichotomy between the naked and covered end states is also discussed in connection with possible observational signatures in the early-time evolution of black-hole shadows.

</details>


### [76] [Covariant Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations in Energy-Momentum Squared Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19879)
*Eduardo Bittencourt,Mariam Campbell,Peter K. S. Dunsby,Sergio E. Jorás*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在能量-动量平方引力（Energy–Momentum Squared Gravity）的扩展框架下，利用协变1+1+2半标架形式体系研究静态球对称恒星结构。通过将非线性物质修正重新解释为有效完美流体，导出保持标准TOV形式的平衡方程，并利用自治平面动力系统对恒星相空间进行全局定性分析，同时讨论了与广义相对论的等价区间及边界匹配条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扩展引力理论中理解非线性物质修正如何影响恒星的平衡与稳定性，并建立一套统一的协变描述框架，以超越广义相对论（general relativity）的经典TOV方程适用范围。

Method: 采用协变1+1+2半标架形式体系（covariant 1+1+2 semi-tetrad formalism），引入有效流体的重新诠释，将平衡方程化为自治平面动力系统（autonomous planar dynamical system），并通过有限和渐近临界点（finite and asymptotic critical points）进行全局定性分析。

Result: 非线性物质修正可重新解释为有效完美流体，使平衡方程保持TOV标准形式；线性物态方程下可恢复广义相对论基准，识别出精确、渐近或分段等价于广义相对论的扇区；发现尘埃组态（dust configurations）下平面约化失效，需考虑完整三维协变流；恒星表面匹配条件为有效压强为零（p_eff(R)=0），不一定等同于物理压强为零。

Conclusion: 扩展的能量-动量平方引力框架下，恒星结构的定性行为可通过动力系统方法全局刻画；表面匹配条件与广义相对论存在本质差异，为自束缚物质（self-bound matter）提供了新的理论预言。

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric stellar configurations in an extended class of Energy--Momentum Squared Gravity using the covariant \(1+1+2\) semi-tetrad formalism. For perfect physical fluids, we show that the nonlinear matter corrections can be reinterpreted as an effective perfect fluid, so that the stellar equilibrium equations retain the standard Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff form when written in terms of effective variables. The resulting covariant structure equations are formulated in both metric and dimensionless variables and, whenever an effective closure relation exists, reduce to an autonomous planar dynamical system. This provides a global qualitative description of the stellar phase space in terms of finite and asymptotic critical points.
  Specializing to linear physical equations of state, we recover the general relativistic benchmark and identify sectors that are exactly, asymptotically, or piecewise equivalent to general relativity, as well as sectors -- particularly dust configurations -- for which the planar reduction breaks down and the full three-dimensional covariant flow must be considered. We further recover the standard metric Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equation in terms of effective variables and show that, although the exterior spacetime remains Schwarzschild, the natural matching condition at the stellar surface is \(p_{\rm eff}(R)=0\), which need not coincide with \(p(R)=0\) for self-bound matter.

</details>


### [77] [Cosmological Constraints on Minimal Cubic Galileon Models in Teleparallel Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19905)
*Akbar Davlataliev,Abdurakhmon Nosirov,Odil Yunusov,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Jackson Levi Said*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文在 teleparallel gravity 框架下研究 cubic Galileon 宇宙学模型，利用超新星、宇宙学时计、SH0ES 和重子声学振荡（BAO）等多类观测数据，对含二次和指数势的四种场景进行参数约束，发现固定 $b_1=2$ 的二次势模型在 BAO 数据下优于 $Λ$CDM 的拟合表现，但根据 BIC 准则，$Λ$CDM 仍因参数空间更简洁而更受青睐。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在 teleparallel gravity 框架中引入模型参数 $b_1$ 刻画与标准广义相对论 teleparallel 等效理论的偏离，选取二次势和指数势两种标量场势能，构建四种场景（两种势能下 $b_1$ 自由或固定为 2）；使用 $\text{Pantheon}^+$ Ia 型超新星样本、宇宙学时计测量、SH0ES 信息和 BAO 数据，对宇宙学及模型参数进行约束并比较各场景的观测可行性。

Conclusion: Teleparallel cubic Galileon 宇宙学在现象学上仍具可行性，但关于哈勃张力（Hubble tension）的更明确结论需要进一步的一致性检验。

Abstract: Cubic Galileon cosmological models provide a well-motivated framework for investigating late-time cosmic acceleration beyond the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm. In this work, we study observational constraints on cubic Galileon models within the teleparallel gravity framework, where deviations from the standard teleparallel equivalent of general relativity are encoded through the model parameter $b_1$. We consider two scalar-field potentials, namely quadratic and exponential potentials, and analyze four representative scenarios: quadratic and exponential potentials with $b_1$ treated as a free parameter, together with the corresponding cases in which $b_1=2$ is fixed. We find that the considered teleparallel cubic Galileon models can accommodate the late-time expansion history, although the statistical preference depends on the choice of potential and on whether $b_1$ is fixed or varied. In particular, the fixed-$b_1$ model with a quadratic potential provides the most competitive fit among the Galileon scenarios when BAO data are included, showing a lower $χ^2_{\min}$ than $Λ$CDM and comparable support according to the AIC criterion. However, the BIC criterion continues to favor the minimal $Λ$CDM model because of the larger parameter space of the extended models. These results suggest that teleparallel cubic Galileon cosmologies remain phenomenologically viable, while a stronger claim regarding the Hubble tension requires further consistency tests.

### [78] [On the Plebanski Formulation with Energy Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20042)
*Jack C. M. Hughes,Joudy F. Jamal Beek,Fedor V. Kusmartsev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Plebanski形式体系中，通过在代数曲率空间中利用Kulkarni-Nomizu乘积将无迹能量-动量张量提升为(1,1)分量，并提取其手征分量，系统构造了Plebanski物质源项$T^i$，同时验证了该构造与手征Bianchi恒等式共同保证了能量-动量守恒律；以球对称电磁应力-能量张量为例，反自对偶部分的场方程得到了Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解，从而为将度规物质源翻译为Plebanski方程所需的反自对偶源项提供了系统化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Plebanski形式体系中物质的耦合不如度规形式直观，因为能量-动量张量$T_{\mu\nu}$是对称的，而Plebanski变量天然取值于2-形式的自对偶/反自对偶霍奇分解（self-dual/anti-self-dual Hodge decomposition），因此需要一种系统的方法将度规物质源转换为Plebanski框架所需的源项。

Method: 利用Kulkarni-Nomizu乘积（Kulkarni-Nomizu product）将无迹能量-动量张量$\hat T_{\mu\nu}$提升到代数曲率空间的(1,1)分量中，然后提取其手征分量（chiral components），从而显式构造Plebanski物质源$T^i$。该构造复现了Krasno基于自对偶基$\Sigma^i$和$\hat T_{\mu\nu}$给出的$T^i$定义。

Result: 验证了物质耦合的手征场方程通过手征Bianchi恒等式$d^A F^i=0$蕴含了通常的守恒律$\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu}=0$。将构造应用于球对称电磁应力-能量张量时，反自对偶部分的Plebanski场方程给出了Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter解（Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter solution）。

Conclusion: 该研究为将度规物质源系统地翻译为Plebanski场方程所需的反自对偶源项（anti-self-dual source terms）提供了系统化处方（systematic prescription）。

Abstract: In Plebanski's formulation the coupling of matter is less direct than in the metric formulation since the energy-momentum tensor $T_{μν}$ is symmetric, while the Plebanski variables are naturally valued in the self-dual/anti-self-dual Hodge decomposition of 2-forms. An explicit construction of the Plebanski matter source $T^i$ is obtained by lifting the trace-free energy-momentum tensor $\hat T_{μν}$ into the $(1,1)$ component of the algebraic curvature space using the Kulkarni-Nomizu product, and then extracting its chiral components. This construction reproduces the definition for $T^i$ in terms of the self-dual basis $Σ^i$ and $\hat T_{μν}$ introduced by Krasnov. We also verify that the matter-coupled chiral field equations imply the usual conservation law $\nabla_μT^{μν}=0$ through the chiral Bianchi identity $d^A F^i=0$. As an application, the construction is applied to a spherically symmetric electromagnetic stress-energy tensor, where the anti-self-dual part of the matter-coupled Plebanski field equations yields the Reissner-Nordström-de Sitter solution. The result gives a systematic prescription for translating metric matter sources into the anti-self-dual source terms required by the Plebanski field equations.

### [79] [Regular Black Holes from Anisotropic Source with Hydrodynamic Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20109)
*Hassan Firouzjahi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入各向异性（anisotropic）能量动量张量，研究了由不同流体状态方程（equation of state）$P(ρ)$生成的规则黑洞（regular black hole）解，发现$P(ρ)$在大距离处存在根和极大值，导致声速平方$c_s^2$变号并引发潜在流体力学不稳定性；亚光速约束会排除能量密度呈指数衰减的模型，并建立了强能量条件破缺、压力取根与取极大值三个位置之间的普适层次关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规则黑洞内部几何趋近德西特（dS）度量，但其精确解的构造依赖于能量动量张量的形式；本文旨在通过各向异性分解和流体力学状态方程，系统探索规则黑洞解的空间并分析其动力学稳定性。

Method: 将能量动量张量分解为各向同性（isotropic）和各向异性（anisotropic）分量，假设流体力学状态方程$P=P(ρ)$，寻找球对称规则黑洞解；考察不同$P(ρ)$形式，分析声速平方$c_s^2$的符号变化及亚光速条件对模型参数的约束。

Result: $P(ρ)$在大距离处存在一个根和一个极大值；$c_s^2$在压力达到极大值时变号，暗示流体力学不稳定性；亚光速（subluminal）约束排除了能量密度呈指数衰减的模型；强能量条件（strong energy condition）被破坏的位置、压力取根的位置和压力取极大值的位置之间存在普适的层次关系。

Conclusion: 各向异性规则黑洞解的稳定性强烈依赖于$P(ρ)$的形式，声速变号是潜在不稳定信号，亚光速条件可作为筛选可行模型的强判据，三类临界点之间的层级顺序具有普适性。

Abstract: We study regular black hole solutions sourced by an anisotropic energy momentum tensor. It is well known that the geometry of the interior of a spherically symmetric regular black hole approaches the dS metric. Having decomposed the energy momentum tensor into its isotropic and anisotropic components, we assume a hydrodynamic equation of state, $P= P(ρ)$, for the pressure, and look for spherically symmetric, regular black hole solutions. We consider different forms of $ P(ρ)$ which yield the previously known regular black hole solutions, as well as various new metrics. We show that the profile of $ P(ρ)$ has a root and a maximum as it approaches $0^+$ at large distances. Consequently, the square of the sound speed of perturbations, $c_s^2$, changes sign at the point where $P$ reaches its maximum, indicating a potential hydrodynamic instability. In addition, imposing the subluminal bound on $c_s$ puts strong constraints on the model parameters, excluding models in which the energy density has an exponential fall off. We establish a universal hierarchy among the relative positions at which the strong energy condition is violated, at which $P$ has its root, and at which $P$ attains its maximum.

### [80] [The auxiliary-metric formulation of Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20247)
*Bayram Tekin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过引入辅助度规将Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity重整为多项式形式，简化了真空分析、二次作用量与AdS背景上的守恒量计算，并隔离了非线性自由度问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: New Massive Gravity在曲率高阶项上是不完整的，BINMG通过度规与爱因斯坦张量平移的行列式完成了对曲率所有阶的扩展，但原始形式复杂。将BINMG重写为多项式形式有助于简化分析和揭示其物理性质。

Method: 引入独立辅助度规$q_{μν}$，其代数运动方程$q_{μν}=g_{μν}+\fracσ{m^2}G_{μν}(g)$精确恢复行列式作用量的正则分支并对无限曲率级数进行重新求和。利用密度化变量$P^{μν}=\sqrt{-q}\,q^{μν}$，使三维作用量变为多项式形式，所有导数依赖集中体现在耦合项$P^{μν}G_{μν}(g)$中。

Result: 唯一真空在一行内得到；二次作用量产生单个Pauli-Fierz有质量自旋-2场，Fierz-Pauli调谐（Fierz-Pauli tuning）由公式自然生成而非人为施加。在局域AdS背景上，守恒荷（BTZ质量和角动量）、中心荷（central charge）及熵均简化为爱因斯坦结果乘以一个共同因子。该形式还在正确变量下隔离了非线性自由度问题。

Conclusion: 新的多项式形式大幅简化了BINMG的代数计算，揭示了其与Einstein引力和Pauli-Fierz场的深层联系，并为完整的自由度计数（Dirac count）提供了独立的研究基础。

Abstract: Born-Infeld New Massive Gravity (BINMG) completes New Massive Gravity to all orders in curvature through the determinant of the metric shifted by the Einstein tensor. We recast it with an independent auxiliary metric $q_{μν}$, whose algebraic equation of motion $q_{μν}=g_{μν}+\fracσ{m^2}G_{μν}(g)$ recovers the determinant action exactly on the regular branch and resums the infinite curvature series into a single relation. In the densitized variable $P^{μν}=\sqrt{-q}\,q^{μν}$ the three-dimensional action is polynomial, with all derivative dependence carried by the coupling $P^{μν}G_{μν}(g)$. The formulation makes known properties follow with substantially less algebra: the unique vacuum follows in one line, and the quadratic action yields a single Pauli-Fierz massive spin-2 field with the Fierz-Pauli tuning generated rather than imposed. On locally AdS backgrounds the conserved charges, BTZ mass and angular momentum, central charge, and entropy reduce to the Einstein results times a common factor. The formulation also isolates the nonlinear degree-of-freedom problem in the right variables, leaving the full Dirac count to separate work.

### [81] [An explicit and differentiable Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer transform for gravitational-wave data analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20269)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发并开源了wdm_transform包，实现了WDM小波包时频变换的正逆变换，提供NumPy和JAX两个后端，并通过LISA银河双星在平稳噪声模型下的贝叶斯推断实例验证了WDM域似然的数值正确性。

Conclusion: 该工作为系统性优化WDM铺砌（tilings）铺平了道路，尤其适用于未来探测器面临的非平稳噪声、随机背景和数据间隙等场景，并有助于与其它时频表示进行直接比较，以应对未来引力波数据分析的挑战。

Abstract: The Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM) time-frequency transform has been widely used in gravitational-wave astronomy, yet a self-contained, mathematically explicit reference for practitioners remains lacking. This is especially true for those wishing to adopt the transform in modern Python and JAX inference workflows. We present wdm_transform, an open-source Python package implementing the WDM wavelet-packet time-frequency transform, and document its mathematical foundations, statistical properties, and practical implementation for gravitational-wave data analysis. The package supplies NumPy and JAX backends, both transforms (forward and inverse) validated to floating-point precision, with the JAX backend enabling GPU-accelerated transforms of million-point data streams in tens of milliseconds. As a worked example, we verify that the WDM-domain likelihood reproduces frequency-domain posteriors for a resolved LISA galactic binary under a shared stationary noise model, confirming numerical equivalence of the two representations in that controlled setting. This work paves the way for systematic optimisation of WDM tilings, a particularly promising direction for the non-stationary noise, stochastic backgrounds, and data gaps anticipated in future detectors, and for direct comparisons with alternative time-frequency representations needed to meet the challenges of future gravitational-wave data analysis.
