### [82] [Constitutive birefringence and critical curves in the rotating García--Díaz black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20284)
*Ariel Guzmán,Mohsen Fathi,J. R. Villanueva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在旋转 García–Díaz 解（爱因斯坦引力与非线性电动力学耦合）中研究高频电磁传播。通过对 Fresnel 特征问题求解，得到两个有效的光学度规，它们产生依赖于偏振的临界轮廓 Γ₊ 和 Γ₋，并在观察者天球上表现出双折射分裂。该分裂由非线性本构响应产生，受自旋和观测倾角调制，建立了局域 NLED 响应与观测屏上偏振依赖临界结构之间的直接几何联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非线性电动力学（NLED）与引力耦合系统中，光的传播不再仅由时空度规的零锥决定，因为 NLED 场本身充当光学介质，其本构关系决定了物理光学锥。因此，需要系统地理解 NLED 响应如何影响高频电磁波传播，特别是偏振相关的双折射效应。

Method: 从混合电磁势出发，将场 F 与激发 P 投影到主标架（principal tetrad）上，获得对齐标量 E、B、D、H，并通过映射 (D,B)→(E,H) 重构局域正则本构支。将得到的响应矩阵代入 Fresnel 特征问题，在扰动阶次下将四次型 Fresnel 方程因式分解为两个二次分支，各定义一支有效光学度规。进一步分析两个光学度规的 Carter 型 Hamilton–Jacobi 分离，计算临界常数与非稳临界族，并将其投影到有限距离观察者的天球上，得到临界轮廓 Γ₊ 和 Γ₋。

Result: 两个光学度规均允许 Carter 型 Hamilton–Jacobi 分离，拥有各自的径向和角向势、临界常数与非稳临界族。投影到天球上的两个临界轮廓 Γ₊ 和 Γ₋ 在麦克斯韦（Maxwell）极限下重合，而当非线性本构响应激活时发生分裂。通过最大角分离、相对直径偏移和归一化双折射宽度定量描述了该分裂。数值扫描显示，分裂由本构响应产生，被自旋重新分布，并在扰动域内对局域投影变化保持稳定。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了局域 NLED 本构响应与观察者屏幕上偏振依赖临界结构之间的直接几何联系。双折射分裂的强度由非线性耦合、自旋和观测倾角共同决定，表明了在强场引力环境中利用偏振观测探测非线性电磁响应机制的可行性。

Abstract: We study high-frequency electromagnetic propagation in the rotating García--Díaz solution of Einstein gravity coupled to NLED. In this system, light is not governed only by the null cone of the spacetime metric, because the NLED field also behaves as an optical medium whose constitutive response determines the physical optical cones. Starting from the mixed electromagnetic potentials, we project the field $F$ and the excitation $P$ on a principal tetrad and obtain the aligned scalars $E$, $B$, $D$ and $H$. These scalars allow us to reconstruct the regular local constitutive branch connected with Maxwell theory through the map $(D,B)\mapsto(E,H)$. We then insert the resulting response matrix into the Fresnel characteristic problem. At the perturbative order considered here, the Fresnel quartic factorizes into two quadratic branches, each defining an effective optical metric. Both optical metrics admit Carter-type separation of the Hamilton--Jacobi equation and possess their own radial and angular potentials, critical constants and unstable critical families. By projecting these families onto the celestial sphere of a finite-distance observer, we obtain two critical contours, $Γ_+$ and $Γ_-$, which coincide in the Maxwell limit and split when the nonlinear constitutive response is active. We quantify this birefringent splitting through the maximum angular separation, the relative diameter shift and the normalized birefringent width. Numerical scans over the nonlinear coupling, spin and observer inclination show that the splitting is generated by the constitutive response, redistributed by rotation and stable under local projection changes within the perturbative domain. This provides a direct geometrical link between the local NLED response and a polarization-dependent critical structure on the observer screen.

### [83] [Impossibility of superluminal signalling rules out causal loops in conical spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20476)
*Maarten Grothus,V. Vilasini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究解决了非超光速信号原则（NSS）与可操作检测因果环在 (1+1) 维以上闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中是否兼容的关键开放问题。结果表明，在一大类“锥形”时空中（包括 d>1 维闵可夫斯基时空），NSS 原则排除了所有经典、量子及后量子理论中可操作检测的因果环，从而确立了 NSS 与因果禁止原则之间的关系本质上依赖于时空几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对包含 d>1 维闵可夫斯基时空在内的一类“锥形”时空（conical spacetimes），在经典、量子及后量子理论（post-quantum theories）框架下，分析 NSS 原则对可操作检测因果环的约束能力。

Result: 在 d>1 维的锥形时空中，非超光速信号原则（NSS）能够排除所有可操作检测的因果环（operationally detectable causal loops）。这一结论在经典、量子及后量子理论中均成立。

Conclusion: 非超光速信号原则（NSS）与因果环禁止原则之间的关系并非普适，而是本质上依赖于时空的几何结构。

Abstract: In PRL 129, 110401 it was shown that it is theoretically possible to have operationally detectable causal loops without violating the principle of no superluminal signalling (NSS) in (1+1)-Minkowski spacetime. Whether or not such causal loops are also possible in $d > 1$ spatial dimensions, has remained a key open question. We resolve this question by showing that in a wide class of "conical" spacetimes, including Minkowski with d > 1, NSS does rule out all operationally detectable causal loops, in classical, quantum and post-quantum theories. This establishes that the relationship between the relativistic principles of NSS and no causal loops depends inherently on the geometry of spacetime.

### [84] [Propagation of Dirac spherical waves in the expanding universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20483)
*Karen Yagdjian*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文给出了膨胀宇宙中狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）球对称解的显式公式。初始值可以是类氢原子波函数或闵可夫斯基空间（Minkowski space）中的球面波，随后在具有德西特尺度（de Sitter scale）膨胀的弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克时空（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker space-time）中传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推导膨胀宇宙背景下狄拉克方程球对称解的显式表达式，从而将闵可夫斯基空间中的已知波函数（如类氢原子波函数）推广到膨胀宇宙（expanding universe）情形。

Method: 基于狄拉克方程在FLRW时空（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker space-time）中的形式，结合德西特尺度（de Sitter scale）的膨胀因子，推导球对称解的显式公式。

Result: 获得了狄拉克方程在膨胀宇宙中的球对称解的显式公式，该解可承接闵可夫斯基空间中的初始波函数（如类氢原子波函数或球面波）并随后在膨胀时空中演化。

Conclusion: 所获得的显式解为研究膨胀宇宙中狄拉克粒子（尤其是具有类氢初始态的粒子）的传播行为提供了精确的数学描述。

Abstract: The explicit formulas for the spherical solutions of the Dirac equation in the expanding universe are given. The initial value of the solution can be, in particular, a wave function of the hydrogen-like atom or a spherical wave in the Minkowski space, that then propagates in the Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker space-time, which is expanding with the de~Sitter scale

</details>


### [85] [Higher Lovelock Curvature Terms Favor Local Nakedness in Dust Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20540)
*Apratim Ganguly,Radouane Gannouji,Akshay Kumar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在球对称尘埃塌缩中，高阶Lovelock项不会恢复局域宇宙监督（local cosmic censorship），反而促进中心壳聚焦奇点（shell-focusing singularities）的局域可见性。最高非零Lovelock阶数N控制近奇点塌缩与陷阱面形成，增大N会扩大产生出射径向零测地线（outgoing radial null rays）的非均匀初始数据类，且在临界奇数维分支中奇点自动局域可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验高阶曲率Lovelock引力（higher-curvature Lovelock gravity）是否能够恢复球对称尘埃塌缩中的局域宇宙监督（local cosmic censorship），即探究高维修正引力是否阻止裸奇点（naked singularity）的形成。

Method: 通过分析球对称尘埃塌缩在Lovelock引力中的动力学行为，计算视界曲线（apparent-horizon curve）与奇点曲线（singularity curve）的相对标度，引入陷阱指数（trapping exponent）β_N和奇点曲线修正阶数ℓ，推导局域可见性条件ℓ < β_N，并区分非临界维度和临界奇数维分支两个情形。

Result: 非临界维度（D-1-2N>0）下，陷阱指数β_N = (D-1)/(D-1-2N)控制视界曲线趋近奇点曲线的行为；增大N扩大满足局域可见性条件ℓ < β_N的初始数据类。在临界奇数维分支（D=2N+1）中，中心附近不形成视界，奇点曲线的任何向外开口都导致局域可见性。局域可见奇点沿出射零测地线为Królak-强（Królak-strong），在阈值处达到Tipler强度（Tipler strength）。束缚与非束缚塌缩的非临界指数不变，能量函数仅改变奇点曲线开口。

Conclusion: 高阶Lovelock项不仅不恢复局域宇宙监督，反而使中心奇点更容易局域可见，且可见奇点具有强曲率奇点（strong curvature singularity）性质。

Abstract: We show that higher-curvature Lovelock terms do not restore local cosmic censorship in spherical dust collapse, but instead promote the local visibility of central shell-focusing singularities. On the collapse branch with positive highest-order Lovelock coefficient \(c_N\), the highest nonvanishing Lovelock order \(N\) controls both the near-singularity collapse and the formation of trapped surfaces. In noncritical dimensions, \(D-1-2N>0\), the apparent-horizon curve approaches the singularity curve with trapping exponent \(β_N=(D-1)/(D-1-2N)\). Comparing this scale with the first nonvanishing correction \(r^\ell\) to the singularity curve gives the local-visibility condition \(\ell<β_N\), provided the singularity curve opens outward. Thus increasing \(N\) enlarges the class of inhomogeneous initial data producing outgoing radial null rays from the central singularity. In the critical odd-dimensional branch, \(D=2N+1\), no apparent horizon forms sufficiently close to the center, so any outward opening of the singularity curve gives local visibility. The locally visible singularities are Królak-strong along the emerging null rays, with Tipler strength reached at threshold. For bound and unbound collapse, the noncritical exponents are unchanged: the energy function modifies the opening of the singularity curve, while in the critical branch it enters the leading terminal collapse velocity.

### [86] [Thermodynamic Measure of Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20231)
*Ishanu Chattopadhyay*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出智能（intelligence）可通过“稀有-有效未来”（rare-valid futures）的合法放大（lawful amplification）来定义和测量，并证明递归自模拟（recursive self-simulation）是达成高“稀有-有效提升”（rare-valid lift）的必要且近乎充分的条件，从而将智能置于一个普适的热力学（thermodynamic）度量框架下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决智能能否被量化测量的问题，并提出一个基于热力学（thermodynamics）的通用定义，以涵盖从被动物质到大型语言模型（large language models, LLMs）乃至类麦克斯韦妖（Maxwell-demon）信息引擎在内的各类系统。

Method: 从“智能系统必须对世界及其自身位置进行建模”这一前提出发，导出递归自模拟（recursive self-simulation）架构。通过热力学度量（thermodynamic measure）“稀有-有效提升”（rare-valid lift）来量化智能，并给出该架构与这一度量之间的必要性（necessity）和条件性近乎充分性（conditional near-sufficiency）陈述。

Result: 核心结果表明：高稀有-有效提升要求内部模拟以高保真度（high fidelity）识别稀有-有效未来；反之，当保真度高且模拟包含有效策略（effective policy）时，可达的提升接近致动受限最优（actuation-limited optimum）。因此递归自模拟对高热力学智能（thermodynamic intelligence）是必要且近乎充分的。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架使智能能够在普适尺度上被测量，覆盖从被动物质、反馈控制器、大型语言模型、作为文本生成器的人类到类麦克斯韦妖信息引擎等多种系统。

Abstract: Can intelligence be measured? We propose that intelligence can be defined as the lawful amplification of rare but valid futures: a system increases the probability of outcomes that would be unlikely under passive dynamics but remain admissible under the constraints of the domain. We start with the premise that an intelligent system must model the world and its own place within it. Because the system is part of the world it models, this leads naturally to recursive self-simulation: the system represents futures in which its own actions are part of the trajectory. Our central results give a necessity statement and a conditional near-sufficiency statement connecting this architecture to a precise thermodynamic measure of lawful amplification of rare-valid futures: high rare-valid lift is impossible unless the internal simulation identifies rare-valid futures with high fidelity; conversely, when rare-valid fidelity is high and the simulation contains an effective policy, the achievable lift approaches the actuation-limited optimum. Thus recursive self-simulation is not merely a plausible feature of intelligence but, under the stated assumptions, is necessary and nearly sufficient for high thermodynamic intelligence. The resulting framework makes intelligence measurable on a universal scale, from passive matter and feedback controllers, large language models, and humans as text generators to Maxwell-demon-like information engines.

### [87] [Three-dimensional Foliated Fractional Quantum Hall Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19426)
*Sahana Das,Navketan Batra,Andrea Kouta Dagnino,Dan Mao,Nicolas Regnault,Glenn Wagner,Titus Neupert*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究三维分层拓扑序（foliated topological orders），重点分析填充因子 ν=1/3 的堆叠劳克林态（Laughlin states）层间相互作用下的稳定性及其向非阿贝尔斐波那契分形相（foliated non-Abelian Fibonacci phase）的自发层三聚化转变，通过最多10层的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和微扰解析计算验证了相的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究三维分层系统中任意子（anyons）仅可在层内自由移动、无法在层间跳跃的叶状拓扑序（foliated topological order）的物理性质，具体关注堆叠的二维电子气在强磁场下是否能在引入层间相互作用后仍保持稳定，以及能否出现新的拓扑相。

Method: 采用最多10层的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）数值计算与微扰解析计算（perturbative analytical calculations）相结合；通过准空穴计数（quasihole counting）以及与从共形场论（conformal field theory）导出的模型波函数（model wave function）的重叠计算来识别相变。

Result: (i) 解耦的劳克林态在引入层间相互作用后仍保持稳定；(ii) 系统可进入自发层三聚化（spontaneously layer-trimerized）的叶状非阿贝尔斐波那契相（foliated non-Abelian Fibonacci phase）；(iii) 在9层系统中，采用层内和邻近层间赝势相互作用（pseudopotential interactions）时确认了叶状斐波那契相的存在。

Conclusion: 数值结果表明，这些拓扑相可能在强磁场下的分层范德华晶体（layered van der Waals crystals）以及多层异质结构（multilayer heterostructures）中实现。

Abstract: Foliated topological orders in three dimensions are layered systems in which anyons are free to move within a layer but cannot hop between them. A simple model with such a phase is a stack of decoupled two-dimensional electron gases in a strong magnetic field, each in the same fractional quantum Hall state. By focusing on the case of filling $ν=1/3$ of the lowest Landau level in each layer, we show that (i) the limit of decoupled Laughlin states is stable upon introducing interlayer interactions and (ii) the system can enter a spontaneously layer-trimerized foliated non-Abelian Fibonacci phase. We support our claims by numerical exact diagonalization of up to 10 layers as well as perturbative analytical calculations. Specifically, we show that the foliated Fibonacci phase exists in the 9-layer system with pseudopotential interactions within and between neighboring layers. We identify the phase via quasihole counting and by calculating the overlap with a model wave function which we derive from the associated conformal field theory. Our numerical results suggest the possibility of realizing these phases in layered van der Waals crystals in strong magnetic fields, as well as in multilayer heterostructures.

</details>


### [88] [Many-Body Protection of Topological Edge Memory in Strong Interacting Quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19437)
*Yuxiao Hang,Stephan Haas,Rishabh Jha*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究邦德交替XXZ链（相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型）中量子淬火（quantum quench）后拓扑边界态的记忆是否能在非可积相互作用系统中存活。结果表明：淬火后哈密顿量是否自由或真正相互作用是关键区分；自由情形下边界模返回幅度呈$t^{-3/2}$衰减，真正相互作用情形下有限时间稳定性界和矩阵乘积态模拟均显示相互作用能显著延长边界记忆，揭示了一种非可积系统中的多体保护机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子淬火将边界态（edge states）驱离平衡后，拓扑初态的记忆是否能在非可积（non-integrable）、相互作用系统中长期存活，这一问题此前未获充分探索。

Method: 采用邦德交替XXZ链（bond-alternating XXZ chain），即相互作用的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型，分析所有初/末哈密顿量在单粒子与多体组合下的淬火协议；自由末态哈密顿量下用关联矩阵方法（correlation-matrix approach）精确求解，相互作用末态哈密顿量下建立有限时间稳定性界（finite-time stability bounds），并用矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）模拟进行数值验证。

Result: 自由淬火后边界模返回幅度以$t^{-3/2}$衰减，初态相互作用仅通过缀饰单体密度矩阵进入；真正相互作用淬火后，远离局部共振时第一二聚体磁化在可任意大功率的逆二聚体耦合时间窗口内保持稳定；MPS模拟显示末态哈密顿量中的相互作用显著延长边界记忆，但各向同性SU(2)点附近存在局部抑制。

Conclusion: 在非可积系统中，相互作用可以作为一种多体保护机制（many-body protection mechanism）延长拓扑边缘态的有限时间记忆，而不会像混沌动力学那样迅速抹去初态信息。

Abstract: Quantum quenches drive edge states far from equilibrium, yet whether the memory of a topological initial state survives in a non-integrable, interacting system has remained largely unexplored. We study this question in the bond-alternating XXZ chain -- an interacting Su--Schrieffer--Heeger model hosting symmetry-protected topological edge modes with markedly enhanced boundary magnetization -- and analyze quenches across all combinations of single-particle and many-body initial and final Hamiltonians. The results organize by a single distinction as we rigorously establish in this work: whether the post-quench Hamiltonian is free or genuinely interacting. For a free post-quench Hamiltonian, the dynamics is solved exactly by a correlation-matrix approach; the boundary-mode return amplitude decays as $t^{-3/2}$, and initial interactions enter only through a dressed one-body density matrix. For a genuinely interacting post-quench Hamiltonian, finite-time stability bounds prove that away from local resonances the first-dimer magnetization remains stable on time windows growing as arbitrarily large powers of the inverse inter-dimer coupling. Matrix product state simulations across all four protocols show that interactions in the final Hamiltonian markedly extend finite-time boundary memory -- with local suppression near the isotropic $SU(2)$ point -- revealing a many-body protection mechanism in a non-integrable system where scrambling would otherwise wash out initial-state memory fast.

</details>


### [89] [Creating and Driving a Twist Soliton on a Magnetic Skyrmion Tube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19900)
*Shoya Kasai,Kotaro Shimizu,Shun Okumura,Yukitoshi Motome*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了磁性斯格明子管（skyrmion tube）中的扭转自由度（twist degree of freedom），发现通过热猝灭动力学可产生局域化扭转孤子（twist soliton），并揭示了其依赖于手性的电流驱动非线性运动、磁场对速度的增强效应以及通过霍尔测量（Hall measurement）识别扭转孤子的方法，从而拓展了斯格明子管物理的三维自旋织构应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究关注三维斯格明子管（skyrmion tube）的动力学和涌现性质，但仅限于简单堆叠二维斯格明子。本文旨在超越这一图像，探索沿管方向引入扭转（twist）如何影响斯格明子管的动力学和涌现响应。

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟（numerical simulation）与基于集体坐标（collective coordinates）的解析计算相结合的方法，研究扭转孤子的形成与动力学行为。

Result: （1）扭转可通过热猝灭动力学（thermal quench dynamics）作为局域化的扭转孤子（twist soliton）产生；（2）扭转孤子表现出依赖于扭转手性（twist chirality）的电流驱动非线性运动；（3）垂直于管方向的磁场分量可显著增强其运动速度；（4）与扭转孤子相关的涌现电场（emergent electric field）可通过霍尔测量（Hall measurement）识别扭转孤子及其手性符号。

Conclusion: 扭转自由度是斯格明子管物理中不可或缺的因素，研究结果为利用三维自旋织构（three-dimensional spin texture）开发自旋电子学器件（spintronic device）奠定了基础。

Abstract: A magnetic skyrmion tube is a three-dimensional topological soliton formed by stacking two-dimensional skyrmions along the out-of-plane direction. Recent real-space observations of skyrmion tubes have stimulated growing interest in their dynamics and emergent properties. Here, we go beyond simple skyrmion stacking and investigate how a ``twist" introduced along the tube direction affects the dynamics and emergent responses of skyrmion tubes. We find that such a twist can be created as a localized texture, termed a twist soliton, through thermal quench dynamics. By complementarily combining large-scale numerical simulations with analytical calculations based on collective coordinates, we clarify its current-driven nonlinear motions that depend on its twist chirality. Remarkably, its velocity can be substantially enhanced by a magnetic-field component perpendicular to the tube. Furthermore, the associated emergent electric field enables identification of the twist soliton, including the sign of its chirality, through Hall measurements. Our results reveal the twist degree of freedom as an essential ingredient of skyrmion-tube physics and pave the way for the development of spintronic devices exploiting the three-dimensional nature of spin textures.

### [90] [Anomalous Transverse Response in Nodal line Semimetal Mn$_{3}$SnC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20182)
*Sunil Gangwar,C. S. Yadav*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在反钙钛矿Mn₃SnC中，反常霍尔效应（AHE）和反常能斯特效应（ANE）主要由内禀贝里曲率（Berry curvature）效应主导，并通过莫特关系（Mott's relation）建立了AHE与ANE之间的统一关联。反铁磁（AFM）和铁磁（FM）磁振子对电子的散射在反常能斯特信号中均有体现。|α^A_xy|/σ^A_xy 比值达到 k_B/e 的显著份额，表明贝里曲率对ANE具有重要贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究拓扑表面态与磁性相互作用所导致的非常规输运行为，特别是反钙钛矿材料中异常输运现象的微观机制。

Method: 通过实验测量反钙钛矿Mn₃SnC中的反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）和反常能斯特电导率（anomalous Nernst conductivity），并利用莫特关系（Mott's relation）将二者统一关联。分析反铁磁（AFM）和铁磁（FM）磁振子散射对反常能斯特信号的影响，并考察 |α^A_xy|/σ^A_xy 比值。

Result: Mn₃SnC中的反常输运（AHE和ANE）主要由内禀贝里曲率效应主导；AHE与ANE之间满足莫特关系所描述的统一关联；反铁磁和铁磁磁振子散射均在反常能斯特信号中有所体现；|α^A_xy|/σ^A_xy 比值达到 k_B/e 的显著份额。

Conclusion: 反钙钛矿Mn₃SnC中的AHE和ANE受内禀贝里曲率效应控制，贝里曲率对反常能斯特效应具有显著贡献，这为理解拓扑材料中反常输运的微观机制提供了依据。

Abstract: The interplay of topological surface states and magnetism gives rise to unconventional transport behaviors such as the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) and anomalous Nernst effect (ANE). Antiperovskites such as Mn$3$SnC, which are nodal-line semimetals and exhibit concurrent antiferromagnetic (AFM) and ferromagnetic (FM) ordering, provide a fertile ground for anomalous transport phenomena. Here, we report that the anomalous transport (AHE and ANE) in this compound is predominantly governed by the intrinsic Berry-curvature effect. We establish a unified relationship between the AHE and ANE using Mott's relation. Electron scattering by both AFM and FM magnons is manifested in the anomalous Nernst signal. The ratio of the anomalous Nernst conductivity to the anomalous Hall conductivity, $|α^A{xy}|/σ^A_{xy}$, constitutes a sizable fraction of $k_B/e$, indicating a strong Berry-curvature contribution to the ANE.

### [91] [Superconductivity and non-Fermi liquid metals in a charge-1/3 anyon fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20403)
*Zhengyan Darius Shi,T. Senthil*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了在ν=2/3 Jain分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）中掺杂电荷1/3任意子形成的流体，提出一种味对称配对态（SC*态）——一种电荷-2e凝聚体与残余Z₂拓扑序共存的状态，并探讨了弱配对与强配对 regimes 的手征中心荷差异（c_-=7/2 vs c_-=2），以及低掺杂下的非费米液体Z₃正交金属（Orthogonal Metal）相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标准复合费米子（composite fermion）描述下，掺杂的任意子（anyon）分裂为三种平移相关的味（flavor）次级复合费米子，其规范中介相互作用驱动了强烈的味间配对不稳定性。作者此前分析了一种味不对称配对态并得到了电荷有序费米液体（charge-ordered Fermi liquid）；本文受近期论文启发，探索一种替代的味对称配对态，以揭示其是否具有截然不同的物理性质。

Method: 采用复合费米子（composite fermion）理论框架，对味对称配对态进行理论分析，将其与先前提出的有效场论进行对比，并系统研究弱配对（weak pairing）与强配对（strong pairing）两个 regime 下的拓扑序特征。

Result: 味对称配对态是一个SC*态，即电荷-2e凝聚体与残余Z₂拓扑序共存的状态；弱配对与强配对具有相同的固有拓扑序（intrinsic topological order），但手征中心荷（chiral central charge）分别为c_-=7/2和c_-=2。低掺杂下存在一个近似的SU(3)对称 regime，系统实现为具有三个电荷1/3费米口袋（fermion pockets）且无清晰电子准粒子的非费米液体Z₃正交金属（Z₃ Orthogonal Metal）。

Conclusion: 掺杂驱动的FCI到超导体转变中，局域任意子演化为Bogoliubov准粒子（Bogoliubov quasiparticles）而非涡旋（vortices）；同时讨论了多种可能基态的 energetics 及其对摩尔材料（moire materials）实验的启示。

Abstract: We revisit the charge-1/3 anyon fluid obtained by doping the $ν= 2/3$ Jain fractional Chern insulator (FCI). In the standard composite fermion description, the doped anyons fractionalize into three translation-related flavors of secondary composite fermions, whose gauge-mediated interactions drive a robust inter-flavor pairing instability. In our previous work, we analyzed a flavor-asymmetric paired state and obtained a charge-ordered Fermi liquid. Inspired by a recent paper, we consider an alternative flavor-symmetric paired state and show that it is an SC* state: a charge-$2e$ condensate that coexists with residual $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological order. The weak and strong pairing regimes share the same intrinsic topological order but differ in chiral central charge, giving $c_- = 7/2$ and $c_- = 2$. We further show how other proposed effective field theories fit within the same composite fermion description, and argue that across the doping driven FCI-to-superconductor transition, localized anyons evolve into Bogoliubov quasiparticles rather than vortices. At low doping, we identify an approximate SU(3)-symmetric regime in which the system instead realizes a non-Fermi liquid $\mathbb{Z}_3$ Orthogonal Metal with three charge-1/3 fermion pockets and no sharp electron quasiparticle. Finally, we comment on the energetics of various possible ground states and discuss implications for experiments in moire materials.

</details>


### [92] [Effects of nonlocal interactions on s- and d-wave superconducting correlations in the extended Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20260)
*Pavol Farkasovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过精确对角化和量子蒙特卡洛模拟，系统研究了扩展哈伯德模型中非局域相互作用对超导配对关联的影响，揭示了不同非局域项对s波和d波配对对称性的差异化调控作用，并指出超出最小哈伯德模型的处理对于理解非常规超导至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）仅包含局域库仑相互作用和最近邻跳跃，无法充分描述真实强关联体系中丰富的非局域相互作用效应。本文旨在系统考察多种非局域相互作用项对超导配对关联（superconducting pairing correlations）的影响，以更真实地理解非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）的微观机制。

Method: 采用 Lanczos 精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法在 $4\times4$ 团簇上进行分析，并结合投影子量子蒙特卡洛（projector quantum Monte Carlo）模拟对特定参数区域进行验证。在扩展哈伯德模型中，除了已有的在位库仑相互作用和最近邻跳跃外，额外引入次近邻跳跃、最近邻库仑相互作用、关联跳跃、交换相互作用以及配对跳跃等非局域项。

Result: 非局域相互作用对超导配对关联具有高度非平凡且对称性依赖的影响：在位排斥与次近邻跳跃协同增强 d 波配对倾向；关联跳跃和最近邻库仑相互作用强烈促进 s 波关联；交换和配对跳跃相互作用在超过一定临界强度后有效抑制超导；所有非局域项同时存在时，相图呈现不同配对对称性之间的复杂竞争与交织。

Conclusion: 扩展相互作用在塑造强关联系统的配对景观中起关键作用，仅依赖最小哈伯德模型不足以真实描述非常规超导，必须对非局域相互作用进行全面处理。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of nonlocal interactions on superconducting correlations within the extended Hubbard model. In addition to the on-site Coulomb interaction and nearest-neighbor hopping, we include next-nearest-neighbor hopping together with several physically relevant nonlocal terms, namely nearest-neighbor Coulomb interaction, correlated hopping, exchange interaction, and pair hopping. Using Lanczos exact diagonalization on a $4\times4$ cluster, supported by projector quantum Monte Carlo simulations for selected parameter regimes, we analyze pairing correlations in both the s- and d-wave channels. We demonstrate that nonlocal interactions exert a highly nontrivial and symmetry-dependent influence on superconducting correlations. While the on-site repulsion in cooperation with next-nearest-neighbor hopping enhances d-wave pairing tendencies, correlated hopping and nearest-neighbor Coulomb interaction strongly promote s-wave correlations, whereas exchange and pair-hopping interactions can efficiently suppress superconductivity beyond relatively small critical strengths. When all nonlocal interactions are considered simultaneously, the resulting phase diagrams reveal a complex interplay and competition between different pairing symmetries. Our results highlight the crucial role of extended interactions in shaping the pairing landscape of strongly correlated systems and demonstrate that a comprehensive treatment beyond the minimal Hubbard model is essential for a realistic description of unconventional superconductivity.

</details>


### [93] [All-In-All-Out Pyrochlore Iridates as Noncollinear Spin-Orbit Coupled Counterparts of Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20296)
*Yang Yang,Turan Birol,Rafael M. Fernandes,Natalia B. Perkins*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过微观模型证明，烧绿石铱氧化物（pyrochlore iridates）中的全入全出态（AIAO state）构成一种由强自旋轨道耦合（SOC）稳定的非共线d波交变磁体（noncollinear d-wave altermagnet），其对称性导致动量依赖的自旋劈裂和零动量处的能带劈裂，为交变磁性在强自旋轨道耦合材料中的非共线对应物提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）中动量依赖的自旋劈裂模式也可以在具有大自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）的非共线磁性系统中出现，但此类对应关系尚未被系统建立。本文旨在从微观模型出发，揭示烧绿石铱氧化物中的AIAO态作为非共线d波交变磁体的本质，并建立其对称性框架。

Method: 采用基于烧绿石格点的微观jeff=1/2紧束缚模型（tight-binding model），通过群论分析（group-theory analysis）和平均场计算（mean-field calculations）研究电子相互作用驱动的AIAO相及其对称性质。

Result: AIAO序参量变换为A2g−八极磁矩（octupolar magnetic moment），破坏时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）同时保持空间反演（inversion）和零净磁化。该对称性同时导致了：（1）与共线d波立方交变磁体类似的自旋极化、动量依赖的能带简并消除；（2）在零动量处也存在能带劈裂，后者可由类似于立方半导体Luttinger-Kohn模型的低能模型描述。

Conclusion: 烧绿石铱氧化物可作为非共线交变磁对应物的材料平台，该研究为强自旋轨道耦合材料中自旋劈裂现象提供了普适的对称性理论框架。

Abstract: Altermagnets are collinear magnetically ordered states that exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting in the absence of net magnetization and spin-orbit coupling (SOC). Related spin-splitting patterns, however, can also emerge in noncollinear magnetic systems with large SOC. Here we show, via a microscopic model, that the all-in-all-out (AIAO) state in pyrochlore iridates constitutes a noncollinear counterpart of a $d$-wave altermagnet stabilized by strong SOC. Starting from a microscopic $j_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1/2$ tight-binding model on the pyrochlore lattice, we demonstrate that electronic interactions favor the AIAO phase and analyze its symmetry properties. We show that the AIAO order parameter transforms as an $A_{2g}^{-}$ octupolar magnetic moment, breaking time-reversal symmetry while preserving inversion and zero net magnetization. Using group-theory analysis and mean-field calculations, we demonstrate that this symmetry enforces both a spin-polarized momentum-dependent lifting of band degeneracies that is similar to that of a collinear $d$-wave cubic altermagnet, but also a band splitting at zero-momentum. We show that the latter feature is captured by a low-energy model similar to the
  Luttinger-Kohn model for cubic semiconductors. Our results identify pyrochlore iridates as a platform for noncollinear counterparts of altermagnetism and provide a general symmetry framework for spin-split phenomena in spin-orbit coupled materials.

</details>


### [94] [Fractional excitations in Kitaev quasi-one-dimensional chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20309)
*Ritwika Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文从Kitaev蜂窝模型出发，截断其几何结构构造了一个准一维Kitaev自旋链，该链展现出分数化马约拉纳激发、手征拓扑相与零能边缘模，并通过动力学自旋关联函数提供了可实验观测的特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kitaev蜂窝模型因其量子自旋液体基态（quantum spin liquid ground state）、分数化马约拉纳激发（fractionalized Majorana excitations）和拓扑性质而引发广泛关注，但一维系统中能否复现这些特征尚不明确。本文旨在通过构造准一维Kitaev自旋链，建立二维Kitaev自旋液体与一维量子线之间的概念桥梁。

Method: 从Kitaev蜂窝模型中截断出一个准一维的Kitaev-like自旋链；通过分析马约拉纳能带结构（Majorana band structure）识别色散带与平带，并考察能隙闭合处的临界各向异性；引入开放边界条件（open boundary conditions）研究零能边缘模；通过引入负plaquette畴区调控局域plaquette模；计算动力学自旋关联函数（dynamical spin correlation function）以揭示激发谱特征。

Result: 马约拉纳能带结构同时包含色散带（dispersive bands）和平带（flat bands），在临界各向异性处能隙闭合，将平凡拓扑相与手征拓扑相（chiral topological phases）分开；开放边界下，手征拓扑区域存在由手征对称性（chiral symmetry）保护的零能边缘模（zero-energy edge modes），系统属于BDI对称性类，具有量子化绕数（quantized winding number）；激发谱中在零能附近出现局域plaquette模，可通过负plaquette畴区进行调控；动力学自旋关联函数展现出与分数化激发相关的宽连续谱，以及来自边缘马约拉纳模的特征低能谱权重。

Conclusion: 该准一维Kitaev自旋链具有区别于传统海森堡自旋链的独特特征，为手征拓扑序（chiral topological order）提供了实验上可观测的指纹信号，从而在二维Kitaev自旋液体与Kitaev一维量子线之间建立了概念上的桥梁。

Abstract: The Kitaev honeycomb model has attracted significant interest due to its quantum spin liquid ground state, fractionalized Majorana excitations, and topological properties. Motivated by these features, we introduce a quasi-one-dimensional Kitaev-like spin chain derived from a truncated honeycomb geometry. The resulting Majorana band structure contains both dispersive and flat bands, with a gap closing at a critical anisotropy that separates trivial and chiral topological phases. Under open boundary conditions, the topological regime hosts zero-energy edge modes protected by chiral symmetry, placing the system in the BDI symmetry class with a quantized winding number. In the excited spectrum, localized plaquette modes emerge near zero energy and can be tuned by introducing domains of negative plaquettes. The dynamical spin correlation function reveals broad continua associated with fractionalized excitations, together with characteristic low-energy spectral weight from edge Majorana modes. These features distinguish the present system from conventional Heisenberg spin chains and provide experimentally relevant fingerprints of chiral topological order. Our model thus establishes a conceptual bridge between the two-dimensional Kitaev spin liquid and Kitaev's one-dimensional quantum wire.

### [95] [Non-Hermitian Skin Effect Enhances Pairing Correlations in Moiré Hubbard Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20425)
*Yang Zhou,Jianwen Chen,Ruipeng Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）能够通过通道选择性（channel-selective）机制增强莫尔哈伯德体系（moiré Hubbard systems）中的配对关联：趋肤诱导的局域化放大边界态密度，在中等非互易强度窗口（γ∈[0.5,1.2]t）内加强局域配对倾向。通过精确对角化和非厄米DMRG计算，论文映射了(U,γ)相图，发现双占据数（double occupancy）呈现非单调行为，配对磁化率（pairing susceptibility）在on-site通道中增加21%，同时竞争的反铁磁关联被抑制22%，总配对磁化率在3×3团簇上增长98%。论文不声称长程超导序，但通过BCS标度估计给出了穹顶形的Tc(γ)指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）能否在强关联晶格体系（如莫尔哈伯德系统）中增强配对关联（pairing correlations），进而为理解非常规超导机制提供新的物理视角。

Method: 采用开边界三角晶格上的非厄米哈伯德模型（non-Hermitian Hubbard model），通过精确对角化（exact diagonalization）在3×3团簇上映射(U,γ)相图；辅以独立的非厄米DMRG（non-Hermitian DMRG）计算进行佐证。通过分析双占据数（double occupancy）D(γ)和配对磁化率（pairing susceptibility）χ_SC的通道分解来表征NHSE的效应。

Result: 双占据数D(γ)呈现非单调行为，上升最高达21%后下降，反映NHSE增强边界配对与过度局域化之间的竞争。配对磁化率的通道分解显示NHSE具有通道选择性：on-site配对增加21%，竞争的反铁磁关联（antiferromagnetic correlations）被抑制22%，总配对磁化率在3×3团簇上增长98%。BCS标度估计给出穹顶形（dome-shaped）的Tc(γ)曲线。

Conclusion: NHSE能以通道选择性方式增强有限团簇中的配对关联，而非源于平庸的密度重分布（density redistribution）。该效应在相干驱动型（coherent-drive）与库主导型（reservoir-dominated）莫尔器件中应能观察到可区分的实验响应。论文明确不声称长程超导序（long-range superconducting order）。

Abstract: We show that the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) can enhance pairing correlations in moiré Hubbard systems through a channel-selective mechanism: skin-induced localization amplifies the boundary density of states, strengthening local pairing tendencies within an intermediate ``golden window'' of non-reciprocity $γ\in[0.5,1.2]\,t$. Using exact diagonalization of the non-Hermitian Hubbard model on triangular lattices with open boundaries, we map the $(U,γ)$ phase diagram. The double occupancy $D(γ)$ exhibits non-monotonic behavior -- rising by up to 21\% then declining -- reflecting a competition between NHSE-enhanced boundary pairing and over-localization. A decomposition of the pairing susceptibility $χ_{\mathrm{SC}}$ on the $3\times3$ cluster reveals that the NHSE acts \emph{channel-selectively}: it enhances on-site pairing ($+21\%$) while simultaneously suppressing competing antiferromagnetic correlations (22\% reduction), so that the total pairing susceptibility, dominated by the on-site channel, grows by $+98\%$ on that cluster. These trends are corroborated by an independent non-Hermitian DMRG calculation and establish an enhancement of finite-cluster pairing correlations rather than trivial density redistribution. We do not claim long-range superconducting order. A BCS scaling estimate converts the same pairing-response signal into a dome-shaped $T_c(γ)$ fingerprint, suggesting an experimentally distinguishable response in coherent-drive versus reservoir-dominated moiré devices.

</details>

*Emile Pangburn,Igor de Melo Froldi,Anurag Banerjee*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解析和数值方法对魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）中拓扑重费米子模型的描述是否现实尚不完全清楚，尤其是局域近似（如Hubbard-I）可能无法正确刻画局域磁矩与巡游狄拉克电子之间的耦合。

Method: 提出一种超越单格点极限的Hubbard算符方法（Hubbard operator approach），纳入非局域关联（non-local correlations）；以格点正则化模型上的精确行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）模拟作为基准进行对比验证。

Result: 常用的局域近似（如Hubbard-I）无法捕捉局域与巡游自由度之间的耦合，在局域磁矩区域给出错误的谱性质；而Hubbard算符方法在参数范围内的关联函数和谱特征均与精确数值方法高度吻合。

Conclusion: Hubbard算符方法为MATBG中拓扑重费米子模型提供了可控且准确的描述，克服了局域近似的局限性，是研究该体系中局域与巡游电子共存问题的有效工具。

Abstract: The topological heavy-fermion model provides a minimal framework for describing the coexistence of localized moments and itinerant Dirac electrons in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG). Several analytical and numerical methods have been applied to this model; however, whether they provide a realistic description of MATBG remains incompletely understood. In this work, we develop an Hubbard operator approach that incorporates non-local correlations beyond the single-site limit. We benchmark the approximate calculations against numerically exact determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations of a lattice-regularized model. We show that commonly used local approximations, such as Hubbard-I, fail to capture the coupling between localized and itinerant degrees of freedom, leading to incorrect spectral properties in the local-moment regime. In contrast, the Hubbard operator method provides a controlled description of both correlation functions and spectral features over a regime of parameters, in good agreement with exact numerical methods.

### [97] [Transfer-matrix functions for algebraically decaying interactions in variational infinite matrix product states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20522)
*Qi Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需有限极点和指数和代理（finite-pole sum-of-exponentials surrogate）的变分无限矩阵乘积态（variational infinite matrix product state, iMPS）方法，直接通过连接转移矩阵（connected transfer matrix）和矩阵函数（matrix function）处理代数衰减长程相互作用，并利用Krylov方法和Fréchet伴随（Fréchet adjoint）实现稳定梯度计算。基准测试表明该方法可避免代理哈密顿量带来的临界偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准无限矩阵乘积态（iMPS）算法在处理具有代数衰减（algebraically decaying）相互作用的哈密顿量时，通常需要先将其替换为有限极点的指数和代理（finite-pole sum-of-exponentials surrogate），这一过程会引入哈密顿量表示残差（Hamiltonian-representation residual），可能影响计算精度。

Method: 固定截断维数$D$的变分能量求解无需引入代理哈密顿量，而是通过连接转移矩阵（connected transfer matrix）直接求和代数长程尾项：形式为$e^{\mathrm{i} Qr}/r^α$的尾项表示为矩阵函数$F_{α,Q}(\widetilde{T}_A)=\operatorname{Li}_α(e^{\mathrm{i} Q}\,z)/z$。矩阵函数的作用通过Krylov方法计算，并通过结合Fréchet伴随（Fréchet adjoint）与隐式不动点微分（implicit fixed-point differentiation）获得稳定梯度。

Result: 在长程自由费米子（long-range free fermions）和逆平方海森堡族（inverse-square Heisenberg family，包括Haldane–Shastry点）的基准测试中验证了该转移矩阵函数公式的有效性。长程伊辛链（long-range Ising chain）计算表明，在固定且已知的临界场下，有限极点代理哈密顿量会使临界诊断偏离临界点，而矩阵函数方法能保留目标代数哈密顿量的预期临界特征。

Conclusion: 所提出的转移矩阵函数公式避免了有限极点哈密顿量表示引入的偏差，能够更准确地处理代数衰减长程相互作用下的临界问题。

Abstract: Variational infinite matrix product state (iMPS) calculations usually make Hamiltonians with algebraically decaying interactions compatible with standard MPO algorithms by first replacing the target Hamiltonian with a finite-pole sum-of-exponentials surrogate, thereby introducing a Hamiltonian-representation residual. We formulate the fixed-$D$ variational energy without introducing such a surrogate. For a fixed finite-$D$ MPS, the algebraic tail can be summed directly through the connected transfer matrix: the tail $e^{\mathrm{i} Qr}/r^α$ is represented by the matrix function $F_{α,Q}(\widetilde{T}_A)$, with $F_{α,Q}(z)=\operatorname{Li}_α(e^{\mathrm{i} Q}\,z)/z$. We evaluate the resulting matrix-function action using a Krylov method and obtain stable gradients by combining a Fréchet adjoint with implicit fixed-point differentiation. Benchmarks on long-range free fermions and the inverse-square Heisenberg family, including the Haldane--Shastry point, validate the transfer-matrix-function formulation. A long-range Ising-chain calculation illustrates a practical consequence of avoiding a finite-pole Hamiltonian representation. At a fixed, independently known critical field, finite-pole surrogate Hamiltonians can bias a critical diagnostic away from criticality, whereas the matrix-function calculation retains the expected critical signatures of the target algebraic Hamiltonian.

</details>

### [98] [Cosmic Structure Formation in a Viable Power-Law f(R) Gravity Model: Growth Dynamics, Stability, and Observational Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19402)
*Murli Manohar Verma*

Main category: physics.gen-ph

TL;DR: 本文在幂律修正引力模型 $f(R)=R+R^{1+δ}/R_c^δ$ 框架下，研究了宇宙大尺度结构的演化，推导了修正的扰动方程并分析了物质密度扰动增长率、增长指数及可观测物理量 $fσ_8(z)$，发现曲率修正可在与晚期加速膨胀兼容的前提下增强物质扰动增长，且模型满足理论自洽性条件（无鬼、Dolgov–Kawasaki 稳定性、正标量质量、稳态 de Sitter 解及变色龙屏蔽机制）。与代表性可行 $f(R)$ 引力模型的比较表明该理论仅需单一偏差参数即可实现一致的宇宙学演化，其结构增长和有效引力耦合的修正可为未来大尺度结构和弱引力透镜巡天提供可检验的观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 $f(R)$ 修正引力理论通常需要多个参数来描述偏离广义相对论（General Relativity）的效应，本文旨在探索仅含单一偏差参数 δ 的幂律修正引力模型是否能同时解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀与物质扰动增长，并为可观测的大尺度结构信号提供理论预言。

Method: 在度规 $f(R)$ 引力框架下研究背景宇宙学动力学，通过引入与附加标量自由度（scalar degree of freedom）相关的有效引力耦合（effective gravitational coupling）导出修正的线性物质密度扰动方程，进而计算增长因子（growth factor）、对数增长率（logarithmic growth rate）、增长指数（growth index）及可观测组合 $fσ_8(z)$。

Result: 曲率修正（curvature correction）在合适的模型参数 δ 下能够增强物质扰动的增长，同时与观测到的晚期加速膨胀兼容；模型满足无鬼条件（ghost-free condition）、Dolgov–Kawasaki 稳定性判据、正标量质量（positive scalaron mass）、稳态 de Sitter 解及变色龙屏蔽机制（chameleon screening mechanism）等理论自洽性约束。

Conclusion: 该幂律修正引力理论仅凭一个偏差参数即可实现与其他代表性可行 $f(R)$ 引力模型一致的宇宙学演化，其对结构增长和有效引力耦合的修正有望通过即将开展的大尺度结构（large-scale structure）和弱引力透镜（weak-lensing）巡天进行检验，从而为探测曲率引起的引力修正提供观测途径。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of cosmic structures in the power-law modified gravity model $f(R)=R+R^{1+δ}/R_c^δ$, where the dimensionless parameter $δ$ characterizes deviations from General Relativity. The background cosmological dynamics and the evolution of linear matter density perturbations are studied within the framework of metric $f(R)$ gravity. The modified perturbation equation is derived by introducing an effective gravitational coupling associated with the additional scalar degree of freedom, and the evolution of the growth factor, logarithmic growth rate, growth index, and the observable quantity $fσ_8(z)$ are investigated. The results show that the curvature correction enhances the growth of matter perturbations while remaining compatible with the observed late-time accelerated expansion for suitable values of the model parameter. The theoretical viability of the model is established through the ghost-free condition, Dolgov--Kawasaki stability criterion, positive scalaron mass, stable de Sitter solution, and chameleon screening mechanism. Comparison with representative viable $f(R)$ gravity models shows that the present theory achieves a consistent cosmological evolution with a single deviation parameter. The predicted modifications in the growth of structures and the effective gravitational coupling provide observable signatures that can be tested by forthcoming large-scale structure and weak-lensing surveys, providing a means to test curvature-induced modifications of gravity.

</details>

### [99] [Reflection-Positive Construction of a Four-Dimensional SU(N) Yang-Mills Theory with Mass Gap and Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19362)
*Mir Faizal,Arshid Shabir*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文从欧几里得观点出发，仅基于正性（positivity）与局域性（locality）要求，通过反射正定晶格表述、收敛的特征展开（character expansion）与多尺度分析，严格证明了纯 SU(N) 杨-米尔斯理论在连续极限下具有指数聚类、严格正则的弦张力（string tension）、质量间隙（mass gap）以及静态夸克间的线性势（confinement）；并且论证了强耦合与渐近自由弱耦合两种途径殊途同归，将质量间隙与禁闭（confinement）确立为非阿贝尔真空的自然属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希望从最小公理要求——正性与局域性——出发，导出纯 SU(N) 杨-米尔斯理论在连续极限下禁闭与质量间隙的严格数学证明，并打破强耦合与弱耦合构造之间的鸿沟。

Method: 采用反射正定（reflection-positive）的晶格表述构造转移算符（transfer operator）并证明其具有一致能隙；利用收敛的特征展开（character/polymer expansions）在晶格尺度上直接证明威尔逊圈面积律（area law）；通过有限范围、规范协变的多尺度分析（multiscale analysis）将单尺度性质逐级传递至连续极限，并以交错不等式（interlaced inequalities）控制缺陷累积；借助 Osterwalder-Schrader 重构将欧几里得结果转化为闵可夫斯基理论；使用单尺度 Lipschitz 控制与伸缩论证（telescoping argument）统一不同反射正定切片，确保极限测度的唯一性与普适性（universality）。

Result: 在连续极限下获得了指数聚类（exponential clustering）、严格正的弦张力、位于真空之上的谱间隙（spectral gap）以及静态电荷间的线性势，从而给出了禁闭的具体图像；强耦合与弱耦合两种途径收敛于同一个连续理论。

Conclusion: 质量间隙与禁闭并非需要额外假设的奇迹，而是正性、局域性与重整化（renormalization）协同作用的自然结果，展示了非阿贝尔真空固有的结构属性。

Abstract: In the Euclidean view one must first require that positivity not be violated, and from this modest demand, together with locality, a great deal follows: starting from a reflection-positive lattice formulation of pure SU(N) Yang-Mills theory we obtain a transfer operator with a uniform gap, while large Wilson loops already show an area law by means of convergent character (polymer) expansions; a finite-range, gauge-covariant multiscale analysis then carries these features from one scale to the next with interlaced inequalities whose small defects can be summed, so that exponential clustering and a strictly positive string tension endure in the continuum; the Osterwalder-Schrader reconstruction turns these Euclidean facts into a Minkowski theory with a self-adjoint Hamiltonian, the spectral gap lying above the vacuum and the linear potential for static charges appearing, which gives a concrete picture of confinement; the construction depends on no special regulator, for a single-scale Lipschitz control and a telescoping argument bind all admissible reflection-positive slicings into a unique limiting measure and thus secure universality; moreover, the same framework admits entry from weak coupling, so that the continuum reached from strong coupling meets the one approached along an asymptotically free trajectory, yielding one and the same theory; in my view this is how mathematical clarity and physical insight cooperate: positivity, locality, and renormalization working together so that the mass gap and confinement are not marvels to be assumed, but natural properties of the non-Abelian vacuum.

### [100] [Confining Flux Tube in the Trace Deformed (2+1) Dimensional SU(2) Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20270)
*Claudio Bonati,Michele Caselle,Alessio Negro,Dario Panfalone,Lorenzo Verzichelli*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本论文通过(2+1)维迹变形(trace deformed)SU(2)杨-米尔斯(Yang-Mills)理论的晶格模拟，发现重禁闭相中的通量管(flux tube)不再由标准Nambu-Goto有效弦描述，而是由包含外曲率项(extrinsic-curvature term)的Polchinski-Yang刚性弦解准确描述，并观察到通量管横向轮廓和宽度的显著偏差，以及重禁闭线从连续到一级相变的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究迹变形SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论在重禁闭相(reconfined phase)中通量管的有效弦描述，探索该相是否与标准禁闭相存在本质不同的有效弦动力学。

Method: 使用(2+1)维格点规范理论(lattice gauge theory)模拟，在高于标准退禁闭温度的温度下分析Polyakov圈关联子(Polyakov-loop correlators)，提取有效弦的基态能量，并计算通量管的横向轮廓。

Result: 随着迹变形参数增大，标准Nambu-Goto有效弦描述（包括高阶修正）无法拟合数据；深重禁闭区域的数据可由Polchinski-Yang刚性弦解精确描述；通量管横向轮廓和内在宽度(intrinsic width)相对标准杨-米尔斯行为出现显著偏离；重禁闭线随变形参数增大由连续相变变为一级相变。

Conclusion: 重禁闭相实现了与普通禁闭相定性不同的有效弦动力学（外曲率项主导），提示其与标准禁闭属于不同的有效弦机制。

Abstract: We study the confining flux tube in the reconfined phase of trace deformed SU(2) Yang-Mills theory in (2+1) dimensions. Using lattice simulations above the standard deconfinement temperature, we analyze Polyakov-loop correlators and extract the ground state energy of the effective string. We show that the usual Nambu-Goto effective string description, including its standard higher-order corrections, fails to reproduce the data as the trace deformation is increased. Remarkably, deep in the reconfined regime the results are instead accurately described by the Polchinski-Yang rigid-string solution, corresponding to an effective string dominated by an extrinsic-curvature term. We further investigate the transverse profile of the chromo-electric flux tube and find significant deviations from the standard Yang-Mills behavior, including a substantial modification of the intrinsic width. Finally, we present an exploratory study of the phase diagram, finding evidence for a transition from a continuous to a first order reconfinement line as the deformation parameter increases. These results suggest that the reconfined phase realizes a qualitatively different effective-string regime from ordinary confinement.

### [101] [Solving Nonequilibrium Dynamics via Influence Matrix Bootstrap: Floquet-PXP Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19430)
*Xiao-Yang Yang,He-Ran Wang,Zhong Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过张量网络方法（influence matrix）发展了一套广义拉链条件（generalized zipper conditions）和数值自举方法（bootstrap method），在“Rule 201”量子元胞自动机（这是一个可积的PXP哈密顿量的Trotter化）中精确求解了非平衡局域动力学，并揭示了隐藏马尔可夫序（hidden Markov order）等多时间关联结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可积系统（integrable systems）对理解量子多体物理至关重要，但其非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium integrable dynamics）的精确刻画仍然是一个重大挑战。现有方法通常只能有效描述基态和热力学等平衡性质，缺乏统一且解析可控的非平衡分析框架。

Method: 采用张量网络方法中的影响矩阵（influence matrix），发展广义拉链条件（generalized zipper conditions）以精确求解局域动力学；引入数值自举方法（bootstrap method）求解有限但较大键维的影响矩阵；利用裂分指标矩阵乘积态（split-index matrix-product-state）表示多时间关联结构。

Result: 发现了依赖于初始态（initial-state dependence）的丰富非平衡行为；给出了在局域非可积扰动下持存振荡动力学的解析结果；得到了满足守恒律约束的非热弛豫（non-thermal relaxation）的解析结果；对广泛初始态类获得了纠缠增长（entanglement growth）的数值精确结果；识别出隐藏马尔可夫序（hidden Markov order），即动力学编码的记忆可分解为有限长和长程分布两部分。

Conclusion: 该工作在一个单一解析可处理模型中实现了对非热化（nonthermalizing）和热化（thermalizing）非平衡动力学的统一研究，且可在Rydberg原子阵列等现代量子模拟器中进行实验检验。

Abstract: Studies of integrable systems have profoundly deepened the fundamental understanding of quantum many-body physics. While equilibrium properties such as ground states and thermodynamics can often be characterized efficiently, accurately characterizing nonequilibrium integrable dynamics remains a significant challenge. Here, we address this problem in the "Rule 201" quantum cellular automaton, an integrable Trotterization of the PXP Hamiltonian. Using the tensor-network approach of the influence matrix, we develop local conditions called generalized zipper conditions that allow exact solutions of local dynamics. We also introduce a numerical bootstrap method for solving influence matrices with finite but relatively large bond dimensions. This uncovers a rich landscape of nonequilibrium behavior exhibiting initial-state dependence. As an example, we investigate the fate of persistent oscillating dynamics under local non-integrable perturbations, and present analytical results for non-thermal relaxation constrained by conservation laws. We also obtain numerically exact results for entanglement growth across a broad class of initial states. Furthermore, from an information-theoretic perspective, we identify a refined structure of multitime correlations termed the hidden Markov order: the memory encoded in the dynamics separates into finite-length and long-range distributed components, which becomes transparent in an exact split-index matrix-product-state representation of the influence matrix. Our approach enables unified investigations of nonthermalizing and thermalizing regimes of nonequilibrium dynamics within a single analytically tractable model, and can be tested experimentally in state-of-the-art quantum simulators such as Rydberg atom arrays.

### [102] [Quantum deformations of $\mathcal{U}(\mathfrak{sl}(2, \mathbb{R}))$. Part I: Fidelity and experimental benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19462)
*V. Mariscal,J. J. Relancio,L. Santamaría-Sanz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了Hopf代数 $\mathcal{U}(\mathfrak{sl}(2, \mathbb{R}))$ 的标准量子 $q$-形变（$q$-deformation）与非标准 $h$-形变（$h$-deformation）对多量子比特系统的影响。通过变形代数的克莱布施-高尔登系数（Clebsch-Gordan coefficients）构造 $N$ 量子比特希尔伯特空间态，证明这些态自然与 $q$-和 $h$-形变的基特尔-肖尔模型（Kittel-Shore models）哈密顿量的本征态一致，并基于保真度（fidelity）计算分析了两种形变对量子关联的不同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子 $q$-形变与非标准 $h$-形变这两种Hopf代数变形对多量子比特系统的影响，并在代数构造与实验相关的量子资源之间建立桥梁。

Method: 利用变形代数的克莱布施-高尔登系数构造 $N$ 量子比特的希尔伯特空间态；将这些态与 $q$-和 $h$-形变的基特尔-肖尔模型哈密顿量的本征态进行对应；计算相对于未变形态的保真度，分析少量子比特系统（包括迪克态（Dicke states）与非迪克态（non-Dicke states））以及宏观极限（$N \to \infty$）下的量子关联变化；对任意迪克态推导出闭式公式。

Result: $q$-形变平滑地修改态，与原始构型保持残余交叠；$h$-形变则使态迅速正交于未变形对应态。两种模型均需标准的 $N^{-1}$ 重标度以在宏观极限下维持保真度稳定性。

Conclusion: 两种形变展现出不同的行为模式，但在宏观极限下均需 $N^{-1}$ 重标度来保证保真度稳定，为代数变形在量子信息实验中的应用提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This work explores the effects of both the standard quantum $q$-deformation and the non-standard $h$-deformation of the Hopf algebra $\mathcal{U}(\mathfrak{sl}(2, \mathbb{R}))$ on multi-qubit systems. By constructing the states of a Hilbert space of $N$ qubits through the Clebsch-Gordan coefficients associated with the deformed algebras, we show that these states naturally coincide with the eigenstates of the Hamiltonian of the $q$- and $h$-deformed Kittel-Shore models. We compare the resulting deformed states with those typically targeted in quantum information experiments, providing a bridge between algebraic constructions and experimentally relevant quantum resources. Fidelities with respect to the undeformed states are computed to establish how the quantum correlations are affected, both for few-qubit systems (including Dicke and non-Dicke states), and in the macroscopic limit ($N \to \infty$) through closed-form formulas derived for arbitrary Dicke states. The results reveal different behaviors between the two deformations. The $q$-deformation smoothly modifies the states and maintains a residual overlap with the original configurations, while the $h$-deformation rapidly makes the states orthogonal to their undeformed counterparts. Both models demand a standard $N^{-1}$ rescaling to preserve fidelity stability in the macroscopic limit.

</details>


### [103] [Quantum Dynamics from Lax Pair Theory: A Reconstruction from Spectrum Preservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19664)
*Péter Szabó*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从最小公理化基础出发，仅基于希尔伯特空间可观测量（Hilbert-space observables）和等谱演化（isospectral evolution）的假设，重建了酉量子动力学（unitary quantum dynamics），证明了海森堡方程、薛定谔方程、守恒律等标准结果可作为定理而非假说推导出来，其中哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）不是预设的，而是作为等谱可观测量流（isospectral observable flow）所需的生成元（generator）自然涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子力学公理体系中，动力学方程（如海森堡方程和薛定谔方程）通常被作为基本假说（postulates）直接引入。本文旨在探索能否以更精简、更基本的假设为基础，从数学上推导出这些标准动力学结构，从而揭示量子动力学的深层逻辑基础。

Method: 作者将物理时间演化（time evolution）定义为厄米可观测量（Hermitian observables）上的连续单参数流（continuous one-parameter flow），并唯一要求该流保持观测量的谱（spectra），即测量可能结果的集合不变。在此基础上，利用Lax对理论（Lax pair theory）作为数学桥梁，推导出量子力学的标准动力学方程。

Result: 研究表明，仅凭等谱演化假设便足以强制导出量子动力学的Lax形式（Lax form）。由此，海森堡方程、含时与不含时薛定谔方程、守恒律（conservation laws）以及好量子数（good quantum numbers）均可作为定理而非假说得到证明。哈密顿量并非预先假定，而是作为实现等谱可观测量流所需的生成元自然涌现。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，量子动力学的核心结构可以从更基础的测量结构（measurement structure）出发，通过Lax对理论这一数学工具得以重建，从而揭示了希尔伯特空间测量结构与标准量子演化之间缺失的动力学桥梁。这一公理化简化有助于更深入地理解量子力学的基本逻辑框架。

Abstract: We reconstruct unitary quantum dynamics from a minimal axiomatic foundation built on Hilbert-space observables and isospectral evolution. The only dynamical assumption is that physical time evolution is a continuous one-parameter flow of Hermitian observables that preserves their spectra, i.e. the possible outcomes of measurement. We show that this assumption is already sufficient to force the Lax form of quantum dynamics. The Heisenberg equation, the time-dependent and time-independent Schrödinger equations, conservation laws, and good quantum numbers then follow as theorems rather than postulates. In this formulation, Lax pair theory supplies the missing dynamical bridge between the measurement structure of a Hilbert space and standard quantum evolution: the Hamiltonian is not assumed, but emerges as the generator required for an isospectral observable flow.

</details>


### [104] [Optimal Shadow Estimation with Minimal Measurement Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20003)
*Zhiyao Yang,Datong Chen,Huangjun Zhu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明阴影估计（shadow estimation）中，最坏情况最优性需要Θ(d²)个测量基，而平均情况最优性仅需Θ(d)个测量基，揭示了二者之间的根本复杂性分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管3-设计（3-design）协议在最坏情况下达到最优性能，但实现这种最优性所需的最小测量基数量一直未明确，作者旨在解决这一理论空白。

Method: 通过理论证明Θ(d²)个测量基对最坏情况最优阴影估计既是必要的也是充分的，并构造了显式基族；同时证明任何态2-设计（state 2-design）足以实现平均情况最优性，并推导了Haar随机态的强集中性（strong concentration）。

Result: 最坏情况性能需要Θ(d²)个测量基，而平均情况性能仅需Θ(d)个测量基；平均情况下归一化可观测量的阴影均方范数（mean squared shadow norm）被一个普适常数界住，且一般纯态保真度估计的样本复杂度为常数。

Conclusion: 建立了最坏情况与平均情况阴影估计之间的基本复杂度分离，具有重要的量子信息理论意义，并可通过互不偏基（mutually unbiased bases）、循环测量或浅层对数深度电路等易于实现的2-设计方案，以极其简单的测量策略实现最优平均情况协议。

Abstract: Shadow estimation is a powerful framework for predicting quantum properties from randomized measurements. While $3$-design protocols achieve optimal worst-case performance, the minimal number of measurement bases required for such optimality has remained open. Here we prove that $Θ(d^2)$ measurement bases are both necessary and sufficient for worst-case optimal shadow estimation and construct an explicit basis family. In stark contrast, any state $2$-design already suffices for average-case optimality: the mean squared shadow norm of normalized observables is bounded by a universal constant, and we prove strong concentration for Haar-random states, yielding constant sample complexity for generic pure-state fidelity estimation. Easily implementable $2$-designs -- from mutually unbiased bases, cyclic measurements, or shallow $\mathcal{O}(\log n)$-depth circuits -- enable optimal average-case protocols with remarkably simple measurement strategies. Our results establish a fundamental complexity separation: worst-case estimation requires $Θ(d^2)$ bases, whereas average-case performance requires only $Θ(d)$ bases, with broad implications for quantum information theory and near-term experiments.

</details>


### [105] [String dynamics of a (2+1)D U(1) quantum link model on a digital quantum computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19601)
*Anthony Gandon,Alessandro Mariani,Debasish Banerjee,Emilie Huffman,Gurtej Kanwar,Francesco Tacchino,Uwe-Jens Wiese,Ivano Tavernelli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在IBM量子硬件上实现了(2+1)维U(1)纯规范理论的量子链模型（quantum link model），利用最多112个量子比特通过数字量子模拟（digital quantum simulation）研究弦的实时动力学，实验结果在短时间与张量网络（tensor network）计算一致，长时间与热平均一致，并在相变附近成功观测到大尺度弦涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: (2+1)维U(1)纯规范理论（pure gauge theory）始终处于禁闭相（confining phase），弦张力（string tension）为零的非零弦张力在静态荷之间产生特征线性势，使其成为检验研究禁闭规范理论弦动力学的量子计算方法的理想测试平台。

Method: 将U(1)量子链模型（quantum link model）在量子计算机上实现，用量子比特自由度表示模型的对偶高度变量（dual height variables），从而高效实现面元相互作用（plaquette interactions）；采用定制晶格几何以匹配IBM量子硬件的重六边形（heavy-hexagonal）结构，最小化非相邻量子比特交互；通过对简单初始弦态进行量子淬火（quantum quench）探测弦的横向量子涨落。

Result: 数字量子模拟实验最多使用112个量子比特，短时间结果与参考张量网络计算吻合良好，长时间结果与热平均一致；相变附近淬火动力学中初始弦呈现跨越两个空间维度的涨落；误差缓解（error-mitigated）估计器在该区域仍给出准确预测，噪声导致的局域规范对称性（local gauge symmetries）破坏程度与有限键维数张量网络结果相当。

Conclusion: 基于量子链模型和对偶高度变量的量子计算方案能够有效模拟禁闭规范理论的弦实时动力学，在相变附近的大涨落区域依然保持准确性，为现有量子硬件超越传统量子蒙特卡洛方法（quantum Monte Carlo）研究实时弦动力学提供了可行的实验路径。

Abstract: The (2+1)D U(1) pure gauge theory always exists in the confining phase, with strings of non-zero string tension giving a characteristic linear potential between static charges. This makes it a useful testing ground for quantum computing methods designed to study string dynamics of confining gauge theories. Here we implement a minimal U(1) quantum link model on a quantum computer with qubit degrees of freedom representing the dual height variables of the model. This facilitates an efficient realization of plaquette interactions and enables effective calculations of real-time dynamics that are inaccessible to traditional quantum Monte Carlo. A specifically tailored lattice geometry is chosen to match the heavy-hexagonal geometry of the IBM quantum hardware used here, minimizing non-adjacent qubit interactions. By performing quantum quenches from a simple initial string state, we probe the transverse quantum fluctuations of the string before it thermalizes. Our experimental results from digital quantum simulations, with up to 112 qubits, show good agreement with reference tensor-network calculations at short times and with thermal averages at long times. Near the phase transition, the quench dynamics exhibit large fluctuations of the initial string that extend across both spatial dimensions of the lattice. Nonetheless, our error-mitigated estimators from the quantum hardware also give accurate predictions in that regime, with noise-induced violations of local gauge symmetries comparable to finite-bond-dimension tensor-network results.

</details>


### [106] [Many-body chirality of topological stabilizer states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20472)
*Tyler D. Ellison,Dongjin Lee,Zhi Li,Amin Moharramipour,Yasamin Panahi,Beni Yoshida*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出多体手性（many-body chirality）的量子信息表征：系统与其复共轭态之间无法通过有限深度局域操作相互转化。针对 $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ 任意子（anyon）理论的稳定子实现，严格证明了这种阻挫的存在性，并展示了超越传统诊断（如手征中心荷、模数对易子）的手性形式，以及固有的多体虚数性（many-body imaginarity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管手性（chirality）在实验和理论上已被广泛研究，但基于多体量子态纠缠结构（entanglement structure）的量子信息论表征尚未建立。该工作旨在填补这一空白，从纠缠与局域操作的角度定义多体手性。

Method: 将多体手性定义为量子态无法通过有限深度局域操作（finite-depth local operations）转化为其复共轭态（complex conjugate）的阻挫。针对 $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ 任意子理论的稳定子（stabilizer）实现进行严格分析，并检验其与模数对易子（modular commutator）、手征中心荷（chiral central charge）等传统诊断的关系。

Result: 证明复共轭可由局域量子信道实现当且仅当底层任意子数据是镜像不变的（mirror invariant）；发现了一种传统诊断无法检测的手性形式；证明了该阻挫本质上是四体（four-partite）的，而三体纠缠结构不可见；对于 $d>2$ 的 $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ 态，证明了其具有固有的多体虚数性，且包含了非多体手性的态。

Conclusion: 多体手性可作为量子信息论概念被严格定义，揭示了超越传统物理诊断的新颖手性形式，且与多体虚数性存在部分重叠但不等价的关系。

Abstract: A defining feature of chirality is the distinction between a system and its mirror image. Despite extensive experimental observations of chiral phases and theoretical advances, a quantum-information theoretic characterization of chirality based solely on the entanglement structure of many-body quantum states remains elusive. Here, we introduce the notion of many-body chirality by formulating it as an obstruction to transforming a quantum state into its complex conjugate through finite-depth local operations. We rigorously establish many-body chirality for stabilizer realizations of $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ anyon theories, proving that complex conjugation can be implemented by local quantum channels if and only if the underlying anyon data are mirror invariant. This reveals forms of chirality that evade conventional diagnostics, including examples with vanishing modular commutator, vanishing chiral central charge, and commuting-projector realizations. We further show that this obstruction is intrinsically four-partite, while invisible to tripartite entanglement structure. Finally, we prove that $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ states with $d>2$ possess intrinsic many-body imaginarity: their complex phase structure cannot be removed by finite-depth local unitaries. Remarkably, this includes states that are not many-body chiral.

### [107] [Quantum circuit decomposition of the tangent-fermion Dirac operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19020)
*C. W. J. Beenakker*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明切向费米子离散化（tangent-fermion discretization）能够规避格点狄拉克算符的费米子加倍（fermion doubling）问题，通过将狄拉克方程重写为局部算子束（local operator pencil）的广义本征值问题，实现与格点大小无关的线性组合幺正算符（LCU）表示，为量子算法提供高效的块编码（block-encoding）原语。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格点上的狄拉克算符（Dirac operator）无法同时满足局域性（locality）和无费米子加倍（fermion doubling），除非破坏基本对称性。避免加倍的非局域、保持对称的离散化方案在量子电路中以线性组合幺正算符（linear-combination-of-unitaries, LCU）形式表示时，其项数和范数（次归一化因子）均随格点大小增长，损害了量子算法的效率。

Method: 将狄拉克方程重写为一个广义本征值问题（generalized eigenvalue problem），采用局部算子束（local operator pencil）的形式。该算子束中的每个成员都具有精确的LCU表示，其项数与格点大小无关，且次归一化因子（subnormalization factor）量级为1，与椭圆算子（elliptic operators）相当。

Result: 切向费米子离散化（tangent-fermion discretization）逃脱了前述障碍，实现了与格点大小无关的LCU项数以及量级为1的次归一化因子，从而提供了一种高效的块编码（block-encoding）原语。

Conclusion: 该方案为无费米子加倍的狄拉克谱（Dirac spectra）和格林函数（Green functions）提供了高效的块编码原语，有望提升相关量子算法的效率。

Abstract: The Dirac operator on a lattice cannot be both local and free of fermion doubling, at least not without breaking fundamental symmetries. Non-local, symmetry-preserving discretizations that avoid doubling have a quantum circuit representation as a linear-combination-of-unitaries (LCU) in which both the number of terms and their norm (the subnormalization factor) grow with the lattice size, compromising the efficiency of a quantum algorithm. We show that the tangent-fermion discretization escapes this obstruction when the Dirac equation is written as a generalized eigenvalue problem with a local operator pencil: Each member of the pencil has an exact LCU, with term count that is independent of lattice size and with subnormalization factor of order unity, on a par with elliptic operators. This provides an efficient block-encoding primitive for Dirac spectra and Green functions without fermion doubling.

### [108] [Nonequilibrium steady states induced by stochastic mid-circuit measurements and resets on a quantum computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19027)
*Jakob Murauer,Sabine Tornow,Gabriele Perfetto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过在超导量子处理器上实现含噪离散时间随机重置（stochastic resetting）协议，首次从实验上验证了量子多体系统在随机测量和条件重置驱动下可以达到非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady states），并展示了该稳态与弗洛凯横场伊辛模型（Floquet transverse-field Ising model）量子相变相关的交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置已被理论证明是一种驱动量子多体系统达到非平衡稳态的有效协议，但缺乏量子硬件上的实验验证。该工作旨在填补这一空白，提供首个实验层面的确认。

Method: 首先构建了一个含噪离散时间理论框架，其中酉门（unitary gates）与含噪的中电路投影测量（mid-circuit projective measurements）及条件重置交替进行。随后在超导量子处理器上对最多N=7个量子比特执行该协议，并以相互作用的弗洛凯横场伊辛模型作为酉动力学的代表性案例。

Result: 理论预测的含噪条件重置稳态与实验观测在定量上吻合。该稳态表现出与模型平衡量子相变（equilibrium quantum phase transition）相关的交叉行为（crossover behavior）。

Conclusion: 本研究为在含噪量子器件上制备集体稳态铺平了道路，并可能推动涉及中电路测量的量子算法的进一步发展。

Abstract: Stochastic resetting has emerged as a versatile protocol to drive quantum many-body systems to non-equilibrium steady states by interspersing unitary dynamics with measurements and resets at random times. In spite of this, a quantum hardware validation of such non-equilibrium steady states is still missing. Here, we achieve this goal by first formulating a noisy discrete-time theory where unitary gates alternate with noisy mid-circuit projective measurements and conditional resets. This noisy conditional resetting theory is then demonstrated on a superconducting quantum processor for up to $N=7$ qubits. We consider, as a paradigmatic case, the unitary dynamics of the interacting Floquet transverse-field Ising model. The stationary state of the noisy conditional resetting agrees quantitatively with the experiments, and it shows crossover behavior related to the equilibrium quantum phase transition of the model. Our results might thus pave the way for the preparation of collective stationary states on noisy quantum devices and for further developments of quantum algorithms involving mid-circuit measurements.

### [109] [Random Local Stabilizer Codes in Three Dimensions without String or Self-Similar Fractal Logical Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19873)
*Han Yan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种名为“qutrit随机立方码”（qutrit random cubic codes）的局部qutrit CSS稳定子哈密顿量族，通过空间变化的稳定子构造打破了平移不变性，证明了其不存在弦逻辑算子（no-string property），并通过数值观察发现其基态简并指数、非收缩平面逻辑算子和电荷推进诊断等性质均与平移不变的fracton码不同，表明约束随机性能够从根本上改变稳定子码的性质并改善自校正性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错码（quantum error-correcting codes, QECs）是被动自校正量子计算的关键组件，但弦逻辑算子（string logical operators）的存在会导致恒定能量势垒的误码过程，阻碍自校正能力的实现。Haah码（fracton码）虽能禁止弦逻辑算子，但其平移不变结构仍支持具有对数能量势垒的自相似分形逻辑算子（self-similar fractal logical operators），因此需要探索新的构造方法以进一步提升自校正性能。

Method: 构造了一族名为“qutrit随机立方码”的局部qutrit Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）稳定子哈密顿量，其具有与Haah Code 1类似的立方体检验（cube-check）结构，但稳定子（stabilizers）在空间上随机变化，从而打破了平移不变性（translation-invariant structure）。

Result: 理论上证明了这些模型保留了无弦性质（no-string property）；数值上观察到三个关键性质：对于奇偶边长L，最小基态简并指数（ground-state degeneracy exponent）分别为k=2（奇数L）和k=4（偶数L）；非收缩平面逻辑算子（noncontractible plane-logical operators）张满整个逻辑空间；电荷推进诊断（charge-push diagnostics）显示自相似分形算子不存在。

Conclusion: 结果表明，约束随机性（constrained randomness）能够从根本上改变稳定子码的性质并改善其自校正性能，同时指向了超出经典拓扑序（topological order）和fracton序的更广泛的量子纠错码与量子相家族。

Abstract: Quantum error-correcting codes (QECs) are essential components quantum computation and have deep connections to quantum phases of matter. A key obstruction to passive self-correcting QECs is the presence of string logical operators, which can generate logical errors through constant-energy-barrier processes. Haah's Codes (fracton codes) showed that three-dimensional stabilizer codes can forbid such string logical operators, but their translation-invariant structure supports self-similar fractal logical operators with a logarithmic energy barrier. We introduce the qutrit random cubic codes, a family of local qutrit Calderbank-Shor-Steane stabilizer Hamiltonians with similar cube-check structure as Haah's Code 1 but built from spatially varying stabilizers. We prove that these models retain the no-string property and numerically observe that they have properties distinct from translation-invariant fracton codes: the smallest ground-state degeneracy exponent is $k=2$ for odd $L$ and $k=4$ for even $L$; noncontractible plane-logical operators span the entire logical space; and charge-push diagnostics show that the self-similar fractal operators are absent. These results demonstrate that constrained randomness can fundamentally change the nature of stabilizer codes and improve their self-correction properties. They further point to broader families of quantum error-correcting codes and quantum phases beyond canonical topological and fracton orders.

### [110] [Optimizing resource allocation for accuracy in noisy variational quantum algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20153)
*Harshit Verma,Thomas Ayral,Alexia Auffèves,Robert Whitney*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对含噪中等规模量子（Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum, NISQ）算法，发展了一种噪声-度量-资源方法论，通过模拟变分量子本征求解器（Variational Quantum Eigensolver, VQE）构建现象学模型，在电路规模与迭代次数之间寻找最优平衡点，以最小化实现给定算法精度的资源成本（即总量子门操作数）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为实现量子算法的全部潜力，需要优化方法以在最小资源成本下达到目标输出精度；当前缺乏针对NISQ算法中算法精度、资源成本与硬件噪声之间复杂关系的系统建模与优化框架。

Method: 利用VQE模拟构建现象学模型，以总量子门操作数作为算法资源成本度量，考虑量子电路规模（小电路不精确，大电路噪声高）与电路迭代次数之间的微妙权衡，采用噪声-度量-资源方法论识别最优电路规模与迭代次数组合。

Result: 该方法能够找到在给定目标精度下最小化资源成本的“最佳点”（电路规模与迭代次数的平衡点），同时也能给出在固定资源成本下最大化算法精度的电路规模。

Conclusion: 该研究为在含噪真实硬件（包括使用误差缓解（error mitigation）的硬件）上近期部署变分算法提供了实用指导原则。

Abstract: For quantum algorithms to achieve their full potential, we need methodologies to optimize them, such as reaching a given output accuracy with minimal resource costs. Here, we develop such a methodology for a class of Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) algorithms. We leverage simulations of a Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) to propose a phenomenological model of such algorithms that captures the complex relationship between algorithmic accuracy, algorithmic resource costs, and the noise that exists in realistic quantum hardware. For this, we take the algorithmic resource cost to be the total number of quantum gate-operations in the algorithm; minimizing this cost typically makes the algorithm faster and more energy-efficient. We consider the subtle trade-off between quantum circuit size (small circuits are too imprecise, but large ones are too noisy), and the number of iterations of that quantum circuit for the full algorithm to sufficiently converge. Using a noise-metric-resource methodology, we identify the sweet spot (of circuit size versus iterations) that minimizes the algorithmic resource costs for a desired algorithm accuracy. It also gives the circuit size that maximizes algorithm accuracy for a fixed resource cost. Our methodology provides a practical guideline for near-term deployment of variational algorithms on realistic noisy hardware, including hardware that uses error mitigation.

### [111] [Vine Codes: Low-Overhead Quantum LDPC Codes on a Planar Square Grid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20263)
*Georgia M. Nixon,Campbell K. McLauchlan,Charles C. L. van Rest*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“Vine Codes”——一种可在超导平面方栅格上通过最近邻两量子比特门实现的新型量子低密度奇偶校验（qLDPC）码。与表面码相比，Vine Codes 在电路距离7时可将数据与测量量子比特减少约28%，在距离10时总量子比特数减少约18%，且在近端噪声率（10⁻³）下性能更优。此外，本文引入“Flip-Vine Codes”，支持单量子比特横向克利福德门，并系统列举了所有稳定子权重不超过9的Vine Codes。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面码（surface code）虽然适合超导硬件，但量子比特（qubit）开销巨大；而新型量子低密度奇偶校验（qLDPC）码虽能降低开销，却需要难以在超导平台实现的长程连接。本文旨在设计一种兼具表面码硬件友好性与qLDPC码低开销优势的纠错码方案。

Method: Vine Codes 推广了Gehér等人（2025）提出的“Directional Codes”，将原本局限于环面（torus）的构造扩展至具有开放边界条件（open boundary conditions）的平面方栅格，通过引入路由量子比特（routing qubits）实现。本文通过大规模数值搜索寻找候选码，并采用电路级噪声模拟（circuit-level noise simulations）进行性能评估。

Result: 找到了多个候选Vine Codes，如[[121,4,6]]、[[221,6,7]]和[[234,9,6]]码。在电路距离（circuit distance）为7时，数据与测量量子比特减少约28%；即使计入路由量子比特，在电路距离10时总量子比特数仍比表面码减少约18%，且高距离下优势更显著。在10⁻³噪声率下，Vine Codes以更少量子比特实现优于表面码的性能。本文还给出了稳定子权重（stabiliser weight）不超过9的所有唯一Vine Codes的完整列表。

Conclusion: Vine Codes 在超导硬件平台上实现了qLDPC码的低开销优势，为大规模量子计算提供了一条可行路径。此外，“Flip-Vine Codes”具备单量子比特横向克利福德门（transversal Clifford gates），有利于容错逻辑门操作和魔法态培养（magic state cultivation）。广义开放边界的构造进一步拓展了边界条件的灵活性，超越了表面码和tile码常见的X/Z边界。

Abstract: The surface code is a promising route towards large-scale quantum computing, requiring only nearest-neighbour gates amenable to superconducting hardware. However, surface codes incur large qubit overheads. Novel quantum low-density parity check (qLDPC) codes promise to reduce overheads but require long-range connections that are difficult to achieve on superconducting platforms. Here, we introduce "Vine Codes" - qLDPC codes that are implementable on a planar square grid through nearest-neighbour, two-qubit gates native to superconducting platforms (iSWAP and CZ). Our approach generalises "Directional Codes" recently introduced by Gehér et. al. (2025) which are constrained to a torus. In contrast, vine codes have open boundary conditions constructed with the aid of routing qubits. We perform extensive numeric searches and find promising candidate vine codes, e.g. [[121,4,6]], [[221,6,7]], and [[234,9,6]] codes. We verify the circuit distances and show that data and measure qubits required can be reduced by up to ~28% relative to the surface code at a circuit distance of 7. Even including routing qubits, vine codes require fewer total qubits than the surface code (e.g. ~18% reduction at circuit distance 10) and benefits are expected to increase at higher distances. We perform circuit-level noise simulations to demonstrate that under a realistic noise model and at a near-term noise rate of $10^{-3}$, vine codes can perform better than the surface code while using fewer qubits. We give an exhaustive list of all unique vine codes up to stabiliser-weight 9. We additionally introduce "Flip-Vine Codes" which possess single-qubit transversal Clifford gates useful for fault-tolerant logic and magic state cultivation. We furthermore construct examples of generalised open boundaries for vine codes that go beyond the familiar X/Z boundaries of the surface and tile codes.

</details>


### [112] [Extracting the physical content of Liouvillian eigenmodes: Semiclassical quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20271)
*Ashlin V Thomas,Felix Fritzsch,Masudul Haque,Shovan Dutta*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为开放量子系统（open quantum systems）引入一种基于准概率（quasiprobability）的相干性度量，将Liouvillian本征模（Liouville eigenmode）解释为一组相干性（coherences）。利用该度量发现，在多种线性和非线性阻尼下，振子（oscillator）在相空间（phase space）中仍保持量子化的"轨道"（orbits），从而为开放系统提供了半经典量子化（semiclassical quantization）的表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在封闭量子系统中，单个能量本征态（energy eigenstate）可理解为物理激发，但开放量子系统的Liouvillian具有不同的右本征态（right eigenstates）和左本征态（left eigenstates），它们随时间衰减且难以解释。作者希望提出一种有物理动机的度量来弥合这一理解上的鸿沟。

Method: 引入一种将两类本征态结合的准概率度量（quasiprobability measure），将Liouvillian本征模解释为一组相干性。该相干性度量与返回概率（return probability）紧密关联，并允许在"双重"相空间（"doubled" phase space）中将模可视化为准概率分布。

Result: 对于一大类线性和非线性阻尼（linear and nonlinear damping），振子在相空间中仍保持量子化的"轨道"，从而为开放系统提供了半经典量子化的表述。这些轨道具有可测量的动力学特征，在热浴（thermal bath）存在时会像能级一样被展宽。

Conclusion: 对于二次系统（quadratic systems），该结果将哈密顿系统中起核心作用的不变环（invariant tori）概念进行了推广。

Abstract: Unlike in closed quantum systems where individual energy eigenstates are understood as physical excitations, open quantum systems have distinct right and left eigenstates of the Liouvillian that decay with time and are difficult to interpret. Here we introduce a physically motivated quasiprobability measure combining the two types of eigenstates that interprets a Liouville eigenmode as a set of coherences. This coherence measure is intimately connected to the return probability and allows one to visualize the modes as quasiprobability distributions in a "doubled" phase space. Using this measure we show that, remarkably, an oscillator retains its quantized "orbits" in phase space for a large class of linear and nonlinear damping, thus providing a formulation of semiclassical quantization for open systems. The orbits have measurable dynamical signatures and are broadened in the presence of a thermal bath, similar to energy levels. For quadratic systems, our results yield an extension of the concept of invariant tori, which play a central role in Hamiltonian systems.

</details>


### [113] [Proposal of quantum arrival-time measurement with a Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20278)
*Pascal Naidon,Lucas Happ,Denis Boiron*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用超冷原子的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）设计一套现实的实验方案，通过测量探测器上的到达通量（arrival flux）而非直接测量到达时间，来区分不同的到达时间理论预言，从而解决量子理论中关于粒子到达探测器所需时间的长期争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子理论中长期存在一个基础性问题：粒子到达探测器需要多长时间？目前存在多种理论预测，但缺乏能够明确区分这些预测的实验手段。

Method: 提出基于超冷原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate of ultracold atoms）的现实实验方案。核心创新在于不直接测量粒子的到达时间（arrival time），而是测量到达通量（arrival flux）随探测器位置的变化函数。

Result: 该方案解决了将探测器置于系统附近所带来的实际困难，同时产生的信号能够明确区分不同的理论预测。

Conclusion: 该实验方案有望为解决量子理论中这一基础性问题的数十年争论提供前景。

Abstract: This work shows how a Bose-Einstein condensate of ultracold atoms could be used to address a long-standing question in quantum theory: how much time does it take for a particle to reach a detector? To this end, we propose a realistic experimental setup, whose key idea is not to measure arrival times directly, but the arrival flux on the detector as a function of its position. This novel approach not only solves practical issues with having a detector close to the system, but also results in signals that allow to unambiguously distinguish different theoretical predictions. This proposal raises prospects for resolving the decades-old debate on this fundamental issue.

### [114] [Phase locking nuclear spins in silicon with spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20340)
*Habitamu Y. Walelign,Manas Ranjan Sahu,John M. Nichol*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用量子点（quantum dot）中电子的自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）作为内部相位参考，实现了对$^{29}$Si核自旋系综（nuclear spin ensemble）的相位锁定（phase-locking），无需外部微波控制场，从而测量了核自旋的相干进动（coherent precession）和非均匀退相干（inhomogeneous dephasing），并通过多体数值模拟验证了实验结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核自旋（nuclear spins）具有极长的相干时间（coherence times），在量子信息处理（quantum information processing）中潜力巨大，但其相干控制通常依赖外部相位参考（如微波控制场）。本文旨在探索仅利用内部电子自旋-轨道耦合作为相位参考，实现对核自旋系综的相干控制。

Method: 在硅量子点（silicon quantum dot）中对$^{29}$Si核自旋系综施加量子点电子驱动，利用内部电子自旋-轨道耦合（electronic spin-orbit coupling）作为相位参考，使核自旋根据驱动协议的时序和自旋-轨道耦合相位进行自对齐（self-align），实现相位锁定（phase-locking）。同时结合多体电子-核系统的详细数值模拟（numerical simulations）进行验证。

Result: 通过上述方法成功实现了核自旋的相位锁定，并测量了核自旋的相干进动（coherent precession）和非均匀退相干（inhomogeneous dephasing）。数值模拟结果与实验观测相吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作开辟了无需外部微波场即可对固态核自旋系综（solid-state nuclear spin ensembles）进行相干控制的新途径。

Abstract: Because they have such long coherence times, nuclear spins have extraordinary potential for use in quantum information processing devices. However, coherent nuclear spin control generally requires external phase references, such as microwave control fields. Here, we phase-lock a $^{29}$Si nuclear spin ensemble in a silicon quantum dot using only the internal electronic spin-orbit coupling as a phase reference. When driven with the quantum-dot electrons, the nuclear spins align themselves to a phase determined by the electronic spin-orbit coupling and the timing of the drive protocol. This enables us to measure the coherent precession and inhomogeneous dephasing of the nuclear spins. We corroborate our results with detailed numerical simulations of the many-body electron nuclear system. Our work opens new routes for coherently controlling solid-state nuclear spin ensembles.

### [115] [Interaction geometry and ground-state properties of sparse quantum lattice models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20387)
*Alex Gunning,Sebastian Schmid,Zhengxiao Liu,Sridevi Kuriyattil,Aydin Deger,Andrew J. Daley*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究稀疏可调长程量子模型中相互作用几何如何影响低能相，重点分析连接度随系统大小对数增长的图类，揭示了对称性与几何阻挫在驱动、抑制和重塑基态相变中的作用，并通过幂次图（power-of-p graphs）和斐波那契图（Fibonacci graphs）等实例建立了统一的有效几何原理（effective-geometry principle）框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解相互作用几何（interaction geometry）如何塑造稀疏可调长程量子模型的低能相结构，尤其是图连接性中的对称性（symmetry）与几何阻挫（geometric frustration）对基态相变（ground-state phase transitions）的影响机制。

Method: 聚焦于连接度随系统大小对数增长的一类图，以幂次图（power-of-p graphs）和斐波那契图（Fibonacci graphs）为核心示例进行对比分析：幂次图中偶数和奇数p值表现出截然不同的行为，斐波那契图则缺乏离散自相似性但具有短程与长程极限间的直接几何映射。

Result: 偶数p的幂次图继承了幂次二模型（power-of-two model）丰富的相结构，而奇数p的幂次图受几何阻挫主导；斐波那契图提供了不同的相变行为案例。

Conclusion: 所有模型中的相结构与临界性（criticality）均受同一有效几何原理的支配，为实验上可实现的（experimentally motivated）长程量子系统建立了统一的框架。

Abstract: We investigate how interaction geometry shapes the low-energy phases of sparse tunable long-range quantum models. We focus on a class of graphs whose degree grows logarithmically with system size, and show how symmetry and frustration in graph connectivity can drive, suppress, and reshape ground-state phase transitions. The central examples are power-of-$p$ graphs, where even and odd values of $p$ exhibit qualitatively distinct behaviour: even-$p$ graphs inherit the rich phase structure of the power-of-two model, while odd-$p$ graphs are governed by geometric frustration. Fibonacci graphs provide a contrasting case, lacking the discrete self-similarity of the power-of-$p$ family but exhibiting a direct geometric mapping between the short- and long-range limits. Across our models, we find that phase structure and criticality are governed by the same effective-geometry principle, unifying our framework for experimentally motivated long-range quantum systems.
