### [116] [Topological Codes Based on Space Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20548)
*Chong-Yuan Xu,Ze-Chuan Liu,Yong Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一类称为空间群码（space-group codes）的CSS码，通过将点群操作（point-group operations）与平移操作相结合来构造拓扑码（topological codes），并利用环模（ring-modules）及其不变量理论（invariant theory）分析其拓扑性质。这类码在保持拓扑性的同时展现出更强的局域性（locality），为拓扑码与量子计算平台的协同设计提供了更广阔的设计空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拓扑码的代数构造和分析大多假设平移不变性（translation invariance），这限制了拓扑码的设计空间。作者试图通过在构造中引入点群操作（point-group operations），探索更一般化条件下的拓扑码存在性。

Method: 提出一类基于空间群（space groups）的Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）码，即空间群码（space-group codes）。其校验算子（check operators）由空间群上的群代数模板（group-algebra templates）构建，同时包含平移与点群操作。采用环模（ring-modules）及其不变量理论（invariant theory）分析这类码的拓扑性质。

Result: 空间群码在理论上看似会增加实际实现的复杂性，但研究发现它们比纯粹基于平移的已有码具有更强的局域性（greater locality）。

Conclusion: 该框架扩展了拓扑码的设计景观，为拓扑码与量子计算平台的协同设计（co-design）开辟了更广泛的设计空间。

Abstract: Topological codes form one of the most important classes of stabilizer codes. Most existing algebraic constructions and analyses of topological codes assume translation invariance. Here we show that topological codes can arise in more general settings by incorporating point group operations. The central construction is a class of Calderbank-Shor-Steane (CSS) codes called space-group codes, whose check operators are built from group-algebra templates over space groups that combine translations with point-group operations. We develop methods for analyzing topological properties of space-group codes using ring-modules and their invariant theory. At first glance, space-group codes might appear to complicate practical implementation; however, we find that they can exhibit greater locality than previous codes based purely on translations. Our framework thus extends the landscape of topological codes and opens up a broader design space for the co-design of topological codes with quantum computing platforms.

### [117] [Trace anomaly and interior curvature of neutron stars in energy-momentum squared gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20203)
*Ratikanta Swain,Sayantan Ghosh,Bharat Kumar*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文研究能量-动量平方引力（EMSG）中中子星内部的迹反常（trace anomaly）能否像在广义相对论（GR）中一样组织内部结构和曲率。采用物质-几何明确分离的方法，发现EMSG模型中迹反常的径向分布仍单调递增，曲率不变量与迹反常之间也存在有组织的对应关系，但分布随EMSG耦合强度和致密度系统性地分裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在能量-动量平方引力（energy-momentum squared gravity, EMSG）中，中子星内部的时空由有效热力学变量源产生，这些变量不必与物理流体压强和能量密度一致。因此，尚不清楚致密物质的迹反常——量子色动力学（QCD）中衡量共形对称性破缺程度的量——是否仍能像在广义相对论（general relativity, GR）中一样组织内部剖面和曲率。

Method: 采用明确的物质-几何分离方案：迹反常仅从流体部分计算，而时空曲率标量则从实际源产生修正Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程的变量构造。使用五种相对论平均场物态方程（equation of state, EOS）进行计算。

Result: 在所有可接受的EMSG模型中，径向迹反常剖面从星核到表面单调递增，与GR一致，但随EMSG耦合强度系统性地分裂，且分裂程度随恒星致密度的增加而增大。曲率不变量（curvature invariants）与迹反常作图时仍呈现有组织的带状分布，其中里奇收缩（Ricci contraction）的组织最紧密，而里奇标量（Ricci scalar）对物态方程的敏感性最高。EMSG效应在可观测星体中较小，但在刚性、超致密构型中最大。

Conclusion: 即使在引力与物质非线性耦合的情况下，迹反常仍可作为描述内部几何结构的有用热力学标签。

Abstract: In energy-momentum squared gravity (EMSG), the spacetime inside a neutron star is sourced by effective thermodynamic variables that need not coincide with the physical fluid pressure and energy density. It is therefore an open question whether the trace anomaly of dense matter -- the QCD measure of how strongly conformal symmetry is broken -- still organizes interior profiles and curvature in the same way it does in general relativity (GR). We adopt a clear matter-geometry separation: the trace anomaly is computed from the fluid sector alone, while spacetime curvature scalars are built from the variables that actually source the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations. For five relativistic mean-field equations of state, the radial trace-anomaly profiles increase monotonically from core to surface in all accepted EMSG models, as in GR, but split systematically with the EMSG coupling strength; the splitting grows with stellar compactness. Despite this deformation, curvature invariants still fall onto organized bands when plotted against the trace anomaly, extending the GR thermodynamic-geometric correspondence. The Ricci contraction shows the tightest organization, whereas the Ricci scalar remains the most equation-of-state sensitive. EMSG effects are modest for observationally accessible stars but largest in stiff, ultracompact configurations, indicating that the trace anomaly remains a useful thermodynamic label for interior geometry even when gravity couples nonlinearly to matter.

Abstract: We present a study of charge sharing and electronic cross-talk in second-generation Large-Area Picosecond Photodetectors (LAPPD Gen 2). The LAPPD is a vacuum-based device consisting of a photocathode, two microchannel plates, and a resistive anode that capacitively couples to an 8 $\times$ 8 pixelated readout board (25.4 mm $\times$ 25.4 mm pixel area). Using a picosecond pulsed laser, we measure signal distributions across the resistive anode and quantify coupling between target and neighboring pixels. We further examine the relationship between dark-count rate and LAPPD voltage settings, identifying decay behavior characterized by fast, intermediate, and slow relaxation timescales. We additionally observe the LAPPD behaving as a resonant cavity by injecting electrical pulses into the readout board. To further interpret observed signals, we develop a pulse-classification method and identify additional features at approximately 60 ns and 110 ns. Finally, we implement a first-principles Monte Carlo simulation to model the radial and temporal distributions of observed signals, including contributions from electron backscatter and potential ion afterpulsing. The simulation shows reasonable agreement with the experimentally derived pulse classifications.

### [119] [Interpretable Meta-Learning for Multi-Objective Chemical Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20497)
*Antonio Varagnolo,Yulia Pimonova,Michael G. Taylor,Raphaël Pestourie,Nicholas E. Lubbers*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合可解释线性元学习（linear meta-learning）与自适应置信度不确定性量化（adaptive-confidence uncertainty quantification）的模块化流水线，并将其嵌入高效全局优化（EGO）框架中，用于多目标分子发现。实验表明，该方法在自旋交叉金属-有机配合物的帕累托搜索中比基线性能提升78%，且动态置信度调优进一步优于静态校准结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出模块化流水线，结合可解释线性元学习模型与自适应置信度不确定性量化，集成到高效全局优化（Efficient Global Optimization, EGO）框架中，用于多目标分子发现。线性元学习首次被部署在多目标化学搜索场景中：通过跨化学目标和廉价辅助属性进行训练，元学习替代模型获得可迁移的化学知识，能够从有限数据中快速适应新目标。此外，引入自适应置信度调优算法（adaptive confidence-tuning algorithm），随分子搜索动态重新校准探索-利用（exploration-exploitation）权衡。

Result: 在自旋交叉（spin-crossover）金属-有机配合物的大规模真实搜索中，基线的帕累托性能比元学习替代方案差78%。动态置信度调优进一步在超过50%的静态校准前沿上占据优势。

Conclusion: 线性元学习在多目标化学搜索中具有显著优势，动态置信度调优有效解决了主动搜索中标准不确定性估计在校准方面的挑战，提升了分子发现的效率与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Navigating the vast space of synthetically accessible molecules demands surrogate models that are interpretable and capable of handling multiple competing objectives at the same time. Deep learning approaches struggle to satisfy them under the computational constraints of quantum-level chemistry. Here, we introduce a modular pipeline that combines interpretable linear meta-learning models and adaptive-confidence uncertainty quantification into an Efficient Global Optimization (EGO) framework for multi-objective molecular discovery. For the first time, linear meta-learning is deployed in a multi-objective chemical search setting: by training across chemical objectives and cheap auxiliary properties, the meta-learned surrogates acquire transferable chemical knowledge that adapts rapidly to new objectives from limited data. Evaluated empirically on a real large scale search for spin-crossover metal-organic complexes, the baseline performs 78% worse in Pareto sense than the meta-learning alternative. We also address the calibration challenges inherent to active search. Since optimal candidates typically lie precisely in the distributional tails, standard uncertainty estimates fail. We introduce an adaptive confidence-tuning algorithm that dynamically recalibrates the exploration-exploitation trade-off as the molecular search evolves. Empirically, dynamic confidence tuning further dominates over 50% of the statically calibrated front.

### [120] [Statistical Field Theory for Weak Gravitational Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19472)
*Zheng Zhang,Philip Bull,Chris Clarkson,Andrina Nicola*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文将弱引力透镜（weak gravitational lensing）重新表述为一种随机场理论（stochastic field theory），基于Sachs光学标量（Sachs optical scalars）由随机Ricci聚焦（Ricci-focusing）和Weyl剪切（Weyl-shearing）场驱动。通过路径积分（path integral）生成透镜观测量的n点关联函数（n-point correlation functions）的图展开，传统计算作为最低阶线性传播极限出现。非线性Sachs演化（nonlinear Sachs evolution）与驱动场非高斯性（driving-field non-Gaussianity）耦合，产生层级混合（hierarchy mixing），并由一个选择规则（selection rule）控制耦合结构。该形式论并非近似方案，而是统一框架的范式转换（paradigm shift）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准弱透镜计算将透镜效应视为物质场沿视线方向的线性重映射，忽略了非线性Sachs演化与驱动场非高斯性之间的耦合效应。现有方法无法自然纳入高阶物质统计、随机性及小尺度效应，亟需一个更统一的理论框架。

Method: 将弱透镜效应重新表述为一种随机场理论，其Sachs光学标量由随机Ricci聚焦场和Weyl剪切场驱动。利用路径积分生成透镜观测量的任意n点关联函数的图展开，将其组织为线性响应、非线性传播和驱动场累积量（driving-field cumulants）三个部分。

Result: 传统计算作为最低阶线性传播极限出现。非线性Sachs演化与驱动场非高斯性耦合，导致物质累积量层级（matter cumulant hierarchy）混合入透镜层级（lensing hierarchy）。一个选择规则控制耦合结构：n点观测量的直接贡献来自n点驱动场累积量，其主要层级混合修正来自(n+1)点累积量经一次非线性Sachs相互作用，更高阶累积量仅在高阶进入。以两点函数为例，其被Ricci聚焦和Weyl剪切的压缩三点累积量（squeezed three-point cumulants）修正，使小尺度模式调制大尺度，并同等馈入透镜E模和B模。

Conclusion: 该形式论并非一种受限的近似方案，而是一种范式转换：提供了一个统一框架，能够自然地容纳路径修正、高阶物质统计、随机性以及小尺度效应。

Abstract: Standard weak-lensing calculations treat lensing as a linear remapping of the matter field along the line of sight. We instead formulate lensing as a stochastic field theory for the Sachs optical scalars, driven by random Ricci-focusing and Weyl-shearing fields. The resulting path integral generates a diagrammatic expansion for arbitrary $n$-point correlation functions of lensing observables, organised into linear response, nonlinear propagation, and driving-field cumulants. The conventional calculation emerges as the lowest-order, linear-propagation limit. Beyond it, nonlinear Sachs evolution couples to driving-field non-Gaussianity, mixing the matter cumulant hierarchy into the lensing hierarchy. A selection rule governs the couplings: an $n$-point observable receives a direct contribution from the $n$-point driving-field cumulant, and its leading hierarchy-mixing correction from the $(n+1)$-point cumulant via one nonlinear Sachs interaction, with higher cumulants entering only at higher order. The two-point function, for instance, is corrected by squeezed three-point cumulants of Ricci focusing and Weyl shearing, letting small-scale modes source larger scales and feeding the lensing $E$- and $B$-modes equally. Rather than a restrictive approximation scheme, the formalism is a paradigm shift: a unified framework naturally accommodating path corrections, higher-order matter statistics, stochasticity, and small-scale effects.

</details>


### [121] [Reheating as a variational probe of cosmological observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19513)
*Jinn-Ouk Gong*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文将再加热（reheating）重新表述为状态方程历史空间中的一个约束变分问题（constrained variational problem），并通过引入正则化泛函框架（regularized functional framework）在最小物理假设下识别出极值化给定宇宙学观测量的再加热历史。通过对瞬时引力波、诱导引力波和原初黑洞的示例应用，发现不同观测量会选择再加热历史空间中性质不同的区域，表明宇宙学观测量定义了该空间中的不同极值方向，可用于系统性地探索暴胀后膨胀历史空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文将再加热问题形式化为状态方程（equation-of-state）历史空间中的约束变分问题，并引入一个正则化泛函框架（regularized functional framework）。在该框架下，通过极值化给定的宇宙学观测量（cosmological observable）来确定再加热历史，仅依赖最少的物理假设。

Result: 研究发现，不同的宇宙学观测量——如瞬时引力波（prompt gravitational waves）、诱导引力波（induced gravitational waves）和原初黑洞（primordial black holes）——在再加热历史空间中选择性质上不同的区域。这表明观测量定义了再加热历史空间中的不同极值方向（extremal directions）。

Conclusion: 该正则化变分框架为系统性地探索暴胀后膨胀历史（post-inflationary expansion histories）提供了一种新的工具。宇宙学观测量可以作为再加热历史空间中的极值方向，从而在不需要详细微观模型的情况下约束再加热过程。

Abstract: We formulate reheating as a constrained variational problem in the space of equation-of-state histories, rather than attempting to describe it through microscopic models. We introduce a regularized functional framework that identifies reheating histories which extremize a given cosmological observable under minimal physical assumptions. As illustrative applications, we consider prompt gravitational waves, induced gravitational waves, and primordial black holes. We find that different observables select qualitatively different regions of reheating-history space. These examples demonstrate that cosmological observables define distinct extremal directions in reheating-history space and can therefore be used to systematically explore the space of post-inflationary expansion histories.

### [122] [Finite-Core Signatures in LISA-Band Wave-Optics Lensing by Low-Mass Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19995)
*Dejiang Li,Tonghua Liu,Kai Liao,Beining Xia,Cuihong Wen,Jieci Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测低质量暗物质晕与次晕的内部密度轮廓（inner density profile）是理解暗物质本质的关键，但由于其质量较低，传统观测手段难以有效约束。引力波透镜效应（gravitational lensing）在LISA（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna）波段可提供新的探测途径。

Method: 通过比较固定质量的Navarro-Frenk-White（NFW）透镜与带核心的NFW（cored-NFW）透镜，将两种密度轮廓传播至复波动光学放大因子（complex wave-optics amplification factor），从而分离出有限核心部分的信号。同时采用SIDM（self-interacting dark matter）启发的等温核心轮廓进行验证。

Abstract: LISA-band gravitational waves from massive binary black holes can be diffractively lensed by low-mass dark matter halos and subhalos, so their frequency-dependent amplification can probe the inner density profile. We isolate the generic finite-core part of this signal by comparing fixed-mass Navarro-Frenk-White (NFW) and cored-NFW lenses and propagating both profiles to the complex wave-optics amplification factor. A finite core smooths the time-delay response and reshapes the diffraction peak; an NFW template with a lower concentration can mimic part of the effect, but structured complex residuals remain after time and phase alignment. The residual peaks for intermediate cores, $r_c/r_s\simeq0.25$--$0.3$. An SIDM-inspired isothermal-core profile gives the same qualitative response, showing that the signal is not an artifact of one cored parameterization. For a fiducial LISA source, an appreciable mismatch requires favorable near alignment and $M_{\rm vir}\gtrsim 10^7M_\odot$. The result is a finite-core baseline for isolated line-of-sight halos and for subhalos perturbing strongly lensed macro-images.

The model naturally predicts an effective phantom-crossing behaviour at intermediate redshifts while remaining free from the theoretical instabilities commonly associated with phantom scalar-field models. ### [125] [Self-Calibration of the Neutrino-Argon Cross Section with Solar Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18347)

TL;DR: 本文提出利用太阳中微子数据本身即可高精度测量DUNE实验中MeV能区的带电电流ν_e+^{40}Ar截面，在9–15 MeV范围内可实现≤2%的精度，为超新星和大气中微子研究奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE的MeV物理项目依赖于带电电流（charged-current, CC）ν_e+^{40}Ar截面的高精度知识。现有间接约束精度约10%，而唯一直接测量不确定度高达约50%，亟需改进。

Method: 利用太阳中微子数据本身进行截面测量，结合对⁸B通量和存活概率的独立知识，以及构成截面的Fermi和Gamow-Teller跃迁（Gamow-Teller transitions）的角分布特征。提出直觉分组与主成分分析（Principal Component Analysis, PCA）两种方法提取跃迁强度。

Result: 在悲观的探测假设下（但假设探测器不确定性可控），在9–15 MeV能区可实现截面精度≤2%。

Conclusion: 该结果将为研究更高能量（几十MeV）下的截面提供重要基础，核碎裂道（nuclear breakup channels）的加入使复杂性显著增加，但降低不确定性对超新星（supernova）和大气中微子（atmospheric neutrino）研究至关重要。

Abstract: The success of DUNE's MeV physics program depends upon high-precision knowledge of the charged-current (CC) $ν_e+\mathrm{^{40}Ar}$ cross section. While there are indirect constraints at the 10% level for the nuclear transitions that constitute this cross section, the only direct measurement in the MeV range has an uncertainty of $\sim$50%. We show, surprisingly, that the cross section can be precisely measured using the solar-neutrino data themselves. This is possible because of independent knowledge of the $^8$B flux and survival probability, plus the distinctive angular distributions of the Fermi and Gamow-Teller transitions that comprise the cross section. We propose new methods to extract the transition strengths, considering both intuitive groupings and a Principal Component Analysis. Under pessimistic assumptions about detection, but taking detector uncertainties to be controlled, we demonstrate that a precision of $\lesssim$2% on the cross section can be achieved in the 9-15 MeV energy range. These results will be an important foundation for studying the cross section up to several tens of MeV, where the complexity increases significantly due to nuclear breakup channels but where reducing uncertainties is critical for supernova and atmospheric neutrino studies.

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造了一个仅依赖衰变产物四动量的角观测量（angular observable）：对于来自轻介子衰变（light meson decays）的矢量玻色子，该观测量表现出各向异性分布；对于标量粒子，则表现为各向同性分布。

Result: 在DUNE、SHiP和FASER2等实验的框架下，该角观测量能够在尚未被排除的较大参数空间区域中有效识别中介粒子的自旋（mediator spin）。

Conclusion: 所提出的角观测量为实验鉴别长寿命暗扇区粒子的自旋提供了一种可行的方案，明确了未来多个前沿实验对自旋参数的探测能力。

Abstract: A variety of experiments are operating or planned to search for displaced decays of light long-lived dark sector particles. In case such a state is discovered, the next step is determining its quantum numbers. We identify an angular observable, reconstructible solely from the decay products' four-momenta, that exhibits an anisotropic distribution for vector bosons from light meson decays and an isotropic distribution for scalars. We demonstrate that searches at DUNE, SHiP and FASER2 will be able to identify the mediator spin in sizable regions of yet unconstrained parameter space.

### [127] [Real and Virtual Propagation in Neutrino Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19548)
*Kenji Nishiwaki,Kin-ya Oda,Juntaro Wada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在波包量子场论（wave-packet quantum field theory）框架下，重新审视了真空中中微子味振荡（flavor oscillations）的时间演化。通过鞍点法（saddle-point method）解析传播时间积分，推导出适用于短传播时间的味改变振幅（flavor-changing amplitude）表达式，发现振荡仅当传播时间超过由外波包能量不确定度（energy uncertainty）和传播粒子衰变宽度（decay width）共同设定的阈值时才出现。低于该阈值时，中间态表现为纯虚粒子（purely virtual state）。该结果扩展了 Jacob-Sachs（Grimus-Stockinger）定理的适用范围，并表明该定理在短传播时间下仍具有更高的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论主要在长传播时间（距离）极限下描述味振荡行为，但短时间/短距离下的振荡机制尚不清晰。本文旨在推导出对短传播时间同样有效的味改变振幅表达式，并揭示振荡发生的阈值条件。

Method: 采用波包量子场论（wave-packet quantum field theory）框架，利用鞍点法（saddle-point method）显式计算与传播时间相关的积分，从而得到广义的味改变振幅表达式。

Result: 振荡仅当传播时间超过由外波包能量不确定度和传播粒子衰变宽度所确定的阈值时才发生；短于该阈值时，中间粒子表现为无法传播宏观距离的纯虚态（purely virtual state）。此外，Jacob-Sachs 定理在短传播时间下仍具有比以往预期更高的准确性。

Conclusion: 该形式不仅适用于中微子，也适用于其他传播粒子。未来能量分辨率的提高可能使这一阈值变得可观，从而为实验检验从虚传播到实传播的转变提供可能。

Abstract: We revisit flavor oscillations in vacuum in terms of the propagation time of intermediate states. In the limit of a long propagation time (or distance), degenerate intermediate states exhibit oscillatory behavior, as described by the Jacob--Sachs (or Grimus--Stockinger) theorem within wave-packet quantum field theory. By explicitly evaluating the relevant integrals using the saddle-point method, we derive an extended expression for the flavor-changing amplitude that remains valid even for shorter propagation times. We show that oscillations occur only when the propagation time exceeds a threshold set by the energy uncertainty of the external wave packets and by the decay width of the propagating particle. For shorter propagation, the intermediate particle behaves as a purely virtual state, in the sense that it cannot propagate over a macroscopic distance. Although a direct experimental test of the transition from virtual to real propagation is challenging, since it typically occurs at microscopic scales, our result implies that the Jacob--Sachs theorem holds to higher accuracy than previously expected, even at short propagation times. Our formalism applies not only to neutrinos but also to other propagating particles, and future improvements in energy resolution may make this threshold observable.

</details>


### [128] [Charged Lepton Flavor Violation at Neutrino Telescopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19723)
*Writasree Maitra,Carlos A. Argüelles,P. S. Bhupal Dev,Ivan Martinez-Soler,Manibrata Sen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用中微子望远镜（neutrino telescopes）及其大量宇宙线缪子样本搜索带电轻子味破坏（CLFV），具体以IceCube数据为例，探索μ子到τ子的转换过程。通过模型无关的有效场论（EFT）算符和具体的轴矢量Z'模型给出灵敏度，并与低能实验和未来对撞机结果比较，展示了中微子望远镜作为CLFV研究互补手段的潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电轻子味破坏（CLFV）的任何观测都将是超越标准模型（Beyond-the-Standard-Model）物理的明确信号，但现有搜索手段有限，因此需要探索新途径。

Method: 利用IceCube宇宙线缪子数据集，提出在探测器内部搜索μ子到τ子（muon-to-tau conversion）的CLFV过程。采用模型无关的有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）算符描述CLFV相互作用，并进一步考虑轴矢量Z'（axial-vector $Z'$）互动的具体实现。

Result: 给出了IceCube对相关EFT能标的灵敏度，以及在Z'质量-耦合强度平面上的灵敏度区间。此外，还展示了下一代中微子望远镜（如IceCube-Gen2和HUNT）的预期灵敏度。

Conclusion: 中微子望远镜能够提供与低能CLFV搜索以及当前和未来对撞机实验互补的强大探测能力，是CLFV研究的新兴有力工具。

Abstract: Any observation of charged lepton flavor violation (CLFV) would be a clear signal of beyond-the-Standard-Model physics. Here, we propose a novel CLFV search using neutrino telescopes with their large cosmic-ray muon samples. Specifically, we use a recent IceCube cosmic-ray muon dataset and propose a new search for muon-to-tau conversion inside the IceCube detector. We illustrate our idea with CLFV interactions described by model-independent Effective Field Theory (EFT) operators and present the IceCube sensitivity on the relevant EFT scale. We also consider a specific realization of the EFT operator in terms of an axial-vector $Z'$ interaction and show sensitivities in the $Z'$ mass-coupling plane. We compare our sensitivities with those from low-energy CLFV searches, as well as from current and future collider experiments. We also show projections from next-generation neutrino telescopes, such as IceCube-Gen2 and HUNT, and demonstrate how neutrino telescopes can provide a powerful complementary probe of CLFV.

Abstract: We assess the tension between theoretical predictions and the values quoted by the Particle Data Group (PDG) for the partial decay width and branching fraction associated with the radiative charmonium decay $J/ψ\toγη_c$. A profile scan over the most recent PDG data depending on the branching fraction $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ suggests that the correlation between measured branching fractions is compatible with lattice QCD determinations of the partial decay widths $Γ(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ and $Γ(η_c\toγγ)$. We propose a theoretically grounded photon line shape for the radiative decay spectrum and a prescription for the extraction of (product) branching fractions involving the magnetic dipole (M1) transition $J/ψ\toγη_c$. This approach obviates the need to modify the photon energy spectrum line shape using empirical damping functions, as done in the most recent experimental extractions of $\mathcal{B}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ from the photon line shape, thereby eliminating an inherent ambiguity in the determination of the derived observables.

### [130] [New Avenues of Heavy Neutral Lepton at Muon Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19906)

TL;DR: 本文提出在多TeV缪子对撞机中，通过新矢量玻色子聚变过程（$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ 和 $Z'Z'\to NN$）产生重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton），并分析了对应的轻子数破坏信号（lepton number violation signals）。新过程不受希格斯玻色子间混合角 $\alpha$ 的抑制，能量阈值要求更低，为重中性轻子的探测提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多TeV缪子对撞机（muon collider）中，初态辐射效应使其可视为电弱玻色子对撞机（electroweak boson collider），矢量玻色子聚变（vector boson fusion）截面随能量对数增长，成为主导产生模式。在$U(1)$规范扩展的跷跷板模型（seesaw model）中，重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton, $N$）与新规范玻色子$Z'$和重希格斯$H$存在额外相互作用。传统$WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$过程受希格斯玻色子间小混合角$\alpha$的抑制，因此需要探索不依赖该混合角的新产生机制。

Method: 基于$U(1)$规范扩展的跷跷板模型，研究了两种新矢量玻色子聚变产生重中性轻子的过程：含重希格斯的中介过程$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$，以及不含重希格斯的直接过程$Z'Z'\to NN$。随后分析对应的轻子数破坏信号：在含重希格斯通道中通过$μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- H \to μ^+μ^- NN$，在无重希格斯通道中通过$μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$，并考虑$N\to μ^\pm jj$衰变，$W$玻色子衰变产生的两个喷注（jets）被处理为一个fat-jet $J$。

Result: 新过程$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$不受希格斯玻色子间小混合角$\alpha$的抑制，避免了传统$WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$产生通道的主要局限。同时，即使重希格斯质量大于对撞能量（$m_H> \sqrt{s}$），直接对产生过程$Z'Z'\to NN$仍然可行，提供了更大的参数空间。

Conclusion: 多TeV缪子对撞机通过新矢量玻色子聚变过程（$Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ 和 $Z'Z'\to NN$）为重中性轻子的产生提供了替代路径。这些新通道有助于探测重中性轻子的内禀特征，并可通过轻子数破坏信号在实验中进行检验。

Abstract: With initial state radiation, the multi-TeV muon collider can be regarded as an electroweak boson collider. The dominant production mode of the certain process becomes the vector boson fusion channel, because the corresponding cross section typically increases logarithmically at high energies. This also holds true for new physics beyond the standard model. Within the $U(1)$ gauged extension of seesaw models, the heavy neutral lepton has additional interactions with the new gauge boson $Z'$ and heavy Higgs $H$. In this paper, we investigate the production of heavy neutral lepton $N$ via the new vector boson fusion processes $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ with and $Z'Z'\to NN$ without heavy Higgs at the multi-TeV muon collider. Different from the canonical vector boson fusion processes $WW/ZZ\to H\to NN$, the new process $Z'Z'\to H\to NN$ is not suppressed by the small mixing angle $α$ between the Higgs bosons. Meanwhile, the pair production process $Z'Z'\to NN$ is also viable even for heavy Higgs $m_H> \sqrt{s}$. Therefore, these new avenues provide alternative pathways to probe the intrinsic feature of the heavy neutral lepton. We then perform a detailed analysis of the lepton number violation signals via the new vector boson fusion with heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- H \to μ^+μ^- NN$ and without heavy Higgs $μ^+μ^-\to μ^+μ^- NN$, followed by $N\to μ^\pm jj$, where the two jets from $W$ boson decay are treated as one fat-jet $J$.

### [131] [$Ξ_{cc}^{++}-Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ Transitions as a Two-Charm-Selective Portal to Ultra-Low-$Q$ Charged Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19991)
*Yong Du*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用 LHCb 观测到的双粲重子（doubly charmed baryon）$Ξ_{cc}^{+}$，提出 $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ 作为检验带电电流（charged-current）新物理的零检验（null test），并识别出一种双粲选择性的带电电流新物理门户（portal），该门户在双粲重子中的矩阵元非零，但在π介子、核子、原子核及单粲介子中领头阶为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用 LHCb 实验新观测到的 $Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ 所开启的超低 $Q$ 值跃迁 $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$，为带电电流新物理提供一个具有实验动机的零检验。

Method: 通过两体和三体衰变分析，评估对有效重子层次耦合（effective baryon-level couplings）的灵敏度；针对普适轻带电标量 $φ^+$ 模型，综合电弱精确检验（electroweak-precision）和β衰变（beta-decay）约束与 LHCb 预期灵敏度进行比较。

Conclusion: 识别出一种双粲选择性的带电电流门户，其领头算符在双粲重子中具有非零矩阵元，但在π介子、核子、原子核和单粲介子中的领头阶为零。在此类模型中，$Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ 跃迁可提供对该门户相互作用的最直接探测。

Abstract: The recent LHCb observation of $Ξ_{cc}^{+}$ opens the ultra-low-$Q$ transition $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ as an experimentally motivated null test of charged-current new physics. Our two- and three-body analyses show sensitivity to effective baryon-level couplings of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6}-10^{-7})$ for MeV-scale recoil momenta. We establish a practical no-go result for a universal light charged scalar $φ^+$: with a first-generation $φ^+\bar u d$ coupling, existing electroweak-precision and beta-decay constraints are parametrically stronger than the projected LHCb sensitivity. We then identify a two-charm-selective charged-current portal whose leading operator has a nonzero matrix element in doubly charmed baryons but vanishes at leading order in pions, nucleons, nuclei, and singly charmed mesons. In this class of models, $Ξ_{cc}^{++}\toΞ_{cc}^{+}$ transitions can provide the leading direct probe of the portal interaction.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: $2τ\:+\:2b\:+$ 缺失横动量（missing $E_T$）通道为搜索扩展希格斯扇区中的非标准VLQ衰变提供了一条有前景且大致正交（orthogonal）的路径。基于渐近显著性（Asimov significance）评估的发现灵敏度表明，对VLQ质量最高约1.9 TeV可实现发现级灵敏度。

Abstract: Extensions of the Standard Model featuring both an enlarged scalar sector and vector-like fermions arise naturally in a wide class of well-motivated theoretical frameworks. In such scenarios, vector-like Quarks (VLQs) can exhibit non-standard decay modes involving additional Higgs states, giving rise to distinctive collider signatures that remain largely unexplored by existing experimental searches. We investigate the prospects of probing this possibility at the high-luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) through the decay of vector-like top partner ($T$) to charged Higgs ($H^{\pm}$) followed by the decay, $H^\pm\toτν$, producing a final state containing two tau leptons, two $b$-jets, and missing transverse energy. A model-independent collider analysis is performed using global kinematic observables constructed from visible objects and the missing transverse momentum vector to suppress the dominant backgrounds. Polarization-sensitive observables built from the hadronic $τ$ decay products are also examined as complementary probes of the spin-$0$ origin of the $τ$ leptons. The expected discovery sensitivity is evaluated using the Asimov significance for an integrated luminosity of $3$ ab$^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=14$ TeV. Our results demonstrate that the $2τ\:+\:2b\:+$ missing $E_T$ channel provides a promising and largely orthogonal avenue to search for non-standard VLQ decays in extended Higgs sectors, with discovery-level sensitivity achievable for VLQ masses up to approximately $1.9$ TeV.

Abstract: Recent experimental advances in the baryon sector, including the observation of doubly charmed states, have renewed interest in the production mechanisms of increasingly heavy hadronic systems, calling for precision and uncertainty-controlled descriptions. We present the OMG3Q1.1 framework for the fragmentation of same-flavor all-heavy $Ω_{3Q}$ baryons in high-energy hadronic collisions. The construction combines diquark-inspired inputs for constituent-heavy-quark and gluon channels with threshold-aware DGLAP evolution within the HF-NRevo scheme. A replica-based strategy consistently quantifies perturbative missing-higher-order effects (F-MHOUs) and nonperturbative wave-function uncertainties (F-NPWFs), yielding the first uncertainty-resolved fragmentation-function set for the $Ω_{3Q}$ sector. ### [134] [Theory Calculations for LDMX and LOHENGRIN beyond Coherent Bethe-Heitler Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20327)
*Martin Schürmann,Herbert K. Dreiner,Rhorry Gauld*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究大多仅考虑暗光子仅耦合于标准模型带电轻子、且发生在相干贝特-海特勒（Bethe-Heitler）电子-原子核散射中的信号特征，缺乏对更全面物理过程的系统计算。本文旨在填补这一空白，为下一代暗物质轻暗物质实验（LDMX、DarkSHINE、LOHENGRIN）提供更完整的信号与背景预测。

Result: 给出了各类过程的数值截面和微分分布结果，包括信号与主要背景。发现LOHENGRIN实验需要扩展其强子量能器（HCAL）以有效压制来自衍射散射（diffractive scattering）的背景过程。在真实实验选择条件下，相干贝特-海特勒散射之外的贡献对暗光子相关质量范围内信号和背景的预测影响有限。

Conclusion: 高阶辐射过程和虚暗光子贡献在现有实验选择下对信号与背景的修正有限；LOHENGRIN需额外硬件升级以应对衍射散射背景。该工作为未来轻暗物质实验的信号建模和实验设计提供了更精确的理论基础。

Abstract: The Light Dark Matter eXperiment (LDMX), DarkSHINE, and LOHENGRIN are proposed new experiments. They aim to search for missing momentum signals sourced by the direct production of dark photons with masses in the MeV-GeV range in bremsstrahlung processes, in which an electron beam of a few GeV scatters off a fixed target. So far, the signal characteristics, i.e. the behavior of the recoiling electron, have mostly been studied in coherent Bethe-Heitler electron-nucleus scattering with a dark photon that couples only to the Standard Model charged leptons. In this work, we present the calculations of the differential cross sections of all contributing real emission processes up to third order in the electromagnetic fine structure constant and fourth order in the kinetic mixing parameter associated with the dark photon. We consider a dark photon coupling to both the beam electron and the hadronic target and we take into account the scattering off both the target nucleus and its nuclear constituents. Besides real emission processes, we also discuss virtual dark photon contributions and their relevance for the signal prediction. After discussing the different phase space regions and constraints emerging from the experimental setups, we show numerical results of the cross sections and differential distributions, including the signal and dominant background. Within our framework, we find that the LOHENGRIN experiment will require an extension of its HCAL to effectively veto background processes originating from diffractive scattering. Apart from that, the contributions beyond coherent Bethe-Heitler scattering, in the presence of realistic experimental selections, have only a limited effect on the predicted signal and background in the relevant dark photon mass range.

### [135] [Partial-wave unitarity and long-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19432)
*Ryan Plestid,Pablo Quílez Lasanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在包含无质量粒子的理论中，通过修正的微扰理论构造分波振幅（partial-wave amplitudes）的方法，解决了由t通道前向散射奇点导致的标准固定阶表达式失效的问题。研究发现，前向散射区域存在普适描述，可消除重整化标度依赖性，使分波振幅成为定义明确的单标度对象，并给出了逐阶计算的实用方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在包含无质量粒子的理论中，t通道（前向散射）奇点导致标准固定阶展开下的分波振幅（partial-wave amplitudes）定义不良，从而阻碍了系统可改进的分波幺正性界（partial-wave unitarity bounds）的建立。因此，需要一种新的方法来正确构造分波振幅。

Method: 采用修正的微扰理论（modified perturbation theory），将长程相互作用（long-range interactions）纳入考虑，重点分析离壳库仑模（off-shell Coulomb modes）的作用。通过研究前向散射区域的普适行为，构造了重整化标度无关的分波振幅。

Result: 发现前向散射区域存在一种普适描述（universal description），使得振幅不再依赖于重整化标度（renormalization scale）。所得分波振幅成为定义明确的单标度对象，消除了对红外正规化子（infrared regulator）的虚假依赖。

Conclusion: 提出了一种在微扰论中逐阶计算分波振幅的实用方法，解决了由无质量粒子前向散射奇点引起的幺正性分析难题。

Abstract: Theories with massless particles contain $t$-channel (forward scattering) singularities that cause standard fixed order expressions for partial-wave amplitudes to be ill-defined. This presents an obstruction to systematically improvable partial-wave unitarity bounds. In this work, we study the construction of partial-wave amplitudes in a modified perturbation theory that incorporates long-range interactions focusing on the role of off-shell Coulomb modes. We find that there exists a universal description of the forward scattering region that renders the amplitudes renormalization scale independent. The resulting partial-wave amplitudes become well defined single-scale objects without spurious dependence on the infrared regulator, and we present a practical method for their computation order-by-order in perturbation theory.

</details>


### [136] [The $B^+ \to K^+ ν\bar ν$ decay as a QCD axion search: comparing reinterpretation approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20525)
*Merna Abumusabh,Giulio Dujany,Diego Guadagnoli,Méril Reboud,Claudio Toni*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文指出，对Belle II $B^+ \to K^+\nu\bar\nu$数据的两项独立分析在$B^+ \to K^+ a$（a为类轴子暗物质粒子）衰变分支比上限上存在约四倍的差异，其根源在于运动学变量空间的选择。核心指标是重建双中微子不变质量$q^2_{\rm rec}$的分辨率：精细分箱能分辨窄的轴子信号，而粗分箱会将其稀释到背景区间。基于BDT训练的分类轴对$B^+ \to K^+ a$几乎无助，因该轴与$q^2$不相关。数值检验证实了这些预期；纳入次领头形状系统学只会降低上限，使基于$q^2_{\rm rec}$的界更保守。重新分析确认运动学轴选择本身即可解释四倍的灵敏度差异，且$B^+ \to K^+ a$上限在$q^2_{\rm rec}\times\eta({\rm BDT}_2)$空间中随$B^+ \to K^+\nu\bar\nu$的类标准模型（SM-likeness）程度显著变化，从而失去了$q^2_{\rm rec}$方法的双探针（dual-probe）特征。结论是：当信号形状与BDT训练信号明显不同时，由BDT变量主导的似然函数对重新解释（reinterpretation）的能力受限，因此建议实验合作组在发布基于BDT的似然函数时，同时发布物理变量空间中的似然投影，以最大化测量的可重新解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释Belle II $B^+ \to K^+\nu\bar\nu$数据中，两项独立分析在$B^+ \to K^+ a$分支比上限上出现约四倍差异的原因，并揭示运动学变量选择对此类超越标准模型（BSM）重新解释的影响。

Method: 追溯因子四差异的来源至运动学变量空间的选择，重点分析重建双中微子不变质量$q^2_{\rm rec}$的分箱精细度；通过数值测试比较基于$q^2_{\rm rec}$方法与BDT方法对轴子信号的鉴别能力；开展专门的重新分析，检验$q^2_{\rm rec}\times\eta({\rm BDT}_2)$空间中$B^+ \to K^+ a$上限的变化。

Result: 精细的$q^2_{\rm rec}$分箱能有效分辨窄轴子信号，而粗分箱会将其稀释；BDT轴与$q^2$不相关，对$B^+ \to K^+ a$的鉴别能力极弱；引入次领头形状系统学反而降低$B^+ \to K^+ a$上限，使基于$q^2_{\rm rec}$的界更保守；运动学轴选择本身即可解释四倍的灵敏度差异。

Conclusion: 当信号形状与BDT训练信号差异显著时，BDT主导的似然函数对BSM重新解释的适用性有限；建议实验合作组在发布BDT基似然函数的同时，提供物理变量空间中的似然投影，以提升测量的可重新解释性。

Abstract: Two recent independent analyses of Belle II $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ data yield limits on ${\mathcal B}(B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a)$ -- the two-body mode to a light invisible particle such as the QCD axion -- differing by a factor of roughly four; we trace this to the choice of kinematic variable space. The central figure of merit is the resolution in the reconstructed di-neutrino invariant mass $q^2_{\rm rec}$: fine-grained binning resolves the narrow axion signal, while coarse binning dilutes it into a background-dominated range. A BDT axis trained on $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ adds little discriminating power for $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$, as this axis is largely uncorrelated with $q^2$. These expectations are confirmed by a set of numerical tests. The subleading shape systematics omitted from our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach {\em lower}, not raise, the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ limit: by better accommodating the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$ shape, they leave less room for the axion signal, making our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based bound conservative, if anything. A dedicated reanalysis confirms that the kinematic-axes choice alone accounts for the factor-of-four sensitivity difference, and that the $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ a$ bound varies sizeably within the $q^2_{\rm rec}\timesη({\rm BDT}_2)$ space, depending on the SM-likeness of $B^+ \! \to \! K^+ν\barν$, thus losing the dual-probe feature of our $q^2_{\rm rec}$-based approach. These results point to a broader consideration: likelihoods dominated by BDT variables are of limited use for reinterpretations when the signal shape differs appreciably from the BDT's training signal. We therefore advocate that experimental collaborations publish likelihood projections in physical variable spaces alongside BDT-based likelihoods, to maximise the reinterpretability of their measurements.

</details>


### [137] [Phase Transitions and Gravitational Wave Production at the End of Thermal Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20392)
*Hyukjung Kim,İlayda Kuzu,Kerem Özsoy,Zeynep Kahraman,Wan-Il Park,Heeseung Zoe*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了终止热膨胀（thermal inflation）的一级相变（first-order phase transition），通过半解析反弹作用（bounce action）计算与三维朗之万格子（Langevin lattice）模拟相结合，验证了相变通过局域气泡成核（bubble nucleation）与生长进行，并评估了由此产生的随机引力波信号（stochastic gravitational-wave signals），预言该信号位于未来探测器（如BBO和DECIGO）的灵敏度范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对热膨胀终止阶段的一级相变动力学及其对应的引力波（gravitational wave）信号缺乏系统量化，需要结合解析与数值方法进行精确表征。

Method: 采用半解析方法计算反弹作用（bounce action），并与CosmoTransitions数值结果对比；随后引入包含哈勃膨胀（Hubble expansion）及温度演化的三维朗之万格子（Langevin lattice）模拟，研究相变的实时演化过程。

Result: 格子动力学与反弹作用估计一致，相变通过局域气泡成核（bubble nucleation）和生长完成，而非相混合不稳定性（phase-mixing instability）。基于相变参数估算的气泡碰撞（bubble collisions）和等离子体声学运动（acoustic motions）产生的引力波谱（gravitational-wave spectra）位于BBO和DECIGO的探测灵敏度范围内。

Conclusion: 热膨胀终止的一级相变可产生可探测的随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background），为未来空间引力波观测台提供了可供检验的预言信号。

Abstract: We investigate the first-order phase transition that terminates thermal inflation and evaluate the associated stochastic gravitational-wave signals. The transition is first characterized through semi-analytic calculations of the bounce action, which are compared with numerical results obtained using CosmoTransitions. We then study its real-time evolution in a three-dimensional Langevin lattice simulation that incorporates Hubble expansion and the corresponding temperature evolution throughout the transition. The lattice dynamics are consistent with the bounce-action estimates: the transition proceeds through localized bubble nucleation and subsequent bubble growth, rather than through a phase-mixing instability. Using the resulting transition parameters, we estimate the gravitational-wave spectra generated by bubble collisions and acoustic motions in the plasma. The predicted stochastic background lies within the projected sensitivity ranges of future gravitational-wave observatories, including BBO and DECIGO.

### [138] [Constraining ADD black holes at the LHC with $\sqrt{s} = 14$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19839)
*Ashfaque Ahmad,Sudhir Kumar Gupta,Abbas Ali*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在ADD模型框架下，利用大型强子对撞机（LHC）在质心能量14 TeV、积分光度349.4 fb⁻¹的数据，通过引入参数ζ来考虑黑洞形成过程中的能量损耗，对微观黑洞质量M_B给出了约束上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在ADD模型（ADD model）的背景下，微观黑洞可能在LHC对撞中产生。本文旨在通过考虑黑洞形成过程中的能量损耗效应，对微观黑洞质量M_B给出更现实的约束。

Method: 基于LHC在质心能量（centre-of-mass energy）√s = 14 TeV、积分光度（integrated luminosity）349.4 fb⁻¹的数据，在ADD模型中引入参数ζ表征黑洞形成过程中的能量损耗（loss），系统分析不同额外维数（extra dimensions）D和约化普朗克标度（reduced Planck scale）Λ_D下的质量约束。

Result: 对于D=3且Λ_D≈1 TeV，ζ=0时M_B≤11.83 TeV被排除；Λ_D=9 TeV时对应值约为10.33 TeV。损耗增大时约束显著降低，例如ζ=0.35时M_B降至7.65 TeV（Λ_D=1 TeV）和6.82 TeV（Λ_D=9 TeV）。在95%置信水平（C.L.）下，当D增至7时，上述极限分别变为12.03/10.88 TeV（ζ=0）和7.80/7.03 TeV（ζ=0.35）。

Conclusion: 黑洞形成过程中的能量损耗对质量约束有显著影响，损耗越大则质量下界越低；额外维数增加也会略微提升质量排除界限。

Abstract: We explore microscopic black holes at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) in the context of the ADD model for the centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 14~\mathrm{TeV}$ at an integrated luminosity of $349.4~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ and provide constraints on the black hole mass, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ by taking into account the effects of loss during the formation process of black holes through the parameter $ζ$. Our analysis reveals that for $ζ= 0$, black holes with $M_{\mathrm{B}} \leq 11.83~\mathrm{TeV}$ are disfavored in the case of three extra dimensions ($\mathcal{D}$), for the reduced Planck scale ($Λ_{\mathcal{D}}$) of about a TeV. The corresponding values for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 9~\mathrm{TeV}$ turned out to be about $10.33~\mathrm{TeV}$. A significant reduction in the aforementioned limits is observed while the loss gets higher, e.g. for $ζ= 0.35$, $M_{\mathrm{B}}$ reduces to $7.65 (6.82)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$. These limits change to $12.03 ~(10.88)~\mathrm{TeV}$ and $7.80~ (7.03)~\mathrm{TeV}$ respectively for $ζ= 0~(0.35)$ for $Λ_{\mathcal{D}} = 1 (9)~\mathrm{TeV}$ at 95\% C.L. in case $\mathcal{D}$ is raised to seven.

</details>


### [139] [String Axiverse Enhancement of Superradiant Dark Matter Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20524)
*Diogo S. Gorgulho,Jacob A. Litterer,João G. Rosa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了弦轴子（string axion）发射对轻质原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）通过蒸发（evaporation）和超辐射（superradiance）产生暗物质的影响。结果表明，现实弦论构造中预测的大量轻轴子种数（约100–10^5种）能显著增强超辐射效率，从而扩大“微玻色子星”（micro-boson stars）作为暗物质候选者的参数空间；同时，轴子种数过多会导致PBH过快蒸发，妨碍超辐射云达到最大质量；此外，PBH蒸发发射的轴子对复合时期相对论性自由度的贡献可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中暗物质（dark matter）的起源尚不明确，而原初黑洞（PBHs）被视为可能的暗物质产生源之一。弦论（string theory）预测存在大量超轻轴子（axion）物种，这些轴子可能通过PBH的超辐射和蒸发过程影响暗物质生成，但此前缺乏系统研究。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究弦轴子（string axion）发射对轻质原初黑洞（PBHs）暗物质产生的影响，同时考虑蒸发（Hawking evaporation）和超辐射（superradiance）两种机制。利用弦论构造中预测的大量轻轴子种数（约100–10^5种）作为输入参数，分析其对PBH自旋及超辐射效率的反馈效应。

Result: 发现大量轻轴子物种可显著增强超辐射效率，进而扩大暗物质以“微玻色子星”（micro-boson stars，即超辐射暗物质云的自引力残余）形式存在的参数区域（暗物质质量、PBH质量与自旋）。但轴子种数过多时，PBH蒸发过快，超辐射云无法达到最大质量。此外，蒸发过程中发射的轴子对复合时期（recombination）的相对论性自由度贡献极小，不可观测。

Conclusion: 弦轴子景（string axiverse）显著扩展了PBH通过超辐射产生暗物质的可行参数空间，使微玻色子星成为暗物质的重要候选者；但轴子物种数量存在上限，超出则抑制超辐射云的形成。蒸发轴子对宇宙微波背景（CMB）的影响可忽略，因而与现有观测一致。

Abstract: We study the effects of string axion emission on dark matter production by light primordial black holes (PBHs), through both evaporation and superradiance. We show, in particular, that the Hawking emission of $\mathcal{O}(100-10^5)$ light axion species predicted in realistic string theory constructions can significantly enhance the efficiency of superradiance, given the associated increase in the PBH spin. The string axiverse thus significantly expands the parametric regions (dark matter mass and PBH mass and spin) for which a sizeable fraction of dark matter may presently be in the form of ``micro-boson stars'': the self-gravitating remnants of superradiant dark matter clouds. Conversely, for too large a number of axion species PBHs evaporate too quickly for superradiant clouds to attain their maximum mass. Finally, assuming that all dark matter is produced by PBHs (through both superradiance and Hawking emission), we show that the axions emitted during PBH evaporation give an immeasurably small contribution to the relativistic degrees of freedom at recombination.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所提出的新技术有效解决了Larin方案在混合规范扇区中的计算问题，为高精度标准模型唯象学提供了必要的三圈修正。

Abstract: Defining $γ_5$ within dimensional regularization remains a fundamental challenge. Larin's prescription addresses this by introducing additional renormalization constants to restore standard and chiral Ward identities. While these constants are known up to four loops in pure quantum chromodynamics, current precision Standard Model phenomenology requires extending these corrections to mixed gauge sectors. In this article, we propose a novel technique utilizing form factors and the universality of infrared divergences to compute these constants. Applying this framework, we present the new three-loop results for the renormalization constants, as well as the pure-singlet contributions to the quark axial-vector form factor, for a mixed $SU(N) \times U(1)$ gauge group.

In particular, we can prove the existence of a phase transition, thereby settling a recent conjecture by Byun, Forrester, Majumdar and Schehr.

### [142] [NNNN: Neural Networks for Newtonian Noise Mitigation at the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19907)
*Jan Kelleter,Patrick Schillings,Jonathan Kuckert,David Bertram,Markus Bachlechner,Achim Stahl,Johannes Erdmann*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用神经网络（neural network）基于合成地震仪阵列数据预测牛顿噪声（Newtonian noise）的能力，并与维纳滤波器（Wiener filter）进行对比。在稳态波场中两者性能相近，但在处理单一主导性事件时，卷积神经网络（CNN）和图神经网络（GNN）可将预测误差降低15-80倍，噪声幅度谱密度降低10-30倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来地基引力波探测器（如爱因斯坦望远镜）的低频灵敏度将受限于地震波引起的牛顿噪声。传统方法通过地震仪阵列测量位移场来预测并抑制该噪声，但现有预测方法在非稳态事件中性能有限，需探索更优的预测模型。

Method: 研究基于合成数据方法：模拟随机平面波（random plane wave）和高斯波包（Gaussian wave packet）的密度涨落，据此计算牛顿噪声与位移场。采用神经网络（含卷积神经网络和图神经网络）与维纳滤波器同时进行预测，评估两者在稳态波场和单一主导性长/短期事件下的表现。

Result: 在近似稳态波场中，神经网络与维纳滤波器性能相近，网络略优。在单一主导性事件场景下，卷积神经网络和图神经网络的预测误差优于维纳滤波器15-80倍（因频率和阵列配置而异），对应的牛顿噪声幅度谱密度降低10-30倍。

Conclusion: 神经网络，特别是卷积神经网络和图神经网络，在预测非稳态牛顿噪声事件方面显著优于传统维纳滤波器方法，有望为未来引力波探测器的噪声抑制提供更有效的技术路径。

Abstract: The gravitational effects of seismic waves, so-called Newtonian noise, will likely limit the low-frequency sensitivity of future ground-based gravitational wave detectors, such as the Einstein Telescope. It has been proposed to mitigate this noise source by predicting it from measurements of the surrounding seismic displacement field using an array of seismometers. In this paper, we investigate the Newtonian noise prediction abilities of neural networks based on synthetic data from such seismometer arrays and compare the results with the Wiener filter as benchmark. We developed a simulation that generates density fluctuations of random plane waves and Gaussian wave packets, and that calculates the resulting Newtonian noise and displacement field. We investigate the performance on approximately stationary wave fields and single dominating long- and short-term events. For the first case, we observe comparable performance of neural networks and the Wiener filter with the networks performing slightly better. For the second case, however, we find that convolutional neural networks and graph neural networks can outperform the Wiener filter by factors of 15-80, depending on the frequency and the array configuration, and that they can reduce the corresponding Newtonian noise amplitude spectral density by factors of 10-30.

</details>

### [143] [Observation of complete delocalization in disordered photonic lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19436)
*Biplab Pal,Rodrigo A. Vicencio*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文报道了在完全无序的钻石-点链（diamond-dot chain）中，安德森局域化（Anderson localization）完全消失、粒子完美透射的反常现象，并通过理论推导、数值模拟和飞秒激光写入光子晶格实验加以验证。此外，研究还发现当施加π有效磁通时，同一系统会出现极端局域化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在完全无序的晶格系统中是否存在安德森局域化完全消失、实现完美透射的反常现象，并揭示其背后的几何条件。

Method: 作者通过解析推导给出透明窗口（transparent window）产生的几何条件证明，利用数值模拟进行理论验证，并在飞秒激光写入的钻石-点光子晶格（femtosecond laser-written diamond-dot photonic lattices）中通过光透射概率实验进行直接观测。

Result: 在完全无序的钻石-点链中观察到安德森局域化完全消失与粒子完美透射；在施加π有效磁通时，同一系统出现与具体几何无关的极端局域化。

Conclusion: 该结果为在完全无序晶格系统中实现从弹道输运（ballistic transport）到零透射的能量传输控制提供了优秀平台。

Abstract: We present the exceptional phenomenon of complete absence of Anderson localization, and perfect transmission of particles, in a completely disordered diamond-dot chain. We analytically show a proof for the condition to observe this exceptional phenomenon, based on a transparent window emerging from a geometrical condition. We support our theoretical prediction by numerical simulations and direct experimental observation of the transmission probabilities of the light in a femtosecond laser-written diamond-dot photonic lattices. We additionally show that for a $π$ effective magnetic flux, extreme localization of the light in the same system may occur, independently on the specific geometry. Our results open up an excellent platform for controlling the transmission of energy from ballistic to zero transmission, in a completely disordered lattice system..

</details>


### [144] [Truncated Wigner dynamics of biclique quantum spin glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20187)
*Dries Sels*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本论文采用离散截断维格纳近似（TWA）研究双团簇量子自旋玻璃的近绝热动力学，在极小计算成本下成功复现了小系统的样本间涨落、临界指数以及近期量子实验，并可扩展至数万量子比特。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋玻璃（quantum spin glasses）常被用作研究量子优化算法（quantum optimization algorithms）的测试平台，并屡次被声称具有量子优势；然而对其近绝热动力学的精确且可扩展的模拟方法仍有待检验。本研究旨在验证截断维格纳近似（truncated Wigner approximation, TWA）能否在较大系统规模下有效捕捉相关物理量。

Method: 采用离散截断维格纳近似（discrete truncated Wigner approximation, TWA）对双团簇（biclique）量子自旋玻璃模型进行近绝热动力学（near adiabatic dynamics）模拟。在小系统上进行基准测试，评估TWA在不同退火时间下对Edwards-Anderson序参数（Edwards-Anderson order parameter）样本间涨落的复现能力，并通过Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）提取临界指数（critical exponents）。

Result: 在小系统基准测试中，TWA能够以较高保真度复现Edwards-Anderson序参数的样本间涨落，且保真度随系统尺寸增大而提高。从Binder累积量中提取的临界指数与理论预期一致，并成功复现了近期量子实验的结果。该方法的计算成本极低，可轻松应用于数万量子比特规模。

Conclusion: 截断维格纳近似（TWA）是一种计算高效且可扩展的方法，能够准确描述双团簇量子自旋玻璃的近绝热动力学。该方法不仅复现了关键的统计物理量和实验观测结果，还为大规模量子优化算法的经典模拟提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Quantum spin glasses are often considered testbeds for studying quantum optimization algorithms and as such have been the subject of various quantum advantage claims. Here we investigate the near adiabatic dynamics of biclique quantum spin glasses within the (discrete) truncated Wigner approximation (TWA). Benchmarks on small systems show that TWA recovers sample-to-sample fluctuations of the Edwards-Anderson order parameter, over a wide range of annealing times, with increasing fidelity when the system size increases. We extract critical exponents from the Binder cumulant in line with theoretical expectations, reproducing recent quantum experiments. The computational cost of the method is minimal and it can easily be applied to tens of thousands of qubits.

</details>

### [145] [Universal Properties of Nonlinearly Perturbed Maxwell Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19845)
*Tengyang Liu,Yisong Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，一种广义的非线性微扰麦克斯韦电磁理论具备三个普适基本性质：有限能量的点电荷、排除有限能量的磁单极与对偶电荷的戴恩（dyon），以及点电荷有效半径的任意小性与相关的局域不可探测性。第三个性质为电子的不可见性提供了经典解释。该理论以尽可能一般的非线性轮廓对麦克斯韦理论进行最小微扰，同时保持上述三个普适性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell theory）在描述点电荷时存在发散困难，并且无法自然解释电子作为点电荷为何不可见。本文试图通过引入一种广义的非线性微扰，构建一个能够同时保证点电荷能量有限、排除磁单极（magnetic monopole）与戴恩（dyon），并解释电子不可见性的经典电磁理论。

Method: 作者对麦克斯韦理论施加一种尽可能一般的非线性微扰轮廓（nonlinearity profile），使得该非线性理论在最小程度偏离线性麦克斯韦理论的前提下，维持三个普适性质：有限能量点电荷、排除有限能量磁单极与戴恩，以及点电荷有效半径的任意小性。

Result: 该非线性电磁理论产生的三个普适性质中，第三个性质——点电荷有效半径的任意小性及相关的局域不可探测性——为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供了一个经典解释，符合其有效半径极小的观测事实。

Conclusion: 作者提出的非线性微扰麦克斯韦理论在保持三个普适性质的前提下，以经典方式解释了点电子的不可见性，为理解电磁学中的点电荷奇异性问题提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We show that a general nonlinearly perturbed Maxwell theory of electromagnetism possesses three universal fundamental properties:
  (i) A finite-energy electric point charge.
  (ii) Exclusion of finite-energy magnetic monopoles and dually charged dyons.
  (iii) Arbitrary smallness of the effective radius of a point electric charge and the associated local undetectedness of the electric charge and energy.
  In particular, this last property offers a classical explanation for the invisibility of the electron, as a point electric charge, in accordance with the smallness of its effective radius.
  This nonlinear theory of electromagnetism has the feature that it minimally perturbs the Maxwell theory with a nonlinearity profile that is as general as possible such that the three universal properties stated above are all maintained.

</details>


### [146] [Dirac structures on tangent bundles: a geometric framework for variational principles, constrained dynamics, and symmetry reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20012)
*Hiroaki Yoshimura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由拉格朗日二次型和约束分布自然诱导的切丛上的狄拉克结构（Lagrange–Dirac structure），为包括非完整系统、退化拉格朗日系统和对称系统在内的 Lagrange–Dirac 动力学系统提供了统一的几何框架，并建立了相应的变分原理、约化理论以及在带电粒子、电路和理想流体等系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Lagrange–Dirac 动力学系统（如非完整（nonholonomic）系统、退化拉格朗日（degenerate Lagrangian）系统和对称（symmetric）系统）缺乏统一的几何描述。本文旨在引入一种自然诱导于拉格朗日二次型（Lagrangian two-form）和约束分布的 Dirac 结构，以提供统一的几何框架，并发展相应的变分原理和约化理论。

Method: 在切丛（tangent bundle）上引入 Lagrange–Dirac 结构，该结构由（可能退化的）拉格朗日函数诱导的拉格朗日二次型与约束分布共同定义。基于此结构，提出 Lagrange–d’Alembert–Dirac 原理作为切丛上的内蕴变分原理（intrinsic variational principle）。对于具有李群对称性（Lie group symmetry）的系统，发展约化理论，导出约化的 Lagrange–Dirac 结构和 Euler–Poincaré–Dirac 方程。

Result: 在超正则（hyperregular）情形下，系统恢复为 Lagrange–d’Alembert 方程的一阶形式。非完整动力学虽不保持拉格朗日二次型，但底层 Lagrange–Dirac 结构在规范变换（gauge transformation）下保持，表现出自然的规范协变性（gauge covariance）。约化理论导出了 Euler–Poincaré–Dirac 方程及对应的约化变分原理。无限维扩展至理想流体（ideal fluids）时，自然地纳入不可压缩约束（incompressibility constraint）并恢复欧拉方程（Euler equations）。

Conclusion: Lagrange–Dirac 结构为多种动力学系统提供了统一的几何语言和变分框架。理论在带电粒子、电路和速度线性拉格朗日系统等例子中得到了验证，且无限维推广成功应用于理想流体力学。

Abstract: We introduce a Dirac structure on the tangent bundle of a configuration manifold, called a \textit{Lagrange--Dirac structure}, which is naturally induced by the Lagrangian two-form associated with a (possibly degenerate) Lagrangian and a constraint distribution. This structure provides a unified geometric framework for Lagrange--Dirac dynamical systems, encompassing nonholonomic, degenerate Lagrangian, and symmetric systems. In the hyperregular case, the system recovers a first-order formulation of the Lagrange--d'Alembert equations. Although nonholonomic dynamics does not preserve the Lagrangian two-form, we show that the underlying Lagrange--Dirac structure is preserved up to gauge transformations, yielding a natural gauge covariance property.
  We also formulate an intrinsic variational principle directly on the tangent bundle, referred to as the \textit{Lagrange--d'Alembert--Dirac principle}, which recovers Hamilton's principle in the unconstrained case and the Lagrange--d'Alembert principle in the hyperregular constrained case. Furthermore, we develop a reduction theory for systems with Lie group symmetry, deriving a reduced Lagrange--Dirac structure over the Lie algebra that yields the Euler--Poincaré--Dirac equations and a corresponding reduced variational principle. Finally, we illustrate the theory through examples including charged particles, electric circuits, and systems with Lagrangians linear in velocity, and present an infinite-dimensional extension to ideal fluids that naturally incorporates the incompressibility constraint and recovers the Euler equations.

</details>


### [147] [On the Emergence of Discrete Spectrum for Weakly Disordered Schrödinger Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20505)
*Stanislav Molchanov,Oleg Safronov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了受局部负势扰动（localized negative potential）的安德森算子（Anderson operator）的谱性质，精确估计了由吸引势诱导的负本征值（bound states）数量，揭示了随机性如何增强本征值界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对无序系统中吸引势扰动所产生的离散谱（discrete spectrum）缺乏精确的定量估计，本文旨在填补这一空白，建立对负本征值数目的严格上界。

Method: 考虑随机薛定谔算子（random Schrödinger operator）\(H = -Δ + \ve \sum_{n} ω_n χ_n - V\)，其中未受扰的算子呈现无序能量景观；通过分析安德森局域化（Anderson localization）与势的束缚能力（binding capacity）之间的竞争，对离散谱施加定量界限。

Result: 获得了由局部负势扰动诱导的负本征值数目的精确估计（precise estimates），即关于离散谱的定量上界。

Conclusion: 随机性能够增强本征值界限（eigenvalue bounds），这一结果为理解无序系统中的束缚态形成提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate the spectral properties of the Anderson operator perturbed by a localized negative potential, \(-V\). Specifically, we analyze the random Schrödinger operator defined by \(H = -Δ+\ve \sum_{n} ω_n χ_n - V\), where the unperturbed operator exhibits a disordered energy landscape. Our primary focus is to establish precise estimates on the number of negative eigenvalues (bound states) induced by the attractive perturbation. By analyzing the competition between Anderson localization and the binding capacity of the potential, we provide quantitative bounds on the discrete spectrum. These results offer new insights into how randomness enhances the eigenvalue bounds.

### [148] [Unleashing Emergent Fermions with Rydberg Atom Simulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19444)
*Hanteng Wang,Xingyu Li,Shang Liu,Yingfei Gu,Chengshu Li*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出两种利用里德伯原子模拟器（Rydberg atom simulator）的可重构几何特性来表征临界量子多体系统中涌现费米子（emergent fermions）的互补方案：模拟模式中通过组装可展莫比乌斯带几何实现反周期边界条件并测量玻色与费米态的能量比；数字模式中用量子电路执行费米子版的Kibble-Zurek过程，直接探测费米子标度形式，且可重构性带来指数级加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验探测玻色系统中非局域定义的涌现费米子（emergent fermions）是一个公认的困难问题。里德伯原子模拟器（Rydberg atom simulator）因其可重构几何特性而具有独特潜力，但尚未被系统用于解决这一挑战。

Method: 提出两种互补方法：(1) 模拟模式（analog mode）中将里德伯原子组装成可展莫比乌斯带几何，在保持局域耦合条件下实现反周期边界条件（antiperiodic boundary conditions），从而容纳费米子态并进行光谱测量；(2) 数字模式（digital mode）中用量子电路执行费米子版的Kibble-Zurek ramping过程，直接解析费米子标度形式（fermionic scaling form），利用可重构性实现电路深度开销为$O(\log L\log\log L)$的指数级加速。

Result: 模拟模式下，光谱测量可揭示玻色态与费米态之间的普适能量比（universal energy ratios）；数字模式下，Kibble-Zurek过程直接得到费米子标度形式，且可重构性使得电路深度仅需$O(\log L\log\log L)$，实现指数级加速。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了里德伯原子模拟器（Rydberg atom simulator）作为探测非局域定义涌现费米子的独特且强大的实验平台，为临界量子多体系统中这一长期难题提供了可行的实验路径。

Abstract: Rydberg atom simulators, in both analog and digital modes, have attracted significant recent interest due to their versatile geometric reconfigurability. In this work, leveraging this feature, we propose two complementary approaches, one for each mode, to characterize emergent fermions in critical quantum many-body systems. In the analog mode, we assemble the Rydberg atoms in a "developable" (namely, preserving local couplings) Möbius band geometry to realize antiperiodic boundary conditions, where fermionic states reside. Spectroscopic measurement in this sector then reveals universal energy ratios of the bosonic and fermionic states. In the digital mode, we carry out a fermionic version of Kibble-Zurek ramping with a quantum circuit, directly addressing the fermionic scaling form. Reconfigurability allows an exponential speed-up of this task, with an $O(\log L\log\log L)$ circuit-depth overhead. Our work establishes the Rydberg atom simulator as a uniquely powerful platform to attack the notoriously difficult issue of experimentally probing emergent fermions that are nonlocally defined in a bosonic system.

</details>


### [149] [Effects of interaction range on the mean-field dynamics of Bose polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20020)
*Piotr Wysocki,Ubaldo Cavazos Olivas,Marek Tylutki,Krzysztof Jachymski*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究三维玻色极化子（Bose polaron）在有限程相互作用（finite range interactions）和竞争长度尺度（competing length scales）条件下的性质，发现弛豫动力学通过阻尼振荡（damped oscillations）发生，且平衡过程对杂质-环境相互作用的类型敏感；离子-原子类型的相互作用会导致更长的弛豫时间和更显著的振荡，有效质量（effective masses）在两种场景下差异显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究三维玻色极化子问题在有限程相互作用和竞争长度尺度下的性质，特别是静态和非平衡（out of equilibrium）动力学行为，以理解杂质-环境相互作用类型对弛豫过程的影响。

Method: 在杂质参考系中研究系统的静态和非平衡性质，分析杂质与宿主气体之间的动量转移（transfer of momentum），并对比不同杂质-环境相互作用类型（离子-原子系统 vs. 局域相互作用势）的影响。

Result: 弛豫动力学通过杂质速度（impurity velocity）的阻尼振荡发生，振荡行为对相互作用强度存在简单依赖关系；平衡过程对相互作用类型敏感：离子-原子系统在强耦合（strong coupling）区域下呈现更长的弛豫时间和更显著的振荡；两种场景的有效质量差异显著，即使极化子云（polaron cloud）中原子数目相近。

Conclusion: 杂质-环境相互作用的类型（有限程序 vs. 局域势）显著影响玻色极化子的弛豫动力学和有效质量，提示在描述实际物理系统（如离子-原子体系）时需考虑相互作用的有限程特征。

Abstract: We consider the three-dimensional Bose polaron problem in the regime of finite range interactions and competing length scales. Working in the reference frame of the impurity, we study both static and out of equilibrium properties of the system, in particular the transfer of momentum between the impurity and the host gas. We find that relaxation dynamics can occur via damped oscillations of the impurity velocity with simple dependence on the interaction strength. Furthermore, the equilibration process is sensitive to the type of the impurity-bath interaction. Specifically, interatomic forces describing ion-atom systems lead to much longer timescales and more pronounced oscillations in the strong coupling regime with respect to local interaction potentials. We also find that the effective masses can differ by a large amount between the two scenarios, even if the number of atoms in the polaron cloud remains similar for both cases.

</details>

Method: 采用含时Gross-Pitaevskii方程进行解析与数值求解，分析了相互作用BEC在靠近陷阱探测条件下的飞行时间行为。

Abstract: The times of flight of an atomic Bose-Einstein condensate are theoretically investigated in the experimentally unexplored regime corresponding to detection close to the trap of the condensate. For this purpose, a time-dependent Gross-Pitaevskii equation is solved analytically and numerically.

### [151] [Polaronic hybridization of atoms, dimers and trimers in a Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20440)
*Carsten Robens,Arthur Christianen,Alexander Y. Chuang,Huan Q. Bui,Yiming Zhang,Richard Schmidt,Martin Zwierlein*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过射频谱学实验，首次在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中的玻色极化子（Bose polaron）体系中观测到清晰的三体关联信号，并揭示由裸原子、NaK二聚体与Na₂K三聚体相干杂化形成的极化子混合态，该特征可由一个无自由参数的三能级模型描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻色极化子（Bose polaron）问题理论上预言存在由多玻色子与杂质形成束缚态所导致的强关联现象，但此前一直缺乏直接的实验证据。

Method: 实验上采用射频谱学（radiofrequency spectroscopy）技术，将$^{40}$K杂质原子浸入$^{23}$Na的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中，通过测量谱学特征识别极化子杂化态。

Result: 观测到清晰的极化子杂化态，可理解为裸原子、NaK二聚体（dimer）与Na₂K三聚体（trimer）通过与凝聚体之间的相干粒子交换（coherent particle exchange）耦合形成的叠加态。主要谱学特征可由一个无自由参数的三能级模型（three-level model）定量描述。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，凝聚体环境能够相干地杂化不同组成和质量的束缚态，该机制与粒子物理中由卡比博-小林-益川矩阵（Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa matrix, CKM matrix）描述的夸克味混合（quark-flavor mixing）现象具有相似性。

Abstract: The Bose polaron problem of an impurity immersed in a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) has been predicted to feature strong correlations arising from bound states of multiple bosons with the impurity. While direct experimental evidence has so far remained elusive, here we observe clear signatures of three-body correlations in Bose polarons. We perform radiofrequency spectroscopy on $^{40}$K impurities in a BEC of $^{23}$Na and identify polaronic hybrid states that can be understood as superpositions of the bare atom, a NaK dimer and a Na$_2$K trimer, coupled through coherent particle exchange with the condensate. We show that the main spectroscopic features are captured by a simple three-level model without free parameters. Our work shows how a condensate environment can coherently hybridize bound states of different composition and mass, reminiscent of quark-flavor mixing described by the Cabibbo-Kobayashi-Maskawa (CKM) matrix in particle physics.

</details>


### [152] [Smooth time-dependent control of dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20507)
*Chris Whitty,Aitor Alaña,Michele Modugno,Xi Chen,Géza Tóth,Andreas Ruschhaupt,Eugene Ya. Sherman*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用捷径到绝热（shortcuts to adiabaticity）技术，通过时间依赖的散射长度控制，设计从超流（superfluid）到超固体（supersolid）相变的高保真度量子态制备协议，以克服偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中有限时间演化带来的激发问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的超固体相在基态密度上呈现出调制结构，但有限时间演化产生的激发使得该调制基态的制备极具挑战性。因此，需要开发有效的控制协议来抑制激发并实现高保真度的相变过程。

Method: 采用捷径到绝热技术，设计了两种控制协议：一是基于分离变量假设（separable ansatz）的变分方法，利用欧拉-拉格朗日方程（Euler-Lagrange equations）描述超流态的演化；二是直接优化协议，研究从超流到超固体的相变过程。两种方法均通过调节时间依赖的散射长度（time-dependent scattering length）来实现控制。

Result: 分析了所开发协议在不同演化时间下的保真度（fidelity），评估了两种控制方案在抑制激发和实现相变方面的表现。

Conclusion: 利用捷径到绝热技术，通过时间依赖的散射长度控制，可以有效实现偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体从超流到超固体相的高保真度量子态制备，为实验上克服有限时间演化带来的挑战提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We consider protocols for control of dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates where the critical role is played by the long-range anisotropic interatomic magnetic dipole-dipole interaction. The phase diagram of such a condensate has been explored theoretically and experimentally with certain values of the interatomic scattering length corresponding to superfluid and supersolid phases, where supersolidity appears as a modulation in the ground state density. Preparation of this modulated ground state is challenging, since excitations appear as a result of a finite-time evolution required to produce qualitative changes in the wavefunction density. To solve this problem we consider the time-dependent control of a dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate using shortcuts to adiabaticity techniques, concentrating on design of the time-dependent scattering length, a parameter of the system easily tunable by contemporary experiments. The first technique is the variational approach based on the Euler-Lagrange equations for a separable ansatz describing the evolution of the superfluid state. Secondly, we study the transition from superfluid to supersolid using a direct optimization protocol. We discuss the fidelity of the developed protocols in terms of the evolution time.

### [153] [Second order explicit splitting scheme for fluid-poroelastic structure interaction problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19811)
*Yifan Wang,Jeonghun Lee,Suncica Canic*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对流体-多孔弹性结构相互作用（fluid-poroelastic structure interaction）中的显式耦合稳定性问题，提出并严格分析了一种全离散、二阶精度的显式分裂格式（explicit splitting scheme），用于求解固定域上的含时 Stokes-Biot 问题。该方法通过 Robin 重构结合 BDF2 时间步进与 Adams-Bashforth 界面外推，实现了两个子问题的独立并行求解，并在抛物型 CFL 条件下证明了稳定性和先验误差估计。数值实验验证了二阶时间收敛与最优阶空间收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体-多孔弹性结构相互作用问题中，显式处理 Stokes-Biot 界面耦合条件（Stokes-Biot interface coupling condition）易导致数值不稳定，且现有方法在精度与可证明性方面存在不足。因此，需要开发一种既高效又具有严格理论保证的显式分裂算法。

Method: 该方法采用 BDF2 时间离散结合二阶 Adams-Bashforth 界面外推，并通过 Robin 重构（Robin reformulation）解耦界面条件，形成 Stokes 子问题与 Biot 子问题独立并行的分区算法（partitioned algorithm）。分析方面，利用 BDF2 能量恒等式（BDF2 energy identities）、界面项的尖锐分解以及离散迹估计（discrete trace estimates）建立稳定性，并通过基于 Fortin 投影（流体变量）和 Ritz 型投影（多孔弹性变量）的投影框架推导先验误差估计。

Result: 在抛物型 CFL 条件下建立了封闭的稳定性界（closed stability bound）。先验误差估计表明，流体速度、结构速度、孔隙压力（pore pressure）和弹性位移的总误差在整体能量范数（bulk energy norms）中由网格尺寸的 k 次方（k 从 1 到 3）与时间步长的平方之和的常数倍控制。数值实验证实了二阶时间收敛与最优阶空间收敛，并在移动域 Navier-Stokes 算例中展示了方法的适用性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的显式分裂格式兼具理论严谨性与实际可用性：严格的稳定性与误差分析为其提供了可靠性保证，而数值结果则验证了理论预期的收敛阶和算法在更复杂流动场景（如移动域 Navier-Stokes）中的扩展潜力。

Abstract: Efficient and provably accurate partitioned methods for fluid-poroelastic structure interaction remain challenging because explicit treatment of the Stokes-Biot interface coupling condition can compromise stability. In this work, we develop and analyze a fully discrete, second-order, explicit splitting scheme for the time-dependent Stokes-Biot problem on fixed domains. The method combines BDF2 time stepping with second-order Adams-Bashforth extrapolation of interface data through a Robin reformulation, yielding a partitioned algorithm in which the Stokes and Biot subproblems are solved independently and in parallel at each time step.
  The main analytical contribution is a rigorous stability and error analysis for this second-order explicit coupling strategy. Using BDF2 energy identities, a sharp decomposition of the extrapolated interface terms, and discrete trace estimates, we prove a closed stability bound under a parabolic CFL condition. We then derive an a priori error estimate through a projection-based framework using a Fortin projection for the fluid variables and Ritz-type projections for the poroelastic variables. The analysis identifies consistency defects from BDF2 time discretization, Adams-Bashforth interface extrapolation, and the projected kinematic relation. It shows that the total errors in fluid velocity, structure velocity, pore pressure, and elastic displacement are bounded by C times the sum of the kth power of the mesh size and the square of the time step, for k from 1 to 3, in bulk energy norms.
  Numerical experiments with manufactured solutions confirm second-order temporal convergence and optimal-order spatial convergence. We also include a moving-domain example with Navier-Stokes fluid flow, demonstrating applicability beyond the fixed-domain Stokes-Biot setting analyzed.

</details>


### [154] [Moreau-Yosida-based Kohn-Sham Inversion for Periodic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19471)
*Vebjørn H. Bakkestuen,Michael F. Herbst,Vegard Falmår,Markus Penz,Andre Laestadius*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文在Moreau-Yosida正则化密度泛函理论框架下，研究了周期系统的密度-势反演问题，从理论和数值两方面进行了分析，证明了非相互作用动能泛函在所选拓扑下的下半连续性，并利用近端映射实现了反演方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）中，从给定电子密度恢复出对应的外势（即密度-势反演）是一个基础但困难的逆问题。本文旨在为周期系统（periodic systems）建立一套严格的数学框架，以解决Moreau-Yosida正则化DFT中的反演问题。

Method: 研究在周期齐次Sobolev空间（periodic homogeneous Sobolev space）中构建理论框架，利用Moreau-Yosida正则化技术处理密度泛函理论中的不光滑性。通过极限过程恢复Kohn-Sham理论中的交换关联势（exchange-correlation potential）。核心分析工具是证明非相互作用动能泛函（non-interacting kinetic-energy functional）在所选拓扑下的下半连续性（lower semicontinuity），并引入近端映射（proximal mapping）及其算法实现作为反演方案的核心。

Result: 数值实验展示了该方法在Kohn-Sham方程和Gross-Pitaevskii方程（Gross-Pitaevskii equations）上的性能与性质，验证了所提反演方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文为周期系统中密度-势反演问题提供了严格的理论保证和可行的数值算法，通过正则化框架和下半连续性证明，确保了反演过程的数学严谨性。

Abstract: Density-potential inversion for periodic systems within Moreau-Yosida-regularised density-functional theory is investigated, both theoretically and numerically. We develop the framework in a periodic homogeneous Sobolev space and use it to recover the exchange-correlation potential of Kohn-Sham theory through a limiting procedure. A key analytical ingredient is the proof of lower semicontinuity of the non-interacting kinetic-energy functional in the chosen topology. The proximal mapping, together with its algorithmic evaluation, plays a central role in the resulting inversion scheme. Numerical experiments illustrate the performance and properties of the method for both the Kohn-Sham and Gross-Pitaevskii equations.

### [155] [Variational Polaron Theory for Ground States of Strongly Coupled Light-Matter and Electron-Phonon Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19748)
*Nguyen Thanh Phuc*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于态依赖极化子变换（state-dependent polaron transformation）的非微扰变分基态框架，结合乘积态假设（product-state ansatz）和二阶微扰修正（second-order perturbative correction），在极强耦合（ultrastrong-coupling）体系中实现精确的基态建模，Dicke模型和Holstein模型的基准测试显示能量误差分别低于0.2%和0.5%。该框架在弱耦合和强耦合极限下均渐近正确，在固定极化子变换最不可靠的中间耦合区间依然保持高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强光-物质耦合与电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）会生成由虚玻色子激发（virtual bosonic excitations）修饰的基态，使得裸态截断（bare-state truncation）和微扰方法（perturbative approach）在极强耦合（ultrastrong-coupling）区间变得不可靠，因此需要一种非微扰的变分框架来准确描述此类系统。

Method: 提出一种基于态依赖极化子变换（state-dependent polaron transformation）的非微扰变分方法，结合乘积态假设（product-state ansatz）和对残余物质-玻色子纠缠（residual matter-boson entanglement）的二阶微扰修正（second-order perturbative correction）。通过优化变换框架，在无限耦合极限（infinite coupling）下使变换后的框架渐近解耦：线性耦合项被抵消，且非对角物质跃迁（off-diagonal matter transitions）被位移振子重叠（displaced-oscillator overlaps）所抑制。

Result: Dicke模型基准测试复现了基态能量、量子保真度（fidelity）和超辐射相变（superradiant transition），二阶能量误差低于0.2%；Holstein模型基准测试误差低于0.5%，并阐明了平移对称性（translational symmetry）对波函数质量的影响。

Conclusion: 该穿靴基态框架（dressed-basis framework）能够对强耦合光-物质系统和电子-声子系统进行非微扰建模，在弱耦合、强耦合和中间耦合区间均保持高精度，为极强耦合体系的研究提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Strong light-matter and electron-phonon coupling generate ground states dressed by virtual bosonic excitations, making bare-state truncations and perturbative treatments unreliable in the ultrastrong-coupling regime. We introduce a nonperturbative variational ground-state framework based on a state-dependent polaron transformation, combined with a product-state ansatz and a second-order perturbative correction for residual matter-boson entanglement. We show that the optimized transformed frame becomes asymptotically decoupled at infinite coupling, because the leading linear coupling is canceled while off-diagonal matter transitions are suppressed by displaced-oscillator overlaps. The approach is asymptotically correct in both weak- and strong-coupling limits and remains accurate in the intermediate regime, where fixed polaron transformations are least reliable. Dicke-model benchmarks reproduce ground-state energies, fidelities, and the superradiant transition, with second-order energy errors below 0.2%. Holstein-model benchmarks yield errors below 0.5% and clarify how translational symmetry affects wave-function quality. This dressed-basis framework enables nonperturbative modeling of strongly coupled light-matter and electron-phonon systems.

### [156] [Ricci flow for the Bures--Helstrom qubit metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19493)
*Andrew Lesniewski*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子比特（qubit）状态空间上Bures–Helstrom度量的里奇流（Ricci flow），证明了该度量是爱因斯坦度量（Einstein metric），其几何流作为收缩自相似解（homothetic shrinker）演化，并在有限时间内通过塌缩极限离开非退化黎曼度量锥（cone of nondegenerate Riemannian metrics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bures–Helstrom度量是量子比特状态空间上最小的单调黎曼度量（monotone Riemannian metric），与量子费舍尔信息（quantum Fisher information）密切相关。本文旨在明确描述其里奇流演化行为，并分析其在几何流框架下的动力学性质。

Method: 采用旋转对称规范（rotationally symmetric gauge）下的坐标表述，将里奇流表述为径向时滞（radial lapse）与扭曲因子（warping factor）的耦合系统；通过Hamilton–DeTurck规范选择（gauge choice）将其约化为单个标量方程。进一步在DeTurck移动标架中，将平方扭曲函数满足的方程化为线性受迫热方程（linear forced heat equation）。

Result: Bures–Helstrom度量为爱因斯坦度量，其几何流为同伦收缩自相似解g(t)=(1-4t)g_BH，标量曲率为6/(1-4t)，灭绝时间（extinction time）T=1/4。度量在t<T时保持在单调锥内，仅在塌缩极限（collapsed limit）下离开非退化黎曼度量锥。体积归一化流（volume-normalized flow）下该度量为不动点，线性化算子为平移后的圆球拉普拉斯算子Δ_{S^3}+3，谱为σ_ℓ=-(ℓ-1)(ℓ+3)，去除缩放模（scaling mode）后的能隙（spectral gap）为5。

Conclusion: Bures–Helstrom度量在里奇流下的演化具有精确解析形式，揭示了量子几何信息与几何流之间的内在联系。该度量作为体积归一化流的不动点及其谱分析，为量子信息几何中的稳定性研究提供了基础。

Abstract: The Bures--Helstrom metric is the minimal monotone Riemannian metric on the state space of a qubit. With the quantum Fisher normalization used here, it identifies the Bloch ball with a geodesic hemisphere of the unit round three--sphere. We describe its Ricci flow explicitly. In a general rotationally symmetric gauge the flow is a coupled system for the radial lapse and warping factor; a single scalar equation appears only after a Hamilton--DeTurck gauge choice. In the corresponding moving DeTurck frame the squared warping function $Ψ=Φ^2$ satisfies the linear forced heat equation \begin{equation*} D_tΨ=Ψ_{ss}-2, \end{equation*} while the fixed-lapse coordinate form contains the associated transport term. Since the Bures--Helstrom metric is Einstein, the geometric flow itself is the homothetic shrinker \begin{equation*} g(t)=(1-4t)g_{\mathrm{BH}}, \end{equation*} with scalar curvature $6/(1-4t)$ and extinction time $T=1/4$. Thus the metric remains inside the monotone cone for all $t<T$ and leaves the cone of nondegenerate Riemannian metrics only through the collapsed limit. We also record the volume--normalized flow, for which the Bures--Helstrom metric is a fixed point. Its linearization is the shifted round--sphere Laplacian $Δ_{\mathbb S^3}+3$, with spectrum \begin{equation*} σ_\ell=-(\ell-1)(\ell+3), \end{equation*} and spectral gap $5$ after removal of the scaling mode.

</details>
