### [157] [High-Power Laser Drives Motion in Ultra-thin Photonic Crystal Lightsails via Radiation Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20149)
*Lucas Norder,Ata Keşkekler,Richard A. Norte*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报告了迄今最大的亚波长系留光帆：纳米级厚度、毫米级宽度的氮化硅薄膜，其上图案化了数十亿个孔洞。该结构通过共振光子模式实现99%反射率，在极低面密度下承受太阳表面量级的激光强度，并产生高达1.75微米的辐射压位移，比此前光帆光机械响应提升了50,000倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光驱动光帆（laser-driven lightsail）是加速超轻型航天器至高速的一种有前景的途径，但其实现需要在极低质量、大面积照明和高功率密度耐受性三者间取得平衡，此前尚无实验能将所有约束结合到单一结构中。

Method: 制备了纳米级厚度、毫米级宽度的氮化硅（silicon nitride）薄膜，并图案化数十亿个亚波长孔洞，通过共振光子模式（resonant photonic modes）实现高反射率。

Result: 该光帆在亚波长厚度下实现99%反射率，结合了超低面密度（areal density）与高反射性；辐射压位移（radiation-pressure displacement）达1.75微米，较此前提升50,000倍；在太阳表面量级的定向激光强度下仍保持高反射率。

Conclusion: 该工作为高功率纳米光子学（high-power nanophotonics）、定向能系统（directed-energy systems）和光驱动推进（light-driven propulsion）建立了实验平台，界定了超薄光子材料在强光加载下的实际极限。

Abstract: Laser-driven lightsails have emerged as a promising route for accelerating ultralight spacecraft to high speeds using beamed optical energy. Realizing this concept pushes the limits of light-matter interaction, materials science, structural engineering, and nanomechanical design. A central challenge is to create nanophotonic reflectors that combine ultralow mass, large illuminated area, and survival under high optical power densities. No previous experiment has combined these constraints in a single structure sufficient to produce measurable radiation-pressure displacement. Here, we report the largest subwavelength tethered lightsails to date: nanoscale-thickness, millimeter-wide silicon nitride membranes patterned with billions of holes. Despite their subwavelength thickness, they achieve 99% reflection through resonant photonic modes, combining ultralow areal density with high reflectivity. Their compliance enables radiation-pressure displacements of up to 1.75 micrometer, a 50,000-fold increase over previous lightsail optomechanical responses. These thin mirrors are shown to withstand and maintain high reflectivity under directed laser intensities comparable to optical intensities at the surface of the Sun. Together, these results establish a testbed for high-power nanophotonics, directed-energy systems, and light-driven propulsion, defining the practical limits of ultrathin photonic materials under intense optical loading.

</details>


### [158] [Plasma Etch Process Optimization for Photonic-Grade Diamond-on-Insulator Substrates and Thickness Evaluation using Colorimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20412)
*Tianyin Chena,Alessio Mirandaa,Leyla Ramia,Ryoichi Ishihara,Salahuddin Nur*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种等离子体刻蚀工艺，用于制备大面积的薄膜金刚石绝缘体（DOI）衬底，并在此衬底上制造了自支撑的光子芯片。结合比色法厚度评估方法，为金刚石纳米光子器件的可扩展制造和集成量子系统提供了有效平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石色心量子比特（diamond color-center qubit）与光子电路集成具有高保真度初始化和读取等优势，但异质外延生长的单晶金刚石（SCD）和光子级金刚石绝缘体（DOI）衬底尺寸有限，难以与现有制造工艺集成，限制了大规模应用。

Method: 开发了一种电感耦合等离子体反应离子刻蚀（ICP-RIE）配方，用于减薄直接键合的(100)SCD薄膜；利用比色法（colorimetry）分析金刚石在SiO₂上的可见度，通过标准光学显微镜图像以5 nm分辨率自动外推金刚石厚度，并与白光干涉仪（WLI）测量结果进行验证。

Result: 成功将10 μm厚的金刚石板减薄至≤300 nm，在0.5×0.5 mm²面积上厚度均匀约300 nm、表面粗糙度<0.5 nm，且键合界面保持完整。在DOI衬底上通过标准两步光刻工艺制造了金刚石光子芯片，无需复杂薄膜转移或 pedestal 形成。比色法厚度评估与WLI测量结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 所开发的DOI衬底制备工艺和比色法厚度评估方法为金刚石纳米光子器件的可扩展制造提供了有效平台，为大规模集成量子系统铺平了道路。

Abstract: Diamond color-center qubits integrated with photonic circuits can be initialized, manipulated, entangled, and read individually with high fidelity, making them attractive for large-scale modular quantum computers, quantum networks, and distributed quantum sensing. However, the limited size of heteroepitaxially grown single-crystal diamond (SCD) and photonic-grade diamond-on-insulator (DOI) substrates remains a challenge for integration with existing manufacturing processes. Here, we develop a plasma etch recipe to thin direct-bonded (100) SCD membranes (<50 $μ$m) into large-area, thin-film DOI substrates, and demonstrate free-standing photonic chiplets fabricated from the resulting DOI. The ICP-RIE recipe preserves diamond bonding, provides sufficient micromasking and surface-quality control, and enables thin-film DOI manufacture. We thin a 10 $μ$m diamond plate bonded to SiO$_2$/Si and obtain a photonic-grade DOI substrate with diamond thickness $\leq$300 nm. The DOI film is around 300 nm thick over 0.5 $\times$ 0.5 mm$^2$, with surface roughness < 0.5 nm, while the bonding interface remains intact. Diamond photonic chiplets are fabricated on this DOI substrate using a standard two-step lithography process, without complex thin-film transfer, under-etching, or pedestal formation. We also present a colorimetric study of diamond visibility on SiO$_2$ and quantify color differences across thicknesses in common colorimetric spaces. This analysis enables automatic diamond-thickness extrapolation from standard optical microscope images with 5 nm resolution, in good agreement with white-light interferometry (WLI) measurements. The DOI substrate and colorimetric thickness-evaluation method provide an effective fabrication platform and reliable validation route for scalable manufacturing of diamond nanophotonic devices, opening a path toward large-scale integrated quantum systems.

</details>

### [159] [Optical spin injection in graphane and fluorographene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19571)
*Angélica Marina López-Martínez,César Castillo-Quevedo,Cesar Camas-Flores,Analila Luna-Valenzuela,Jose Luis Cabellos*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）研究了石墨烷（graphane）和氟化石墨烯（fluorographene）在不同化学计量构型下的光学自旋注入响应，发现氟化石墨烯之字形（zigzag）构型在带边及宽光子能量范围内可获得高达98%的自旋极化电子，且响应几乎完全来源于顶部价带中C-p和F-p混合态的带间跃迁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定石墨烷和氟化石墨烯的何种化学计量构型能产生最强的自旋极化（spin polarization）程度。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行理论计算，并通过带分辨分解方案（band-resolved decomposition scheme）对价带和导带跃迁的贡献进行分析。

Result: 氟化石墨烯之字形（zigzag）构型在带边及宽范围激发光子能量下实现了98%的自旋极化电子，其自旋极化响应度（${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$）表现最佳；其他构型的${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$约为83–100%，但仅限于窄能量范围。低自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）下，极化度在宽能量范围接近100%；高耦合下强响应仅出现在窄能量区域。此外，氟化石墨烯zigzag构型的${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$谱几乎完全来自仅涉及顶部价带（C-p和F-p混合态）的跃迁。

Conclusion: 氟化石墨烯之字形构型因其独特的电子结构，在宽光子能量范围内实现接近完全的自旋极化，是光学自旋注入应用的潜在候选材料；自旋-轨道耦合强度对极化响应的能量范围具有显著调控作用。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the optical spin-injection response in different stoichiometric configurations of graphane and fluorographene using density functional theory. Our goal is to determine which configuration yields the strongest degree of spin polarization. The results show that the fluorographene zigzag configuration yields the best degree of spin polarization response (${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$), with 98\% spin polarized electrons at the band edge and over a wide range of excitation photon energies. In contrast, other graphane and fluorographene configurations achieve a ${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$ of roughly 83--100\%, but only within a limited photon-excitation energy range. In structures with low spin-orbit coupling, the degree of spin polarization is close to 100\% over a wide range of photon energies. For higher spin-orbit coupling, this strong response appears, but only in a narrow photon energy region. Additionally, under the band-resolved decomposition scheme, the contributions of different band-to-band transitions to the ${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$ spectrum are identified by summing only the selected valence and conduction bands. Our findings show that almost the entire ${\cal DSP}^{\mathrm{z}}$ spectrum of the fluorographene zigzag configuration comes from transitions that involve only the top valence band, which is a mixture of C--p and F--p states.

</details>


### [160] [Boltzmann-constrained extraction of spin splitting and momentum relaxation in d-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19785)
*Y. X. Gao,Z. W. Fan,Q. S. Yao,Y. D. Ji,H. Geng*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文针对交变磁体（altermagnet）中自旋分裂与散射的不可区分性问题，提出了一种基于物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural network, PINN）的玻尔兹曼方程求解方法，利用费米能级依赖的输运特性与严格物理约束实现自旋分裂与散射参量的分离，在中等测量噪声下仍能达到亚百分比的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）具有无需自旋-轨道耦合即可实现自旋分裂（spin-split）的电子结构，但实验输运测量通常将本征自旋分裂与外禀散射贡献混合在一起，难以区分二者。该不可区分性（identifiability problem）严重阻碍了对交变磁体本征输运性质的准确表征。

Method: 在一个统一的半经典框架下，从弹道输运到扩散输运范围内分析二维d波交变磁体。构建一个物理信息神经网络（PINN），使其充当可微的玻尔兹曼方程求解器（differentiable Boltzmann solver），严格施加接触注入、局域粒子守恒和全局电流连续性约束，并利用稀疏的电导谱驱动模型，以解锁耦合参数。

Result: 交变磁耦合强度α与动量弛豫时间τ₀在纵向电导中相互补偿，形成严重的参数简并（parameter degeneracy）。自旋依赖的费米面各向异性产生显著的尺寸效应，两个自旋通道在相同器件几何中展现出截然不同的有效弛豫长度。PINN方法成功解耦上述参数，在中等测量噪声下仍能达到亚百分比的精度。

Conclusion: 结合输运的费米能级依赖性与严格物理约束，是实现交变磁导体中自旋分裂与散射分离的稳健途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit spin-split electronic structure without requiring spin-orbit coupling, but transport measurements generally mix intrinsic spin splitting with extrinsic scattering. We examine this identifiability problem for a two-dimensional d-wave altermagnet within a unified semiclassical framework spanning ballistic to diffusive transport. The spin-dependent Fermi-surface anisotropy produces a pronounced size effect, where vastly different longitudinal velocities cause the two spin channels to exhibit markedly different effective relaxation lengths within the same device geometry. However, the altermagnetic coupling $α$ and the momentum relaxation time $τ_0$ strongly compensate each other in longitudinal conductance, creating a severe parameter degeneracy. To lift this degeneracy, we formulate a physics-informed neural network (PINN) to act as a differentiable Boltzmann solver that strictly enforces contact injection, local particle conservation, and global current continuity. Driven by sparse conductance spectra, this neural solver leverages the Fermi-level dependence of transport to unlock the coupled parameters simultaneously, achieving sub-percent accuracy even under moderate measurement noise. These results show that combining the Fermi-level dependence of transport with strict physical constraints provides a robust route to separating spin splitting from scattering in altermagnetic conductors.

</details>


### [161] [Symmetry enforced quantum spin Hall effect in Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19903)
*Fanzheng Chen,Lixin Zhang,Shuaishuai Niu,Junfeng Ren,Weijiang Gong,Xiangru Kong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过对称性分析和第一性原理计算，将量子自旋霍尔效应（QSHE）的研究范围从非磁性材料拓展至交错磁体（altermagnets），揭示了自旋-谷锁定或自旋-谷-层锁定的普遍存在，并预言了单层Nb2SeTeO和双层Hf3Se3Te2分别具有不同锁定特征的交错磁QSHE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子自旋霍尔效应（QSHE）的研究受限于非磁性材料，因为磁性无序会破坏拓扑量子态的稳定性。本文旨在将QSHE的研究范畴拓展至交错磁体（altermagnets），探索磁性体系中拓扑相的新可能性。

Method: 首先建立对称性约束条件，识别所有能实现交错磁QSHE（altermagnetic QSHE）的磁点群（magnetic point groups）；随后通过对称性分析揭示自旋-谷锁定（spin-valley locking）或自旋-谷-层锁定（spin-valley-layer locking）的普遍存在；最后结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与理论模型进行验证。

Result: 单层Nb2SeTeO表现出具有自旋-谷锁定特征的交错磁QSHE；双层Hf3Se3Te2展现出具有自旋-谷-层锁定特征的交错磁QSHE。能带反转（band inversion）与自旋-谷锁定的协同相互作用共同产生了螺旋边缘态（helical edge states）。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了交错磁性与量子自旋霍尔拓扑相之间的内在对称性关联，为磁性拓扑系统的研究和下一代自旋电子学（spintronic）器件的开发提供了新的理论视角和研究平台。

Abstract: The quantum spin Hall effect (QSHE) has attracted widespread attention due to its dissipationless transport, which is protected by non-trivial topological invariants and helical edge states. Because even weak magnetic disorder can destroy the stability of topological quantum states, current research on the QSHE has primarily focused on non-magnetic materials. In this work, we extend the research scope of the QSHE to altermagnets. We establish the relevant symmetry constraints and identify all magnetic point groups that can realize the altermagnetic QSHE. Symmetry analysis reveals that pronounced spin-valley locking or spin-valley-layer locking universally exists in these systems. The concerted interaction between band inversion and spin-valley locking collectively gives rise to the helical edge states. Using first-principles calculations and theoretical models, we demonstrate that monolayer Nb2SeTeO exhibits an altermagnetic QSHE characterized by spin-valley locking, while bilayer Hf3Se3Te2 manifests an altermagnetic QSHE featuring spin-valley-layer locking. This work clarifies the intrinsic symmetry correlation between altermagnetism and quantum spin Hall topological phases, providing a brand-new theoretical perspective and research platform for exploring magnetic topological systems and developing next-generation spintronic devices

</details>


### [162] [Designing all possible logic gates in phononic lattices: A theoretical study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19973)
*Swaraj Biswas,Santanu K. Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用声子环（phononic ring）系统在纳米尺度实现热逻辑门（thermal logic gates）的方案，通过在环附近放置原子位点作为输入，基于非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's function formalism）计算声子透射概率作为逻辑输出，成功实现了全部七种标准逻辑门操作，并在宽频范围内验证了其有效性与普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纳米尺度实现热逻辑门是声子学（phononics）和热计算领域的重要目标，现有方案在逻辑门种类覆盖和频率普适性方面仍存在局限，亟需提出一种能够实现全部标准逻辑操作且具有广泛适用性的新方案。

Method: 采用声子环系统，在环附近放置两个原子位点作为两输入逻辑门的输入端，放置单个邻近位点作为单输入逻辑门输入端；逻辑输出编码为声子透射概率（phonon transmission probability），并基于非平衡格林函数形式对其进行计算；通过适当调节环-电极结（ring-electrode junction）构型，实现不同逻辑门操作。

Result: 成功实现了全部七种标准逻辑门，包括三种基本逻辑门（fundamental gates）和四种组合逻辑门（combinatorial gates），且这些逻辑操作在不同声子频率区间（phonon frequency regimes）均可实现；所提出的逻辑操作在宽频声子频率范围内保持有效。

Conclusion: 该方案在宽声子频率范围内均能实现可靠的热逻辑门操作，表明所提出的方法具有良好的通用性和可靠性，为纳米尺度热逻辑器件的设计提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We propose a scheme for realizing thermal logic gates at the nanoscale using a phononic ring system. Two atomic sites, placed in close proximity to the ring, serve as the inputs for two-input logic operations, while a single proximity site is employed for single-input logic functionality. The logic output is encoded in the phonon transmission probability, which is calculated within the framework of non-equilibrium Green's function formalism. By appropriately tuning the ring-electrode junction configuration, all seven standard logic gates, comprising three fundamental and four combinatorial operations, are successfully realized in different phonon frequency regimes. Our results suggest that the proposed logic operations remain valid over a broad range of phonon frequencies, highlighting the generality and reliability of the proposed approach.

</details>


### [163] [Tunneling-induced translation of intact $π$-radical clusters on Au(111)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20038)
*Jacob D. Teeter,Kateryna Averchenko,Maximilian Eliasch,Stefan Müllegger*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在6.2 K低温下使用STM对Au(111)表面上由三个α,γ-双二苯基-β-苯基烯丙基（BDPA）分子自组装形成的三元团簇进行探针诱导的平移与旋转操纵，并验证团簇结构的完整性维持。通过持续且重复的团簇拖拽操作，构建多个团簇的人工组装体。

Result: 三元BDPA自由基团簇在针尖诱导的平移和旋转过程中，其自然团簇结构保持完整。成功地实现了团簇的持续和重复拖拽，并以此构建了由多个团簇组成的人工组装体。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了低温STM可对表面π自由基团簇进行整体可控操纵，为表面自旋组装体的创建与研究开辟了新的可能性。

Abstract: The scanning tunneling microscope (STM) is a powerful tool for investigating and manipulating molecules on surfaces. We demonstrate with a low-temperature STM operated at 6.2 K the controlled manipulation of ternary clusters of persistent molecular $π$ radicals as a whole. The ternary clusters $-$ each self-assembled from three $α,γ$-bisdiphenylene-$β$-phenylallyl (BDPA) molecules on Au(111) $-$ maintain their natural cluster structure throughout tip-induced translation and rotation relative to the surface. Sustained and repeated dragging of radical clusters is shown to facilitate the construction of artificial assemblies of several clusters. Our results provide new opportunities for the creation and investigation of radical-based spin assemblies on surfaces.

### [164] [Electric-field-driven magnetic switching and tightly bound interlayer excitons in bilayer CrSBr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20159)
*Xiubin Li,Yu Sun,Xuanji Wang,Chunyan Wang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Sheng Liu,Ting Yu,Liang Li,Tao Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在双层CrSBr（一种环境稳定的二维范德华反铁磁体）中，通过电场驱动实现了反铁磁态与铁磁态之间的可逆切换，揭示了线性磁电效应与电场调控层间交换耦合两种共存机制，为低功耗自旋光电器件提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在二维范德华磁体中实现电场对磁有序（magnetic order）的控制是低功耗自旋技术（spin-based technologies）的核心目标。尽管CrSBr因其强磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）和稳健的激子-自旋耦合（exciton-spin coupling）被视为理想平台，但此前尚未实现对其磁相的电场的确定性控制。

Method: 采用双栅极（dual-gated）结构的双层CrSBr器件，在不进行有意载流子掺杂（intentional carrier doping）的条件下施加电场；同时利用光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）测量表征层间激子（interlayer exciton）的性质，并通过电场依赖的磁相变（magnetic phase transition）分析其作用机制。

Result: 实现了电场驱动的反铁磁态（antiferromagnetic state）与铁磁态（ferromagnetic state）之间的可逆切换。光致发光测量发现了一种紧密结合的层间激子，其本征偶极矩（intrinsic dipole moment）仅为约1 e·Å。电场依赖的磁相变揭示了两种共存机制：反铁磁态下的线性磁电效应（linear magnetoelectric effect）以及电场调控的层间交换耦合（interlayer exchange coupling），两者的相互作用导致了临界磁场（critical magnetic field）的非对称演化。

Conclusion: 研究确立了双层CrSBr作为一种有望用于电控自旋-光电子功能（spin-optoelectronic functionalities）的二维材料，为低功耗自旋基技术提供了新的物理机制和实验基础。

Abstract: Electric field control of magnetic order in two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals magnets is a central goal for low-power spin-based technologies. In the ambient-stable antiferromagnet CrSBr, strong magnetic anisotropy and robust exciton-spin coupling provide a favorable platform, yet deterministic electric field control of its magnetic phases has not been achieved. Here we demonstrate electric-field-driven reversible switching between antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic states in dual-gated bilayer CrSBr without intentional carrier doping. In parallel, photoluminescence measurements resolve a tightly bound interlayer exciton with an intrinsic dipole moment of only ~1 e angstrom. The electric field dependence of the magnetic phase transition reveals two coexisting mechanisms: a linear magnetoelectric effect in the antiferromagnetic state and an electric-field-modulated interlayer exchange coupling. Their interplay accounts for the asymmetric evolution of the critical magnetic field. Our results establish bilayer CrSBr as a promising 2D material for electrically controlled spin-optoelectronic functionalities.

</details>


### [165] [Transient triplet blockade in Andreev junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20170)
*R. Taranko,J. Baranski,A. Jankiewicz,K. Wrzesniewski,I. Weymann,T. Domanski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了超导体-正常金属引线间的双量子点串联结中，在非平衡条件下出现的时变三重组态（triplet configuration），分析了该组态对亚能隙电荷输运的抑制效应及其时间演化特征，并指出其对超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）操作的潜在意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡条件下双量子点系统中三重组态（triplet configuration）的时变行为及其对亚能隙（subgap）电荷输运的影响，为超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）的操作提供理论基础。

Method: 采用解析和数值计算方法，分析初始条件或外加磁场（external magnetic field）下三重组态（triplet configuration）的临时出现及其时域演化特征，并对时间尺度进行估算。

Result: 当两个量子点均被相同自旋（identical spin）的电子单占据时，点内电子配对（on-dot electron pairing）被抑制，显著影响亚能隙（subgap）电荷输运；解析和数值计算给出了三重组态（triplet configuration）演化的特征时间尺度，该特征可在时间分辨隧穿测量（time-resolved tunneling measurements）中观测到。

Conclusion: 三重组态（triplet configuration）的非平衡特征可能与常规和/或拓扑（topological）实现的超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）操作相关。

Abstract: We study the time-dependent triplet configuration, appearing under nonequilibrium conditions in a nanoscopic junction with two quantum dots coupled in series between superconductor and normal metallic lead. We show that in the situation, when both quantum dots are singly occupied by identical spin electrons, the on-dot electron pairing is suppressed what substantially affects the subgap charge transport. We investigate processes in which such configuration can be temporarily encountered, either due to the initial conditions or by imposing the external magnetic field. Our analytical and numerical calculations provide estimations for the temporal scales, characterizing evolution of the triplet configuration which could be manifested in the time-resolved tunneling measurements. Such nonequilibrium features of the triplet configuration might be relevant to operations on superconducting qubits, in their conventional and/or topological realizations.

### [166] [Diagnosing the origin of quantum oscillation beating in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20339)
*Akash Adhikary,Sunit Das,Divya Sahani,Aveek Bid,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了石墨烯基六角晶格系统中磁量子振荡拍频节点的载流子密度与磁场标度关系，通过区分赝磁场、谷不平衡、自旋-轨道耦合能隙等不同机制，给出定量约束条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯基六角系统中存在多种导致磁量子振荡（magnetic quantum oscillations）拍频（beating）的物理机制，包括应变诱导的赝磁场（pseudomagnetic field）、不平衡的谷布居（valley population）、谷依赖能移、自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）导致的能带劈裂以及Kekulé畸变（Kekulé distortion），需要一种方法区分这些机制的贡献。

Method: 基于Onsager量子化关系（Onsager's quantization relation）出发，推导拍频节点（beating nodes）的临界载流子密度$N_c$与临界磁场$B_c$之间的标度关系（scaling relations）。

Result: 赝磁场给出$N_c \propto B_c^2$的标度关系，而密度无关的谷不平衡给出$N_c \propto B_c$。Zeeman型自旋-轨道耦合导致的Dirac能隙也给出二次方标度，但节点序列不同：赝磁场下$N_{c,j} \propto (2j+1) B_{c,j}^2$，而能隙下$N_{c,j} \propto (2j+1)^2 B_{c,j}^2$，其中$j$为拍频节点指标。

Conclusion: 这些结果为石墨烯基系统中谷依赖和自旋依赖的能带劈裂的不同微观起源提供了定量约束条件。

Abstract: Magnetic quantum oscillations are usually periodic in inverse magnetic field, and their amplitude can show beating when two nearby frequencies interfere. In graphene-based hexagonal systems, such beating can arise from strain-induced pseudomagnetic fields, unequal valley populations, valley-dependent energy shifts, spin-orbit coupling-induced band splitting, or Kekulé distortions. Here, we show that the carrier density and magnetic field dependence of the beating nodes can distinguish these mechanisms. Starting from Onsager's quantization relation, we derive scaling relations for the critical carrier density $N_c$ for the beating nodes as a function of critical magnetic field $B_c$. A pseudomagnetic field gives $N_c\propto B_c^2$, whereas a density-independent valley imbalance gives $N_c\propto B_c$. A constant Dirac-band energy splitting by Zeeman-like spin-orbit coupling also gives quadratic field scaling, but with a different node sequence: $N_{c,j}\propto(2j+1)B_{c,j}^2$ for a pseudomagnetic field and $N_{c,j}\propto(2j+1)^2B_{c,j}^2$ for energy splitting, where $j$ labels the beating node indices. These results provide quantitative constraints on different microscopic origins of valley- and spin-dependent band splittings in graphene-based systems.

</details>


### [167] [Charge imprinting biases topology of correlated insulator in hBN-aligned rhombohedral multilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20377)
*Lei Qiao,Xin Lu,Fu-Chun Zhang,Jianpeng Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）计算，揭示了菱面体多层石墨烯-六方氮化硼（RMG-hBN）体系中，价带电荷纹理（valence-band charge texture）作为远程莫尔界面（remote moiré interface）调控关联拓扑（correlated topology）的微观机制：hBN排列通过电荷印记（charge imprinting）效应，作用于远离界面的传导电子，决定绝缘态是平庸（trivial）还是陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 明确菱面体多层石墨烯（rhombohedral multilayer graphene）与六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）对齐体系中，hBN堆叠在关联陈相（correlated Chern phases）中的微观作用尚不清楚，尤其当活性载流子（active carriers）远离莫尔界面（moiré interface）时。

Method: 采用哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）计算方法，扫描层数（layer number）、扭转角（twist angle）、位移场（displacement field）、填充数（filling）和hBN对齐方式（hBN alignment）等参数空间。

Result: 关联绝缘体（correlated insulator）在小扭转角和中等层数（N≃6）时最为稳定，此时带隙抑制（bandwidth suppression）与波函数层离域化（layer delocalization）取得平衡。填充ν=1时，远距离莫尔条件下绝缘态的拓扑性质受电荷印记（charge imprinting）强烈影响：hBN对齐通过莫尔势（moiré potential）塑造界面附近占据价带电荷纹理，再通过长程库仑作用（long-range Coulomb interactions）作为远程静电模板（remote electrostatic template）影响掺杂的传导电子，从而倾向形成与平庸绝缘体对应的三角电荷局域化（triangular charge localization）或与陈绝缘体兼容的蜂窝状电荷网络（honeycomb-like charge network）。

Conclusion: 价带电荷纹理是远程莫尔界面调控多层石墨烯中关联拓扑的一种微观路径。

Abstract: Rhombohedral multilayer graphene aligned with hexagonal boron nitride (RMG-hBN) hosts correlated Chern phases, but the microscopic role of hBN stacking remains unclear, especially when the active carriers are displaced away from the moiré interface. Using Hartree-Fock calculations over layer numbers, twist angles, displacement fields, fillings, and hBN alignments, we show that correlated insulators are most robust at small twist angles and intermediate layer number ($N\simeq 6$), where bandwidth suppression is balanced by layer delocalization of the wavefunctions of the active carriers. Under moiré-distant conditions at filling $ν=1$, the topology of the insulating state is strongly biased by charge imprinting: the hBN alignment shapes the occupied valence-band charge texture near the interface via moiré potential, which acts through long-range Coulomb interactions as a remote electrostatic template for doped conduction electrons. Depending on the alignment, this template favors either triangular charge localization associated with trivial insulators or honeycomb-like charge networks compatible with Chern insulators. Our results identify valence-band charge textures as a microscopic route by which a remote moiré interface controls correlated topology in multilayer graphene.

</details>


### [168] [Mixed Floquet Lattice model for gapless topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20378)
*Goutham Vinjamuri,Ashutosh Dubey,Ankur Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了由两个不可公度驱动（incommensurate drives）在弗洛凯合成维度（Floquet synthetic dimensions）中实现时间反演破缺的外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal），发现混合弗洛凯晶格（mixed Floquet lattice）仅能在动量分辨（momentum-resolved）意义上捕获外尔半金属拓扑，而整体实空间响应遵循赖斯-梅尔型（Rice-Mele-type）泵浦结构，表明半金属相不能直接移植到弗洛凯合成维度框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间反演破缺的外尔半金属如何在弗洛凯合成维度中实现，并考察驱动合成晶格中的拓扑频率转换（topological frequency conversion）行为。关键在于检验已有的全能隙拓扑绝缘体（fully gapped topological insulators）的弗洛凯合成维度方法能否直接推广到无能隙半金属体系。

Method: 构建一个在一维真实空间加两个合成维度（1 real + 2 synthetic）的混合维晶格模型，其中两个不可公度驱动相位作为合成动量（synthetic momenta），生成混合弗洛凯能带结构中的外尔点（Weyl points）。利用能带简并（band degeneracies）相关的拓扑性质，分析两个驱动之间的能量转移。

Result: 在固定真实动量 $k_x$ 下，功率转移（power transfer）测量了 $k_x$ 分辨的陈数（Chern number）并检测外尔节点（Weyl nodes）的分离；但总功率转移不重现静态外尔半金属相图，而是遵循有效的赖斯-梅尔型泵浦结构。这表明混合弗洛凯晶格仅在动量分辨意义下捕获外尔半金属拓扑，整体实空间响应存在本质差异。

Conclusion: 与全能隙拓扑绝缘体不同，无能隙半金属相不能直接翻译到弗洛凯合成维度。研究揭示了受驱动外尔系统独特的动力学相结构，并建立了混合弗洛凯晶格作为探索非平衡无能隙拓扑（non-equilibrium gapless topology）的平台。

Abstract: We investigate the realization of a time-reversal-broken Weyl semimetal in Floquet synthetic dimensions generated by two incommensurate drives, in the spirit of topological frequency conversion in driven synthetic lattices PRX 7, 041008 (2017). The system is described by a one-dimensional lattice model in a mixed $(1~\mathrm{real}+2~\mathrm{synthetic})$-dimensional setting, where the driving phases act as synthetic momenta and generate Weyl points in the mixed Floquet band structure. Using the topology associated with these band degeneracies, we analyze the energy transfer between the two drives. We find that the mixed Floquet lattice captures the Weyl-semimetal topology only in a momentum-resolved sense: for fixed real momentum $k_x$, the power transfer measures the $k_x$-resolved Chern number and detects the separation of the Weyl nodes. However, the full real-space response is qualitatively different. The total power transfer does not reproduce the static Weyl-semimetal phase diagram, but instead follows an effective Rice-Mele-type pumping structure. Thus, in contrast to fully gapped topological insulators, gapless semimetallic phases do not straightforwardly translate to Floquet synthetic dimensions. Our results reveal a distinct dynamical phase structure of driven Weyl systems and establish mixed Floquet lattices as a platform for exploring non-equilibrium gapless topology.

### [169] [Fourier-Helgason transform as infinite geodesic time limit in geometric quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20290)
*Ana Cristina Ferreira,Joachim Hilgert,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文解决了非紧对称空间 $G/K$ 上傅里叶-赫尔加森变换（Fourier-Helgason transform, FH 变换）与几何量子化（geometric quantization）之间在 $G$ 非复时的分歧，通过引入无限时间极限下的量子测地线变换（quantum geodesic transform, QGT），证明了该变换在相因子修正下与 FH 变换等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lisiecki（1987）发现，对于非复 Lie 群（noncomplex Lie groups），Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg（BKS）配对与 FH 变换不等价且非酉（nonunitary），这与复情形的几何解释形成矛盾。本文旨在解决这一分歧。

Method: 首先证明水平极化（horizontal polarization）是垂直极化在测地流（geodesic flow）推动下的无限时间极限；然后将测地流提升为量子丛上的交错酉平行输运，称为量子测地线变换（QGT）；最后证明 QGT 在测地时间趋于无穷时存在良定义极限。

Result: QGT 的无穷时间极限在 Harish-Chandra $c$-函数（Harish-Chandra $c$-function）的相位修正和一个无关乘法常数下，精确等于 FH 变换。

Conclusion: 本文成功将 FH 变换纳入几何量子化框架，消除了 $G$ 为复与非复情形之间的理论不一致性，为调和分析与几何量子化之间建立了统一联系。

Abstract: The Fourier-Helgason (FH) transform for a noncompact symmetric space $G/K$ establishes the direct integral decomposition of the unitary representation of $G$ on $L^2(G/K)$ into irreducible principal series representations.
  By applying techniques of geometric quantization to the symplectic manifold $T^*(G/K),$ Lisiecki in 1987 gave a geometric interpretation of the FH transform in the case when $G$ is complex. He defined for general $G$ a ''horizontal'' polarization on $T^*(G/K)$ and showed that, for complex $G$, the Blattner-Kostant-Sternberg (BKS) pairing between the Schrödinger vertical polarization Hilbert space, $L^2(G/K)$, and the Hilbert space of horizontally polarized functions coincides with the FH transform. However, in the same paper, Lisiecki showed that for noncomplex Lie groups the BKS pairing is nonequivalent to the FH transform and nonunitary in general.
  In the present paper, we resolve this discrepancy between the FH transform and geometric quantization in the case when $G$ is not complex.
  First, we show that the horizontal polarization is the infinite-time limit of the push-forward of the vertical polarization with respect to the geodesic flow for a $G$-invariant Riemannian metric. Then we lift the geodesic flow to an intertwining unitary parallel transport on the quantum bundle that we call quantum geodesic transform (QGT). Finally we show that the QGT has a well-defined limit, as the geodesic time goes to infinity, and that it is equal, up to the phase of the Harish-Chandra $c$-function and an irrelevant multiplicative constant, to the FH transform.

</details>

Method: 基于理论分析提出假设：一个世纪前发生的罕见极高能（数十PeV）相对论性中子双束喷发事件是远距离TeV伽马信号的来源。中子束在远距离飞行中通过β衰变产生电子，电子再通过逆康普顿散射与星际红外光子相互作用产生硬伽马射线。

Conclusion: SS433中观测到的意外远距离TeV伽马双束信号可能是过去一个世纪内罕见的高能中子双束喷发事件的遗迹，而非当前内部喷流过程的直接产物。该机制涉及中子β衰变与逆康普顿散射的级联过程。

Abstract: The SS433, a well-known binary system with an internal black hole, have shown since half a century, an inner (a few year light distances) twin precessing jets spirals. These beams are made by tidal forces while stripping mass from large stellar companion feeding an inner BH accretion disk and an orthogonal accelerating twin jet. From it, the radio, X gamma jet emission. A couple of years ago H.E.S.S telescope as well as HAWC and LHAASO array detectors, discovered also the surprising signature of an unexpected far twin separated gamma beam at tens TeV energy. At a hundred light years distances from its central source. We suggest that it is the legacy of a past rare eruption, a century ago, of tens PeV (10^16 eV) relativistic twin neutron beams. Their beta decay in flight at far distances, into proton, neutrino and in particular into tens TeV electrons, could feed the observed TeV gamma traces. They are originated by the same secondary tens TeV electrons emitting hard gamma, by Inverse Compton Scattering onto interstellar infrared photons.

### [171] [The t-Split Two-Periodic Aztec Diamond Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19507)
*Meredith Shea*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种将阿兹特克钻石模型（Aztec diamond model）划分为两个不等大区域（分别称为主导侧与非主导侧）并赋予不同二周期权重（two-periodic weighting）的变体——t-分裂二周期阿兹特克钻石（t-split two-periodic Aztec diamond）。推导了该模型的关联核（correlation kernel）的积分表达式，给出了标度极限行为的部分描述及剩余部分的猜想。主导侧的极限形状仅取决于自身权重，与非分裂情形相同；而非主导侧的极限形状则同时依赖于两侧权重及界面位置。最后，讨论了主导侧二周期参数趋于0时的完整极限形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往工作仅关注将阿兹特克钻石模型等分为两个区域并施加不同二周期权重的情形（即分裂二周期阿兹特克钻石模型）。本研究将其推广至两个区域不等大的情况，以探索不对称分割对极限形状和标度极限行为的影响。

Method: 采用t-分裂二周期阿兹特克钻石模型，其中两个子区域的大小渐近固定且不等。推导了模型关联核的积分表达式，并基于此分析标度极限行为。对于标度极限的完整描述，给出了部分结果和一个猜想。

Result: 主导侧的极限形状仅由其自身权重决定，与未分裂的二周期阿兹特克钻石模型相同；非主导侧则展现出依赖两侧权重及界面位置的新型极限形状。当主导侧二周期参数趋于0时，给出了完整的极限形状描述。

Conclusion: 不对称分割下的二周期阿兹特克钻石模型揭示了非主导侧依赖于全局参数的新型极限形状，丰富了阿兹特克钻石模型家族中非对称权重配置的相图。

Abstract: In this work we consider an Aztec diamond model split into two unequal regions which are asymptotically fixed in size. Each region is weighted with a distinct two-periodic weighting. We refer to this model as the t-split two-periodic Aztec diamond, to signify its difference from the previous work title Split Two-Periodic Aztec Diamond, where the model was split into two equal regions. We derive an integral expression for the correlation kernel of the model and give a partial description of the scaling limit behavior, along with a conjecture for the remainder. We refer to the larger and smaller sides of the model as the dominant and non-dominant sides, and to the location of the weight change as the interface. The dominant side exhibits a limit shape that depends only on its own weighting and is identical to that of the two-periodic Aztec diamond, while the non-dominant side appears to have a novel limit shape that depends on both weightings and the location of the interface. Lastly, we consider the complete limit shape in the case where the dominant side two-periodic parameter goes to 0.

</details>

### [172] [Mass Extinctions by Gravitational Tides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17105)
*Daniele Fargion*

Main category: physics.pop-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出外太阳系中的矮行星或行星质量天体因引力摄动偶尔进入内太阳系，与早期地球发生擦边飞越或近地交会，留下强烈潮汐印记（巨浪、大规模火山活动、海退、流星雨和气候扰动），这些机制可能在过去6亿年间多次导致生物大灭绝，并在更早的地球历史中反复发生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于观测证据表明外太阳系存在大量行星质量或矮行星天体，以及月球形成需要早期地球与火星大小天体碰撞的假说，作者试图论证更可能发生的擦边飞越事件而非直接撞击，可以解释地质记录中与生物大灭绝相关的多种异常现象。

Method: 本文采用综述性论证方法，综合近期与历史观测证据、地质记录中的相关性分析以及天体动力学机制，提出擦边飞越或近地交会事件（grazing or near Earth flybys）留下的潮汐印记（tidal signatures）——包括巨浪、大规模火山活动、海退、规律性流星雨和重大气候扰动——与过去6亿年间多次生物大灭绝之间存在关联。

Result: 地质记录中发现的特殊相关性表明，上述潮汐机制可能在过去6亿年间促成了多次重大生物大灭绝事件；类似事件在地球早期历史中也可能多次发生；此外，小型行星被大行星（尤其是太阳）吸积的事件在过去40亿年中可能更为频繁，并可能对行星及地球产生额外温度变化。

Conclusion: 与直接撞击相比，外太阳系天体与地球的擦边飞越更为可能，且其引发的连锁潮汐效应（而非单纯撞击）可能是地质历史上多次生物大灭绝的重要驱动因素，该机制在太阳系演化过程中具有普适性。

Abstract: Past and recent observations suggest that many planetary mass or dwarf planet objects may exist in the outer Solar System. Gravitational perturbations may occasionally bring some of them into the inner Solar System. The early, rare collision between the early Earth and a Mars sized body is generally invoked to explain the formation of the Moon. More probable than a direct impact, are grazing or near Earth flybys of similar objects. Such passages may have left strong tidal signatures: giant waves, large volcanic episodes, sea regressions, coherent meteor showers, and major climatic perturbations. These mechanisms could have contributed to several major biological mass extinctions over the past $600$ million years, as suggested by peculiar correlations in the geological record. Similar events may have occurred several times during the earlier history of Earth. Accretion of mini planets by largest planets and in particular by the Sun may also have occurred many more times over the last four billion years. Possibly producing additional temperature variations on planets and Earth.

### [173] [Poisson and Jacobi structures from 2-covariant tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20030)
*Manuel de León,Xavier Gràcia,Rubén Izquierdo-López,Ángel Martínez-Muñoz,Xavier Rivas*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，通过研究由非退化2-协变张量诱导的泊松结构与雅可比结构，推导出 Schouten-Nijenhuis 括号的计算公式，该公式给出了存在泊松或雅可比结构的障碍，并统一还原了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和切触几何中的经典括号，最后刻画了胖纤维丛和 p 阶几乎余辛结构确定雅可比括号的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 泊松结构（Poisson structure）与雅可比结构（Jacobi structure）在经典力学的几何描述中扮演基础性角色，且多数情况下对应的双向量场由非退化2-协变张量诱导。现有研究缺乏一个统一的框架来构建这些张量所诱导的关联括号。

Method: 在适当的张量假设下，利用特定分布的曲率（curvature）和微分形式的外微分（exterior derivative），推导出关联双向量场的 Schouten-Nijenhuis 括号公式。通过该公式刻画存在泊松或雅可比结构的障碍，并应用于辛几何、局部共形辛几何、余辛几何和切触几何等经典情形。

Result: 得到了计算关联双向量场的 Schouten-Nijenhuis 括号的统一公式，该公式以分布的曲率和微分形式的外微分表示，给出了存在泊松结构或雅可比结构的障碍条件。成功恢复了辛几何、局部共形辛几何、余辛几何和切触几何中的经典括号。进一步刻画了胖纤维丛（fat bundles）和 p 阶几乎余辛结构（almost cosymplectic structures of order p）确定雅可比括号的充要条件。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一框架能够系统地处理由非退化2-协变张量诱导的泊松与雅可比结构，其导出的障碍条件为判断几何结构是否构成泊松或雅可比括号提供了有效工具，并统一涵盖了多种经典几何情形。

Abstract: Poisson and Jacobi structures play a fundamental role in the geometric description of many systems arising in classical mechanics. In most cases, the corresponding bivector field is induced by a non-degenerate 2-covariant tensor. In this paper, we present a unified framework for constructing the associated brackets by studying the Poisson and Jacobi structures induced by these tensors. More specifically, under suitable assumptions on the tensor, we derive a formula for computing the Schouten-Nijenhuis bracket of the associated bivector field in terms of the curvature of a certain distribution and the exterior derivative of a differential form. This formula provides the obstruction to the existence of a Poisson or Jacobi structure. To illustrate the theory, we recover the classical brackets associated with symplectic, locally conformally symplectic, cosymplectic, and contact geometries. Finally, we characterize the conditions under which fat bundles and almost cosymplectic structures of order $p$ determine a Jacobi bracket.

</details>


### [174] [The alignment time function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20481)
*Marco van den Beld-Serrano*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入一个同时衡量类时向量场与函数梯度之间错位程度并惩罚零梯度的泛函，证明了在光滑稳定因果时空中存在唯一的光滑时间函数（即“对齐时间函数（alignment time function）”），并建立了其陡峭性可提升、在度量和向量场的C^p收敛下稳定、以及继承对称性等基本性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 给定一个固定的、指向过去的类时（timelike）向量场，是否存在一个时间函数（time function），使其梯度与该向量场达到最优对齐（optimal alignment）。

Method: 引入一个泛函（functional），该泛函一方面衡量类时向量场与适当Sobolev函数梯度之间的错位程度（misalignment），另一方面对零梯度（null gradients）施加惩罚。在光滑稳定因果（smooth stably causal）时空的紧致子集上，利用Sobolev指数和零梯度惩罚强度的适当假设，证明存在唯一光滑时间函数作为该泛函的极小元。

Result: 存在唯一的光滑时间函数（称为对齐时间函数）使所考虑的泛函达到最小。该函数具有以下性质：存在规范程序可提升其陡峭度（steepness）；在底流形的度量和向量场的C^p收敛下具有稳定性；继承度量和给定向量场所共有的对称性（symmetries）。

Conclusion: 证明了在光滑稳定因果时空中，对齐时间函数的存在性、唯一性及若干重要性质，为时间函数与给定类时向量场的最优匹配提供了严格的变分框架。

Abstract: Given a fixed past-directed timelike vector field, does there exist a time function whose gradient is optimally aligned with it? We address this question by introducing a functional that, on the one hand, captures the misalignment between the timelike vector field and the gradients of suitable Sobolev functions, and, on the other hand, penalizes null gradients. Our analysis focuses on compact subsets of smooth stably causal spacetimes. More precisely, we prove that, under suitable assumptions on the Sobolev index and the strength of the null gradient penalization, there exists a unique smooth temporal function which minimizes the considered functional. We refer to this minimizer as the \emph{alignment time function}. Furthermore, several useful properties of the alignment time function are established: there exists a canonical procedure to improve its steepness, it is stable under $C^{p}$ convergence of the underlying metrics and vector fields and it inherits the symmetries shared by the metric and the given vector field.

</details>

### [175] [Determination of the intrinsic mechanical quality factor in high-stress silicon nitride resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20354)
*Geena Benga,Vincent Dumont,Wei Wang,Nicola Cavalleri,Ariane Giesriegl,Silvan Schmid,Christian L. Degen,Antonius Armanious,Alexander Eichler*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合自动模式识别（automated mode identification）与系统化振铃下降测量（ringdown measurements）的鲁棒方法，用于量化氮化硅纳米机械谐振器中的本征品质因子（intrinsic quality factor $Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$）。将该方法应用于高应力氮化硅薄膜，发现$Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$随厚度存在系统依赖性，尤其在超薄极限下无法用现有模型描述。作者引入了一个包含厚度依赖损耗通道的现象学模型来解释该趋势，为理解本征耗散（intrinsic dissipation）并直接抑制其损耗通道开辟了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期通过应力诱导耗散稀释（stress-induced dissipation dilution）与模态形状工程（mode-shape engineering），氮化硅纳米机械谐振器的机械品质因数已被推至超高值，但这些机制并未改变本征品质因子$Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$。因此，直接针对本征损耗本身进行优化成为进一步提升$Q$值的未开发路径，而这首先需要可靠地量化$Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$——这一目标迄今具有挑战性。

Method: 开发了一种鲁棒的方法学，将自动模式识别（automated mode identification）与对大量机械模态的系统化振铃下降测量（systematic ringdown measurements）相结合，以量化本征品质因子$Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$。

Result: 将该方法应用于高应力氮化硅薄膜，揭示了$Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$对厚度的系统依赖性，特别是在超薄极限下，现有模型无法描述该趋势。作者提出了一个包含厚度依赖损耗通道（thickness-dependent loss channel）的现象学模型（phenomenological model）来拟合该行为。

Conclusion: 该方法和模型为理解本征耗散（intrinsic dissipation）的微观机制以及直接抑制其损耗通道开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Recent advances in silicon nitride nanomechanical resonators have pushed mechanical quality factors to ultra-high values by combining stress-induced dissipation dilution with mode-shape engineering. Neither mechanism alters the intrinsic quality factor $Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$. Targeting the intrinsic loss itself therefore remains an untapped route to even higher $Q$. Doing so first requires reliable quantification of $Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$, which has proven challenging. Here we present a robust methodology that quantifies $Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$ by combining automated mode identification with systematic ringdown measurements over a large number of mechanical modes. Applied to high-stress silicon nitride membranes, it reveals a systematic dependence of $Q_{\mathrm{intr}}$ on thickness that cannot be described using established models, particularly in the ultra-thin limit. We account for this trend with a phenomenological model that incorporates a thickness-dependent loss channel. Together, our method and model open a route toward a microscopic understanding of intrinsic dissipation and toward directly mitigating its loss channels.

</details>

### [176] [Trends, Volatility, Correlations, and Critical Phenomena in Financial Markets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20145)
*Sara A. Safari,Christoph Schmidhuber*

Main category: q-fin.ST

TL;DR: 本文基于当前市场趋势强度，通过二次多项式模型预测未来波动率（volatility）与相关性（correlation），发现在强上升或下降趋势中波动率和相关性会逐日增加，且下降趋势中效应尤为显著。该结果改进了市场风险预测，并支持将金融市场建模为近临界点（critical point）晶格气体（lattice gas）的近期提议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究利用当前趋势强度的三次多项式（cubic polynomial）建模未来预期收益，但尚未系统探讨趋势对波动率和相关性的影响。本文旨在弥补这一空白，通过量化趋势与波动率、相关性之间的关系，提升市场风险预测能力。

Method: 基于当前市场趋势强度，采用二次多项式（quadratic polynomial）对未来的波动率和相关性进行建模。该方法是对常见的均值回复模型（mean-reversion model）的精细化改进。

Result: 实证发现，在强上升或下降趋势期间，波动率和相关性会逐日递增，其中下降趋势（down-trend）中的效应更为突出。该效应可通过当前趋势强度的二次多项式精确量化。

Conclusion: 本文结果通过纳入市场趋势改进了市场风险预测，并为将金融市场建模为近临界点晶格气体的最新理论提议提供了实证支持。

Abstract: We forecast future volatilities and correlations of financial markets based on the current trends in these markets. This complements previous work that models future expected returns by a cubic polynomial of the current trend strength. Empirically, we observe that volatilities and correlations tend to increase day after day in times of strong up- or down-trends. This effect is particularly pronounced in down-trends. It can be accurately quantified by quadratic polynomials of today's trend strengths, which refine common mean-reversion models of volatilities and correlations. Our results improve the prediction of market risk by accounting for market trends. They also support a recent proposal to model financial markets by a lattice gas near its critical point.

</details>

### [177] [Electrical magnetochiral anisotropy in Rashba superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19421)
*Joaquim Telles de Miranda,Maxim Khodas,Alex Levchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文从理论上研究了二维非中心对称超导体中高阶Lifshitz不变量（higher-order Lifshitz invariants）对非互易电荷输运（nonreciprocal charge transport）的贡献，通过群论方法系统构建了允许的Lifshitz不变量及其对应的非互易电流矢量结构，并利用含时Ginzburg-Landau理论分析了涨落区间的非线性输运行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶Lifshitz不变量在具有Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）的二维非中心对称超导体中如何导致非互易电荷输运现象，填补该领域在理论层面的系统性分析空白。

Method: 采用对称性约束的群论方法（group-theoretical methods）系统构造允许的Lifshitz不变量并推导非互易电流的矢量结构；应用广义含时Ginzburg-Landau理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory），同时纳入Aslamazov-Larkin贡献（涨落诱导的Cooper对）和Maki-Thompson贡献（Cooper通道中的量子干涉），并分析无序散射（disorder scattering）和退相干（dephasing）的影响。

Result: 在超导态中，高阶Lifshitz不变量导致临界电流非互易性（critical-current nonreciprocity）；在接近超导转变的正常态中，这些项产生显著的磁手征各向异性（magnetochiral anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 高阶Lifshitz不变量是二维非中心对称超导体中非互易输运的重要来源，其效应在超导态和涨落区间均体现为不同的可观测现象，且无序和退相干会对非互易响应产生调控作用。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the role of higher-order Lifshitz invariants in nonreciprocal charge transport in two-dimensional noncentrosymmetric superconductors with Rashba spin-orbit coupling. In the superconducting state, these symmetry-allowed terms give rise to critical-current nonreciprocity, while in the normal state near the superconducting transition they generate a pronounced magnetochiral anisotropy. Using symmetry-constrained group-theoretical methods, we systematically construct the allowed Lifshitz invariants and derive the corresponding vector structure of the nonreciprocal current. To describe nonlinear transport in the fluctuation regime, we apply a generalized time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory that incorporates both the Aslamazov-Larkin contribution from fluctuation-induced Cooper pairs and the Maki-Thompson contribution associated with quantum interference in the Cooper channel. We further analyze the effects of disorder scattering and dephasing on the resulting nonreciprocal response.

</details>


### [178] [Direct Observation of Channelised Supercurrents in a Kagome Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20157)
*Matthijs Rog,Tycho J. Blom,Reinier Q. Regter,Andrea Capa Salinas,Dalal Benali,Jinwon Lee,Daan B. Boltje,Mark H. Fischer,Titus Neupert,Stephen D. Wilson,Milan P. Allan,Kaveh Lahabi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用超导量子干涉仪（SQUID）显微镜，在CsV3Sb5-xSnx kagome超导薄片中观测到由窄超流通道构成的网络结构，这些通道在临界温度出现并保持稳定，其非线性行为与约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）网络一致，从而为AV3Sb5家族中反常输运现象（如零场二极管效应等）提供了新的空间分辨解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AV3Sb5（A=Cs, K, Rb）kagome超导体展现出反常输运性质（如本征约瑟夫森结、高阶库珀配对、零场二极管效应），现有理论无法解释；当前研究瓶颈在于缺乏关于输运的空间分辨信息，因此需要直接观测超电流的空间分布以揭示其微观机制。

Method: 采用最新开发的超导量子干涉仪（SQUID）显微镜，对CsV3Sb5-xSnx薄片进行空间分辨成像，观测超电流通道的分布及其随温度与电流的变化行为，并对比掺杂与未掺杂样品的差异。

Result: 在掺杂样品中观测到窄超电流通道网络，这些通道在临界温度出现并在所有温度和电流下保持稳定；非线性行为与约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）网络一致，自然解释了已观测到的输运异常；未掺杂样品的此类现象显著弱化，表明与电荷密度波（CDW）、无序及电子关联相关。

Conclusion: 该研究为强关联电子系统中的电荷输运和竞争序（competing orders）的局域研究建立了新前沿，为AV3Sb5 kagome超导体的反常输运性质提供了新的理解视角。

Abstract: Superconductors are many-body quantum states in which current flows without dissipation. Theory predicts that supercurrents follow a relatively simple spatial pattern in both conventional and unconventional superconductors. Recent studies into the AV3Sb5 (A = Cs, K, Rb) family of Kagome superconductors indicate that CsV3Sb5 has unconventional transport properties that cannot be accounted for with these simple theories, including reports of intrinsic Josephson junctions, higher order Cooper pairing and the zero field diode effect. Attempts to interpret these findings have focused on the interplay of superconductivity with the unconventional charge density wave (CDW) order in these materials, with which superconductivity competes. A current roadblock to understanding how these kagome superconductors give rise to their intriguing properties is the lack of spatially resolved information about transport. Here we show, using a recently developed superconducting quantum interference device (SQUID) microscope, that flakes of CsV3Sb5-xSnx host a network of narrow supercurrent channels. These supercurrent channels emerge at the critical temperature and remain stable for all temperatures and currents. Their non-linear behaviour is consistent with a network of Josephson junctions linked by narrow supercurrent filaments, which naturally leads to the observed transport anomalies. Intriguingly, these observations are much weaker in undoped samples, which suggests links to the physics of charge density waves, disorder, and electronic correlations, all of which are greatly influenced by the doping strength. These results establish new frontiers for the local investigation of charge transport and competing orders in strongly correlated electron systems, and shine a new light on the anomalous transport properties of the AV3Sb5 kagome superconductors.

</details>


### [179] [Majorana modes in helical altermagnet without net magnetism and spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20259)
*Xing-Jian Yi,Yue Mao,Cheng-Ming Miao,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出在螺旋交变磁体（helical altermagnet）表面的金属纳米线上实现拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）和马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states, MBSs）的方案，无需传统的自旋-轨道耦合和净磁化，并通过规范变换（gauge transformation）揭示了螺旋框架诱导的自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）与交变磁性（altermagnetism）对时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的破缺。通过调节化学势、交变磁强度和螺旋频率可调控拓扑超导相，输运计算显示纳米线末端和畴壁处分别呈现2e²/h和4e²/h的量子化电导特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统实现马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states）的方案通常依赖自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和净磁性（net magnetism），材料限制较大。该研究旨在消除以上两项必要条件，提出在螺旋交变磁体（helical altermagnet）表面构建拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）的新路径。

Method: 采用规范变换（gauge transformation）将问题映射到便于分析的框架，证明螺旋结构可自然产生自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking），而交变磁性（altermagnetism）破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。通过调节化学势（chemical potential）、交变磁强度（altermagnet strength）和螺旋频率（helical frequency）来实现对拓扑超导相（topological superconducting phase）的调控。输运计算分别采用金属引线（metal lead）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）探测纳米线末端和畴壁（domain wall）处的电导信号。

Result: 输运计算揭示出量子化电导（quantized conductance）特征：在具有相反手性（opposite chirality）的纳米线末端检测到2e²/h的零偏压峰（zero-bias peak），在其畴壁处检测到4e²/h的隧穿电导（tunneling conductance）。

Conclusion: 该方案为寻找马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states）提供了新的视角，无需传统的自旋-轨道耦合和净磁性，拓展了拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）的可实现平台。

Abstract: We propose a scheme to realize topological superconductor and Majorana bound states (MBSs) in a one-dimensional metal nanowire on the surface of a helical altermagnet and in proximity to an s-wave superconductor, removing the requirement of conventional spin-orbit coupling and net magnetism. Through gauge transformation, we demonstrate that the helical frame naturally induces spin-momentum locking while the altermagnetism breaks time-reversal symmetry. The topological superconducting phase is well tuned by chemical potential, altermagnet strength, and helical frequency. Besides, our transport calculation results reveal quantized conductance signatures: a 2e2/h zero-bias peak at nanowire ends and a 4e2/h tunneling conductance at the domain wall of nanowires with opposite chirality, detected via metal lead and scanning tunneling microscopy, respectively. Our research offers new perspectives on finding MBSs.

</details>


### [180] [Spin transport in a normal meta-altermagnetic superconducting nanowire junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20279)
*Xing-Jian Yi,Yi-Xin Dai,Yue Mao,Qing-Feng Sun*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数方法（nonequilibrium Green's function method），构建一维纳米线置于s波超导体（s-wave superconductor）表面并与交变磁体邻近的混合体系，计算正常金属-交变磁超导纳米线界面的等自旋安德烈夫反射系数（equal spin Andreev reflection coefficient）。

Result: 在正常金属-交变磁超导纳米线界面处观测到非零的等自旋安德烈夫反射系数，证实了自旋三重态库珀对的注入。自旋输运特性可通过化学势（chemical potential）和自旋偏压取向（spin bias orientation）有效调控。

Conclusion: 本文提出的交变磁超导纳米线体系为实现无耗散自旋输运提供了一条可行途径，且体系的输运性质具有良好的可调控性。

Abstract: Spin triplet superconductors are considered a promising platform for dissipationless spin transport, where spin currents are carried by spin triplet Cooper pairs. In this paper, we propose that the spin triplet superconductivity and spin supercurrent can be engineered in an altermagnetic superconducting nanowire, where a one-dimensional nanowire is placed on the surface of an s-wave superconductor and in proximity to the altermagnet. Using the nonequilibrium Green's function method, we demonstrate a nonzero equal spin Andreev reflection coefficient at the normal metal-altermagnetic superconducting nanowire interface, thereby verifying the injection of spin triplet Cooper pairs. Furthermore, we systematically investigate the spin transport properties in this hybrid system under a spin bias. Our results demonstrate that these properties can be effectively tuned by the chemical potential and spin bias orientation. Our proposal provides a pathway toward realizing dissipationless spin transport.

### [181] [Thermal reconstruction as a method of substrate preparation for highly crystalline superconducting TiN resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20317)

### [182] [Magnetic configurations and excitations in high-$T_{c}$ multilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20533)
*Jun Zhan,Xianxin Wu,Jiangping Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过多轨道巡游电子框架（multi-orbital itinerant framework）研究双层与三层镍酸盐（nickelates）的磁基态和横向自旋激发，发现磁激发是磁有序的灵敏探针，并支持多层镍酸盐中磁性具有共同的巡游起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示双层与三层镍酸盐的磁基态和自旋激发谱，并通过与实验对比验证其磁有序的巡游电子起源。

Method: 采用多轨道巡游电子框架，结合哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）计算与自旋激发谱分析，研究双层和三层镍酸盐体系的磁有序和横场自旋激发。

Result: 双层体系中单条纹态（single-stripe state）的激发谱在Q_BL处具有各向异性的低能锥，在Γ点附近具有各向同性高能激发，与RIXS和中子散射实验定性一致；双层体系在Q_BL处的镜面对称-偶数（mirror-even）光学层间模能量与Γ处的镜面对称-奇数（mirror-odd）模匹配。三层体系中镜面对称-奇数自旋密度波态（spin-density-wave state）在参数范围内能量更低，含有一个中层的近无能隙模；镜面对称-偶数态仅有一个声学支和两个有隙光学模，与RIXS数据对比支持镜面对称-奇数自旋密度波情景。

Conclusion: 磁激发可灵敏探测多层镍酸盐的磁有序，且其共同特征支持巡游电子起源的磁性机制。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic ground states and transverse spin excitations of bilayer and trilayer nickelates within a multi-orbital itinerant framework. For the bilayer system, although Hartree-Fock calculations slightly favor a double-stripe order, the calculated excitation spectrum of the single-stripe state, characterized by an anisotropic low-energy cone at $Q_{\text{BL}}$ and isotropic high-energy excitations near $Γ$, exhibits good qualitative agreement with recent RIXS and neutron scattering experiments. We further identify mirror-even optical interlayer modes at $Q_{\text{BL}}$ whose energies match the mirror-odd modes at $Γ$. For the trilayer system, both mirror-odd and mirror-even spin-density-wave states can be stabilized near $Q_{\text{TL}}$, with the mirror-odd state lower in energy in the parameter regime studied. The mirror-odd state hosts an additional nearly gapless mode dominated by the middle layer, while the mirror-even state contains only one acoustic branch together with two gapped optical modes. Comparison with available RIXS data favors the mirror-odd spin-density-wave scenario. Our results show that magnetic excitations provide a sensitive probe of the magnetic order and support a common itinerant origin of magnetism in multilayer nickelates.

Method: 采用严格计算机辅助解析方法（rigorous computer-assisted analytical method）与固定坐标系，对四体构型空间进行约化分析，并结合数值方法给出质量比从0到+∞变化时的全局分岔图。

Abstract: We present a complete classification of concave kite central configurations in the planar 4-body problem with three equal masses. There are two different types of central configurations when the fourth mass lies inside or outside the triangle formed by the other three. Using a rigorous computer-assisted analytical method and a fixed coordinate system, we show that the central configurations in each case form a one-parameter family and obtain a complete classification of these configurations. In addition, we rigorously show the existence and types of the bifurcation points in the reduced space. We also provide two numerical global bifurcation pictures in the entire planar 4-body configuration space as the mass ratio varies from $0$ to $+\infty$, including symmetric and asymmetric concave central configurations with three equal masses.

### [184] [Odd fluids from chiral cellular automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19431)
*Andrew A. Allocca,Shiva Heidari,Thomas Iadecola,Armin Rahmani,Pouyan Ghaemi,Sriram Ganeshan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在Frisch-Hasslacher-Pomeau（FHP）元胞自动机模型基础上，通过引入手性两体碰撞规则和系统旋转粒子速度来构造手性推广模型，证明该元胞自动机在粗粒化后能够导出具有奇黏度（odd viscosity）的流体动力学行为，并通过泊肃叶流模拟验证了解析输运系数，从而在微观宇称破缺散射过程与宏观奇流体（odd fluid）流体动力学之间建立了联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 元胞自动机（cellular automaton）在格子气模型（lattice gas model）中被广泛应用于描述流体行为的微观粒子图像，但其在奇黏度流体——一种具有横向输运系数的奇流体——方面的潜力尚未被充分探索。本研究旨在通过构造手性推广的FHP模型，在微观层面引入宇称破缺（parity-breaking）机制，从而从底层实现奇黏度流体的流体动力学描述。

Method: 对经典的基于二维三角格子的Frisch-Hasslacher-Pomeau（FHP）模型进行两项修改：（1）引入手性两体碰撞规则（chiral two-body collision rules）；（2）系统旋转粒子速度以模拟背景磁场效应。通过粗粒化（coarse-graining）过程导出宏观流体方程，并利用泊肃叶流（Poiseuille-flow）模拟对手性FHP元胞自动机进行验证。

Result: 手性推广后的元胞自动机在粗粒化后能够导出具有奇黏度的流体动力学模型。泊肃叶流模拟结果验证了解析推导的输运系数，表明该手性自动机成功实现了从微观宇称破缺散射到宏观奇流体流体动力学的跨尺度关联。

Conclusion: 所构造的手性FHP元胞自动机模型在微观宇称破缺散射过程与宏观奇流体流体动力学之间建立了桥梁，为从底层粒子描述出发研究奇黏度流体提供了新的理论工具和模拟框架。

Abstract: Cellular automata are discrete dynamical systems defined on a lattice, in which each site carries a finite set of states that evolve in time according to local deterministic rules. An important application of cellular automata is in lattice gas models of fluids, where the cellular automaton framework provides a particle-based microscopic description of hydrodynamic behavior. The macroscopic fluid equations emerge after coarse-graining over many lattice sites and time steps, offering a bottom-up route to hydrodynamics. A celebrated example is the Frisch-Hasslacher-Pomeau (FHP) model, an automaton defined on a two-dimensional triangular lattice that yields the two-dimensional Navier-Stokes equations upon coarse-graining. In this work, we construct a parity-breaking generalization of the FHP model through two modifications: introducing chiral two-body collision rules and systematically rotating particle velocities to mimic the effect of a background magnetic field. We show that this automaton yields a hydrodynamic model with odd viscosity, a transverse transport coefficient that is a hallmark of odd fluids. We verify the analytical transport coefficients using Poiseuille-flow simulations of the chiral FHP automaton. Our results demonstrate that the chiral automaton introduced here provides a bridge between microscopic parity-breaking scattering processes and macroscopic odd-fluid hydrodynamics.

### [185] [Exact operator dynamics in Lindbladian Wess-Zumino-Witten conformal field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19465)
*Qicheng Tang,Ruhanshi Barad,Xueda Wen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了与外部环境耦合的开量子多体系统中物理可观测量的时间演化问题，具体针对Wess-Zumino-Witten共形场论中Kac-Moody电流模的Lindblad跳变算符，发现阿贝尔情形下算符动力学可实现精确闭合（closure），从而产生一族可精确求解的耗散动力学；而非阿贝尔情形仅在对称电流模耗散下才出现精确闭合，且仅限于单电流算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开放量子多体系统（open quantum many-body systems）在外部环境耦合下的物理可观测量时间演化是一个自然却困难的问题，精确结果仍然罕见。本文旨在通过研究WZW共形场论（conformal field theories）中具有线性Kac-Moody电流模Lindblad跳变算符（Lindblad jump operators）的系统，探索可精确求解的算符动力学。

Method: 研究基于Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) 共形场论，采用Lindblad主方程框架，其中跳变算符为Kac-Moody电流模的线性函数。通过分析这些Lindbladian生成的精确算符动力学，识别出海森堡方程（Heisenberg equations）闭合的电流算符类，并利用底层电流代数（current algebra）进行解析求解。

Result: 在阿贝尔$U(1)_k$ WZW理论中，算符动力学闭合适用于任意跳变率设置，并包含可精确处理的冷却动力学（cooling dynamics）。在非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）WZW理论中，精确闭合仅出现在对称电流模耗散条件下（向上与向下电流模跃迁率相等），且仅对单一电流算符提供简单闭合演化。一般的不平衡条件（包括冷却所需）会产生额外的非阿贝尔项，阻止算符动力学闭合。

Conclusion: 电流代数在阿贝尔情形下产生了一族广泛的可精确求解耗散动力学，而在非阿贝尔情形中仅筛选出一种特殊的可精确求解动力学，对应于无限温浴（infinite-temperature bath）的情形。

Abstract: Understanding the time evolution of physical observables in open quantum many-body systems coupled to external environments is a natural and difficult problem, and exact results are still rare. In this work, we study this problem for Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) conformal field theories with Lindblad jump operators linear in Kac-Moody current modes. We investigate the exact operator dynamics generated by these Lindbladians, identifying classes of current operators whose Heisenberg equations close and can therefore be solved analytically using the underlying current algebra. In Abelian $U(1)_k$ WZW theories, this closure of operator dynamics holds for arbitrary settings of jump rates and includes exactly tractable cooling dynamics. In contrast, for non-Abelian WZW theories, exact closure occurs only for symmetric current-mode dissipation, where upward and downward current-mode transitions occur with equal rates, and even then it leads to a simple closed evolution only for a single current operator. Generic imbalances, including those needed for cooling, produce additional non-Abelian terms and prevent closure of the opeartor dynamics. Consequently, the current algebra gives rise to a broad family of exactly solvable dissipative dynamics in the Abelian setting, whereas in the non-Abelian case it singles out only a special exactly solvable dynamics corresponding to an infinite-temperature bath.

</details>


### [186] [Norms, overlaps and Yangian descendants for the Haldane--Shastry spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20168)
*Yunfeng Jiang,Jules Lamers,Yuan Miao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Haldane-Shastry自旋链具有完全的Yangian自旋对称性（Yangian spin symmetry），其最高权态（highest-weight states）已知，但后代态的构造尚不完整，而这对于计算多种物理量是必要的。

Method: 本文利用代数Bethe ansatz（algebraic Bethe ansatz）方法，遵循Ferrando等人近期的工作，对后代态进行了详细构造；在极端扭曲（extreme twist）极限下，该构造包含了Gelfand-Tsetlin基（Gelfand-Tsetlin basis）。

Result: 对于这些态，推导出了其模方（norms）与重叠（overlaps）的乘积公式（product formula）和行列式公式（determinant formula）。

Conclusion: 本文填补了Haldane-Shastry模型中Yangian对称性后代态系统构造的空白，为后续计算相关物理量提供了数学工具。

Abstract: The Haldane-Shastry spin chain is a prototypical integrable model with long-range interactions, notable for hosting quasiparticles with fractional statistics and serving as a discrete analogue of a conformal field theory. Its remarkable simplicity is closely tied to a full Yangian spin symmetry. While the highest-weight states for this symmetry are known explicitly, a systematic treatment of the descendant states, needed for the computation of various physical quantities, has remained incomplete. In this work, we provide a detailed construction of these descendants in terms of the algebraic Bethe ansatz following recent work of Ferrando et al. In the limit of extreme twist, it includes the Gelfand-Tsetlin basis. As an application, we derive product and determinant formulae for norms and overlaps of these states.

### [187] [Space-time duality approach to (inhomogeneous) integrable quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20445)
*Riccardo Travaglino,Pasquale Calabrese,Katja Klobas,Bruno Bertini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从第一性原理解决了时空对偶方法（SDA）中一个固有的歧义性问题，并推导出了普适量子淬火后纠缠增长和电荷涨落的闭式解析预测，通过规则54量子元胞自动机（quantum cellular automaton）的精确解和XXZ链的TEBD数值模拟进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡量子多体动力学（non-equilibrium quantum many-body dynamics）的普适性刻画是本世纪物理学研究的关键目标之一，但远平衡条件下相互作用量子物质缺乏统一的理论框架。时空对偶方法（space-time duality approach, SDA）虽提供了新的视角，却存在固有的歧义性，限制了其仅适用于均匀淬火（homogeneous quenches）和对称初态下的电荷涨落问题。

Method: 作者从第一性原理（from first principles）出发，消除了SDA中隐含的歧义，从而推导出一般量子淬火后纠缠增长和电荷涨落的闭式解析表达式（closed-form predictions）。方法的核心是通过时空对偶将非平衡量（如纠缠增长速率和守恒荷涨落）映射到平衡统计力学（equilibrium statistical mechanics）与热力学（thermodynamics）框架中处理。

Result: 研究给出了普适量子淬火后纠缠熵增长和电荷涨落的封闭解析结果。通过规则54量子元胞自动机（Rule 54 quantum cellular automaton）的精确解以及XXZ链的TEBD（time-evolving block decimation）数值模拟进行了基准验证，结果与理论预测吻合。

Conclusion: 本文的工作解决了SDA的歧义性，将其适用范围从均匀淬火和对称初态扩展到一般性量子淬火场景。当专门应用于纠缠熵时，该框架自然复现了准粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）的预言，表明SDA具有统一和拓展现有非平衡理论的能力。

Abstract: Characterising the universal aspects of non-equilibrium quantum many-body dynamics is one of the key goals of this century's physics research. Progress, however, is hindered by the lack of general theoretical frameworks for studying interacting quantum matter far from equilibrium. A recent breakthrough has been the realization that several key non-equilibrium quantities, such as the rate of growth of entanglement or the fluctuations of conserved charges within finite subsystems, can be related to equilibrium properties through a space-time duality that effectively exchanges the roles of space and time. This observation effectively enables the study of non-equilibrium phenomena using tools and concepts borrowed from equilibrium statistical mechanics and thermodynamics. A first proof of principle of this framework, dubbed space-time duality approach (SDA), was provided by interacting integrable systems, where thermodynamic properties can often be characterized exactly, while dynamical quantities typically remain beyond analytical reach. Subsequent developments, however, revealed that the SDA suffered from an intrinsic ambiguity, restricting its applicability to homogeneous quenches and to charge fluctuations arising from symmetric initial states. Here we resolve this ambiguity from first principles and derive closed-form predictions for entanglement growth and charge fluctuations after general quantum quenches. We benchmark our results against the exact analytical solution of the Rule 54 quantum cellular automaton and extensive TEBD simulations of the XXZ chain. Moreover we show that, when specialised to the entanglement entropy, our framework naturally reproduces the predictions of the quasiparticle picture.

### [188] [Scaling, fractal dynamics, and critical exponents in the equilibrium phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20460)
*Adauto F. Souza,Henrique A Lima,Anderson L. R. Barbosa,Fernando A. Oliveira*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究基于Fisher的自关联函数（autocorrelation function）理论，利用现代分数阶微分分析（fractional differential analysis）揭示了标度行为（scaling behavior）、临界指数（critical exponents）与分形几何（fractal geometry）之间的深层联系，为热力学相变（thermodynamic phase transitions）中的临界指数和分形维数提供统一的几何解释，并在Ising、Potts、XY和Heisenberg模型中验证了其预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fisher在欧氏空间中引入的自关联函数及其修正指数eta，无法完整描述临界点T_c处的关联函数行为。Lima等人近期的工作表明，需要分数阶微分分析才能实现该完整描述，本研究旨在进一步揭示标度行为、临界指数与分形几何之间的内在统一性。

Method: 采用现代分数阶微分分析（fractional differential analysis）方法，结合标度理论（scaling theory）与分形几何（fractal geometry），对临界点处的关联函数进行完整描述，并在多个热力学模型中进行理论验证。

Result: 研究提供了临界指数与分形维数之间统一的几何解释，该解释广泛适用于热力学相变（thermodynamic phase transitions）。该方法不适用于缺乏局域序参量（local order parameters）及相关标度不变分形几何的拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）。在Ising、Potts、XY和Heisenberg模型中的预测均得到验证。

Conclusion: 分数阶微分分析能够统一解释热力学相变中的临界指数与分形维数的几何本质，但不适用于拓扑相变。

Abstract: Statistical methods are essential for understanding thermodynamic systems with many degrees of freedom. For systems in equilibrium, a very useful method is that of correlation functions, which establish a correlation between a field phi(x), which depends on the spatial position x, and the same field evaluated at another position, phi(x0). Fisher [Journal of Mathematical Physics 5, 944322 (1964)] introduced the autocorrelation function for fluctuations of the order parameter, which has been an important mathematical tool for understanding second-order phase transitions in equilibrium. However, his analysis is restricted to a Euclidean space of dimension d, and an exponent eta is introduced to correct the spatial behavior of the correlation function at T = Tc. In a recent work, Lima et al. [Phys. Rev. E 110, L062107 (2024)] demonstrated that a modern fractional differential analysis is necessary for a complete description of the correlation function at Tc. In this study, we highlight the deep connection among scaling behavior, critical exponents, and fractal geometry. Our results provide a unified geometric interpretation of critical exponents and fractal dimensions, broadly applicable to thermodynamic phase transitions. However, the approach does not apply to topological phase transitions, which lack local order parameters and the associated scale-invariant fractal geometry. We verify its predictions for several cornerstone thermodynamic models: the Ising, Potts, XY, and Heisenberg systems.

</details>
